Anywola mar Yesu Kristo ma nyakwar Daudi , kendo nyawar Ibrahim e ma :
Ibrahim nonywolo Isaka , to Isaka nonywolo Jakobo . Jakobo nonywolo Juda gi owetene ,
to Juda nonywolo Perez gi Zera , ma min-gi ne Tamar . Perez nonywolo Hezron , to Hezron nonywolo Ram .
Ram nonywolo Aminadab , to Aminadab nonywolo Nashon . Nashon nonywolo Salmon , Ram nonywolo Aminadab , to Aminadab nonywolo Nashon . Nashon nonywolo Salmon ,
to Salmon nonywolo Boaz gi chiege ma Rahab . Boaz nonywolo Obed gi chiege ma Ruth , to Obed nonywolo Jesse .
Jesse to nonywolo Daudi ma ruoth . Daudi nonywolo Solomon gi chi Uria ,
Solomon nonywolo Rehoboam , to Rehoboam nonywolo Abija . Abija nonywolo Asa ,
to Asa nonywolo Jehoshafat . Jehoshafat nonywolo Joram , to Joram nonywolo Uzia .
Uzia nonywolo Jotham , to Jotham nonywolo Ahaz . To Ahaz nonywolo Hezekia ,
To Hezekia nonywolo Manase . Manase nonywolo Amon , to Amon nonywolo Josia .
Josia nonywolo Jekonia gi owetene e ndalo mane odarie jo-Israel kitero Babulon .
To bang’ darogi , Jekonia nonywolo Shealtiel , to Shealtiel nonywolo Zerubabel .
Zerubabel nonywolo Abiud , to Abiud nonywolo Eliakim . Eliakim nonywolo Azor ,
to Azor nonywolo Zadok . Zadok nonywolo Akim , to Akim nonywolo Eliud .
Eliud nonywolo Eliezar , to Eliezar nonywolo Mathan . Mathan nonywolo Jakobo ,
to Jakobo nonywolo Josef chwor Maria . Maria to ema nonywolo Yesu miluongo ni Mesia .
Kamano gin tienge apar gang’wen , chakre Ibrahim nyaka Daudi , kendo tienge apar gang’wen bende , chakre Daudi nyaka chop kinde mane odarie jo-Israel kitero Babulon . Bang’e nitie tienge apar gang’wen , chakre kinde mane odargieno nyaka ndalo nywol Mesia .
Nywol mar Mesia ne chalo kama : Kane Josef osemako keny Maria min Yesu , to pok gikendore , Maria noyudo ni osemako ich kuom teko mar Roho Maler .
To Josef mane kende , ne ng’at ma kare , kendo kaka ne ok odwar kuodo wiye , nochano mondo oketh keny ling’ling’ .
To kane oyudo pod oparo wach , malaika mar Nyasaye nofwenyorene e lek , mowachone niya , “ Josef nyakwar Daudi , kik iluor kawo Maria obed chegi , nikech ich ma en gono oyudo kuom teko mar Roho Maler .
Obiro nywolo wuowi , mi ichak ni Yesu , tiende ni Jawar , nikech enowar joge kuom richogi . ”
Mago duto notimre mondo ochop wach mane Ruoth Nyasaye osemiyo janabi owacho niya :
“ Nyako nomak ich , mi nonywol wuowi , kendo nochake ni Emanuel , tiende ni , Nyasaye ni kodwa . ”
Kuom mano , kane Josef ochiew oa e nindo , nokawo Maria obedo chiege , kaka malaika mar Ruoth nosewachone ,
to ne ok oriwore kode nyaka onywolo wuode . Josef nochako wuowino ni Yesu .
Kane onywol Yesu e dala mar Bethlehem e piny Judea , e ndalo loch ruoth Herode , ajuoke moko moa yo wuok chieng’ nobiro Jerusalem ,
mopenjo niya , “ Ere jalo monywol mondo obed ruodh jo-Yahudi ? Ne waneno suluene kowuok yo wuokchieng’ , omiyo wabiro mondo wamiye duong’ . ”
To kane ruoth Herode owinjo wachno , kibaji nogoye ahinya , kaachiel gi jo-Jerusalem duto .
Ne oluongo jodolo madongo duto mag jo-Yahudi , kod jopuonj Chik , mi openjogi kama onego nywolie Mesia .
Ne gidwoke ni , “ Ibiro nywole Bethlehem e piny Juda , nikech kamano e kaka janabi nondiko , kawacho niya ,
‘ In Bethlehem manie piny Judea , ok itin ngang’ e wang’ jotend Juda . Kuomi ema jatelo ma norit joga Israel nowuogie . ’ . ”
Kuom mano , Herode noluongo ajuoke kande ling’ling’ , mononogi kinde mane sulue onenoree , mi ginyise .
Eka ne oorogi Bethlehem , konyisogi niya , “ Dhiuru umany nyathino matek , to ka usenwang’e , to duogna uru wach , mondo an bende adhi amiye duong’ . ”
Kane gisewinjo gima ruoth owachonigi ne gichako wuoth ka gidhi kendo sulue mane giseneno kowuok cha nochako othinyore nyimgi ka giwuotho , mi otelonigi nyaka odhi ochung’ kama opogore gi kama nyathi nitie .
Kane gineno sulueno , ne gibedo mamor ahinya .
Ne gidonjo e ot , mi gineno nyathino gi Maria min mare , eka ne gigoyo chonggi piny , mi gimiye duong’ . Bang’e ne gigolo mwandu mane gibirogo , mi gimiye dhahabu gi ubani kod manemane , ma gin yien moko mang’ue ng’ar .
To Nyasaye ne osiemogi e lek ni kik gidog ir Herode , omiyo ne gidok thurgi gi yo machielo .
To kane ajuoke osewuok , malaika mar Ruoth nofwenyore ni Josef e lek , mowacho ne niya , “ A malo , ikaw nyathi kod min mare mondo iring idhi Misri , kendo ibed kuno nyaka aduogni wach , nimar Herode biro dwaro nyathino mondo onegi . ”
Kuom mano , Josef noa malo , mokawo nyathino kod min mare , owuokgo dier otieno , kadhi Misri ,
mi odak kuno nyaka Herode otho . Mano notimore mondo ochop gima ne Ruoth Nyasaye omiyo janabi owacho , ni , “ Naluongo wuoda mondo oa Misri . ”
To kane Herode ofwenyo ni ajuokego osewuonde , mirima mager nomake , mi ogolo chik mondo oneg nyithindo duto ma yawuowi man Bethlehem kod manie gwenge mokiewo gi dalano , chakre johigni ariyo kaduogo chien . Noyiero nyithindo ma johignigo koluwore gi ndalo mane ajuoke osenyise ni onenoe sulue .
Kamano gima ne Jeremia janabi owacho , notimore .
Nowacho niya , “ Dwol ne owinjore e dala mar Rama , ne en nduru gi ywak malit . Rahel ema ne ywago nyithinde , kendo ne ok onyal hore , nikech ne gisetho giduto . ”
Bang’ tho Herode malaika mar Ruoth nofwenyore ni Josef e lek , ka en Misri ,
mowachone niya , “ A malo ikaw nyathi kod min mare , idog e piny Israel , nimar joma ne dwaro nego nyathi koro osetho . ”
Kuom mano Josef noa malo , mi okawo nyathi gi min mare , odokgo Israel .
To kane owinjo ni Arkelao osebedo ruoth Judea kar Herode wuon mare , ne oluoro dok kuno . Ne onyise e lek gima onego otim , omiyo ne odhi e piny Galili ,
mi odak e dala miluongo ni Nazareth . Mano notimore mondo ochop gima ne Janabi okoro , ka wacho niya , “ Enoluonge ni ja-Nazareth . ”
E ndalogo , Johana Jabatiso nobiro kalando wach e thim Judea .
Ne owacho niya , “ Lokuru chunyu , nikech Loch Polo chiegni . ”
Johana e jal mane janabi Isaya owuoyo kuome , kowacho ni , “ Ng’at moro kok e thim niya , ‘ Losuru yo ni Ruoth ! Losneuru yo moriere tir . ’ . ”
Johana ne rwako law yie ngamia , kendo ne otweyo okanda mar del e nungone . Chiembe ne mana bonyo kod mor kich mae thim .
Ji nodhi ire koa Jerusalem gi piny Judea duto kod gwenge molworo aora Jordan .
Ne gihulo richogi , kendo nobatisogi e aora Jordan .
To kane Johana oneno jo-Farisai gi jo-Sadukai mathoth kabiro ire , nowachonigi niya , “ Un nyithind thuonde ! En ng’a mane onyisou ni mondo uring utony e kum mabiro ?
Timbeu ema mondo onyis ni uselokoru adier .
To bende kik chunyu wuondu ka uparo ni ubiro tony nikech un nyikwa Ibrahim , nikech awachonu adier ni Nyasaye nyalo kawo kitegi , mi lok nyikwa Ibrahim !
Kata mana kawuono , le oseketi e tiend yien , omiyo yien duto ma ok nyag olemo mabeyo ibiro tong’ oko , mi wit e mach !
An abatisou gi pi , mondo obed ranyisi ni useloko chunyu , to ng’at ma biro bang’a nigi teko moloya , ma kata mana wuochene ok awinjora ting’o . En obiro batisou gi Roho Maler kendo gi mach .
En gi rapiedhi e lwete , ma obiro piedhogo cham duto maler . Enochok chambe e dero , to mihudhi nowang’ gi mach mak tho ! ”
E ndalogo Yesu noa e piny Galili , modhi e aora Jordan mondo Johana obatise .
To Johana notemo tame , kakwere ni , “ An ema onego ibatisa , to kendo in ema ibiro ira mondo abatisi ! ”
To Yesu nodwoke niya , “ We otimre kamano sani , nimar kamano e kaka watimo gik moko duto ma Nyasaye dwaro . ” Mano omiyo Johana ne oyie mondo obatise .
To kane osebatise , nowuok oa e pi mana gikanyono , kendo polo ne oyaworene , mi oneno Roho mar Nyasaye ka lor ka akuru , kabiro kuome .
Eka duol nowuoyo gie polo niya , “ Ma e Wuoda ma ahero . Chunya mor kode . ”
Bang’ mano , Roho notero Yesu nyaka e thim , mondo Satan oteme .
Notueyo chiemo kuom ndalo piero ang’wen , odiechieng’ kotieno mi nodenyo .
Eka Satan nobiro ire , mowachone niya , “ Ka in Wuod Nyasaye adier , to nyis kitegi mondo olokre kuon . ”
To Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Muma wacho ni , ‘ Dhano ok nyal bedo mangima nikech chiemo kende , to obedo mangima gi weche duto mawuok e dho Nyasaye . ’ . ”
Bang’e Satan notero Yesu Jerusalem , Dala Maler , mi okete e osuch Hekalu .
Nowachone niya , “ Ka in Wuod Nyasaye adier , to chikri piny , nikech Muma wacho ni , ‘ Nyasaye noket malaikane mondo oriti Ginitayi gi lwetgi , mondo kik ichwany tiendi e kidi . ’ . ”
Yesu nodwoke niya , “ To Muma wacho bende ni , ‘ Kik item Ruoth Nyasachi . ’ . ”
Eka Satan ne ochako okawe , motere ewi got marabora , monyise pinje duto manie piny , kowuorore kaka gidongo .
Nowachone niya , “ Magi duto abiro miyi , ka igoyo chongi piny , milama . ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Dhi kucha , Satan ! Muma wacho ni , ‘ Ng’ato nyaka lam mana Nyasache , kendo en kende ema nyaka otine . ’ . ”
Bang’ mano , Satan noweyo Yesu mi malaika nobiro motiyone .
Kane Yesu owinjo ni Johana osetue , nowuok modok Galili .
To ne oa Nazareth , mi odhi odak Kapernaum , dala manie dho nam Galili , e piny Zebulun gi Naftali .
Mano notimore mondo gima janabi Isaya okoro otimre .
Isaya nosewuoyo kuom piny Zebulun gi piny Naftali man yo podho chieng’ mar aora Jordan , e yo madhi nam Mediterania , tiende ni Galili piny Ogendini . Nowacho niya ,
“ Oganda mane odak e mudho oseneno ler maduong’ . Adier , ler oserieny kuom joma ne obet e piny motimo tipo mar tho . ”
Chakre kindeno , yesu nochako lando wach , ka nyiso ji niya , “ Lokuru chunyu , nikech Loch Polo chiegni . ”
Kane oyudo Yesu wuotho e dho nam Galili , noneno owete ariyo ma jolupo , ka chiko rech e nam gi tol . Ne gin Simon miluongo ni Petro , gi Andrea owadgi .
Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Luwauru , mondo kar yuayo rech to atimu joywa ji . ”
Gikanyono ne giweyo tondegi , mi giluwe .
Kane oa kanyo modhi nyime , ne oneno owete mamoko ariyo , ma Jakobo gi Johana , yawuot Zebedi . Ne ginie yie gi wuon-gi , ka giloso tondegi . Yesu noluongogi ,
kendo gi kanyono ne giweyo yie gi wuon-gi , mi giluwo Yesu .
Yesu nowuotho e piny Galili duto , ka puonjo ji e utgi mag lemo . Nolando Wach Maber mar Loch Nyasaye , kendo nochango ji duto man gi tuoche mopogore opogore .
Humbe nolak e piny Siria duto , omiyo ji nokelone joma nigi tuoche mopogore opogore , gi joma rem ohingo , kaka joma nigi jochiende gi jondulme kod joathany , mi nochangogi duto .
Ji mang’eny noluwe . Ne gia Galili gi Dekapoli gi Jerusalem gi Judea kod piny man loka Jordan .
Kane Yesu oneno ji ka ng’eny kamano , ne odhi ewi got , mobet piny kuno . Jopuonjrene ne odhi ire ,
mi ochako puonjogi . Nowacho niya :
“ Joma ong’eyo ni ok long’o e nyim Nyasaye gin johawi , nikech gueth mar Loch Polo en margi .
“ Joma okuyo gin johawi , nikech nohogi .
“ Joma muol gin johawi , nikech piny nobed margi .
“ Joma kech gi riyo mar dwaro tim makare oloyo gin johawi , nikech giniyud gima gidwaro .
“ Joma ng’won gin johawi , nikech nong’wonnigi .
“ Joma onge gi richo e chunygi gin johawi , nikech ginine Nyasaye .
“ Jothek gin johawi , nikech noluonggi ni nyithind Nyasaye .
“ Joma isando nikech tim ma kare gin johawi , nikech gueth mar loch polo en margi .
“ Un johawi ka ji yanyou kendo sandou , kawacho weche maricho duto mag miriambo kuomu , nikech an .
Ka gik makamago otimorenu , to beduru mamor ahinya , nikech pok maduong’ okannu e polo , nimar kamano bende e kaka ne gisando jonabi mane okwongonu .
“ Un e kat piny , to ka ndhath kado orumo , dochak oyud ndhadhu nadi ? Ooyo ! Koro oonge gi tich , omiyo ipuke mana oko , kendo ji nyone anyona .
“ Bende un e ler mar piny . Dala moger ewi got ok nyal geng’ore .
Onge ng’ama nyalo moko taya , to umo gi atonga . To okete mana ewi rachungi taya , mondo orieny ni ji duto manie ot .
Kamano un bende , ler maru nyaka rieny e nyim ji , mondo gine timbeu mabeyo , mi gimi Wuonu mae polo duong’ .
“ Kik upar ni asebiro ni mondo aketh Chik Musa kata ni mondo aketh weche jonabi , to asebiro mana ni mondo achopgi .
Adier awachonu ni , kapok polo gi piny orumo , to kata mana nukta achiel mar Chik kata dire achiel matin , ok nolal , nyaka chop gik moko duto timre .
Emomiyo , ng’at moketho kata mana chik achiel matinie moloyo kuom chikegi , kendo opuonjo ji mondo otim kamano , to nokwan ka ng’ama tinie moloyo e Loch Polo . To ng’at morito chikego , kendo opuonjo ji mamoko bende mondo otim kamano , ema nobed maduong’ e Loch Polo .
Awachonu ni , ka ok timbeu beyo moloyo timbe jo-Farisai gi timbe jopuonj Chik , to ok unyal donjo e Piny Ruodh Polo kata matin !
“ Usewinjo ni ne owachi ni kwerewa ni , ‘ Kik ineki , to ng’at moneko nyaka ter e bura . ’ .
An to awachonu ni ng’at ma okecho gi wadgi noter e bura , kendo ng’at monyanyo wadgi , to noyal e Bura Maduong’ , to ng’ato mowacho ni wadgi ni ofuwo , nong’adne buch mach mak tho !
Omiyo ka idhi chiwo ni Nyasaye mich e kendo-mar-misango , to iparo gi kuno ni wadu moro ni kodi gi wach ,
to nyaka iwe michno e nyim kendo-mar-misango kanyo , mi idhi ir waduno piyopiyo mondo ikwong ilos kindi kode . Eka idwogi , ichiw michno .
“ Ka ng’ato odonjoni , to winjri kode piyo ka pod un e yo udhi e bura , nikech ka ok itimo kamano , to onyalo keti e lwet jang’ad bura , mi jang’ad bura chiwi ni askari , mi teri e jela .
Adier awachoni ni koserwaki kanyo , to ok diwuogi ngang’ ka pok ichulo faini duto te !
“ Usewinjo ni ne owachi e ndalo machon ni , ‘ Kik iterri . ’ .
An to awachonu ni , ka ng’ato orango dhako , mi ogombo , to oseterore kode e chunye .
Kuom mano , ka wang’i ma korachwich ema teri e richo , to gole oko iwite kucha , nikech ber wito fuoni achiel , moloyo wito dendi duto e mach mak tho .
To ka lueti ma korachwich ema miyo itimo richo , to ng’ade oko iwite kucha , nikech ber wito fuoni achiel , moloyo wito dendi duto e mach mak tho .
“ Bende ne owachi niya , ‘ Ng’at moriembo chiege , to nyaka mi chiegeno barup weruok . ’ .
An to awachonu ni , ng’at moriembo chiege nikech wach moro amora ma ok mana wach terruok , miyo chiegeno bedo jaterruok . To bende ng’at mokendo dhako ma chwore oriembo , en bende oterore .
“ Usewinjo bende ni ne owachi ni kwerewa niya , ‘ Kik uketh kuong’ruok musetimo , to nyaka utim gima usekuong’oru ni Ruoth ni unutim . ’ .
Anto awachonu ni , kusingoru , to kik ukuong’ru ngang’ , kata gi nying polo , ni kech polo en kom duong’ mar Nyasaye ,
kata kik ukuong’ru gi nying piny , nikech piny en raten tiende , kata kik ukuong’ru gi nying Jerusalem , nikech en e dala mar Ruoth maduong’ .
Kata kik ukuong’ru gi nying wiu , nimar ok unyal loko kata mana yier achiel bed marachar kata marateng’ .
To ka udwaro wacho ni ‘ Ee’ , to wachuru mana ni ‘ Ee’ , to ka en ‘ Ooyo’ , to obed mana ‘ Ooyo’ , nikech gima okadho kanyo to oa mana kuom Satan .
“ Usewinjo ni ne owachi niya , ‘ Wang’ kar wang’ , kendo lak kar lak’ .
An to awachonu ni kik uchul kuor ni joma otimonu marach . Ka ng’ato othalo lembi ma korachwich , to lokne komachielo bende mondo othal .
Kata ka ng’ato dwaro donjoni mondo okaw sadi , to miye koda ka kotini bende .
Kata ka askari moro ochuni ni mondo iting’ne misike mael achiel , to ting’nego moromo mael ariyo .
Bende ka ng’ato okwayi gimoro , to miye ; kata ka ng’ato dwaro holo gimoro kuomi , to kik itamri .
“ Usewinjo ni ne owachi ni , nyaka uher joweteu , to ubed mamon gi wasiku .
An to awachonu ni nyaka uher wasiku , kendo ulam Nyasaye ni joma sandou ,
mondo ubed nyithind Wuonu mae polo , mamiyo chieng’e wuok ni joma richo kod joma beyo . Kodhe bende omiyo chue ni joma timbegi kare , kendo ni joma timbegi richo .
Ka uhero mana joma oherou kende , to ere pok ma uparo ni duyudi ? Donge kata josol osuru bende timo mana kamano ?
Bende ka oweteu kende ema umoso , to koro ere gima ber muloyogo ji ma maoko ? Donge joma kia Nyasaye bende timo mana kamano ?
Emomiyo nyaka ubed malong’o chuth , mana kaka Wuonu mae polo long’o .
“ Beduru motang’ mondo kik utim timbe mabeyo e nyim ji mana ni mondo gineu , nikech kutimo kamano , to onge pok ma unuyud kuom Wuonu mae polo .
Omiyo kuchiwo gimoro , to kik ihul gima itimo , nikech mano e gima joma wuondore ni ohero Nyasaye timo e ut lemo , kendo oko e lela , ni mondo ji opakgi . Adier awachonu niya , gin giseyudo pokgi .
To in , ka ichiwo gimoro , to kik iwe kata mana lueti ma koracham ng’e gima lueti ma korachwich chiwo ,
mondo tim maber mitimono kik ng’ere , to obed maling’ling’ . Eka Wuonu maneno gik motim ling’ling’ nomiyi pokni .
“ Ka ulemo , to kik ubed ka joma wuondore ni ohero Nyasaye , nikech gin gihero lemo ka gichung’ e ut lemo , kendo e akek yore , mondo ji onegi . Adier awachonu ni giseyudo pokgi .
To in , kilemo , to donj e odi kar kendi , ilor dhoot . Eka ilam Wuonu ma ok ne mi Wuonu nogo , maneno gik motim ling’ling’ , nomiyi pokni .
“ To bende ka ulemo , to kik uthor weche manono , kaka joma kia Nyasaye timo . Giparo ni Nyasachgi biro winjogi nikech wechegi mang’enygo .
Ooyo , kik ubed machal gi jogo , nikech Wuonu ong’eyo gik muchando kapok ukwaye .
“ To un onego ulem kama : Wuonwa manie polo , nyingi mondo omi luor .
Lochni mondo obi , kendo dwaroni mondo otimre e piny kaka timore e polo .
Miwa chiemo moromowa kawuono ,
bende wenwae richowa , kaka waweyo ni joma timonwa marach .
Kik iwe wadonj e tem , to reswa e richo , [ nimar loch gi teko kod duong’ gin magi nyaka chieng’ . Amin . ]
“ Ka uweyo ni ji richogi , to un bende Wuonu mae polo nowenu richou .
To ka ok uwe ni ji richogi , to Wuonu mae polo ok nowenu richo musetimo .
“ Ka utueyo chiemo , to kik ujuond wang’u kaka joma wuondore ni ohero Nyasaye timo , nikech gin gijuondo wang’gi mondo ji one maonge kiawa ni gitueyo chiemo . Adier awachonu ni gin giseyudo pokgi .
To in , kitueyo chiemo , to los alosa wiyi kendo ilwok wang’i kaka pile ,
mondo ji kik ng’e ni itueyo chiemo , to mak mana Wuonu ma ok ne ema mondo ong’e , eka Wuonu nogo maneno gik motim ling’ling’ nomiyi pokni .
“ Kik ukan mwandu e piny , kama olwenda kata nyal kethoe gik moko , kendo jokuo bende turo , mi kwelie .
To kanuru mwandu e polo , kama olwenda kata nyal ok kethie gik moko , kendo jokuo bende ok nyal turo , mi kwelie ,
nikech kama mwanduni nitie e kama chunyi bende nitie .
“ Wang’ ng’ato e taya mar ringre , kendo ka wang’e ngima , to dende duto nigi ler .
To ka wang’e ok ngima , to dende duto otimo mudho . Omiyo ka ler ma in go en mana mudho , to koro mano en mudho molil manadi !
“ Onge ng’ama nyalo tiyo ni ruodhi ariyo , nikech dosin gi moro , to ohero machielo , kata domi achiel luor , to ochayo machiel . Omiyo , ok unyal tiyo ni Nyasaye , mi kendo uchak uti ni mwandu .
“ Mano emomiyo awachonu ni kik uparru kuom gima ducham kata ma dumadhi mondo ubed mangima , kata kuom lewni ma durwaki mondo uumgo dendu . Donge ngima duong’ moloyo chiemo ? Koso ringruok donge oloyo law ?
Ok uneye winy ma huyo e kor polo ? Ok gichwo kodhi , bende ok gika cham , kendo dere bende giongego , to Wuonu manie polo pod pidhogi apidha . To un donge uberne moloyo winy ndalo mang’eny ?
Ere ng’ato kuomu ma parruok dimi ndalone medre ?
Ere gima omiyo uparoru kuom lewni ? Parieuru kaka ondanyo mae thim dongo . Ok giti gimoro , bende ok gitwang’ lewni ma girwako ,
to awachonu ni kata mana Solomon gi mwandune duto mathothgo ne ok nyal rwakore maber ka ondanyo .
To ka lum aluma mae thim , ma kawuono nitie , to kiny ipudho kendo ibolo e mach , ema Nyasaye rwako maber kamano , to koro donge doket chunye moloyo kuom rwakou ? Yaye , un joma nigi yie matin-gi !
Emomiyo , kik uparru , kupenjoru ni , ‘ Wabiro chamo ang’o ? ’ Kata ni , ‘ Wabiro madho ang’o ? ’ Kata ni , ‘ Wabiro rwako ang’o ? ’
Mago e gik ma joma kia Nyasaye chandore kadwaro . Un to Wuonu manie polo ong’eyo ni onego uyudgi duto .
To mokwongo dwaruru mondo Loch Nyasaye obedie , kendo utim gik ma Nyasaye dwaro , eka gigo duto nomednu .
Kuom mano , kik uparru kuom gik ma kiny notimre kiny , nikech kiny nobed gi mage owuon . Odiechieng’ kodiechieng’ nigi chandruokne morome .
“ Kik ung’ad ni ji bura , mondo un bbende kik ng’adnu bura ,
nikech yo ma ung’adoe ni ji bura , e yo ma un bende nong’adnue bura , kendo rapim ma upimoe ema un bende nopimnue .
Marang’o ineno mana pilni yath manie wang wadu , to yath maduong’ manie wang’i iwuon to otami neno ?
Ere kaka diwach ni wadu ni , ‘ We agolni pilni yath manie wang’i , ’ ka into yath maduong’ ngolni e wang’i ?
In miwuondori awuondani ! Kwong igol yath maduong’ manie wang’i iwuon , eka ininen maler mondo igol pilni yath manie wang’ wadu !
“ Kik umi guogi gik maler , nimar dipo ka gilokore , gikayou . Bende kik ubol kiteu ma nengogi tek ni nguruwe , nono to ginyonogi gi tiendgi .
“ Kwauru , eka nomiu , kendo dwaruru , eka unuyudi , bende dwong’uru eka noyawnu ;
nikech ng’at mokwayo ema yudo , kendo ng’at modwaro ema nwang’o , bende ng’at modwong’o ema iyawone .
“ Bende nitie ng’ato kwomu , ma , ka nyathine okwaye kuon , to omiye kidi ?
Kata kokwaye rech , to omiye thuol ?
Koro , ka un joma richo kama ema ung’eyo miyo nyithindu gik mabeyo , to Wuonu mae polo donge dibed mamor kuom chiwo gik moko mabeyo ni joma okwaye ?
“ Pile timuru ni jowadu mana kaka duher mondo gin bende gitimnu . Mano e tiend Chik Musa gi tiend puonj Jonabi .
“ Donjuru e rangach madiny , nikech yo madhi e tho lach , bende rangach midonjogo kuno duong’ kendo joma luwe ng’eny .
To yo madhi e ngima diny , bende rangach midonjogo tin , kendo joma nwang’e nok .
“ Beduru motang’ ni jonabi mag miriambo , mabiro iru korwakore gi lep rombe , to chutho gin mana ondiegi mangemo !
Unung’e joma kamago mana gi olemo ma ginyago . Bende ji nyalo pono olemb mzabibu kuom kudho ? Koso digipon ng’owo kuom oriang’ , ka ok mana kuom yiend olemo ?
Yien mabeyo nyago olemo mabeyo , to yien maricho nyago olemo maricho .
Yath maber ok nyal nyago olemo maricho , kendo yath marach ok nyal nyago olemo mabeyo .
To yath ka yath ma ok nyag olemo mabeyo iting’o mi wit e mach .
Mano emomiyo awacho ni , unung’e joma kamago mana gi olemo ma ginyago .
“ Kik upar ni ji duto ma luonga ni , ’ Ruoth , Ruoth , ’ ema nodonji e Piny Ruodh Polo . Ooyo , joma timo gik ma Wuora manie polo dwaro kende ema nodonji .
Ka chieng’ giko ochopo , to ji mathoth nowachna niya , ‘ Ruoth ! Ruoth ! Donge ne wakoro wach e nyingi , kendo wagolo jochiende e nyingi ? Koso donge e nyingi ema ne watimoe honni ? ’
Eka anawachnigi niya , ‘ Ne ok ang’eyou ngang’ ! Ayeuru kuoma un jorichogi ! ’
“ Mano emomiyo ng’at mowinjo wechenagi , mi orito , chalo gi ng’at mariek mane ogero ode ewi lwanda .
Koth ne ochwe maduong’ , mi ohula omol , kendo yamo bende nokudho mogoyo odno , to ne ok opodho , nikech mise mare ne oketi e wi lwanda .
To ng’at ma winjo wechegi , to ok omako , chalo gi ng’at mofuwo mane ogero ode ewi kuoyo .
Koth ne ochue maduong’ , mi ohula omol , kendo yamo bende nokudho mogoyo odno , mi oruombore piny matek ! ”
Kane Yesu osetieko wacho wechego duto , ji ne owuoro puonjne ,
nimar ne ok opuonj kaka jopuonjgi mag Chik puonjo , to ne opuonjo ka ng’at man gi teko .
Kane Yesu oselor oa e got , oganda maduong’ noluwe .
Jadhoho moro nodhi ire mogoyo chonge piny , kawachone niya , “ Jaduong’ , ang’eyo ni inyalo changa , ka ihero timo kamano . ”
Yesu norieyo lwete , momule , kawachone ni , “ Ee , ayie ! Changi , ibed mangima . ” Gikanyono dhohone ne ochango .
Eka Yesu nowachone niya , “ Kik ihul ni ng’ato wachni , to dhiyo ir jadolo mondo orang dendi . Bang’e itim misango mane Musa ogolo chikne mondo otim . Mano biro nyiso ji duto ni koro ichango . ”
Yesu nodonjo Kapernaum , mi jaduong’ lweny moro ma ja-Rumi nobiro ire mohombe mondo okonye , kawacho niya ,
“ Jaduong’ , jatichna nindo e oda kucha , to en gi tuo athany , kendo rem rame malich . ”
Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Ayie . Abiro dhi mondo achange . ”
To jaduong’ lweny nowachone niya , “ Ooyo , jaduong , an ok owinjore idonj e bwo tat oda , to wach mana wach kende , to jatichna biro kwo .
Ang’eyo kamano nikech an bende an ng’at michiko , to an awuon bende an gi askeche ma achiko . Ka awacho ni moro ni , ‘ Dhiyo ! ’ to odhi , kendo ka awacho ni machielo ni , ‘ Bi ! ’ to obiro . Jatichna bende ka awachone ni , ‘ Tim kama’ to otimo . ”
Kane Yesu owinjo kamano , ne owuoro , mi owacho ni joma ne luwe niya , “ Adiera awachonu ni pok anenoe yie machal gi mar ng’atni , kata mana kuom jo-Israel .
Bende awachonu ni ji mang’eny nobi koa yo wuokchieng’ gi yo podho chieng’ , kendo ginibed e Piny Ruodh Polo , ka gichiemo gi Ibrahim gi Isaka kod Jakobo .
To joma ne onego bed kuno nowit oko e mudho mandiwa , kama ywagruok gi muodo lak nitie . ”
Eka Yesu nowacho ni jaduong’ lweny niya , “ Koro dhi adhiya dala ! Kaka iseyieno e kaka gino mondo otimreni . ” Kamano jatichne nochango mana gikanyono .
Yesu nodhi e od Petro , mi oyudo ka min chi Petro nindo , ka nigi midhusu .
Yesu nomako lwet dhakono , mi midhusu mane en-go orumo , kendo noa malo , motiyonigi .
Kane piny ochopo odhiambo , ji nokelo joma thoth man gi jochiende ir Yesu , mi Yesu nogolo jochiendego mana gi wach kende , kendo nochango joma tuo duto .
Mano notimore mondo ochop gima janabi Isaya nosewacho niya , “ En owuon ne okawo midekrewa , kendo noting’o tuochewa . ”
Kane Yesu oneno oganda maduong’ kolwore , nowacho ni jopuonjrene mondo ging’ad nam , gidhi loka machielo .
To japuonj Chik moro nobiro ire , mowachone niya , “ Japuonj , ayie luwi kamoro amora midhiye . ”
To Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Bwe nigi buchegi , kendo winy bende nigi utgi . Wuod Dhano to onge kata gi kama ketie wiye . ”
Eka ng’at moro , mane achiel kuom jopuonjre Yesu , nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Jaduong’ , yiena mondo akwong adog ayik wuora , eka anabi aluwi . ”
Yesu to ne odwoke ni , “ We joma otho oyik jogi motho . In to luwa ! ”
Yesu nodonjo e yie , mi jopuonjrene nodhi kode .
To ahiti malich notugore e nam , mi apaka oimo yie . Yesu to noyudo nindo otero .
Jopuonjrene nosudo ire , mochiewe , kawachone niya , “ Ruoth ! Reswa , watho ! ”
Yesu nodwokogi kapenjogi ni , “ Ere gima omiyo uluor , un joma nigi yie matin-gi ? ” Eka noa malo , mokwero ahiti kod apaka , mi nam okue thi !
Ne giwuoro giduto , ka gipenjore niya , “ Ng’atni en ng’at manadi , ma kata mana yamo gi apaka winje awinjani ? ”
Kane Yesu osechopo loka machielo , e piny jo-Gadara , ji ariyo mowuok kar yiko jomotho nobiro ire . Jogo ne nigi jochiende , kendo ne giger , ma onge ng’ama ne nyalo kadho kanyo .
Ne gigoyo koko ka giwacho niya , “ Yaye , Wuod Nyasaye , ilaro ang’o kodwa ? Koso isebiro mondo isandwa kapok ndalo moketi ochopo ? ”
To kueth maduong’ mag ngurue noyudo kwayo mochwalore gi kanyo .
Jochiendego nokwayo Yesu niya , “ Ka iriembowa , to terwa ir ngurue kande mondo wadonj kuomgi . ”
Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Ara , dhiuru ! ” Omiyo ne gidhi , mi gidonjo kuom nguruego kendo kuethno duto noringo matek , karidore nyaka ei nam , mi pi onegogi pep .
Jokwadh nguruego noringo matek , modok dala , mi ohulo wachno duto , to moloyo ne gihulo gima notimore ni joma ne nigi jochiende .
Kuom mano jogweng’no duto nowuok mondo one Yesu , to kane ginene , ne gikwaye mondo oa e gweng’gi .
Yesu noidho yie , modok loka machielo , mi odhi dalagi .
Ji moko nokelo ng’at man gi tuo athany ire , koting’o e ng’angu . Kane Yesu oneno yie ma jogo nigo , nowacho ni ng’atno niya , “ Bed gi kue ! Richoni oweni . ”
To jopuonj Chik moko noparo e chunygi giwegi ni , “ Jali yanyo Nyasaye ! ”
To Yesu nong’eyo gima giparo , omiyo nowachonigi niya , “ Mar ang’o uparo gik maricho kamago e chunyu ?
Ere gima yot kuom weche ariyogo ? Wacho ni ‘ Richoni oweni’ ? Koso wacho ni , ‘ Chung mondo iwuothi idhi’ ?
To koro abiro nyisou adier ni Wuod Dhano nigi teko mar weyo ni ji richo e piny ka . ” Eka nowacho ni ng’at matuono niya , “ Chung’ ikaw ng’anguni , mondo idog dala . ”
Ng’atno nochung’ , modhi dala .
Kane ji oneno gima otimore , ne giluor , mi gipako Nyasaye kuom miyo dhano teko ma kamano .
Yesu noa kanyo , kendo kane oyudo owuotho , noneno jasol osuru moro miluongo ni Mathayo , kobet kar solo osuru . Yesu nowachone ni , “ Luwa ! ” mi Mathayo noa malo , moluwe .
Bang’e , kane Yesu chiemo e od Mathayo , josol osuru mang’eny kod joricho nobiro , mochiemo kode , kaachiel gi jopuonjrene .
Jo-Farisai moko noneno kamano , mi openjo jopuonjrene ni , “ Ere gimomiyo japuonju chiemo gi josol osuru kod joricho ? ”
To Yesu nowinjo ka gipenjo kamano , omiyo nowachonigi niya , “ Joma ngima ok dwar jathieth , to mak mana joma tuo ema dwaro .
Dhiuru mondo upuonjru tiend gima muma wacho ni , ‘ Ok adwar mondo ji otimna misango , to adwaro mana ni mondo gibed mang’won . ’ . Ne ok abiro mondo aluong joma kare , to abiro mana ni mondo aluong joricho . ”
Bang’e jopuonjre mag Johana Jabatiso nobiro ir Yesu , mopenje niya , “ Ere gima omiyo wan gi jo-Farisai watueyo chiemo pile , to jopuonjreni to ok tim kamano ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Uparo ni wend kisera nyalo bedo mokuyo , ka wuon kisera pod ni kodgi ? Ngang’ ! Mano ok nyalre ! To ndalo biro ma nogolie wuon kisera kuomgi , eka ginitue chiemo .
“ Onge ng’ama nyalo bawo law moti gi rabaw manyien , nikech rabawno dijow lawno , mi med yieche moloyo .
Bende divai manyien mapok ochiek ok nyal ol e ndede moti , nikech ka otim kamano , to ndede diyiechi , mi kethre , kendo divai pukre . Kuom mano , divai manyien iolo mana e ndede manyien , eka divai gi ndede ok kethre . ”
Kane pod Yesu wachonigi wechego , jaduong’ od lemo moro nobiro ire , mogoyo chonge piny , kawachone niya , “ Nyara oa tho sani , to yie ibi iket lweti kuome , mondo obed mangima . ”
Omiyo Yesu noa malo , moluwe . Jopuonjrene bende nodhi kode .
To dhako moro mane iye osechuer kuom higni apar gariyo nosudo gi yoka ng’e Yesu , momulo riak lawe ,
kawacho e chunye niya , “ Ka amulo kata mana riak lawe kende , to abiro chango . ”
Yesu nolokore , moneno dhakono , mi owachone niya , “ Nyara bed gi kue . Yieni ema omiyo ichango . ” Kamano dhakono nochango mana gikanyono .
Kane Yesu ochopo e od jaduong’no noyudo ji ka goyo asili , kendo ywak malit .
Nowachonigi niya , “ Wuoguru uduto ! Nyako ok otho , to onindo aninda . ” To giduto ne ginyiere anyiera .
Eka kane osegol ji oko , Yesu nodonjo e ot , kuma nyako nitiere . Ne omako bade , mi ochung’ .
Bang’e humb wachno nolandore e gweng’no duto .
Yesu noa kanyo , to kane oyudo owuotho odhi , muofni ariyo nochako luwe , ka kok niya , “ Wuod Daudi , yie ikechwa ! ”
Bang’e kane Yesu odonjo e ot , muofnigo nobiro ire , mi openjogi niya , “ Uyie ni an gi teko mar timo gima ukwayono ? ” Ne gidwoke ni , “ Ee , jaduong’ , wayie . ”
Eka Yesu nomulo wengegi kawacho niya , “ Kaka yieu obet , e kaka mondo otimrenu ! ”
Gikanyono wengegi noyawore , to Yesu nokwerogi matek ni kik ginyis ng’ato wachno .
To kata kamano , kane gia kanyo , ne gidhi gilando humb Yesu e gweng’no duto .
E kinde mane jogo dhi , jomoko nokelo ng’ato ma jachien oloko momo ir Yesu .
To ka ne oseriemb jachiendno , ng’atno nochako wuoyo . Ji duto nowuoro , kawacho ni , “ Nyaka nene , pok wanenoe gima kama e Israel ! ”
Jo-Farisai to nowacho niya , “ Ruodh jochiende ema miye teko mogologo jochiende . ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nowuotho e mier madongo gi matindo duto , kapuonjo ji e utgi mag lemo . Nolando Wach Maber mar Loch Nyasaye , kendo nochango tuoche duto mopogore opogore .
Kane oneno ji kaka ng’eny , nokechogi , nikech ne gichandore , kendo gidiwo mana ka rombe ma onge jakwath .
Omiyo nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Cham ochiek mathoth , to jokeyo ema nok .
Emomiyo kwauru wuon puodho mondo oor jotich odhi okane cham . ”
Yesu noluongo jopuonjrene apar gariyo , mi omiyo teko mar golo jochiende , kendo mar chango tuoche duto mopogore opogore .
Jopuonjre apar gariyogo e magi : Mokwongo en Simon , ma bende iluongo ni Petro , gi Andrea owadgi , kod Jakobo gi Johana , ma yawuot Zebedi ,
gi Filipo , gi Bartholomayo , gi Thoma , kod Mathayo ma jasol osuru , gi Jakobo wuod Alfayo , gi Thadayo ,
gi Simon ma jakedo ne piny , kod Judas Iskariot , mane ondhogo Yesu .
Yesu nooro joote apar gariyogo , kowachonigi niya , “ Kik udhi e piny joma ok jo-Yahudi , bende kik udonj e dala jo-Samaria moro amora ,
to dhiuru mana kuom jo-Israel molal ka rombe .
Kamoro amora mudhiye , to landieuru wach niya , ‘ Loch Polo chiegni ! ’
To bende changuru joma tuo , kendo chieruru joma otho , bende puodhuru jodhoho , kendo goluru jochiende . To kaka useyudo nono bende chiwuru nono .
Kik uting’ pesa matin e mifukeu .
Bende kik uting’ mifuke mag wuoth kata sede ariyo , kata wuoche , kata luth , nikech jatich owinjore gi chiembe .
“ To kudonjo e dala moro , bed ni oduong’ kata otin , to ranguru ng’at moyie rwakou , mondo ubed e ode nyaka ua .
Ka udonjo e odno , to mosuru joodno ni , ‘ Okueuru ! ’
Ka weg odno orwakou , to kue mugwedhogigo mondo osik kanyo . To ka ok girwakou to kue mondo oduognu .
To ka ng’ato ok orwakou kata otamore winjo wecheu , to teng’uru buch tiendu ka uwuok e ode kata e dalane .
Awachonu adier ni , Chieng’ Bura , to Nyasaye nokum jodalano malit moloyo kaka nokum jo-Sodom gi jo-Gomora .
“ Winjuru ! Aorou mana ka rombe madhi e dier ondiegi . Emomiyo beduru mariek ka thuol , kendo beduru mamuol ka akuru .
To beduru motang’ ni ji , nimar ginimaku mi yalu e bura , kendo ginichwadu e utgi mag lemo .
Noteru e nyim jotelo , kendo e nyim ruodhi nikech an , mi unuland Wach Maber ni jogo , kendo ni joma ok jo-Yahudi .
To ka gimakou to kik uparru gi weche ma duwachi , nikech ka kinde ma kamano ochopo , to nomiu gima onego uwachi ,
Nimar weche mubiro wacho ok nobed mau , to ginibed mag Roho mar Wuonu .
“ Ng’ato nondhog owadgi mondo onegi , kendo wuone nondhog nyithindgi . Nyithindo bende nolokre gi jonywolgi mi chiwgi mondo oneggi .
Ji duto nobed mamon kodu nikech an , to ng’ama otimo kinda nyaka giko ema nokwo .
Ka gisandou e dala moro , ro ringuru udhi e dala machielo , nikech awachonu adier ni ok unutiek tiju e piny Israel duto , kapok Wuod Dhano obiro .
“ Japuonjre ok duong’ moloyo japuonjne . Misumba bende ok duong’ moloyo ruodhe .
Ber mondo japuonjre obed marom gi japuonjne , kendo misumba bende obed marom gi ruodhe . Ka ji luongo wuon dala ni ruodh jochiende , jo dalane to koro digiyany marom nade !
“ To kik uluor ji , nimar onge gimoro amora mopandi ma ok nong’ere achien kendo onge wach moro maling’ling’ ma ok nofwenyre .
Gima awachonu e mudho , wachuru e lela , kendo gima okuodhnu e itu , to huluru ratiro .
Kik uluor joma nego mana ringruok kende , to ok nyal nego chuny . To luoruru Jal ma nyalo tieko chuny kaachiel gi ringruok e mach mak rum .
Oyundi ariyo donge ing’iewo otonglo achiel kende ? To kata kamano , onge kata achiel kuomgi manyalo lwar piny mak Wuonu ong’eyo .
To un kata mana yie wiu duto bende osekwan !
Kuom mano , kik ubed maluor , nikech un uloyo oyundi ndalo mang’eny .
“ Ng’ato ang’ata mohulo ni en ng’ata e nyim ji , an bende nahul ni en ng’ata e nyim Wuora mae polo .
To ng’at ma okweda e nyim ji an bende anakwede e nyim Wuora mae polo .
“ Kik ugal ni asebiro mondo akel kue e piny . Ooyo , asebiro mana ni mondo akel lweny .
Asebiro mondo athuw ng’ato gi wuon mare , kendo athuw nyako gi min mare , bende mondo athuw chi wuowi gi wuon odgi .
Kamano wasik ng’ato nobed mana joodgi .
Ka ng’ato ohero wuon kata min gi hera matut moloyo hera moherago , to ok oromo bedo ng’ata . Kata ka ng’ato ohero wuode kata nyare moloyo kaka ohera to en bende ok oromo bedo ng’ata .
Ng’at ma ok okawo msalape , kendo oluwa , to ok oromo bedo ng’ata .
Ng’at mohero ngimane , to ngimane nolalne . To ngat mowito ngimane nikech an , to noyud ngimane .
“ Ng’at morwakou , to orwako mana an , kendo ng’at morwaka to orwako mana Jal mane oora .
Ka ng’ato orwako janabi nikech janabino en jaote Nyasaye , to noyud pok ma janabi yudo , kendo ng’at morwako ng’at makare nikech en ng’at makare , noyud pok ma ng’at makare yudo .
Adier awachonu ni , ng’at momiyo japuonjrena moro matinie moloyo kata mana pi mang’ich omodho nikech ng’atno en japuonjrena , noyud pokne maonge kiawa . ”
Kane Yesu osetieko puonjo jopuonjrene apar gariyo , noa kanyo modhi mondo oland Wach Maber kendo opuonji e mier machiegni gi kanyo .
Johana Jabatiso nowinjo gie jela gik mane Kristo timo , omiyo nooro jopuonjrene moko ire ,
mondo odhi openje ni , “ In e jal monego bi , koso pod warit ng’at machielo ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Doguru mondo unyis Johana gik musewinjo , kendo uneno .
Nyiseuru ni muofni neno , pudhe wuotho , jodhoho ichango , joma itgi odino winjo wach , joma otho ichiero , kendo joma odhier ilandonigi Wach Maber .
To ng’at ma wachna ok chwany chunye en jahawi ! ”
Kane oyudo jopuonjre Johana koro dok , Yesu nowuoyo ni ji kuom Johana , kopenjogi niya , “ E kinde mane udhi ir Johana e thim , ang’o mane udhi neno ? Odundu ma yamo yiengo koso ?
To ka ok kamano , to ang’o mane udhi neno ? Koso ne udhi neno ng’at morwakore gi lewni mabeyo ? Ooyo ! Joma rwakore kamano iyudo mana e ut ruodhi !
To kara , ang’o mane udhi neno kuno ? Neno janabi koso ? Adier awachonu ni ne udhi neno ng’at moloyo janabi ,
nikech Johana e jaote ma Muma wuoyo kuome ni , ‘ Eri aoro jaotena otel nyimi , mondo olosni yo . ’ .
Awachonu adier ni , kuom yawuot mon duto , onge moro maduong’ie moloyo Johana Jabatiso . Kata kamano , ng’at matinie mogik e Loch Polo to oloye gi duong’ .
Chakre ndalo Johana Jabatiso nyaka chil kawuono , ji osebedo kadwaro donjo e Piny Ruodh Polo gi teko , kendo joma rateke eme donjoe ,
nikech nyaka chop ndalo mane Johana obiroe , jonabi duto kod kitap Chik Musa nosebedo kanyiso gik mabiro timore ,
kendo ka unyalo yie wachna to ubiro neno ni Johana e Elija mane okor wachne ni nobi .
Ng’at man gi it mar winjo , to mondo owinji !
“ Ere gima dapimgo tieng’ ma kawuononi ? Gichalo gi nyithindo mobet e pap , makok ni jowetegi ni ,
‘ Nende wagoyonu thum , to ne utamoru miel . Bende ka nende wagoyonu nduru , to ne udagi ywak . ’ .
Awachonu kamano nikech Johana nobiro modak katueyo chiemo kendo ka ok madh divai , omiyo ji duto wacho ni jachien ni kode .
Wuod dhano to nobiro ka chiemo kendo metho , omiyo ji duto wacho niya , ‘ Neyeuru jali ! En jawuoro , kendo jamer , bende en osiep josol osuru kod joricho ! ’ To kata kamano , awachonu ni , olemo ma rieko mar Nyasaye nyago ema nyiso ni riekone ni kare . ”
Yesu nochako wuoyo kuom mier mane otimoe honni mang’eny , korogo ni joma odakie nikech ne gitamore loko chunygi .
Nowachonigi niya , “ Yaye , un jo-Korazin ! Mano kaka unune malit ! Yaye , un jo-Bethsaida ! Mano kaka un bende unune malit ! Dine bed ni honni mane otimnu ne otim mana ne jo-Turo gi jo-Sidon , to dikoro ne giseloko chunygi , mi girwako piende gugru , kendo gibukore gi buru !
Awachonu ni , Chieng’ Bura to Nyasaye nokumu malit moloyo kaka nokum Turo gi Sidon .
“ To in dala , mar Kapernaum , iparo ni initing’ri malo nyaka e polo koso ? Ooyo , ibiro boli piny , mana e Piny Joma Otho ! Dine bed ni honni mane otim kuomi ne otim Sodom , to dikoro Sodom pod nitie nyaka chil kawuono !
Awacho ni , Chieng’ Bura to Nyasaye nokumi malit moloyo kaka nokum Sodom ! ”
E kindeno Yesu nowacho niya , “ A Wuora , ma Ruodh polo gi piny , agoyoni erokamano nikech isepando wechegi ni joma riek kod joma osomo , to isenyiso mana ji ajia .
Adier Wuora , osetimore kamano nikech mano e kaka ne long’oni .
“ Wuora oseketo gik moko duto e lweta . To onge ng’ama ong’eyo Wuoro to mak mana Wuowi , kod joma Wuowi omiyo ong’eye .
“ Biuru ira , un duto mujony kendo mugangoru mapek , mondo amiu yueyo .
Rwakuru lodi ma amiyou e ng’utu , kendo puonjreuru kuoma , nikech chunya muol kendo dembore .
Kamano unuyud yueyo e chunyu , nnimar lodi ma amiyou yom , kendo misika yot . ”
Chieng’ Sabato moro e kindego , kane Yesu wuotho e puothe mag ngano , jopuonjrene nodenyo , omiyo ne gichako jako wi ngano mondo gicham .
To kane jo-Farisai oneno kamano , ne giwacho ni Yesu niya , “ Neye kaka jopuonjreni timo gima Chik okwero ni kik tim chieng’ Sabato ! ”
To Yesu nodwokogi kapenjogi niya , “ Pok usomo gima ne Daudi otimo chieng’ mane kech kaye , kaachiel gi joge ?
Donge ne odhi e Od Nyasaye mi ochamo makati miketo e nyim Nyasaye , ma Chikwa okwero ni en kata joge kik cham , to mak mana jodolo kende ?
Koso pok usomo e Chik Musa ni chieng’ Sabato jodolo tiyo e Hekalu , ka ketho chik Sabato , to kata kamano gionge bura ?
Koro anyisou ni nitie gimoro kaeri man gi duong’ moloyo Hekalu .
Muma wacho ni , ‘ Ok adwar mondo ji otimna misango , to adwaro mana ni mondo gibed mang’won . ’ . Dine bed ni uwinjo tiend wachno , to da ok ung’ado bura ni joma ok oketho ,
nikech Wuod Dhano en ruodh Sabato bende . ”
Kane Yesu oa kanyo , nodhi e od lemo moro ,
moyudoe ng’at ma lwete otal . To jomoko ne ni kanyo mane dwaro donjo ni Yesu kuom ketho Chik , omiyo ne gipenje niya , “ Bende Chikwa oyie mondo ochang ng’ato chieng’ Sabato ? ”
Yesu to nodwokogi kapenjogi niya , “ Ka ng’ato kuomu ni gi rombo achiel , mi onyumore e bur chieng’ Sabato , donge doywaye mogole oko ?
Koro dhano to oloyo rombo nyadidi ! Mano nyiso ni Chikwa oyienwa timo gima ber chieng’ Sabato . ”
Eka nowacho ni ng’at ma lwete otalno niya , “ Rie lweti ! ” Ng’atno norieyo lwete , mi lwete odoko mangima mana kaka komachielo .
To jo-Farisai nowuok , modhi ochano kaka digineg Yesu .
Yesu nong’eyo gima ne gidwaro timo , omiyo noa e gweng’no . Ji ma thoth noluwe , kendo nochangogi duto ,
to nokwerogi matek ni kik ginyis ng’ato wachne .
Nokwerogi kamano mondo gima ne Isaya janabi okoro otimre . Nyasaye nosemiyo Isaya owacho niya ,
“ Neuru , ma e jatichna ma aseyiero . En ng’at ma ahero , kendo ma chunya morgo . Anaket Roho mara kuome , kendo enonyis ogendini duto adierana .
Ok nokogi , kata nduru ok nogo , dwonde bende ok nowinji e wang’yore .
Kata mana odundu motore ok enotur , mi owit ka gima nono , kendo ok nosim kata mana taya maliel marachrach , nyaka chop okel bura makare kuonde duto .
Kuom mano , ogendini duto noket geno margi kuome . ”
Ji moko nokelo ni Yesu ng’ato ma jachien oloko muofu kendo momo . Yesu nochange mi koro ne onyalo wuoyo kendo neno .
Ji duto nowuoro , kapenjore niya , “ Bende ng’atni dibed wuod Daudi adier ? ”
To jo-Farisai ka ne owinjo kamano , ne giwacho ni , “ Jali golo jochiende mana nikech Beelzebul ruodh jochiende ema omiye teko mar timo kamano . ”
Yesu nong’eyo gima giparo , omiyo nowachonigi niya , “ Piny moro amora ma joge opogore e kindgi giwegi ok nyal betie . Bende dala kata ot ma joge opogore ok nyal chung’ .
Kuom mano , ka Satan ema golo Satan wadgi , to mano nyiso ni opogore kende owuon . Koro ere kaka lochne dichung’ ?
To bende , ka uwacho ni agolo jochiende gi teko mar Beelzebul , kara jou to yudo teko mar gologi kanye ? Omiyo , ka mano e gima uwacho , to jougo ema biro ng’eng’ou !
To ka agolo jochiende gi teko mar Roho mar Nyasaye , to kara ng’euru ni Loch Nyasaye osechopo kuomu .
“ To bende , onge ng’ama nyalo turo od ng’at maratego , mi kaw mwandune , mak mana ka okwongo otueyo ng’at marategono , eka doyak ode .
“ Ng’at ma ok odokna , to mon koda , kendo ng’at mo ok konya choko romba , to keyo romba akeya .
Mano emomiyo awachonu ni , richo duto mag ji nowenigi kaachiel gi ayany duto magiyanyogo Nyasaye , to ayany ma ng’ato oyanyogo Roho to ok nowene .
Ng’at mowacho wach moro marach kuom Wuod Dhano , to owene , to ng’at mowuoyo marach kuom Roho Maler ok nowene e pinyni kata e piny mabiro .
“ Ka ng’ato dwaro olemo mabeyo , to nyaka obed gi yath maber . To ka en gi yath marach to oyudo mana olemo maricho , nikech yath ing’eyo mana gi olemo monyago .
Un nyithi thuondegi ! Ere kaka weche muwacho dibed mabeyo , to un uwegi un joricho ? Chutho gik mopong’o chuny dhano ema wuok e dhoge .
Ng’at maber golo gik mabeyo kuom mwandu mabeyo mokano e chunye . To ng’at marach to golo mana gik maricho kuom mwandune maricho .
“ Awachonu ni , Chieng’ Bura , ng’ato ka ng’ato nodwok wach kuom weche manono duto mosewacho .
Weche mawuok e dhogi ema nomi ilo bura , kata ema nomi bura loyi . ”
Jopuonj Chik moko kod jo-Farisai moko nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Japuonj , wadwaro mondo itimnwa hono manyiso ni in gi teko moa kuom Nyasaye . ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Tieng’ marach kendo maweyo Nyasayeni kwayo mondo otimnigi ranyisi , to onge ranyisi ma notimnigi mak mana ranyisi mar janabi Jona .
Kaka Jona nobet ei rech mang’ongo kuom ndalo adek , odiechieng’ gotieno , e kaka Wuod Dhano bende nobed ei lowo kuom ndalo adek , odiechieng’ gotieno .
To chieng’ Bura , jo-Nineve nochung’ mi donjnu , nikech kane Jona olandonigi Wach Nyasaye , to ne gilokore mi giweyo richogi , to awachonu ni koro nitie gimoro kaeri man gi duong’ moloyo Jona .
Chieng’ Bura , Ruoth madhako mar piny milambo nochung’ , kendo nodonjnu nikech ne oa kuma bor ahinya mondo obi owinj rieko Solomon . To awachonu ni koro nitie gimoro kaeri man gi duong’ moloyo Solomon .
“ Ka jachien marach osewuok kuom ng’ato , to owuotho kuonde motwo ma pi ongee , kodwaro kar yueyo , to ok oyudi .
Bang’e owacho niya , ‘ We adog e oda , kuma ne aaye . ’ . Kuom mano odok , to oyudo ka ot ni nono , kendo oywe , mi olos maber .
Eka owuok odhi oomo jochiende mamoko abiriyo maricho moloye , kendo gidonjo mi gidag e odno . Kamano achien ngima ng’atno doko marach moloyo kaka ne en chon . Mano bende e kaka notimre ni tieng’ marachni .
Kane Yesu pod wuoyo gi ji , min mare gi owetene nobiro , mochung’ gi oko , kadwaro wuoyo kode .
Eka ng’at moro nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Meru dwaro loso kodi . ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Mama en ng’a ? Koso owetena to ng’a gini ? ”
Bang’ mano nosiemo jopuonjrene gi lwete , kowacho niya , “ Neuru , magi e mama kod owetena ,
nimar ng’ato ang’ata matimo gima Wuora mae polo dwaro e owadwa , gi nyamera , kod mama . ”
Chieng’ onogo , Yesu nowuok e ot , mi odhi obet piny e dhonam , kapuonjo ji .
Oganda mane ochokore molwore ne duong’ ahinya , omiyo nodonjo e yie , mobetie , ka ji to ochung’ gi oko e dhowath .
Noloso kodgi gi ngeche kuom weche mang’eny . Nowachonigi niya , “ Ng’at moro ne odhi chuoyo ,
kendo kane oyudo ochuoyo , kodhi moko nolwar e wang’yo , mi winy obiro mochamo .
To kodhi moko nolwar kama otimo lwanda , ma lowo operoree , mi ne gitwi piyo , nikech lowo ne ok tut .
Bang’e chieng’ nowuok , mowang’o cham mapod tindogo , kendo kaka tiendgi ne ok nyal donjo matut , ne gitwo piyopiyo .
Kodhi moko to ne olwar e kind kudho , kendo kudhogo nodongo , mothung’ogi .
To kodhi moko nolwar e lowo maber , omiyo ne ginyak . Moko nonyago kodhi mia achiel , to moko piero auchiel , to moko piero adek . ”
Eka Yesu notieko kawacho niya , “ Ng’at man gi it mar winjo , to mondo owinji . ”
Jopuonjre Yesu nodhi ire , mopenje ni , “ Ere gima omiyo iwuoyo ni ji gi ngeche ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Un osemiu ng’eyo weche mopondo mag Loch Polo ; ji mamoko to ok omi ,
nimar ng’at man-go ema nomedi , bi bed gi gik mang’eny moloyo . To ng’at maongego noma kata mana matin ma en-go .
Awuoyonigi gi ngeche nikech girango gik moko , to ok gine , bende giwinjo wach , to ok donjnigi , kata ng’eyo tiende bende ok ging’e .
Kamano gima ne Isaya okoro koro timore kuomgi . Nokoro niya , ‘ Winjo to unuwinji , to wach ok nodonjnu ngang’ kendo neno to ununen , to ok unung’e tiend wach ,
nimar chuny ogandani osedoko mapek , kendo gisedino itgi , bende giseumo wang’gi . To ka da ni ok kamano , to dikoro gineno , kendo dikoro itgi winjo wach , bende dikoro wach donjonigi , mi gilokre , giduog ira , kendo achanggi . ’ .
“ To un , un johawi , nikech wengeu neno , kendo itu winjo wach .
Adier awachonu ni jonabi mang’eny nogombo neno gik ma koro unenogi , to ne ok ginyal neno , bende ne gigombo winjo gik ma uwinjogi , to ne ok ginyal winjo . ”
“ To un , chikuru itu mondo uwinj tiend ngech jachuoyo .
Ng’at mawinjo wach Loch Nyasaye , to ok donjne , chalo gi kodhi mane olwar e wang’yo . Ng’ama Rach biro , kendo maye gima ochwo e chunye .
To kodhi mane olwar e lwanda , kama lowo operoree , e jalo ma winjo wach , to yiego piyopiyo gi mor .
To wachno ok moki e chunye , omiyo ok odag aming’a kendo ka chandruok kata sand moro obiro nikech wachno , to opodho piyopiyo nono .
Kodhi mane olwar e kind kudho , to e ng’at mawinjo wach to paro mag piny gi ber mar mwandu thung’o wachno , mi ok nyag gimoro .
To kodhi mane ochwo e lowo maber e ng’at ma winjo wach , kendo donjone . Onyak maber , mana ka kodhi ma moko nyak mia achiel , to moko piero auchiel , kendo moko piero adek . ”
Yesu nogoyonigi ngero machielo niya , “ Loch Polo chalo gi ng’at mane ochwoyo kodhi mabeyo e puothe .
To otieno , kane ji nindo , jasike nobiro mochwoyo ogolo e kind cham .
Kuom mano , kane cham odongo kendo omoyo , to ogolo bende ne nie kindgi .
Jotich wuon puodho nodhi ire , mopenje niya , ‘ Jaduong’ , donge kodhi mabeyo lilo ema nichwoyo e puothi ? Ka kamano , to ogologi oa kure ? ’
En to nodwokogi niya , ‘ Jasigu moro ema otimo kamano ! ’ Eka jotichne nochako openje ni , ‘ Idwaro ni mondo wadhi wapudhgi oko koso ? ’
To nodwokogi ni , ‘ Ooyo , kik utim kamano , dipo ka upudho cham kaachiel gi ogolo .
Wegiuru aweya gidongi giduto , nyaka ndalo keyo chopi , eka ananyis jokeyo ni mondo gikwong gipudh ogolo , gitue wiye wiye mondo giwang’ e mach . Bang’e gika cham , giol e decha . ’ . ”
Yesu nochako ogoyonigi ngero moro niya , “ Loch Polo chalo gi koth karadali mane ng’ato okawo mopidho e puothe .
En kodhi matinie moloyo kodhi mamoko duto , to ka osedongo to odoko yath maduong’ie moloyo yien duto , kendo winy biro mi gedi e bedene . ”
Yesu nochako ogoyonigi ngero machielo niya , “ Loch Polo chalo gi thowi mane dhako moro okawo mobagogo mogo atonge adek , mi bang’e ochiek maber . ”
Kane Yesu puonjo ji wechego duto , to nowuoyonigi mana gi ngeche . Adier , ne ok owachnigi gimoro mak mana e yor ngero .
Mano notimore mondo gima ne janabi owacho otimre . Janabino nowacho ni , “ Anawuo kodgi mana gi ngeche , ka anyisogi gik mosebet kopondo nyaka ne piny chakre . ”
Eka Yesu noweyo ji , modonjo e ot . Jopuonjrene ne odhi ire , mokwaye ni mondo oloknigi tiend ngech ogolo mochwo e puodho .
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Ng’at mane ochwoyo kodhi mabeyo ne en Wuod Dhano ,
to puodho e piny . Kodhi mabeyo to en joma oyie Loch Polo , to ogolo e joma luwo Satan ,
kendo jasigu mane ochwoyo ogolo e Satan . Keyo to e giko piny , kendo jokeyo e malaika .
Kaka ichoko ogolo , kendo iwang’o e mach , e kaka nochok ji , mi wang’ chieng’ giko piny .
Wuod Dhano noor malaikane mondo ochok gik moko duto mamiyo ji ketho , kaachiel gi joma richo , mi ogol oko e pinye ,
kenddo owit e mach mager . Kanyo ywagruok gi muodo lak nobedie !
Bang’ mano , joma kare norieny ka wang’chieng’ e piny Wuon-gi . Ng’at man gi it mar winjo , to mondo owinji !
“ Loch Polo chalo gi mwandu mane opandi e puodho , mi ng’ato oyudo , mi ochako oyiko kendo . Ng’atno nodoko mamor ahinya , omiyo nodhi oloko gige duto pesa , mi oduogo ong’iewo puodhono .
“ Bende Loch Polo chalo gi jaohala madwaro kite ma nengogi tek ,
to ka osenwang’o moro maberie moloyo moko duto , to odhi oloko gige duto pesa , mondo ong’iewego .
“ To bende Loch Polo chalo gi tol mobol e nam , mamako kit rech duto .
Ka osepong’ , to jolupo ywaye oko e dhowath , kendo gibet piny mondo gipog rech . Rech mabeyo giketo e oserni , to maricho giwito oko .
Mano bende e kaka notim ni ji , chieng’ giko piny . Malaika nowuogi kendo nopog joma richo kuom joma beyo ,
mi witi e mach mager . Kanyo ywagruok gi muodo lak nobedie . ”
Bang’ mago duto , Yesu nopenjo jopuonjrene ni , “ Bende wechego duto osedonjonu ? ” Ne gidwoke ni , “ Ee , gisedonjonwa . ”
Eka nomedo wachonigi niya , “ Ka kamano , to japuonj Chik mapuonjore wach Loch Polo chalo gi wuon dala magolo mwandun manyien gi machon kar kenone . ”
Kane Yesu osetieko goyo ngechego , noa kanyo ,
mi odok dalagi . Ne opuonjo e od lemo , mi joma ne owinjo kaka opuonjo nowuoro , mopenjore niya , “ Rieko ma kama , kod teko mar timo honnigi jali oyudo kure ?
Donge en e wuod japecho cha ? Min mare donge iluongo ni Maria ? Koso Jakobo gi Josef gi Simon kod Juda donge gin owetene ?
Donge en e ma nyiminene duto odak kodwa kagi ? Koro gigi duto to oyudo kure ? ”
Kamano ne gisin kode . Yesu to nowachonigi niya , “ Janabi imiyo duong’ kuonde duto , to mak mana jogweng’gi gi joodgi ema ochaye . ”
Ne ok otimo honni mang’eny kuno , nikech jogo ne onge gi yie .
Ndalono ema ne ruoth Herode owinjoe wach Yesu ,
mi owacho niya , “ Nyaka bed ni ng’atni en Johana Jabatiso ! Osechier oa kuom joma otho . Mano ema omiyo en gi tekogi duto . ”
Noyudo ka Herode osemako Johana , motueyo e jela , nikech wach Herodia , chi Filipo owadgi Herode ,
nimar Johana nosiko kakwero Herode ni , “ Ok en gima kare , kawo dhakono . ”
Herode ne dwaro nego Johana , to kata kamano , ne oluoro jo-Yahudi , nikech ne gikawo Johana ka janabi .
To kane sawo mar paro chieng’ nywol Herode ochopo , nyar Herodia nomiel mamit e nyim welo , mi olombo Herode ahinya .
Mano nomiyo Herode okuong’ore ni nyakono ni nomiye gimoro amora mokwaye .
To min nyako nosunde mondo okwa mana wi Johana Jabatiso okelne kanyo e tawo .
Kane ruoth owinje gimaodwaro , chunye nodoko malit . To kata kamano nogolo chik mondo omi nyakono gima okwayo , nikech kuong’ruok mane osekuong’orego e nyim wende .
Ne ooro ng’ato modhi ong’ado wi Johana e jela ,
okelo koketo e tawo , mi omiyonyakono otero ni min mare .
Bang’e jopuonjre Johana nobiro , mi okawo ringre , odhi oyiko . Eka ne gidhi , mi ginyiso Yesu gima osetimore .
Kane Yesu owinjo wachno , noidho yie , modhi kaamoro e bath nam kar kende . To ji nowinjo kamano , mi owuok e miechgi , molworo oko gi tiendgi , kadhi ire .
Omiyo kane Yesu owuok e yie , noneno ji mathoth , kendo nokechogi , mochango joma tuo kuomgi .
Kane piny ochopo odhiambo , jopuonjrene nodhi ire , mowachone ni , “ Piny koro yuso , kendo kaeri en thim , omiyo we ni ji thuolo mondo odhi e mier , ong’iew chiemo ma gibiro chamo . ”
To Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Ok onego gia . Un ema mondo umigi chiemo . ”
Ne gidwoke ni , “ To waonge gi gimoro ka , mak mana makati abich gi rech ariyo kende . ”
Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Kelnagiuru ka . ”
Bang’ mano , nonyiso ji mondo obed piny e lum . Eka nokawo makati abich gi rech ariyogo , mong’iyo malo , kendo ogwedhogi . Ne ong’ingo makatigo , momiyo jopuonjrene , eka jopuonjrene nomiyo ji ,
mi ji duto nochiemo moyieng’ . Bang’e nokwany ng’injo modong’ , mopong’o aditni apar gariyo .
Kar romb chwo mane ochiemo ne alufu abich , ka ok okwan mon gi nyithindo .
Bang’e Yesu nowacho ni jopuonjrene mondo odonj e yie , otel nyime loka machielo , ka en to pod ogonyo ji mondo odog miechgi .
Kane osegonyo ji , nodhi e got kar kende mondo olem , kendo piny ne oyuso kapod en mana kanyo kende .
To yie koro ne ni e chuny nam , ka apaka thage malich , nikech yamo ne ogeng’one .
Yesu nodhi irgi kar koguen ka wuotho ewi pi .
To kane jopuonjre onene kowuotho kamano , ne gibwok ahinya , mi gikok ka giwacho niya , “ Macha jachien ! ”
To gikanyono Yesu nowuoyo kodgi , ka wacho niya , “ Beduru gi kue ! Kik ubed maluor , en mana an ! ”
To Petro nodwoke ni , “ Ruoth , ka en in adier , to wachna mondo awuothi ewi pi , abi iri . ”
Yesu noyiene ni , “ Bi . ” Omiyo Petro nowuok e yie , mowuotho ewi pi , kadhi ir Yesu .
To kane oneno yamo , nobedo maluor , mi ochako nyumore e pi . Ne oywak niya , “ Ruoth ! Resa ! ”
Yesu norieyo lwete piyopiyo , momake , ka wachone ni , “ Yaye ! Mano kaka in gi yie matin ! Marang’o niriwo gi kiawa ? ”
Eka ne gidonjo e yie , mi yamo okue .
Jopuonjre mane nie yie nomiyo Yesu duong’ , kawacho niya , “ Adier in Wuod Nyasaye ! ”
Kane gisetieko ng’ado nam , ne gigowo Genesaret ,
to ji nong’eyo Yesu , omiyo ne gioro wach e gweng’no duto , mi okel joma tuo ire .
Ne gihombe mondo oyie joma tuo omulie kata mana riak lawe kende . Kamano ji duto mane omulo riak lawe nochango .
Bang’e jo-Farisai moko kod jopuonj Chik moko nobiro ir Yesu , koa Jerusalem , mi openje ni ,
“ Ere gima omiyo jopuonjreni oketho tim kwerewa ? Ok gilogi e yo ma Chikwa dwaro ka gidwaro chiemo ! ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Un to , ere gima omiyo uketho chik Nyasaye mana ni mondo urit chikeu uwegi ?
Nyasaye nowacho ni , ‘ Luor meru gi wuoru’ , kendo ni , ‘ Ng’at moyanyo wuon kata min nyaka negi’ .
Un to upuonjo ni , ‘ Gik moko duto ma dakonyigo , asewalo ni tich Nyasaye’ ,
to koro ok onego okony wuon gi gimoro . Mano e kaka umiyo chike Nyasaye bedo kayiem nono , kuluwo chikeu uwegi .
Un joma wuondore ni ohero Nyasayegi ! Isaya ne ni kare kane okoro wach kuomu ni ,
‘ Jogi paka mana gi dhogi , to chunygi bor koda .
Gilama kayiem nono , nimar gipuonjo chike mag dhano , mana ka gima gin chike Nyasaye ! ’ ”
Yesu noluongo ji ire , mi owachonigi niya , “ Winjuru gima awachonu mondo ung’e tiende .
Gik ma donjo e dho dhano ok ema mi dhano dok jaketho , to mana gik mawuok e dhoge ema miyo odoko jaketho ”
Eka jopuonjrene nobiro ire , mopenje niya , “ Bende ing’eyo ni jo-Farisai nende osin kodi , kane giwinjo gima iwacho ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Gimoro amora mane Wuora mae polo ok opidho , ibiro pudho .
Omiyo wegiuru aweya ! Gin jotelo mamuofni . Ka muofu otelo ni muofu wadgi , to donge giduto ginyumore e bur ? ”
To Petro nokwaye mondo onyisgi tiend ngerono .
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Kara un bende weche pok odonjonu ?
Donge uneno ka gik moko duto madonjo e dho dhano kadho e iye , kendo wuok oko ?
To gik mawuok e dho dhano a mana e chunye , kendo mago ema miyo odoko jaketho ,
nikech chuny dhano ema paro maricho nitie , mamiyo otimo gik maricho , kaka nek gi terruok gi wuowo gi kuo gi miriambo , kod kuoth .
Mago e gik mamiyo dhano doko jaketho . To ka ng’ato ochiemo ka ok ologo e yo ma chik dwaro , to mano ok mi odok jaketho . ”
Yesu nowuok , modhi e gweng’ machiegni gi mier mag Turo kod Sidon .
Dhako moro ma nyar Kanaan mane odak e gweng’no nobiro ire , mi okok kaywakne niya , “ Ruoth ! Wuod Daudi ! Yie ikecha . Jachien marach osemako nyara , kendo thage malit . ”
To Yesu ne ok odwoke kata wach achiel . Bang’e jopuonjrene nobiro ire , mokwaye ni , “ Riemb dhakoni odhi , nikech oluwo bang’wa kogoyo koko . ”
Yesu nodwoko ni , “ Ne oora mana ir jo-Israel molal ka rombe . ”
Kane dhakono owinjo kamano , nobiro mopodho e tiend Yesu , koywak niya , “ Ruoth , Konya ! ”
Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Ok en gima ber , wito chiemb nyithindo ni guogi . ”
To dhakono nowachone ni , “ Mano en adier , Ruoth , to kata mana guogi bende chamo ng’injo molwar e bwo mesa wegegi . ”
Mano omiyo Yesu nodwoke niya , “ In dhako man gi yie maduong’ ! Gima idwaro mondo otimreni . ” Kamano nyare nochango gie sano .
Yesu noa kanyo mowuotho koluwo dho nam Galili . Eka nodhi ewi got moro , mobet piny kuno .
Ji mathoth nokelone rang’onde gi muofni gi pudhe gi momni kod jomoko duto matuo . Ne giketogi e nyime , mi ochangogi .
Ji nowuoro kane gineno momni ka wuoyo , kendo rang’onde kochango , gi pudhe kawuotho , kod muofni kaneno , mine gipako Nyasach Israel .
Yesu noluongo jopuonjrene , mowachonigi niya , “ Akecho jogi , nikech gisebet koda kuom ndalo adek , to koro gionge chiemo . To ok adwar weyogi gidog ka gidenyo kamano , nimar dipo ka nong’no oterogi e yo . ”
To jopuonjrene nopenje ni , “ Ere kama dwayudie chiemo e thim ka , ma dirom oganda maduong’ni ? ”
Yesu nopenjogi ni , “ Un gi makati adi ? ” Ne gidwoke ni , “ Wan gi makati abiriyo , kod rech moko manok matindo tindo . ”
Yesu nowacho ni ji duto mondo obed piny .
Eka nokawo makati abiriyo kod rechgo , mogoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano . Nong’ingogi , momiyogi jopuonjrene , eka jopuonjrene nopogo ni ji .
Kamano ji duto nochiemo moyieng’ . Bang’e ne okwany ng’injo modong’ , mi oromo atonge abiriyo .
Kar romb joma chwo mane ochiemo ne alufu ang’wen , ka ok okwan mon gi nyithindo .
Eka Yesu nogonyo ji , moa . En to nodonjo e yie , modhi e gweng’ Magadan .
Jo-Farisai gi Jo-Sadukai nobiro ir Yesu mondo oteme . Omiyo ne giwachone mondo otimnigi hono moro moa e polo manyiso ni Nyasaye ni kode .
To Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Godhiambo ka polo marmar , to uwacho ni piny biro lendo .
To gokinyi ka polo marmar kendo dudo , to uwacho ni koth biro chue . Ka ulony kuom rango polo kamano , mi ung’e gima biro timore , to ang’o momonou fwenyo tiend ranyisi matimore ndalogi ?
Tieng’ marach kendo moweyo Nyasayeni kwayo mondo otimnigi ranyisi , to onge ranyisi ma notimnigi , mak mana ranyisi mar Jona . ” Eka noweyogi , modhi .
Kane jopuonjrene ong’ado nam , modok loka machielo , ne oyudo ni wigi owil gi makati .
Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Yawuru wang’u mondo ubed motang’ ni thop jo-Farisai gi thop jo-Sadukai . ”
To ne gichako wacho e kindgi giwegi ni , “ Owacho kamano nikech ne ok wabiro gi makati . ”
Yesu nong’eyo gima giwacho , omiyo nopenjogi niya , “ Ere gima omiyo uwacho ni ne ok ubiro gi makati ? Mano kaka yie ma un go tin !
Wach pok odonjonu koso ? Ok unyal paro makati abich mane ang’ingo ni ji alufu abich , kod romb aditni mane ukwanyoe ng’injo modong’ ?
Koso ok unyal paro makati abiriyo mane ang’ingo ni ji alufu ang’wen kod kar romb atonge mane upong’o ?
Koro ere gima omiyo ok unyal winjo ni nende ok awuo kodu kuom wach makati ? ” Eka ne ochako owachonigi ni , “ Beduru motang’ ni thop jo-Farisai kod thop jo-Sadukai . ”
Bang’ mano , ne gifwenyo ni ok owachnigi ni mondo giritre kuom thowi , to mana ni mondo giritre kuom puonj mar jo-Farisai kod mar jo-Sadukai .
Kane Yesu ochopo e gweng’ Kaisaria Filipo , nopenjo jopuonjrene niya , “ Uwinjo ka ji wacho Wuod Dhano en ng’a ? ”
Ne gidwoke ni , “ Jomoko wacho ni en Johana Jabatiso , to moko wacho ni en Elija . Moko bende wacho ni en Jeremia , kata achiel kuom jonabi mamoko . ”
Eka Yesu nochako openjogi ni , “ Un to uparo ni an ng’a ? ”
Simon Petro nodwoke ni , “ Ine Mesia , Wuod Nyasaye Mangima . ”
Yesu nowachone niya , “ Simon wuod Jona , in jahawi ahinya ! Dhano ok ema osefwenyni wachni , to mana Wuora mae polo ema osefwenyonigo .
To bende awachoni niya , In Petro , tiende ni lwanda . Ewi lwandani ema anagerie kanisana ma en kanyakla mar joma oyie kuoma , kendo kata mana tho ok noloye .
Anamiyi rayepe mag Loch Polo . Gima ikwero e piny ka , nokwer e polo bende , to gima iyiego e piny ka ema noyiego e polo . ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nokwero jopuonjreene matek ni kik nyis ng’ato ni en Mesia .
Chakre kindeno , Yesu nochako nyiso jopuonjrene malong’o niya , “ Nyaka adhi Jerusalem mondo jodongo gi jodolo madongo kod jopunj Chik osanda , kendo onega , to chieng’ mar adek anachier . ”
To Petro nogole tenge , mokwere niya , “ Ooyo Ruoth ! Gima kamano ok nyal timoreni ngang’ ! ”
To Yesu nolokore , mowacho ni Petro niya , “ Aye nyima Satandni ! Idwaro geng’a , nikech paro mari ok mar Nyasaye , to mana mar dhano . ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Ka ng’ato dwaro luwa , to nyaka okwerre owuon , mi okaw msalape , kendo oluwa ,
nikech ng’at madwaro reso ngimane , to ngimane nolalne , to ng’at mawito ngimane nikech an , to noyud ngimane .
Ere ohala ma ng’ato nyalo yudo , konwang’o piny duto , to owito ngimane ? Koso ang’o ma ng’ato nyalo chiwo kar ngimane ?
Wuod Dhano nobin gi malaikane e duong’ maler mar Wuon mare , eka nomi ng’ato ka ng’ato pok moromo gi timne .
Awachonu adier ni nitie jomoko kuomu ka , ma ok notho kapok oneno Wuod Dhano kabiro gi lochne . ”
Bang’ ndalo auchiel , Yesu nokawo Petro kaachiel gi Jakobo kod Johana owadgi Jakobo , moterogi malo ewi got mabor kar kendgi .
Eka kite nolokore mana e nyimgi ka gineno , mi wang’e orieny ka wang’chieng’ , kendo lepe odoko matar ka pe .
Bang’ mano ne gipo ka gineno Musa kod Elija ka jowuoyo gi Yesu .
Eka Petro nowacho niya , “ Ruoth , bedowa kaeri en gima ber . Ka ihero , to abiro gero kiche adek ka , ma achiel mari , to machielo mar Musa , kendo moro mar Elija . ”
To kane pod owuoyo , bor polo marieny nobiro moumogi gi tipone , kendo ne giwinjo dwol moro ka wacho gie bor polo niya , “ Ma e Wuoda mahero . Chunya mor kode . Winjeuru . ”
Kane jopuonjre owinjo dwolno , luoro nomakogi malich , mi gipodho piny auma .
To Yesu nosudo irgi , momulogi , kawachonigi niya , “ Auru malo ! Kik ubed maluor ! ”
Kamano ne giting’o wang’gi , mi ok gineno ng’ato machielo , to mak mana Yesu kende .
To kane oyudo gilor gia e got , Yesu nokwerogi ni kik ginyis ng’ato hono ma giseneno , nyaka chop chieng’ ma ochierie Wuod Dhano , koa kuom joma otho .
Bang’e jopuonjre nopenjo Yesu niya , “ Ere gima omiyo jopuonj Chik wacho ni Elija nyaka bi mokwongo ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Adier , Elija nyaka bi mokwongo , kendo en ema obiro loso gik moko duto obed kare .
To awachonu ni Elija osebiro , kendo ji ne ok ong’eye , to ne gitimore atima kaka gidwaro . Kamano bende e kaka gibiro sando Wuod Dhano . ”
Bang’ mano jopuonjre nong’eyo ni kara owuoyonigi mana kuom Johana Jabatiso .
Kane gichopo ir oganda , ng’at moro nobiro ir Yesu , mogoyo chonge piny e nyime , kawacho niya ,
“ Jaduong’ , yie ikech wuoda , nikech en gi tuo ndulme , kendo chande marach . Pile pile ogore e mach , kendo e pi .
Nende akele ni jopuonjreni , to ne ok ginyal change . ”
Yesu nowacho niya , “ Yaye ! Ma tieng’ maonge gi yie , kendo mobam manade ! Nyaka karang’o ma onego abedie kodu ? Koso anachandra kodu nyaka karang’o ? ”
Eka Yesu nokwero jachiendno matek , mi owuok oko kuom rawerano , mi rawerano ochango mana gikanyo .
Bang’e jopuonjre nodhi ir Yesu kar kende , mopenje ni , “ Ang’o momiyo wan ne ok wanyal golo jachiendno ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Nende ok unyal gole nikech un gi yie matin . Awachonu adier niya , Da bed ni un gi yie kata matin marom mana gi koth karadali , to duwachi ni godni ni , ‘ Aye ka , dhi kucha’ , mi dodhi . Bende onge gima ditamu timo . [
To jachien ma kamano igolo mana gi lemo kod tueyo chiemo kende . ] ”
To kane oyudo Yesu wuotho gi jopuonjrene e piny Galili , nowachonigi niya , “ Wuod Dhano ibiro keto e lwet ji ,
mi gininege , to chieng’ mar adek nochiere . ” To kane jopuonjre owinjo kamano , ne gibedo gi chuny mokuyo .
Kane Yesu gi jopuonjrene ochopo Kapernaum , josol osuch Hekalu nobiro ir Petro , mopenje ni , “ Bende japuonju golo osuch Hekalu ? ” ( Osuch Hekalu ne en nus-shekel . )
Petro nodwokogi ni , “ Ee , ogolo . ” To kane Petro odonjo e ot , Yesu ema nokwongo wuoyo kode , kapenje niya , “ Simon , in iparo ang’o kuom wach golo osuruni ? Joma nadi magolo osuru ni ruodhi mag pinyni ? Gin jopinje ruodhigo , koso gin jopinje mamoko ? ”
Petro nodwoke ni , “ Jopinje mamoko eme golo . ” Eka Yesu nowachone ni , “ Ka kamano , to kara jopinjegi ok onego chul gimoro .
To kata kamano , ok onego wachwany chuny josol osurugi , omiyo dhiyo , ibol olowu e nam , iywa rech mokwongo . Eka iyaw dhoge , inwang’ie shekel achiel . Kawe , imi josol osurugo , obed osuchwa , wan ji ariyo . ”
E sano jopuonjre nobiro ir Yesu , mopenje ni , “ Ere ng’at maduong’ moloyo e Loch Polo ? ”
Yesu noluongo nyathi matin , mi ochungo e diergi .
Eka nowachonigi ni , “ Adier , akonu ni , ka ok ulokoru , mi udoko machal gi nyithindo matindo , to ok udonj e Piny Ruodh Polo ngang’ .
Ng’at modoko mamuol ka nyathi matinni , ema duong’ie moloyo e Loch Polo .
Kuom mano , ng’at morwako nyathi achiel makama e nyinga , to orwako mana an .
“ Ka ng’ato omiyo achiel kuom joma tindo moyie kuomagi odonjo e richo , to diber moloyo ka otuene pong’ mang’ongo e ng’ute , kendo nyumego e chuny nam !
Gik mamiyo ji donjo e richo nomi ji modak e piny ne malit . Gik ma kamago ok nyal bare mak obetie , to mano kaka nobed malit ni ng’at makelogi !
“ Ka lueti kata tiendi ema teri e richo , to ng’ade oko , iwite kucha , nikech ber donjo e ngima king’ol kata ka in puth , moloyo witi e mach mak rum , ka in gi lwedo ariyo kata tielo ariyo .
Kata ka wang’i ema miyo itimo richo , to gole oko , iwite kucha , nikech ber donjo e ngima ka in gi wang’ achiel , moloyo witi e mach mak rum ka in gi wengeni duto ! ”
“ Neuru ni ok uchayo achiel kuom joma tindogi . Awachonu ni malaika manie polo moritogi neno wang’ Wuora e polo ndalo duto . [
Wuod Dhano nobiro mondo ores joma olal . ]
“ Nyisauru ane gima uparo : ka ng’ato nigi rombe mia achiel , to achiel kuomgi olal , donge dowe rombe mamoko piero ochiko gochiko ka kwayo e kor got , to odhi manyo rombo molalno ?
To awachonu adier ni , ka oyude to obedo mamor gi rombono moloyo rombe pier ochiko gochiko mane ok olal .
Kamano e kaka Wuonu mae polo bende ok dwar mondo achiel kuom joma tindogi olal .
“ Ka wadu moro otimoni marach , to dhi ire mondo inyise wachno ka un kode ji ariyo . Ka owinjo wachni to iloso kindi gi wadu .
To ka otamore winji , to dog ire gi ji ariyo kata ng’at achiel , ‘ mondo weche duto ong’ere malongo’ e nyim joneno adek kata ariyo’ , kaka muma wacho .
To ka otamore winjo jogo , to koro ter wachno ni kanyakla mar jolemo bende . Ka otamore winjo kata mana kanyakla mar jolemo bende , to koro kawe ka ng’at makia Nyasaye , kata ka jasol osuru mamedo gi malang’ .
“ Adier awachonu ni , gima ukwero e piny ka , nokwer e polo bende . To gima uyiego e piny ka ema noyiego e polo bende .
“ Bende awachonu ni , ka ji ariyo kuomu owinjore e piny ni kuom gima gikwayo , to Wuora mae polo nomigi gino ,
nimar kama ji adek kata ji ariyo ochokoree e nyinga , to kanyo an bende antie kodgi .
Bang’e Petro nobiro ir Yessu , mopenje ni , “ Ruoth , owadwa dikethna nyadidi , kapod aweyone aweya ? Dawene nyaka ndalo abiriyo koso ? ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Ooyo , ok awachonu ni mondo iwene kuom ndalo abiriyo , to nyaka iwene kuom ndalo piero abiriyo nyadibiriyo !
Mano emomiyo inyalo pimo Loch Polo gi ruoth moromane dwaro mondo onon kaka jotichne tiyo gi pesane .
To kane ochako kueno , nokelne jotichne moro mane nigi gope moromo siling’ tara gi tara .
To jatichno ne onge gi yo ma dichulgo gopeno , omiyo ruodhe nowacho ni mondo ong’iewe ka misumba , kaachiel gi chiege gi nyithinde kod gige duto , mondo ochulgo gowino .
To jatichno nopodho piny e tiend ruodhe kosaye niya , ‘ Yie , itera mos , to abiro chuli gopi ma an-go duto . ’ .
Kane ruodhe owinjo kamano , nokeche , mogonye , kendo oweyone gowino .
“ To ng’atno nowuok , moromo gi jatich wadgi mane nigi gope moromo siling moko manok kende . Ne omako Ng’atno gi ng’ute , modeyo , kowachone ni , ‘ Chula gopa ma in-go . ’ .
To jatich wadgino nopodho piny e tiende , kahombe niya , ‘ Yie itera mos , to abiro chuli gopi ma an-go duto . ’ .
To jalo notamore weye , modhi otere e jela nyaka chop ochule gope .
Kane jotich wetegi oneno gima otimore , chunygi nodoko malit ahinya , omiyo ne gidhi ir ruodhgi , mi ginyise weche duto .
Eka ruodhgino noluongo ng’atno ire , mowachone niya , ‘ In jatich marachni ! Nende aweyoni gopa duto ma in-go nikech ne ikwaya .
To koro donge owinjore ikech jatich wadu mana kaka an bende nende akechi ? ’
Mirima nomako ruodhno ahinya , mi otero jatichneno e jela , mondo okume kuno nyaka chop ochul gowino duto . ”
Yesu notieko , kawacho niya , “ Mano e kaka Wuora mae polo bende notim ni ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu ma ok oweyo ni wadgi gi chunye duto ! ”
Kane Yesu otieko wacho wechego , noa e piny Galili , modhi e piny Judea man loka aora Jordan .
Ji mang’eny noluwe kuno , mochangogi .
Jo-Farisai moko nobiro ire mondo oteme . Ne gipenje ni , “ Bende Chikwa oyie mondo ng’ato oriemb chiege nikech wach moro amora koso ? ”
To Yesu nodwoko , kapenjogi niya , “ Pok usomo e Muma ni , ‘ Nyaka a chakruok ,
Jachuech nochueyo dichwo gi dhako ? ’ kendo ni , ‘ Mano emomiyo ng’ato weyo wuon gi min , to padore kuom chiege , kendo ji ariyogo doko ringruok achiel’ ?
Kamano koro ok gin ji ariyo , to gin mana ringruok achiel . Kuom mano , gima Nyasaye oseriwo , kik dhano pogi . ”
To jo-Farisaigo nomedo penje niya , “ Ka kamano , to marang’o Musa noketo chik ni ng’ato nyalo riembo chiege , kosemiye barup weruok ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Musa noyienu mondo uriemb mondeu kamano mana nikech wichtekou , to ne ok en kamano nyaka a chakruok .
Awachonu ni ng’at moriembo chiege nikech wach moro amora ma ok mana terruok , to eka bang’e okendo dhako machielo , to mano oterore . ”
Kane jopuonjrene owinjo kamano ne giwachone niya , “ Ka wach dichwo gi dhako chalo mana kamano , to kara ber mondo ji kik kendre ! ”
Yesu to nodwokogi niya , “ Ji duto ok nyal rwako wachni , to mak mana jogo ma Nyasaye owalonigi .
Nitie jomoko mabwoch mane onywol kamano nyaka a ei minegi , kendo nitie bwoch moko ma ji ema oseroyo , to bende nitie jomoko ma ok kendi nikech Loch Polo . Ng’at manyalo rwako wachni to mondo orwaki . ”
Jomoko nokelo ni Yesu nyithindo mondo oket lwete kuomgi , kendo olemnigi , to jopuonjre nokwerogi .
Yesu to nowachonigi ni , “ Weuru nyithindo obi ira ! Kik utamgi , nikech joma kamagi ema yudo gweth mar Loch Polo . ”
Eka noketo lwete kuomgi , mi bang’e owuok odhi .
Wuowi moro nobiro ir Yesu , mopenje niya , “ Japuonj , ere gima ber monego atim mondo ayud ngima mochwere ? ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Ere gima omiyo ipenja gima ber ? Ng’at achiel kende ema ber . To ka idwaro donjo e ngima , to nyaka irit chike . ”
To wuowino nomedo penje ni , “ Gin chike mage monego ariti ? ” Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Kik ineki , kik iterri , kik ikwal , kik ihang wach ,
luor wuoru gi meru , kendo her wadu kaka iherori iwuon . ”
Wuowino to nodwoke ni , “ Mago duto aserito , to koro ang’o mapod orema ? ”
Yesu nowachone niya , “ Ka idwaro doko malong’o chutho , to dhiyo mondo ilok mwanduni pesa , mondo ipog ni joma odhier , eka inibed gi mwandu e polo , to kisetimo kamano , to bi iluwa . ”
Kane wuowino owinjo kamano , noa modhi ka chunye lit , nikech ne en jamoko ahinya .
Bang’ mano , Yesu nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Adier awachonu ni , donjo e Piny Ruodh Polo nobed matek ni jamoko !
To bende awachonu ni , yot ni ngamia kadho e wang’ sandan moloyo jamoko donjo e Piny Ruodh Nyasaye . ”
To kane jopuonjre owinjo wachno , ne giwuoro ahinya , mi gipenjore ni , “ Kara , ere ng’ama dikwo ? ”
Yesu nong’iyo wang’gi tir , mowachonigi niya , “ Dhano ok nyal warore kende , to Nyasaye ema nyalo gik moko duto . ”
Eka Petro nowacho ni , “ To wan waseweyo gik moko duto mondo waluwi . Koro wabiro yudo ang’o ? ”
Yesu nokonigi niya , “ Adier awachonu un museluwa ni , chieng’ chuech manyien , ka Wuod Dhano obet e kom duong’ne to un bende unubed e kombe apar gariyo , kung’ado bura ni dhoudi apar gariyo mag Israel .
Kendo ng’ato ka ng’ato moseweyo udi , kata owetene , kata nyiminene , kata wuon , kata min , kata nyithinde , kata lope , nikech an , noyud gigo nyadi mia achiel , kaachiel gi ngima mochwere bende .
To ji mang’eny ma koro otelo nodog chien , kendo joma koro odong’ chien notel . ”
Eka Yesu nomedo wacho niya , “ Loch Polo chalo gi wuon puoth mzabibu mane owuok gokinyi mang’ich kadhi dwaro jotich mondo otine e puothe .
Ne owinjore gi jotich moko ni obiro chulogi siling’ achiel achiel , odieching’ kodiechieng’ , mi noorogi e puodho .
Ne ochako owuok kar sa adek , mi odhi oyudo jomoko kochung’ achung’a e chiro , ka onge gima gitim .
Nowachonigi niya , ‘ Un bende , dhiuru e puotha , to abiro miyou pok mowinjore . ’ .
Kamano ne gidhi . Eka ng’atno nochako owuok kar sa auchiel , kendo kar sa ochiko , mi odhi oyudo jomoko , kendo owinjorego bende .
Nochako owuok kar sa apar gachiel , mi odhi oyudo jomoko ka pod ochung’ achung’a e chiro , omiyo nopenjogi niya , ‘ Ere gimomiyo ubudho abudha ka onge gima utimo odiechieng’ duto ? ’
Ne gidwoke ni , ‘ Wobudho ka nikech onge ng’at mosemiyowa tich’ . Eka nowachonigi niya , ‘ Kara , un bende dhiuru e puotha mar mzabibu’ .
“ Kane piny ochopo odhiambo , wuon puodho nowacho ni nyapara ni , ‘ Luong jotich mondo obi ichulgi pokgi , kichako gi joma nende obiro achien , kendo itieko gi joma nende obiro mokwongo’ .
Kuom mano , joma ne ochako tich sa apar gachiel mar odhiambo nobiro , moyudo siling’ achiel achiel .
To bang’e kane joma nokwongo ochako tich obiro , ne gigalo ni gibiro nwang’o pok mang’eny mokadho kanyo , to kata kamano , gin bende ne omigi mana siling’ achiel achiel .
To kane gikawo pok gi ne ging’ur ni wuon puodho ka giwacho niya ,
‘ Ji manende obiro achien-gi osetiyo mana kuom sa achiel kende , to ere gima omiyo isemiyogi pok mana marom kodwa ? Wan donge ema wasechandore gi tich matek odiechieng’ ngima , to chieng’ makech chamowa ? ’
To ng’atno nodwoko achiel kuomgi niya , ‘ Omera , onge gima rach ma asetimoni . Donge nende wawinjore kodi ni abiro chuli siling’ achiel ?
Kara , kaw pokni mondo idhi ! An ema ahero miyo joma nende ochako tich achien-gi pok marom gi mau !
Donge an gi ratiro mar timo gima adwaro gi pesana awuon ? Koso in gi nyiego nikech ineno ni an ng’at mang’won ? ’ ”
Eka Yesu notieko , kawacho niya , “ Kamano joma koro odong’ chien notel , to joma koro otelo nodong’ chien ! ”
Kane oyudo Yesu nie yo dhi Jerusalem , nokawo jopuonjrene apar gariyo , motero tenge kar kendgi , mowachonigi ka giwuotho niya ,
“ Winjuru ! Koro wadhi Jerusalem , kuma ibiro chiwie Wuod Dhano e lwet jodolo madongo gi jopuonj Chik . Gining’adne buch tho ,
mi gikete e lwet joma ok jo-Yahudi mondo ochare kendo ochwade mi gure e msalaba . To chieng’ mar adek nochiere . ”
Bang’e min yawuot Zebedi nobiro ir Yesu gi yawuote . Ne ogoyo chonge piny mondo okwaye gimoro .
Yesu nopenje ni , “ En ango’ midwaro ? ” Nodwoke ni , “ Yie igol chik mondo wuoda achiel obed e badi korachwich , to machielo obedi e badi koracham , kisekawo lochni . ”
To Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Ok ung’eyo gima ukwayo ! Uparo ni unyalo madho kikombe mar masira ma abiro madho ? ” Ne gidwoke ni , “ Ee , wanyalo . ”
Eka nowachonigi niya , “ Adier ubiro madho kikombena to yiero ng’ama onego bedi e bada korachwich kata e bada koracham , to ok nie tekona . Wuora ema nochiw kuondego ni joma oseiknigi . ”
Kane jopuonjrene apar modong’ owinjo wachno ne gisin gi owete ariyogo .
To Yesu noluongogi giduto , mowacho nigi niya , “ Ung’eyo ni ruodhi mag piny tiyo jogi gi thuon , kendo jogo man gi loch nigi teko kuom joma gitiyo .
Kuomu to , ok nobed kamano . To ka ng’ato kuomu dwaro bedo gi duong’ , to nyaka obed jatichu ,
kendo ka ng’ato dwaro bedo jatendu , to nyaka obed misumbau ,
mana kaka Wuod Dhano bende ne ok obiro mondo ji otine , to mana ni mondo oti ni ji , kendo mondo ochiw ngimane owargo ji mang’eny . ”
Kane giwuok Jeriko , oganda maduong’ noluwo Yesu .
Muofni ariyo mane obet piny e dir yo nowinjo ni Yesu kadho , omiyo ne gikok niya , “ Wuod Daudi , kechwa ”
Ji nokwerogi ni mondo giling’ , to ne gimedo mana kok matek niya , “ Ruoth , kechwa ! Wuod Dhano , kechwa ! ”
Yesu nochung’ , mi oluongogi , kendo openjogi niya , “ Ere gima udwaro ni mondo atimnu ? ”
Ne gidwoke ni , “ Ruoth , wadwaro mondo iyawnwa wengewa ”
Yesu nokechogi , omiyo nomulo wengegi , mi wengegi oyepo mana gikanyono . Eka ne giluwe .
Kane gichopo Bethfage e got Zeituni , man machiegni gi Jerusalem , Yesu nooro jopuonjrene ariyo nyime , kowachonigi niya ,
“ Dhiuru e dala man nyimu cha , to gikanyono mudonjoe ubiro nwang’o kanyna motue , kaachiel gi nyathine . Gonygiuru mondo ukelna gi .
To ka ng’ato openjou gimoro , to wachneuru ni , ‘ Wuon-gi dwarogi . ’ . Kowinjo wachno , to obiro yie ukawgi mana gi sano . ”
Mano notimore mondo wach mane janabi owacho ochopi . Nowacho niya ,
‘ Nyisuru jo-Sayun ni , Neuru ! Ruoth biro iru , kamuol , kendo koidho kanyna . Chutho oidho kanyna matin . Adier , en mana nyathi kanyna . ’ .
Jopuonjrego nodhi , motimo kaka Yesu nowachonigi .
Ne gikelo kanyna gi nyathine , mi gipedho lepgi e dieng’egi , mi Yesu obetie .
Ji mathoth nopedho lepgi e yo , to jomoko nong’ado bede yien ema opedho e yo .
Joma notelo nyim Yesu , kod joma ne luwo bang’e nokok niya , “ Duong’ obed ni Wuod Daudi ! Ogwedh ng’ama biro e nying Ruoth ! Duong’ obed ni Nyasaye e polo malo ! ”
Kane Yesu odonjo Jerusalem , dala duto nosakni , ka ji penjore ni , “ Jali en ng’a ? ”
To oganda mane kowo Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Ma e Yesu , janabi moa Nazareth e piny Galili . ”
Yesu nodonjo e Hekalu , moriembo ji duto mane loko ohala kendo ng’iewo gik moko kanyo . Nokawo mesni mag jowil pesa , kod kombe mag jolok akuche , mogoyo piny .
Eka nowachonigi niya , “ Ondiki e Muma ni , ‘ Oda noluong ni od lemo . ’ . Un to uloke od jomecho ! ”
Muofni kod rang’onde nobiro ire e Hekalu , mochangogi .
To kane jodolo madongo kod jopuonj Chik oneno honni mane otimo , kendo kaka ne nyithindo kok ei Hekalu ni , “ Duong’ obed ni Wuod Daudi , ” mirima nomakogi ,
mi giwachone niya , “ Bende iwinjo gima jogi wacho ? ” To Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Ee , awinjo . To pok usomo Muma kama wacho ni , ‘ Isemiyo nyithindo mayom , koda ka mago mapod dhoth , paki maber’ ? ”
Bang’ mano noa Jerusalem oweyogi , modhi obworo Bethania .
Kinyne gokinyi , kane Yesu dok Jerusalem , kech nochako kaye .
Noneno ng’owo moro e bath yo , to kane osudo bute machiegni , ne ok oyudo olemo kuome , to mak mana pote kende . Omiyo nowacho ni yadhno niya , “ Kik ichak inyag olemo kendo nyaka chieng ! ” Gikanyono ng’owono notwo .
Kane jopuonjrene oneno gima otimore ni yadhno , ne giwuoro , mi gipenjo niya , “ Ere kaka ng’owoni otwo piyo kama ? ”
To Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Awachonu adier ni , ka un gi yie , ma ok uriwo gi kiawa to un bende unutim gima otim ni ng’owoni . To ok mano kende ema nubed gi teko mar timo , to kata mana godni , kuwachone ni , ‘ Mukri , inyumri e nam , ’ to notimre mana kamano .
Ka un gi yie , to unuyud gimoro amora mukwayo kulemo . ”
