Joma ne oneno gima ne otimore , ne onyiso ji kaka ng’at mane nigi jochiendeno osechango .
Bang’ mano , ji duto mane odak e piny jo-Gerasi nokwayo Yesu mondo oa e pinygi , nikech ne giluor ahinya . Kuom mano Yesu nodonjo e yie mondo oa .
To ng’at mane jochiende owuok kuomeno nohombe ni , “ Yie mondo wadhi kodi . ” To Yesu nokwere , kawachone ni ,
“ Dog dala , mondo inyis ji gik madongo ma Nyasaye osetimoni . ” Kuom mano , ng’atno noa modhi owuotho e gweng’no duto , konyiso ji gik madongo mane Yesu otimone .
Kane Yesu oduogo loka machielo , ji mathoth norwake gi mor , nikech noyudo girite giduto .
Eka ng’at moro ma nyinge Jairo , mane jaduong’ od lemo , nobiro kanyo . Nopodho piny e tiend Yesu , mi okwaye mondo odhi kode ,
nikech nyare achiel kende ma jahigni apar gariyo ne tuo , ohewore . Kane Yesu oyudo dhiyo kuno , ji ne thung’e koni gi koni .
To dhako moro ne ni kanyo mane iye osechuer kuom higni apar gariyo . Kata obedo ni nosetieko mwandune duto kochulo jothieth , to onge kata achiel mane nyalo thiedhe .
Nosudo gi yoka ng’e Yesu , momulo riak lawe , kendo gi kanyono rembe nochok .
To Yesu nopenjo niya , “ En ng’a momula ? ” To kane ji duto okwer , Petro nowachone ni , “ Ruoth ! Ok ineye kaka jogi oluori koni , gi koni , kendo othung’i ? ”
To Yesu nowachone niya , “ Kata kamano , ang’eyo ni ng’ato osemula , nikech awinjo ka teko owuok kuoma . ”
Kane dhakono oneno ni osefwenye , nobiro kokirni , mi opodho piny e tiend Yesu . Eka ne onyise , mana e nyim ji duto kanyo , gima ne omiyo omule , kendo kaka ne ochango mana gi kanyono .
Yesu nowachone niya , “ Nyara , yieni ema omiyo ichango . Dhiyo gi kue . ”
Kane pod Yesu wuoyo , jaote moro nobiro koa e od jaduong’ cha , mowacho niya , “ Nyari osetho , omiyo koro kik ichand Japuonj . ”
Yesu nowinjo kamano , mowacho ni jaduong’no niya , “ Kik ibed maluor , to bed mana gi yie motegno . Nyari biro kwo . ”
Kane ochopo e odno , ne ok oyie ni ng’ato mondo odonj kode , mak mana Petro gi Johana kod Jakobo , kaachiel gi wuon nyathi kod min mare .
Ji duto mane ni kuno ne ywago nyathino malit , komako wigi , to Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Weuru ywak , nikech nyathi ok otho , to onindo aninda . ”
To giduto ne ginyiere anyiera , nikech ne ging’eyo ni nyathi osetho .
To Yesu nomako lwet nyathino , mi owachone matek niya , “ Nyako , a malo ! ”
Chunye nodwogo , mi oa malo mana gikanyono . Eka Yesu nowachonigi ni mondo gimiye chiemo ocham .
Jonywolne nohum nono , to Yesu nokwerogi ni kik ginyis ng’ato gima otimore .
Yesu noluongo jopuonjrene apar gariyo kaachiel , mio miyogi teko mar golo jochiende duto , kod mar chango tuoche duto .
Eka noorogi mondo gidhi giland Wach Loch Nyasaye , kendo gichang joma tuo .
Ne owachonigi niya , “ Ka udhi e wuodhni , to kik uting’ gimoro , kaka ludh wuoth , kata ndede , kata chiemo , kata pesa , kata sede ariyo .
Ot aota ma orwakue to beduru nyaka chop chieng’ ma ua e gweng’no .
To kuwuok kamoro amora ma ok orwakue , to teng’uru buch tiendu , mondo obednigi siem . ”
Kamano joote nowuok mowuotho e mier duto , ka lando Wach Maber , kendo chango ji kuonde duto .
Herode ruodh Galili nowinjo gik moko duto matimore , mi noparore nikech jomoko nowacho ni Johana Jabatiso osechier oa kuom joma otho .
Jomoko to nowacho ni Elija ema ofwenyore , to moko bende nowacho ni achiel kuom jonabi machon ema osechier .
To Herode nowacho niya , “ Johana to ne agolo chik mondo ong’ad wiye oko , to ma en ng’a , matimo gik ma kamagini ? ” Mano omiyo nogombo ahinya mondo one Yesu .
Joote Yesu nodwogo ire monyise gik moko duto mane gisetimo . Eka nokawogi mi gidhi kar kendgi e dala miluongo ni Bethsaida .
To ji nofwenyo kamano , moluwe kuno . Ne orwakogi gi mor , mowuoyo kodgi kuom wach Loch Nyasaye , kendo ochango joma tuo .
Kane chieng’ koro dwaro podho , jopuonjre apar gariyo nobiro ir Yesu , mowachone niya , “ We ji odhi e mier manie gweng’ni mondo oyudie chiemo gi kuonde nindo , nikech kama wantie ni en thim . ”
To Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Un ema mondo umigi chiemo gicham . ” Ne gidwoke niya , “ Wan mana gi makati abich kod rech ariyo kende . Koso idwaro ni mondo wadhi wang’iew chiemo ni jogi duto ? ”
( Ne giwacho kamano nikech joma chwo mane ni kanyo ne dirom alufu abich . ) Yesu nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Nyisuru ji obed piny , kopogore piero abich abich . ”
Jopuonjre notimo kamano , momiyo ji obet piny .
Yesu nokawo makati abich kod rech ariyogo , eka nong’iyo malo , moguedhogi . Nong’ingogi , momiyo jopuonjrene mondo opogni ji ,
kendo giduto ne gichiemo , mi giyieng’ Bang’e ne okwany ng’injo modong’ , mi oromo atonge apar gariyo .
Chieng’ moro Yesu ne lemo kende , ka en gi jopuonjrene . Eka nopenjogi niya , “ Un uwinjo ji wacho ni an ng’a ? ”
Ne gidwoke ni , “ Jomoko wacho ni in Johana Jabatiso , to moko wacho ni in Elija , moko bende wacho ni in achiel kuom jonabi machon mosechier . ”
Eka nopenjogi ni , “ Un to uparo ni an ng’a ? ” Petro nodwoke niya , “ In e Mesia mar Nyasaye . ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nokwero jopuonjrene matek ni kik ginyis ng’ato ni en ng’a .
Bende nowachonigi niya , “ Wuod Dhano nyaka yud masiche mang’eny , kendo jodongo gi jodolo madongo kod jopuonj Chik biro dage . Enonege , to chieng’ mar adek nochier . ”
Eka Yesu nowacho ni ji duto niya , “ Ka ng’ato dwaro luwa , to nyaka okwerre owuon , mi oting’ msalape pilepile , kendo oluwa ,
nikech ng’ama dwaro reso ngimane , ngimane nolalne . To ng’ama owito ngimane nikech an , to nores ngimane .
Ere ohala ma ng’ato yudo , ka onwang’o piny duto , to en owuon owito ngimane , mi olal ?
Ka wi ng’ato kuot koda , kendo kuot gi wechena , to wi Wuod Dhano bende nokuod kode , kobiro e duong’ mare , kod mar Wuon mare , kaachiel gi mar malaika maler .
Adier awachonu ni , nitie jomoko kuomu ka , ma ok notho kapok oneno Loch Nyasaye . ”
Ndalo aboro bang’ wacho wechego , Yesu nokawo Petro gi Johana kod Jakobo , mi odhigo e got mondo olem .
To kane oyudo olemo , lela wang’e nolokore , kendo lepe nodoko matar mang’ang’ni .
Eka ne gipo ka ji ariyo loso kode . Ne gin Musa gi Elija ,
mane jobiro e duong’ maler , mi owuoyo gi Yesu kuom tho mane obiro thogo Jerusalem , mondo ochopgo dwaro Nyasaye .
Nindo notero Petro kod joma ne gin-go , to kane gichiew ne gineno duong’ maler mar Yesu , kaachiel gi ji ariyo mane ochung’ kode kande .
To kane jogo dhi weyo Yesu , Petro nowachone niya , “ Japuonj , bedowa kaeri en gima ber ! Omiyo we wager kiche adek , ma achiel mari , to machielo mar Musa , kendo moro mar Elija . ” ( To chutho ne ok ong’eyo gima owacho . )
Kane pod owuoyo , bor polo nobiro moimogi , kendo jopuonjrego nodoko maluor kane bor polo oimogi kamano .
Eka ne giwinjo duol moro kawacho gie bor polono niya , “ Ma e Wuoda ma aseyiero ! Winjeuru ! ”
To kane dwolno oling’ , ne gineno ka Yesu kende ema odong’ kanyo . Jopuonjre mane oneno gigo ne ok owacho ni ng’ato gimoro amora e ndalogo .
Kinyne ka ne gilor gia e got , oganda maduong’ noromo gi Yesu .
To ng’at moro kuom jogo nokok niya , “ Japuonj , asayi , rangie wuodani ! En e nyathina kende ,
to ka jachien marach obuke , to goye piny , kendo okok matek , kogwecho , kendo dhoge wuok buoyo . Jachiendno sande malit , kendo weye mana ka tekone orumo .
Nende akwayo jopuonjreni mondo ogol jachiendno , to notamogi . ”
Yesu nodwoko niya , “ Yaye , ma tieng’ maonge gi yie , kendo mobam manadi ! Nyaka karang’o ma onego abedie kodu , ka achandora kodu kama ! ” Eka nowacho ni ng’atno ni , “ Kel wuodi ka . ”
To e sa mane nyathino dhi ir Yesu , jachien nogoye piny , moguecho marach . Yesu nokwero jachiendno matek , mi ochango wuowino , eka odwoke ni wuon mare .
Ji duto mane ni kanyo nowuoro ahinya duong’ mar Nyasaye . Kane pod ji hum kuom gik moko duto mane Yesu timo , ne owacho ni jopuonjrene niya ,
“ Chikuru itu maber , mondo uwinj gima awachonuni ; Wuod Dhano ibiro keto e lwet ji . ”
To jopuonjrene ne ok owinjo tiend wachno . Ne opandorenigi mondo kik ging’e tiende , to bende ne giluoro penje .
Mbaka nowuok e kind jopuonjre Yesu ka gipiemore ni ere ng’ama duong’ moloyo kuomgi .
To Yesu nong’eyo gima ne giparo , omiyo nokawo nyathi moro , moketo ochung’ e dire .
Eka nowachonigi niya , “ Ng’ama orwako nyathi ma kama e nyinga , to orwako mana an , kendo ng’ama orwaka , to orwako mana Jal mane oora , nimar ng’at matinie moloyo kuomu duto , e ng’at maduong’ie moloyo . ”
Johana nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Ruoth , ne waneno ng’ato ka golo jochiende e nyingi , to ne wakwere , nikech ok en achiel kuomwa . ”
To Yesu nodwoke kawachonigi niya , “ Kik ukwer ng’at ma kamano , nikech ng’at ma ok mon kodu en jakoru . ”
Kane kinde monego tergo Yesu e polo koro chiegni , ne owuok koketo chunye mondo odhi Jerusalem .
Nooro joote moko mondo otel nyime , mi jootego nodhi e dala jo-Samaria moro mondo olosne kar bworo .
To jodalano nodagi rwako Yesu , nikech nong’ere ni odhi Jerusalem .
To kane jopuonjre Yesu ma Jakobo kod Johana oneno kamano , ne gipenjo Yesu niya , “ Ruoth , idwaro mondo waluong mach oa e polo , obi otiekgi koso ? ”
To Yesu nolokore irgi , mokwerogi ,
eka ne gidhi e dala machielo .
Kane oyudo giwuotho , ng’at moro nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Ayie luwi kamoro amora midhiye . ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Bwe nigi buchegi , kendo winy bende nigi utgi ; Wuod Dhano to onge kata gi kama ketie wiye . ”
Eka Yesu nowacho ni ng’at machielo ni , “ Luwa ! ” To ng’atno nodwoke niya , “ Jaduong’ , yiena mondo akwong adog ayik wuora . ”
To Yesu nokone ni , “ We joma otho oyik jogi motho . Into dhiyo iland Wach Maber mar Loch Nyasaye . ”
Bang’e ng’at moro machielo nowacho ni , “ Jaduong’ , an bende ayie luwi , to mokwongo yie adog ago ni joodwa oriti . ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Ng’at mosiko paro mana chien , ok owinjore gi Loch Nyasaye , mana kaka ng’at ma kosemako kue dhiang’ mochako pur , to osiko ng’iyo mana chien , ok nyal puro maber . ”
Bang’ mano , Ruoth Yesu noyiero ji piero abiriyo gariyo mamoko , moorogi ariyo ariyo , mondo gitel nyime e mier duto kod kuonde duto mane en owuon odwaro dhiye .
Nowacho nigi niya , “ Cham ochiek mathoth , to jokeyo ema nok . Emomiyo kwauru wuon puodho mondo oor jotich odhi okane cham .
Koro dhiuru ! Aorou mana ka rombe madhi e dier ondiegi .
Kik uting’ ofuk pesa , kata sandug wuoth , kata wuoche , kendo kik umos ng’ato e yo kudhi .
Ot aota mudonje , to wachie uru ni , ‘ Kue obed e odni . ’ .
Ka ng’at mohero kue nie odno , to noyud kue muguedhogo odno . To ka onge ng’at mohero kue , to kue muguedhogo odno noduognu .
Beduru mana e odno , kendo chamuru gik ma gimiyou , nikech jatich ber gi pokne ; to kik uring e udi .
Ka udonjo e dala moro , mi jodalano orwakou , to chamuru achama chiemo ma gimiyou .
Bende changuru joma tuo man kuno , kunyisogi ni Loch Nyasaye osesudo machiegni kodgi .
Ka udonjo e dala moro , mi jodalano odagi rwakou , to wuoguru e laru , kendo uwach niya ,
‘ Kata mana buch dalau momoko e tiendewa wateng’onu ! To ng’euru ni Loch Nyasaye osesudo machiegni . ’ .
Awachonu ni Chieng’ Bura , Nyasaye nokum dalano malit moloyo kaka nokum Sodom !
“ Yaye , Un jo-Korazin ! Mano kaka unune malit ! Yaye , un jo-Bethsaida ! Mano kaka un bende unune malit ! Dine bed ni honni mane otimnu , notim mana ni jo Turo gi jo-Sidon , to dikoro ne giseloko chunygi , mi gibet piny ka girwako piende gugru , kendo gibukore buru .
Chieng’ Bura , Nyasaye nokumu malit moloyo kaka nokum Turo gi Sidon !
To in dala mar Kapernaum , iparo ni initing’ri malo nyaka e polo koso ? Ooyo , ibiro boli piny , mana e Piny Joma Otho ! ”
Eka Yesu nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Ng’ama owinjou , owinjo mana an , to ng’ama odagiu , to odagi mana Jal mane oora . ”
Jopuonjre piero abiriyo gariyogo noduogo gi mor , kawacho niya , “ Ruoth , kata mana jochiende bende winjowa ka wakwerogi e nyingi ! ”
Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Ne aneno ka Satan lwar a e polo , mana ka mil polo !
To ng’euru ni asemiyou teko duto mag Jasigu , kendo onge gima nohinyu ngang’ !
To kik ubed mamor ni jochiende winjou , to beduru mamor mana nikech nyingu ondiki e polo . ”
E sa nogo , Roho Maler nomiyo Yesu odoko mamor ahinya , mi owacho niya , “ A Wuora , ma Ruodh polo gi piny , agoyoni erokamano nikech isepando wechegi ni joma riek kod joma osomo , to isenyisogi mana ji ajia . Adier Wuora , osetimore kamano , nikech mano e kaka ne long’oni .
“ Wuora oseketo gik moko duto e lweta . To onge ng’ama ong’eyo Wuowi , mak mana Wuowi kod joma Wuowi omiyo ong’eye . ”
Eka nolokore ir jopuonjrene , mowachonigi kar kendgi ni , “ Un to , un johawi kuom neno gik munenogi !
Awachonu ni , jonabi kod ruodhi mang’eny ne jogombo neno gik ma koro unenogi , to ne ok ginyal neno , bende ne gigombo winjo gik ma uwinjogi , to ne ok ginyal winjo . ”
Japuonj Chik moro ne dwaro temo Yesu , omiyo nochung’ mopenje niya , “ Japuonj , ere gima datim mondo ayud ngima mochwere ? ”
Yesu nodwoke ka penje ni , “ Ang’o mondiki e Muma ? Ere gima isomo kanyo ? ”
Ng’atno nodwoko ni , “ Nyaka iher Ruoth Nyasachi gi chunyi duto , kod paroni duto , kendo gi tekoni duto , kod riekoni duto . Bende nyaka iher wadu kaka iherori iwuon . ”
Yesu nowacho ne ni , “ Idwoko kare ! Tim kamano , eka inibed mangima . ”
To kaka ng’atno ne dwaro nyiso ni penjone riek , nomedo penjo Yesu ni , “ Wadwa to en ng’a ? ”
Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Ng’at moro ne lor koa Jerusalem , dhi Jeriko , mi nopo ka jomecho ogore kuome . Ne gimaye lepe , kendo gigoye , mi giweye kodwaro tho .
To jadolo moro bende noyudo oluwo yorno , to kane oneno ng’atno , nobaro moluwo bath yo komachielo .
Kamano ja-Lawi moro bende mane oyudo oluwo yorno , nonene , to okadho akadha .
To kane ja-Samaria moro ma bende noyudo nie wuoth ochopo kanyo , moneno ng’atno , nokeche .
Nosudo bute , moolo mo kod divai kuonde mohinyore , kendo otueyo . Eka noketo ng’atno e kanje owuon , mi otere e ot moro ma ji bworoe , kendo orite maber .
Kinyne nogolo pesa moko , mi omiyo wuon odno , kowacho ni , ‘ Rit jali maber , to pesa duto ma imedo ritego , an awuon abiro chuli ka aduogo . ’ . ”
Bang’e Yesu nopenjo japuonj Chik cha niya , “ Kuom ji adekgo , ere jal miparo ni notimo ka wadgi ng’at mane jomecho ogoyono ? ”
Nodwoko ni , “ Jal mane otimone maberno . ” Eka Yesu nowachone ni , “ In bende dhi itim kamano . ”
Kane Yesu kod jopuonjrene pod nie wuoth , ne odonjo e dala moro , mi dhako moro ma nyinge Maritha norwake e ode .
Dhakono ne nigi nyamin miluongo ni Maria . Nyamin mareno nobet piny e tiend Ruoth Yesu , kawinjo puonjne .
To chuny Maritha ne chandore nikech tich mang’eny mane otiyo , omiyo nodhi ir Yesu , mowachone ni , “ Ruoth , ok ineye ni nyamera oweya atiyo mana kenda ? Wachne mondo obi okonya ! ”
To Ruoth Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Maritha , Maritha , iparori kendo ithagori gi weche mang’eny kayiem ,
to gimoro achiel kende ema dwarore , kendo Maria ema oseyiero gino . En gima ber moloyo , kendo onge ng’ama nomaye . ”
Chieng’ moro Yesu ne lemo kamoro , to kane otieko lemo , japuonjrene moro nokwaye ni , “ Ruoth , puonjwa lemo kaka Johana nopuonjo jopuonjrene . ”
Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Kulemo , to wachuru kama : Wuonwa , nyingi mondo omi luor . Lochni obi .
Pilepile miwa chiemo moromowa ,
bende wenwae richowa , nikech wan wawegi bende waweyo ni ji duto matimonwa marach , kendo kik iwe wadonj e tem . ”
Eka Yesu nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Ka ng’ato kuomu oyudo wendo dier otieno , donge dodhi ir osiepne moro , mi okwaye niya , ‘ Owadwa , holae makati adek ,
nikech osiepna moro obworo kuoma , to aonge gi gima daket e nyime ! ’
To kamoro osiepneno nyalo dwoke gie ot ni , ‘ We chanda , nikech aseloro dhoot , kendo asenindo , omiyo ok anyal chung’ mondo amiyi gima idwaro . ’ .
To awachonu ni kata ka ng’atno ok oyie chung’ mondo omiye makati nikech wach mar osiepgi kode , to kinda ma jalo timo biro miyo ochung’ , mi omiye gik moko duto modwaro !
“ Bende awachonu ni , kwauru , eka nomiu , kendo dwaruru , eka unuyudi , bende duong’uru , eka noyawnu ,
nikech ng’at mokwayo ema yudo , kendo ng’at madwaro ema nwang’o , bende ng’at modwong’o ema iyawone .
Un ma un weg nyithindo , bende nitie ng’ato kuomu ma ka nyathine okwaye kuon , to omiye kidi , kata ka okwaye rech , to omiye thuol ,
kata ka okwaye tong’ gweno , to omiye thomoni ?
Koro ka un joma richo kama , ema ung’eyo miyo nyithindu gik mabeyo , to Wuonu mae polo donge dibed mamor moloyo kuom chiwo Roho Maler ni joma okwaye ? ”
Ne oyudo Yesu golo jachien kuom ng’ato mane jachien oloko momo , kendo kane jachiendno osewuok , ng’atno nowuoyo mi ji mane ni kanyo nowuoro .
To jomoko kuomgi nowacho ni , “ Beelzebul ruodh jochiende ema omiye teko mogologo jochiende . ”
Jomoko to ne dwaro teme , omiyo ne giwachone ni mondo otimnigi ranyisi moa e polo , manyiso ni Nyasaye ni kode .
To Yesu nong’eyo gima giparo , omiyo nowachonigi niya , “ Piny moro amora ma joge opogore e kindgi giwegi ok nyal betie . Bende ot ma joge opogore ok nyal chung’ .
Kuom mano , ka jo-Satan opogore e kindgi giwegi , to ere kaka lochne dichung’ ? Apenjou kamano nikech uwacho ni agolo jochiende gi teko mar Beelzebul .
To ka mano en adier , kara jou to yudo teko mar gologi kure ? Omiyo ka mano e gima uwacho , to jougo ema biro ng’eng’ou !
To ka agolo jochiende gi teko mar Nyasaye , to kara ng’euru ni Loch Nyasaye osechopo kuomu .
“ Ka ng’at maratego omanore gi gilweny karito dalane , to gige duto onge gima nyalo ketho .
To ka ng’at maratego moloye omonje , mi oloye , to ng’at moloyeno kawo gige mag lweny moritorego , kendo pogo ni joge mwandu ng’atno .
Ng’at ma ok odokna , mon koda , kendo ng’at ma ok konya choko romba , to keyo romba akeya .
“ Ka jachien marach osewuok kuom ng’ato , to owuotho kuonde motwo ma pi ongee , kodwaro kar yueyo . Bang’e ka ok oyudo , to owacho niya , ‘ We adog e oda , kuma ne aaye . ’ .
Kuom mano odok , to oyudo ka ot oywe , mi olos maber .
Eka owuok odhi omo jochiende mamoko abiriyo maricho moloye , kendo gidonjo mi gidag e odno . Kamano achien , ngima ng’atno doko marach moloyo kaka ne en chon . ”
Kane Yesu osewacho kamano , dhako moro noting’o dwonde ei oganda mowachone niya , “ Mano kaka dhako mane onywoli , kendo odhodhi , jahawi ! ”
To Yesu nodwoko ni , “ Joma winjo wach Nyasaye , kendo mako , gin johawi moloyo ! ”
Kane ji mathoth ochokore mothung’o Yesu , ne owacho niya , “ Mano kaka tieng’ ma kawuononi en tieng’ marach ! Gikwayo mondo otimnigi ranyisi , to onge ranyisi ma notimnigi mak mana ranyisi mar Jona .
Kaka Jona nodoko ranyisi ni jo-Nineve , e kaka Wuod Dhano biro bedo ranyisi ni tieng’ ma kawuononi .
Chieng’ Bura , ruoth ma dhako mar piny milambo nochung’ , kendo nodonj ni tieng’ ma kawuononi , nikech ne oa kuma bor ahinya mondo obi owinj rieko Solomon . To awachonu ni nitie gimoro kaeri man gi duong’ moloyo Solomon !
Chieng’ Bura , jo-Nineve bende nochung’ , mi donj ni tieng’ ma kawuononi , nikech kane Jona olandonigi wach Nyasaye , to ne gilokore , mi giweyo richogi , to awachonu ni nitie gimoro kaeri man gi duong’ moloyo Jona .
“ Onge ng’ama moko taya , to pando , kata umo gi atonga . To okete mana ewi rachungi taya , mondo orieny ni joma donjo e ot .
Wang’i e taya mar ringri , omiyo ka wang’i ngima , to dendi duto nigi ler . To ka wang’i ok ngima , to dendi duto otimo mudho .
Kuom mano , bed motang’ , dipo ka ler ma in-go en mana mudho !
Ka dendi duto opong’ gi ler , kendo onge bathe moro motimo mudho , to obiro bedo marieny , mana ka gima taya marieny ema miyi ler . ”
Kane Yesu osetieko wuoyo , ja-Farisai moro noluonge mondo odhi ochiem e ode . Omiyo nodhi , mobet piny mondo ochiem .
To kane ja-Farisaino oneno kochiemo ma ok okwongo ologo e yo ma chikgi dwaro , nowuoro .
Kuom mano , Ruoth Yesu nowachone ni , “ Un jo-Farisai uluoko kang’e agwata kod kang’e tawo , to chunyu opong’ gi mecho kod richo mamoko .
Mano kaka ufuwo ! Donge Jal mane ochueyo ng’e gik moko ema nochueyo koda ka igi bende ?
To chiwuru ni joma odhier gik ma un-go , eka gik moko duto nobednu maler .
“ Mano kaka unune malit , un jo-Farisai ! Uketo chunyu kuom chiwo ni Nyasaye mich mar achiel kuom apar mar apoth gi onyulo , kod alode mamoko duto maonge tich , to uweyo ng’ado bura kare , kendo ok uhero Nyasaye ! Gigo ema onego bed ni utimo to mamokogo bende ok onego uwe mak utimo .
“ Mano kaka unune malit , un jo-Farisai , nikech uhero kombe moyiedhi e ut lemo , kendo uhero mondo omosu kamiyou duong’ kuonde ma ji ochokoree .
Mano kaka unune malit , nikech uchalo gi liete mag joma otho , ma ok oketie alama , ma ji wuotho e wigi ka ok ong’eyo , mi dok magak ! ”
Eka japuonj Chik moro nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Japuonj , ka iwacho kamano , to wan bende iyanyowa ! ”
Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Mano kaka un bende unune malit , un jopuonj Chik , nikech ugango ni ji misike mapek mohewogi ting’o , to un uwegi ok umulgi kata mana gi lith lwetu .
Bende mano kaka unune malit , nikech umwono liete jonabi , to gin mana jonabi ma kwereu ema ne onego !
Kamano unyiso ni uyie gi gima kwereu notimo , nikech gin ema ne ginego jonabi , kendo koro un ema umwono liete jonabigo !
Mano emomiyo rieko Nyasaye nowacho niya , ‘ Abiro oronigi jonabi kod joote , to ginineg moko kuomgi , kendo moko bende ginisandi . ’ .
Kuom mano , tieng’ ma kawuononi biro yudo kum nikech remb jonabi duto mosechuer nyaka ne chue piny ,
chakre remb Habil , nyaka remb Zekaria mane onegi e kind kendo-mar-misango kod Kama Ler mar Hekalu . Adier , awachonu ni tieng’ ma kawuononi noyud kum kuom remogo duto .
“ Mano kaka uneno malit , un jopuonj Chik , nikech usepando rayaw mar dhood rieko . Un uwegi ok usedonjo kanyo , to bende usebedo kutamo joma dwaro donjoe . ”
Kane Yesu osea kanyo , jopuonj Chik gi jo-Farisai nochako bedo mamon kode ahinya , kendo ne gichande gi penjo mang’eny ,
ka gikiyo wach moro marach mawuok e dhoge mondo gimakego .
E kindeno , kane ji osechokore gana gi gana ma koro ginyonore anyona , Yesu nokwongo owuoyo gi jopuonjrene , kowachonigi niya , “ Beduru motang’ ni thop jo-Farisai , ma en mana wuondruok .
Onge gimoro amora mopandi ma ok nong’ere achien , kendo onge wach moro maling’ling’ ma ok nofwenyre .
Kuom mano , gimoro amora musewacho e mudho , nowinji e lela , bende gimoro amora ma usekuodho ni ji kuonde mopondo , nohul ratiro .
“ Un osiepena , awachonu ni kik uluor joma nego mana ringruok kende , to bang’e onge gima rach ma ginyalo medo timo .
To adwaro nyisou ng’at monego uluor ; Luoruru Nyasaye nimar en ema en gi teko , ma , ka oseneg ng’ato to onyalo wito e mach mak tho . Adier awachonu ni , luoruru Jalo !
Oyundi abich donge ing’iewo otonglo ariyo kende ? To kata kamano , onge kata achiel kuomgi ma wi Nyasaye nyalo wilgo .
To un , kata mana yie wiu duto bende osekwan . Kuom mano , kik ubed maluor , nikech un uloyo winy ndalo mang’eny .
“ Awachonu ni ng’ato ang’ata mahulo e nyim ji ni en ng’ata , Wuod Dhano bende nohul ni en ng’ate e nyim malaika mag Nyasaye .
To ng’ato ang’ata ma kweda e nyim ji , Wuod Dhano bende nokwede e nyim malaika mag Nyasaye .
Ng’ato ang’ata mowacho gimoro marach kuom Wuod Dhano , nowene , to ng’at moyanyo Roho Maler ok nowene .
Ka omaku , moteru mondo oyalu e nyim jodong ut lemo , kata e nyim ruodhi , kata e nyim jotelo mamoko , to kik uparru kuom weche ma dudwoki , kata kuom gima duwachi ,
nimar Roho Maler nopuonju gima onego uwachi e sano . ”
Ng’at moro mane nie oganda nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Japuonj , nyis owadwa mondo opogna mwandu mane wuonwa oweyo . ”
To Yesu nodwoke kapenje ni , “ Omera , ng’a moketa jang’ad bura kata jathek e kindu ? ”
Eka nomedo wacho ni ji duto niya , “ Beduru motang’ , mondo uritru kuom gombo duto nikech mwandu ok nyal miyo ng’ato bed mangima , kata dabed ni omew machal nadi . ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nogoyonigi ngero niya , “ Ne nitie jamoko moro man gi puodho ma higa moro nochiego cham mathoth .
Omiyo nochako paro e chunye ni , ‘ Ere gima datim ? Aonge gi kama anyalo kanoe chamba duto . ’ .
Eka nowacho ni , ‘ Ang’eyo gima abiro timo ! Abiro muko derena , mi ago moko madongo moloyogi , mondo akanie chamba kod giga moko duto . ’ .
Bang’e anawach e chunya ni , ‘ An jahawi , nikech asekano gik mathoth , moroma kuom higni mang’eny ! Koro anyalo yueyo ka achiemo kendo ametho , ka amor . ’ .
To Nyasaye nowacho ni ng’atno niya , ‘ In ng’at mofuwo ! Otieno ma kawuononi ang’ nokaw chunyi ! To koro gik misekanogo duto biro konyi gang’o ? ’ ”
Eka Yesu notieko kawacho ni , “ Mano e kaka obet kuom ng’ama choko mwandu ni en owuon , to ok omew e wang’ Nyasaye ! ”
Yesu nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Mano emomiyo awachonu ni kik uparru kuom chiemo ma ducham mondo ubed mangima , kata kuom lewni ma durwaki mondo uumgo dendu ,
nikech ngima duong’ moloyo chiemo , kendo ringruok oloyo law .
Par ane uru winy . Ok gichwo kodhi , kata ok gika cham . Bende gionge dere kata kuonde keno , to Nyasaye pod pidhogi apidha . Unto donge uberne moloyo winy nyadi ng’eny !
Ere ng’ato kuomu ma parruok dimi ndalone medre ?
Koro ka ok unyal timo kata mana gima tin kamano , to ere gima omiyo uparoru kuom weche mamoko ?
Parieuru kaka ondanyo dongo ! Ok giti gimoro , bende ok gitwang’ lewni ma girwako , to awachonu ni kata mana Solomon gi mwandune duto mathothgo ne ok nyal rwakore maber ka ondanyo .
To ka Nyasaye nyalo rwako lum aluma manie thim kawuono , to kiny ipudho kendo ibolo e mach , to koro un dorwaku maber machal nadi ? Yaye , un joma nigi yie matin-gi !
Kuom mano kik uket parou kuom gik ma ducham , kata kuom gik ma dumadhi . Bende kik ubed gi parruok ,
nikech gik makamago ema ogendini duto mae piny chandore kadwaro . Un to , Wuonu ong’eyo ni onego uyudgi .
Kar dwaro gigo , to dwaruru mana ni Loch Nyasaye obedie , eka gigo duto nomedu .
“ Kik uluor , un kueth matinni , nimar Wuonu ohero miyo ubed gi loch kaachiel kode .
Lokuru giu duto pesa mondo upog ni joma odhier , eka ubed gi mwandu mak rum e polo , kuma jakuo ok dhiye , kendo kuma olwenda ok kethie gik moko ,
nikech kama mwanduni nitie , e kama chunyi bende nitie .
“ Ng’wanuru lepu , kendo mokuru techeu mondo ubed moikore .
Beduru ka jotich marito ruodhgi modhi e nyasi kisera , mondo koduogo mi odwong’o , to giyawne piyopiyo .
Mano kaka jotich ma ruodhgi yudo ka neno , kendo oikore , gin johawi ! Awachonu adier ni , ruodhgino nong’wan lepe , kendo nomi gibed piny e mesa , mi omigi chiemo .
Kata ka obiro mana odiwuor kata kogwen , moyudo ka giikore , to mano kaka gin johawi !
Ng’euru ni ka wuon ot ong’eyo sa ma jakuo biroe , to dobed korito ode , motam jakuo turo .
Omiyo un bende beduru kuikoru , nikech Wuod Dhano biro biro e sa ma ok ung’eyo ni onyalo biroe . ”
Petro nopenjo Yesu niya , “ Ruoth , wan kendwa ema igoyonwa ngeroni , koso igoye ni ji duto ? ”
Eka Ruoth Yesu nowacho niya , “ Ere ng’ato kuomu machalo gi jatich mogen kendo mariek , ma ruodhe biro keto mondo orit jotich wetene , kendo opognigi chiemo e kinde mowinjore ?
Jatich ma ka ruodhe oduogo to yudo katiyo kamano , en jahawi !
Adier awachonu ni ruodhe nokete jarit mwandune duto .
To ka en jatich ma paro e chunye ni ruodhe ok bi duogo piyo , to onyalo chako goyo jotich wetene , machwo gi mamon , kendo dochiem achiema , mi omethi , kendo omer .
To chieng’ moro nopo ka ruodhe oduogo e sa ma ok ong’eyo , mi ruodhe nong’ade sirunde sirunde ! Kamano nokume kaachiel gi joma ok oyie kuom Nyasaye .
“ Jatich mong’eyo gima ruodhe dwaro ni mondo otim , to ok tem timo kamano nochwad malit ,
to jatich ma ok ong’eyo gima ruodhe dwaro ni mondo otim , mi oboth motimo gima owinjore gi kum , to nochwad mana matin . Ng’at momi gik mang’eny , nodwar kuome gik mang’eny . Adier ng’at mogen gi gik mang’eny nodwar kuome gik mang’eny moloyo !
“ Ne abiro mondo amok mach e piny , to mad aye bed ni osemoke !
Nitie sand mibiro sandago , to mano kaka chunya parore nyaka chop ayud sandno .
Uparo ni ne abiro mondo akel kue e piny koso ? Ooyo , ok asebiro mondo akel kue , to mana ni mondo akel pogruok !
Chakre ndalogi , ji abich ma joot achiel biro pogore , ka ji adek odok konchiel , to ariyo komachielo .
Wuowi nopogre gi wuon mare , kendo nyako nopogre gi min . Chiwuowi bende nopogre gi wuon odgi . ”
Yesu nowacho bende ni ji niya , “ Ka uneno boche polo koting’ore yo podho chieng’ , to uwacho piyopiyo ni , ‘ Koth biro chue , ’ kendo ochue adier !
To bende ka uneno yamb oro ka kudho , to uwacho ni , ‘ Oro biro wuok , ’ kendo adier , oro wuok .
Un muwuondoru awuondagi ! Ka ulony kuom rango polo gi piny kamano , mi ung’e gima biro timore , to ang’o ma monou fwenyo tiend gik matimore ndalogi ?
“ Marang’o un uwegi ok ung’eyo gima kare monego utim ?
Ka ng’ato odonjoni , to onego item matek mondo uwinjru kode kapok uchopo e od bura , nono to oteri e nyim jang’ad bura , mi jang’ad bura diketi e lwet askari , mi askari boli e jela .
Awachoni ni koserwaki kanyo , to ok diwuog ngang’ kapok ichulo faini duto te ! ”
E kinde nogo , jomoko nobiro , monyiso Yesu wach jo-Galili mane Pilato onego ka jotimo misango .
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Uparo ni jo-Galili noneno masira malit kamano nikech ne gin joma richo moloyo jo-Galili mamoko duto koso ?
Ooyo , awachonu ni ka ok ulokoru uweyo richou , to uduto ubiro tho mana kaka ne githono !
Koso uparo ni ji apar gaboro mane ohinga mar Siloam opodho kuomgi , mi onego kande , ne joketho moloyo jo-Jerusalem mamoko duto koso ?
Ooyo , anyisou ni ka ok ulokoru uweyo richou , to uduto ubiro tho mana kaka ne githono ! ”
Eka Yesu nogoyonigi ngero niya , “ Ng’at moro ne nigi yadh ng’owo e puothe mar mzabibu . Chieng’ moro ne odhi rango ka doyud olemo kuome , to ne ok oyudo .
Eka nowacho ni jalos puodhono ni , ‘ Koro kuom higni adekgi asebedo kabiro ka mondo ayudie olemo kuom ng’owoni , to ok aseyudo gimoro . Omiyo tong’e oko . Ere gimomiyo onego oketh lowo kayiem nono ? ’
To jalos puodho nodwoke niya , ‘ Jaduong’ , yie iweye higani bende . Abiro doye , ma aketne owuoyo .
Kamano , ka onyago olemo higa mabironi , to mano ber . To ka ok onyago , to koro eka nitong’e oko . ’ . ”
Chieng’ Sabato moro , Yesu ne puonjo e od lemo moro .
To e od lemo kanyo ne nitie dhako moro man gi jachien moseloke jamidekre kuom higni apar gaboro , kendo dende ne odolore ma ok nyal riere kata matin .
Kane Yesu onene , ne oluonge ire , mowachone niya , “ Nyarwa , isechango kuom midekreni ! ”
Eka noketo lwete kuom dhakono , mi gikanyono dhakono norioere tir modendo Nyasaye .
Kane jaduong’ od lemo oneno ka Yesu ochango dhakono chieng’ Sabato kamano , mirima nomake , mi owacho ni ji niya , “ Nitie ndalo auchiel ma onego ji tiye , omiyo biuru e ndalogo mondo ochangu , to kik ubi chieng’ Sabato . ”
Ruoth Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Un joma wuondore ni ohero Nyasayegi ! Donge ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu gonyo dhere kata kanje e kul chieng’ Sabato , mi ter modho ?
Koro dhako ma nyakwar Ibrahim , ma jachien osebedo kotueyo kuom higni apar gaboroni , donge ber kogony e tuech ma kamano chieng’ Sabato ? ”
Dwokone nokwodo wi wasike duto , to ji mamoko nodoko mamor kuom gik malich duto mane otimo .
Yesu nopenjo niya , “ Ere kaka Loch Nyasaye chalo ? Ang’o ma dapimego ?
Ochalo gi koth karadali mane ng’ato okawo , mopidho e puothe . Kodhino nodongo , modoko yath maduong’ , kendo winy nogedo e bedene . ”
Yesu nopenjo kendo ni , “ Ang’o ma dapimgo Loch Nyasaye ?
Ochalo gi thowi mane dhako moro okawo , mi odwalogo mogo atonge adek , mi bang’e okuot maber . ”
Kane yesu nie wuoth , kadhi Jerusalem , norawo e mier madongo gi matindo , kendo nopuonjo ji .
Ng’at moro nopenje niya , “ Jaduong’ , ji manok kende ema nokwo koso ? ” Yesu nodwoke niya ,
“ Temuru matek mondo udonj gie dhoot madiny , nikech awachonu ni , ji mang’eny nodwar donjo , to ok gininyal .
Jaduong’ ot biro chung’ , mi lor dhoot , to bang’ mano , kuchung’ oko mi udwong’o kuwacho ni , ‘ Jaduong’ , yawnwa’ , to nodwoku ni , ‘ Ok ang’eyou ! Ua kanye ? ’
Eka nuchak wacho niya , ‘ Ne wachiemo kendo wametho kodi , kendo ne ipuonjo e miechwa . ’ .
To enodwoku ni , ‘ Awachonu ni ok ang’eyou , kata kuma uaye bende ok ang’eyo . Auru kuoma , un joma timbegi richogi ! ’
“ Mano kaka unuyuagru malit , kumwodo laku , ka uneno Ibrahim gi Isaka kod Jakobo kod jonabi duto e Piny Ruoth Nyasaye , to un oriembu oko .
Ji nobi kowuok yo wuokchieng’ kod yo podho chieng’ , kod koa yo nyandwat kod milambo , mi ginibed piny mondo gichiem e nyasi manie piny Ruoth Nyasaye .
Adier , jomoko ma koro odong’ chien notel , to jomoko ma koro otelo nodog chien ! ”
E sanogo , jo-Farisai moko nobiro ir Yesu , mowachone ni , “ Ber mondo ia ka , nikech Herode dwaro negi . ”
To nowachonigi niya , “ Dhiuru unyis andhogano ni , agolo jochiende kendo achango ji kawuono gi kiny , to chieng’ mar adek abiro tieko tija .
To onego adhi nyime gi wuodha kawuono gi kiny kod orucha , nikech janabi ok nyal tho oko kamoro nono , to mak mana Jerusalem .
“ Yaye jo-Jerusalem ! Yaye jo-Jerusalem ! Un munego jonabi , kendo ugoyo joma Nyasaye ooro iru gi kite ! Mano kaka asedwaro mondo achoku duto kaka nyabuch gweno chokon nyithinde e bwombe , to usetamoru .
Koro dalau biro dong’ gunda . Awachonu ni chakre kawuono ok unuchak unena kendo , nyaka kinde chopi ma unuwachie ni , ‘ Ogwedh ng’ama biro e nying Ruoth . ’ . ”
Chieng’ Sabato moro , Yesu nodhi chiemo e od jaduong’ jo-Farisai moro , kendo ji ne ng’iye ahinya .
To e odno ne nitie ng’ato e nyim Yesu ma mbunda ohingo .
Yesu nopenjo jopuonj Chik kod jo-Farisai ni , “ Chikwa oyie mondo ochang ji chieng’ Sabato , koso ok oyie ? ”
To ne ok gidwoke gimoro . Eka nokawo ng’atno mi ochango , kendo oweyo odhi .
Bang’ mano nowachonigi niya , “ Ere ng’ato kuomu ma ka kanje kata rwadhe opodho e bugo chieng’ Sabato , to ok dogole mana gikanyono ? ”
To dwoko penjono notamogi .
Yesu noneno ka welo yiero kombe moyiedhi , omiyo nowachonigi niya ,
“ Ka oluongi e nyasi moro mar kisera , to kik ibed e kom moyiedhi , nikech dipo ka ng’at moluongi oluongo koda ng’at moloyi gi duong’ bende .
Eka kamoro dipo ka ng’at mane oluongouno obiro , mowachoni ni , ‘ Weni jali komino . ’ . Kamano wiyi dikuodi , kidhi bet e kom man chien moloyo .
Kuom mano , ka oluongi kamoro , to dhi ibed mana e kom man chien moloyo , mondo ka ng’ama oluongino obiro , to owachni ni , ‘ Osiepna , sudi ibi nyime ku . ’ . Kamano iniyud duong’ e nyim welo mamoko duto ,
nikech ng’at mating’ore malo nodwok piny , to ng’at madwokore piny noting’ malo . ”
Eka Yesu nowacho bende ni ng’at mane oluongeno ni , “ Ka iluongo ji e chiemb odiechieng’ , kata chiemb otieno , to kik iluong mana osiepeni kata oweteni kata wedeni kata jogweng’u momew , nimar dipo ka gin bende chieng’ moro giluongi , mi gichuli kar luong mane iluongogigono .
To kiloso nyasi , to luong mana joma odhier gi rang’onde gi pudhe kod muofni ,
eka inibed ng’ama oguedhi , nikech gin gionge gima digichulgo . To Nyasaye nochuli chieng’ ma joma kare ochiere . ”
Ng’at achiel kuom joma ne chiemo kod Yesu nowinjo wechego , mowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Mano kaka joma nobet ka chiemo e nyasi manie Piny Ruoth Nyasaye gin johawi ! ”
To Yesu nowachone ni , “ Ng’at moro noloso nyasi maduong’ , mi oluongo ji mathoth .
Kane chiemo oseikore , ne ooro jotichne mondo odhi owach ni joma oluongi niya , ‘ Biuru nikech gik moko duto oseikore . ’ .
To giduto kar rombgi ne gichako wacho weche ma ginyisogo wuon nyasi gimomiyo ok ginyal biro . Ng’at mokwongo nowacho ni jatich mane oor ni , ‘ Aseng’iewo puodho moro , omiyo nyaka adhi anene . Kuom mano wach ni ruodhi mondo ong’wonna . ’ .
Ng’at machielo to nowacho ni , ‘ Aseng’iewo ruedhi apar mag pur , omiyo nyaka adhi atemgi . Kuom mano , wach ni ruodhi mondo ong’wonna . ’ .
Ng’at moro to nowacho ni , ‘ An gi miaha , omiyo ok anyal biro . ’ .
Eka jatich nobiro monyiso ruodhe wechego . Mirima nomako wuon nyasi , mi owacho ni jatichne niya , ‘ Wuogi piyo , idhi e yore gi chirni , mondo ikel joma odhier gi rang’onde gi muofni kod pudhe miyudo . ’ .
To kane jatich oduogo , nowacho ni ruodhe niya , ‘ Jaduong’ , wasetimo kaka nende iwacho , to thuolo pod nitie mar luongo jomoko . ’ .
Eka ruodhe nochako owachone ni , ‘ Dhiyo e wang’yore kod gweng’ duto , iwach ni ji kijiwogi ni nyaka gibi mondo oda opong’ thich !
Awachonu adier ni onge kata ng’at achiel kuom ji mane oluongi ma nobil chiemba . ’ . ”
Chieng’ moro kane oyudo ji mathoth luwo bang’ Yesu , nolokore , mowachonigi niya ,
“ Ka ng’ato obiro ira , to ok ojwang’o wuon kod min , gi chiege gi nyithinde koda ka ngimane owuon , to ok onyal doko japuonjrena .
Bende ng’at ma ok nyal ting’o msalape owuon mi luwa , ok nyal doko japuonjrena .
“ En ng’a kuomu , ma kadwaro gero ot , to ok kwong bed piny , mi pim nengo , mondo one ane kaa en gi pesa moromo tieko tijno ?
Ka ok otimo kamano , to ok dotiek gero odno bang’ keto mise , kendo ji duto moneno gima otimore dinyiere ,
kawacho ni , ‘ Jali nochako gedo , to otame tieko ! ’
“ Koso ka ruoth moro dwaro kedo gi ruoth machielo , donge okwongo obet piny mi one ane ka ji alufu apar ma en-go onyalo chomogo jal mabiro monje gi ji alufu piero ariyo ?
Ka oneno ni ok donyal , to ooro joote ka pod ruoth machielo ni kuma bor , mondo onyise ni odwaro mondo giwinjre e yor kue .
Kamano bende onge ng’ato kuomu manyalo bedo japuonjrena ka ok oweyo gige duto .
“ Kado ber , to ka ndhathe orumo , to ere kaka dumi ochak obed gi ndhadhu kendo ?
Kado ma kamano onge gi tich kuom loso lowo , kata loso pidh owuoyo , omiyo ipuke mana oko . Ng’at man gi it mar winjo , to mondo owinji . ”
Chieng’ moro josol osuru mang’eny kod joricho nosudo but Yesu mondo oyud puonjne .
Eka jo-Farisai kod jopuonj Chik ne jochako ng’ur ni , “ Jali rwako joricho , kendo ochiemo achiema kodgi . ”
To Yesu nogoyonigi ngero niya ,
“ Ka ng’ato kuomu nigi rombe mia achiel , to achiel olalne , donge dowe rombe mamoko piero ochiko gochiko e lek , to odhi manyo achiel molalno nyaka oyudi ?
To koyude , to odoko mamor ahinya kendo oting’e mana e goke ,
kodwoke dala . Bang’e oluongo osiepene kod jogweng’gi , kendo owachonigi niya , ‘ Wachiemuru , nikech amor chutho , nimar aseyudo rombona ma nyocha olal . ’ .
“ Koro akonu ni , kamano bende e kaka mor nobedi e polo kuom jaricho achiel molokore , moloyo mor ma nobed kuom ji piero ochiko gochiko mabeyo , maparo ni ok onego lokre .
“ Koso ka dhako moro nigi siling’ apar mamingli , to achiel olalne , donge domok taya , mi oyue ode komanyo maber kuonde duto nyaka oyude ?
Bang’e oluongo osiepene kod jogweng’gi kaachiel , kendo owachonigi niya , ‘ Wachiemuru nikech amor ahinya , nimar aseyudo pesana manyocha olalna . ’ .
Akonu ni , kamano bende e kaka malaika mag Nyasaye bedo mamor kuom jaricho achiel molokore . ”
Yesu nomedo wacho niya , “ Ng’at moro ne nigi yawuowi ariyo .
Wuowi machogo nowacho ni wuon mare ni , ‘ Wuora , yie ipogna mwandu monego ayudi . ’ . Kuom mano ng’atno nopogo yawuote ariyogo mwandune .
Bang’ ndalo manok , wuowi machogo noloko gige duto pesa , mi owuok odhi e piny moro mabor . Eka nodonjo e ngima mar anjawo kuno , motieko pesane duto .
Kane osetieko pesane duto kamano , kech maduong’ nowuok e pinyno , mi nodoko jachan machandore .
Kuom mano , nodhi mondo oti ni japinyno moro , mi jalo nokete jakwa ngurue .
Nogombo mondo ocham opokla mane ngurue chamo , to bende onge ng’ama nomiye gimoro .
Eka parone nodwogo kare , mi owacho e chunye niya , ‘ Jotich wuora duto nigi chiemo mohingogi , to an kech nega ka !
Abiro dhi kawuora , mi awachne ni , “ Wuora , aseketho e nyim Nyasaye kendo e nyimi ,
ok awinjora koro mondo iluonga ni wuodi , to keta abed achiel kuom jotichni . ” ’
“ Kamano noa malo , mochako wuoth madok ka wuon mare . To kane pod en mabor gi dala , wuon mare nonene . Nokeche , mi oringo okwake , monyodhe .
Eka wuowino nowacho ni wuon niya , ‘ Aseketho e nyim Nyasaye , kendo e nyimi . Ok awinjora koro mondo iluonga ni wuodi . ’ .
To wuon mare nowacho ni jotichne ni , ‘ Goluru law maberie moloyo piyopiyo mondo urwakne , kendo uketne tere e lith lwete . Wuoche bende mondo urwakne e tiende .
Bang’ mano , keluru nyarwath machwe uyang’ mondo wacham wabeduru mamor ,
nikech wuodani ne osetho , to koro ongima kendo ne olal , to koro onwang’e . ’ . Kamano ne gichako timo nyasi ka gimor .
“ E kindeno noyudo ka wuowi maduong’ ni oko e puodho , to kane odwogo mochopo machiegni gi dala , nowinjo ka thum ywak , kendo ji miel .
Omiyo ne oluongo achiel kuom jotich , mopenjo gima timore .
Jatich nodwoke niya , ‘ Owadu odwogo , kendo wuoru oseyang’one nyarwath machwe , nikech odwogo kongima maber . ’ .
To mirima nomako wuowi maduong’ , mi otamore donjo e ot , omiyo wuon mare nowuok , mohombe mondo odonji .
To nodwoko wuon niya , ‘ Parie kaka asetiyoni mana ka misumba kuom higni mathothgi duto , kendo pok aketho chikni kata dichiel , to pod ok imiya kata mana nyadiel mondo ayang’ acham gi osiepena !
To koro ka wuodi mosechamo mwanduni duto gi jochode obiro , to iyang’one nyarwath machwe ! ’
Wuon mare to nokone niya , ‘ Nyathina , ndalo duto in koda , kendo giga duto gin magi .
To owinjore wachiem kendo wabed mamor , nikech owaduni yandi otho , to koro ongima , kendo yande olal , to koro onwang’e . ’ . ”
Yesu nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Ne nitie jamoko moro mane oketo ng’ato mondo orit mwandune . To noyudo wach ni jatijno ketho gige .
Omiyo noluonge , mopenje niya , ‘ En wach mane ma awinjo kuomini ? Tim ane kwan kuom gigo duto mirito , nikech ok inyal dhi nyime gi bedo jarit giga ngang’ ! ’
Eka ng’atno nowacho e chunye niya , ‘ Ere gima koro anyalo timo , ka ruodha ogola e tich ? Aonge gi teko ma dapurgo , bende ok dakuechi nikech aluoro wich kuot .
Ero , koro ang’eyo gima abiro timo mondo ji orwaka e miechgi , koseriemba e tich . ’ .
Eka noluongo jogop ruodhe achiel achiel , mopenjo jagowi mokwongo ni , ‘ In gi gop ruodha moromo ang’o ? ’
Jalo nodwoke ni , ‘ Gopa oromo depe mia achiel mag mo . ’ . To nokone ni , ‘ Bed piny piyopiyo , mondo ikaw kitapi , indikie ni , piero abich . ’ .
Eka nopenjo ng’at machielo niya , ‘ In to gopi oromo adi ? ’ Ng’atno nodwoke ni , ‘ Gunde mia achiel mag cham . ’ . Eka nodwoke ni , ‘ Kaw kitapini , indikie ni piero aboro . ’ .
“ Jamokono nopako jarit gige ma ok kareno kuom riekone , kendo en adier ni joma ok ong’eyo Nyasaye tiyo gi jowadgi gi rieko moloyo rieko ma joma ong’eyo Nyasaye tiyogo gi jowetegi . ”
Eka Yesu nomedo wacho niya , “ Mano omiyo awachonu ni , tiuru gi mwandu mag pinyni kuom mako osiepe , mondo chieng’ ma mwandugo orumo , to orwaku e dala mochwere .
Ng’at ma jaadiera kuom gima tin , doko jaadiera kuom gima duong’ bende . Kamano bende , ng’at ma ok jaadiera kuom gima tin ok nyal bedo jaadiera kuom gima duong’ .
Emomiyo ka ok usebedo joadiera kuom mwandu ma ok ni kare mag pinyni , koro ng’ano ma digenu kuom mwandu madier ?
Koso ka ok usebedo joadiera kuom mwandu ng’at machielo , koro ere ng’ama dimiu mwanduu uwegi ?
“ Onge misumba manyalo tiyo ni ruodhi ariyo , nimar dosin gi moro , to ohero machielo , kata domi achiel luor , to ochayo machielo . Omiyo ok unyal tiyo ni Nyasaye , mi kendo uchak uti ni mwandu . ”
Jo-Farisai , ma gin joma ohero pesa ahinya , nowinjo wechego duto , mi onyiere anyiera .
To Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Un e joma wuorore e nyim ji ni joma kare , to Nyasaye ong’eyo chunyu . Ng’euru ni Nyasaye ochayo gik moko ma dhano kwano ka gik madongo .
“ Chik Musa kod weche jonabi ne nigi teko nyaka chop ndalo Johana , kendo chakre kanyo , Wach Maber mar Loch Nyasaye osebedo kilando , kendo ng’ato ka ng’ato riyore mondo odonjie .
To yot mondo polo gi piny orum , moloyo ka nukta achiel matinie moloyo mar Chik lal .
“ Ka ng’ato oriembo chiege , mi okendo dhako machielo , to oterore . Bende ka ng’ato okendo dhako ma chwore oriembo , to mano bende oterore . ”
Yesu nogoyo nigi ngero niya , “ Ne nitie jamoko moro mane rwako lewni mabeyo ma nengogi tek , kendo ne odak e ngima mamalo , kochamo chiemo mabeyo pilepile .
To bende ne nitie ng’at moro modhier , ma nyinge Lazaro , ma adhonde opong’o dende . Ne ikete e dhoranga jamokono pilepile ,
kendo nogombo chamo ng’injo molwar e bwo mesa jamokono . Kata mana gwogi bende ne biro mi nang’ adhondene .
To mos achien , ng’at modhierno notho , mi malaika noting’e , motere e bath Ibrahim . Bang’e jamokono bende notho , mi oyiki .
Kane en e Piny Joma Otho kisande malit , noting’o wang’e moneno Ibrahim gi kuma bor , kod Lazaro kobet e bathe .
Eka nokok kowacho niya , ‘ Wuonwa Ibrahim , kecha mondo ior Lazaro olut lith lwete e pi , okuego lewa , nikech an gi rem malit e ligegani ! ’
To Ibrahim nodwoke ni , ‘ Wuoda , par ni kane pod ingima ne iyudo gik moko mabeyo , to Lazaro ne yudo gik maricho . To koro sani oneno maber kaeri , ka into inie rem malit .
To bende e kindwa kodi nitie hoho mang’ongo mopogowa , mondo otam joma dwaro kalo kaa koni biro iru , kendo kik ji ng’ad koa koru kabiro koni . ’ .
Eka ng’atno nowacho ni Ibrahim ni , ‘ Wuonwa , ka kamano , to kara ornago e dala wuora ,
mondo osiem owetena abich modong’ kuno , kik gibi kar sand malit . ’ .
To Ibrahim nodwoke niya , ‘ Gin gi weche Musa kod mag Jonabi kuno , omiyo ber mondo giwinjgi . ’ .
To en nowacho ni , ‘ Ooyo wuonwa Ibrahim ! Ka ng’at moa kuom joma otho odhi irgi , eka digilokre . ’ .
Ibrahim to nokone niya , ‘ Ka ok ginyal winjo weche Musa kod Jonabi , to ok giniwinj kata mana ng’at mochier oa kuom joma otho ! ’ ”
Yesu nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Gik mamiyo ji donjo e richo ok nyal bare mak obetie . To mano kaka nobed malit ni ng’at makelogi !
Da obedo maber ka otuene pong’ e ng’ute , mi onyumego e nam , moloyo komiyo achiel kuom joma tindogi odonjo e richo .
Beduru motang’ ! Ka owadu okethoni , to kwere . To koyie kethone , to wene .
Ka okethoni nyadibiriyo e odiechieng’ achiel , mi obiro iri ndalo abiriyo kokwayi mondo iwene , to nyaka iwene . ”
Joote nowacho ni Ruoth Yesu niya , “ Medwa yie . ”
To Ruoth nowachonigi niya , “ Da bed ni un gi yie kata matin marom gi koth karadali , to da uwacho ni yadhni ni , ‘ Pudhri , mondo idhi ipidhri e nam , ’ mi dowinjou .
“ Ere ng’ato kuomu man gi jatich mapuro kata makwayo jambe , ma ka jatichno oa puodho to dowachne ni , ‘ Reti ibi ibed piny mondo ichiem’ ?
Donge dowachne mana ni , ‘ Losna chiemo , kendo iikri mondo igamna gima adwaro kachiemo kendo ametho . Eka bang’e in bende ibi ichiem . ’ .
Koso uparo ni bende dogo ni jatichneno erokamano kuom timo gima nowachone ni mondo otim ?
Kamano e kaka un bende , ka usetimo gik moko duto mane onyisu ni mondo utim , to onego uwach ni , ‘ Wan mana jotich aticha , omiyo onge erokamano monego wayudi , nikech wasetiyo mana tichwa . ’ . ”
Kane Yesu dhi Jerusalem , nowuotho e kind Samaria gi Galili .
Noyudo odonjo e dala moro , mi jodhoho apar noromo kode . Ne gichung’ gi chien ,
mi gikok niya , “ Yesu ! Yie ikechwa . ”
Yesu nonenogi , mowachonigi ni , “ Dhiuru ir jadolo mondo orang dendu . ” To kane oyudo gin e yo gidhi , ne gichango .
Achiel kuomgi , kane oneno ni osechango , nodwogo ir Yesu kopako Nyasaye matek .
Ne ogoyo chonge piny , mokulore e tiend Yesu , kogoyone erokamano . To ne en ja-Samaria !
Yesu nopenjo niya , “ Donge ne gin ji apar mane ochango koso ? Koro ere ji ochiko mamoko ?
Ere gima omiyo japiny moro nononi kende ema oduogo mondo ogo ni Nyasaye erokamano ? ”
Eka nowacho ni ng’atno niya , “ Chungi , idhi . Yieni ema omiyo ichango . ”
Jo-Farisai moko nopenjo Yesu chieng’ ma Loch Nyasaye nobie . Nodwokogi niya , “ Onge ranyisi ma ji biro neno manyiso chieng’ ma Loch Nyasaye biroe .
Bende onge ng’ama nowach ni , ‘ Neuru , erigo ! ’ kata ni , ‘ Echago cha , ’ nikech Loch Nyasaye nie dieru ! ”
Eka nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Ndalo nobi ma unugomb nenoe chieng’ achiel kuom ndalo mag Wuod Dhano , to ok unune .
Bende jomoko nowachnu ni , ‘ Neuru , en kucha ! ’ kata ni , ‘ Neuru , en ka ! ’ To kik uwuog mondo uluwgi ,
nikech kaka mil polo piatore e kor polo koa konchiel nyaka komachielo , e kaka Wuod Dhano bende nobedi chieng’ mobiroe .
To mokwongo nyaka one masiche mang’eny , kendo tieng’ ma kawuononi nyaka dage .
Kaka notimore e ndalo Nowa , e kaka notimre e ndalo Wuod Dhano .
Ji duto nosiko chiemo achiema kendo metho . Chwo ne kendo , kendo nyiri bende ne dhi tedo , nyaka nochopo chieng’ mane Nowa odonjo e yie , mi pi oimo piny , motieko ji pep .
Kamano bende , kaka notimore e ndalo mag Lut , e kaka notimre chieng’ ma Wuod dhano biroe . Ji ne chiemo kendo metho . Ne ging’iewo , kendo ne giloko ohala , bende ne gichwoyo , kendo gigedo .
To chieng’ mane Lut owuokie Sodom , mach kod kite maliel nolwar koa e polo , mi otieko gi pep .
Kamano e kaka notimre chieng’ ma Wuod Dhano nonyisree .
“ Ng’at manie wi tat ode chieng’no kik lor piny mondo ogol gige manie ot odhigo . Bende ng’at man oko e puodho kik dog dala .
Paruru gima notimore ni chi Lut !
Ka ng’ato otemo reso ngimane , to ngimane nolalne , to ka ng’at ma ojwang’o ngimane , nores ngimane .
Awachonu ni , otienono ji ariyo nobed kanindo e kitanda achiel ; achiel nokaw , to machielo nowe .
Mon ariyo bende nobed ka rego kaachiel ; achiel nokaw to machielo nowe . [
Ji ariyo nobed katiyo e puodho ; achiel nokaw , to machielo nowe . ” ]
Eka ne gipenje niya , “ Mano notimre kanye , Ruoth ? ” Nodwokogi ni , “ Kama gimoro othoe ema achudhe chokoree ! ”
Yesu nogoyo ni jopuonjrene ngero moro mondo opuonjgigo lamo Nyasaye pile mak ginyosore .
Nowachonigi niya , “ Jang’ad bura moro ma ok oluoro Nyasaye , kendo ma ok odewo ji , ne odak e dala moro .
To chi liel moro ma bende nodak e dalano ne osiko biro ire pile , kakwaye ni , ‘ Yie ing’adna bura e kinda gi jal ma an-go gi wach . ’ .
Kuom kinde mang’eny jang’ad burano notamore winjo wachne , to bang’e achien nowacho e chunye niya , ‘ Kata obedo ni ok aluoro Nyasaye , kendo ok adew ji kamano ,
to chi lielni chanda , omiyo abiro ng’adone bura kare , mondo kik obemba gi biro ira pile . ’ . ”
Eka Ruoth Yesu nodhi nyime kawacho niya , “ Winjeuru gima ne jang’ad bura ma ok kareno owacho !
Koro donge Nyasaye nong’ad bura kare ni joge moyier , maywakne odiechieng’ gotieno ? Uparo ni dodeki mak okonyogi koso ?
Ooyo ! Awachonu ni nong’adni bura kare piyopiyo . To chieng’ ma Wuod Dhano obiroe e piny , uparo ni nonwang’ joma oyie kuome koso ? ”
Joma ne paro giwegi ni gin joma kare , kendo mane ochayo ji mamoko duto , bende Yesu nogoyonigi ngero kama :
“ Ji ariyo nodhi e Hekalu mondo olem . Achiel ne ja-Farisai , to machielo ne jasol osuru .
Ja-Farisai nochung’ kar kende , mi olemo niya , ‘ A Nyasaye , agoyoni erokamano , nikech ok achal gi jomoko duto , ma jomecho kendo jagang wach kendo ma joma terore . To bende ok achal gi jasol osuruni .
Atweyo chiemo diriyo e juma ka juma , kendo achiwoni achiel kuom apar mag gik moko duto ma anwang’o . ’ .
Jasol osuru to ne ochung’ gi chien kendo ne pok ohedhore kata mana ting’o wiye mondo orang polo , to noywagore malit , kowacho ni , ‘ A Nyasaye , yie ikecha , an ma an jarichoni . ’ . ”
Eka Yesu , notieko kawacho niya , “ Akonu ni ng’atni nodok dala ka ni kare e nyim Nyasaye moloyo ng’at machielo cha , nimar ng’at ma ting’ore malo nodwok piny , to ng’at ma dwokore piny noting’ malo . ”
Jomoko nokelo koda ka nyithindo matindo ir Yesu , mondo oket lwete kuomgi . To jopuonjrene noneno kamano , mokwerogi .
To Yesu noluongogi , kawacho ni . “ Weuru nyithindo obi ira ! Kik utamgi , nikech joma kamagi ema yudo gueth mar Loch Nyasaye .
Awachonu adier ni , Ng’at ma ok oyie Loch Nyasaye gi chuny machalo gi chuny nyathi matin , ok noyud gueth mar lochne ngang’ . ”
Jaduong’ jo-Yahudi moro nopenjo Yesu niya , “ Japuonj ! In , in g’ama ber . Koro ere gima onego atim mondo ayud ngima mochwere ? ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Ang’o momiyo iwacho ni an ng’ama ber ? Onge ng’ama ber , mak mana Nyasaye kende .
Donge ing’eyo chike , mawacho ni , ‘ Kik iterri , kik ineki , kik ikwal , kik ihang wach , ’ kendo ni ‘ Luor wuoru gi meru’ ? ”
Ng’atno nodwoke ni , “ Aserito chikego duto , chakre aa e nyathi . ”
Kane Yesu owinjo kamano , nowachone niya , “ Gimoro achiel ema pod onego itim . Lok gigi duto pesa , mondo ipog ni joma odhier , eka inibed gi mwandu e polo . Ka isetimo kamano , to bi iluwa . ”
Kane ng’atno owinjo kamano , chunye nodoko malit , nikech ne en jamoko ahinya .
Yesu noneno ka chunye lit , mi owacho niya , “ Mano kaka donjo e Piny Ruoth Nyasaye tek ni joma nigi mwandu .
Yot ni ngamia kadho e wang’ sandan , moloyo jamoko donjo e Piny Ruoth Nyasaye ! ”
Joma ne owinjo kowacho kamano , nopenjore ni , “ Kara , ere ng’ama nokwo ? ”
To Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Gik ma dhano ok nyal , Nyasaye ema nyalo . ”
Eka Petro nowachone ni , “ To wan waseweyo miechewa , mwaluwi . ”
Yesu nodwoke , kawachonigi ni , “ Adier awachonu ni , ng’ama oweyo dalane kata chiege kata owetene kata jonywolne kata nyithinde nikech Loch Nyasaye ,
noyud gik mang’eny e pinyni , moloyo mago moseweyo . To e piny mabiro noyudie ngima mochwere . ”
Yesu nokawo jopuonjrene apar gariyo , motero kar kendgi , mi owachonogi niya , “ Winjuru ! Koro wadhi Jerusalem , kuma gik moko duto mane jonabi ondiko kuom Wuod Dhano biro timoree adier .
Ibiro chiwe e lwet joma ok jo-Yahudi , mi jogo nochare kendo noyanye kendo nong’udh kuome olawo .
Bende ginichwade , kendo gininege , to chieng’ mar adek enochier . ”
To jopuonjrene ne ok owinjo tiendn wechego kata achiel , nikech nopandnigi tiende . Kamano ne ok ginyal ng’eyo gima Yesu wacho .
Kane Yesu chiegni chopo Jeriko , muofu moro noyudo obet e bath yo kakuecho .
Muofuno nowinjo ka ji mang’eny kadho , omiyo nopenjo ni , “ Mano en ng’a ? ”
Ne gidwoke ni , “ Yesu , ja-Nazareth ema kadho . ”
Eka ne okok matek niya , “ Yesu , Wuod Daudi , kecha ! ”
Joma ne otelo ne okwere ni mondo oling’ , to nomedo kok matek moloyo ni , “ Wuod Daudi , kecha ! ”
Mano omiyo Yesu nochung’ , mowacho mondo okele ire . Kane osebiro machiegni , Yesu nopenje ni ,
“ Ere gima idwaro ni mondo atimni ? ” Ne odwoke ni , “ Jaduong’ , adwaro ni mondo achak anen kendo . ”
Yesu nowachone ni , “ Nen ! Yieni ema omiyo ichango . ”
Gikanyono wang’e noyepo , mi oluwo Yesu , komiyo Nyasaye duong’ , kendo kane ji duto oneno gima otimore , ne gipako Nyasaye .
Yesu nodonjo Jeriko , kendo kane oyudo okadho e dier dalano ,
Ng’at moro ma nyinge Zakayo ne dwaro nene . Ng’atno ne jasol osuru maduong’ , kendo ne en jamoko .
Ne odwaro neno ni Yesu en ng’ama chalo nadi , to ne ok onyal nene , nikech ji ne ng’eny ahinya , to bende ne en ng’at ma nyadundo .
Kuom mano , noringo odhi nyime , mi oidho ng’owo mondo one Yesu , nikech Yesu ne dhi kadho kanyo .
Kane Yesu ochopo , norango malo , mi owacho ni Zakayo niya , “ Lor piny piyo , nikech kawuono adhi bedo wendo e odi . ”
Zakayo nolor piyo , mi orwako Yesu gi mor .
To kane ji oneno kamano , ne ging’ur , ka giwacho ni , “ Osedhi bedo wendo jaricho ! ”
Zakayo nochung’ , mowacho ni Ruoth Yesu niya , “ Ruoth , abiro pogo nus giga ni jochan , kendo kapo ni asemayo ng’ato gire e yo ma ok kare , to abiro chulo nyading’wen . ”
Yesu nowacho niya , “ Kawuono warruok osebiro e odni , nimar jali bende en nyakwar Ibrahim .
Wuod Dhano nobiro mondo omany joma olal , kendo oresi . ”
Kane pod ji winjo wechego , Yesu nogoyo ngero moro , nikech ne koro ochiegni chopo Jerusalem , kendo ji ne paro ni Loch Nyasaye biro betie mak odeko .
Ne owacho niya , “ Ng’at moro marahuma ne dwaro dhi e piny moro mabor mondo oyud teko mar duogo bedo ruoth e pinygi .
Ne oluongo jotichne apar , mi omiyo ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomgi siling’ alufu achiel achiel , kowachonigi ni , ‘ Lokuru ohala gi pesagi nyaka chop aduogi . ’ .
To jothurgi ng’atno ne osin kode , omiyo ne gioro joote kuma ne odhiyeno gi wach ni , ‘ Ok wadwar mondo jalo obed ruodhwa . ’ .
To kata kamano ne okete ruoth , kendo kane odwogo , nogolo chik mondo jotichne mane osemiyo pesa kande obi ire , mondo one ane ohala ma giseyudo .
“ Ng’at mokwongo nobiro , mowacho niya , ‘ Ruoth , siling’ alufu achiel mane imiya osenywolo siling’ alufu apar ohala . ’ .
Eka ruodhe nodwoke ni , ‘ Ber ahinya , in jatich maber ! Koro kaka iserito gima tinni maber , aketi mondo ibed ruodh mier apar . ’ .
Ng’at mar ariyo bende nobiro mowacho niya , ‘ Ruoth , siling’ alufu achiel mane imiya osenywolo siling’ alufu abich mamoko . ’ .
En bende nodwoke ni , ‘ Bed ruodh mier abich . ’ .
Eka ng’at mar adek nobiro mowacho niya , ‘ Ruoth , pesa mane imiya eri ! Ne aboye gi nanga , mi akane akana ,
nikech ne aluori , nimar in ng’at makoch . In ikawo gima ne ok ikano , kendo ikayo gima ne ok ichwoyo . ’ .
To ruodhe nowachone niya , ‘ In jatich marach ! Abiro ng’adoni bura gi weche ma isewacho gi dhogi iwuon . Kara , in ne ing’eyo ni an ng’at makoch , kendo ni akawo gima ne ok akano , bende ni akayo gima ne ok achwoyo !
To ka kamano , to marang’o ne ok iketo pesana e bengi mondo ka aduogo to akawe kod ohande ? ’
Eka nowacho ni joma ne ochung’ kanyo mondo okaw pesa kuom ng’atno omi jal mane nigi siling’ alufu apar cha .
Ne giwachone ni , ‘ Ruoth , en donge en gi siling’ alufu apar ? ’
To nodwoke ni , ‘ Akonu ni ng’ato ka ng’ato man-go ema nomedi , to ng’at ma ongego , noma kata mana mano matin ma en-go .
To wasika mane ok dwar ni mondo abed ruodhgi to keluru ka mondo uneg mana ka aneno . ’ . ”
Kane Yesu osegoyo ngero kamano , ne otelo odhi Jerusalem ,
kendo kane ochopo machiegni gi Bethfage kod Bethania e got miluongo ni got Zeituni , nooro jopuonjrene ariyo ,
kowachonigi niya , “ Dhiuru e dala man nyimu cha , kendo kudonjo , to ubiro nwang’o nyathi kanyna motue , mapok ng’ato oidho nyaka nene . Gonyeuru ukele ka .
To ka ng’ato openjou gimomiyo ugonye , to dwokeuru ni , ‘ Ruodhwa dware . ’ . ”
Jootego nodhi monwang’o gik moko duto mana kaka nosenyisogi ,
to kane oyudo gigonyo nyathi kanyna , wegi nopenjogi ni , “ Ang’o momiyo ugonyo nyathi kanyna no ? ”
Ne gidwoko ni , “ Ruodhwa dware . ”
Kamano ne gikele ni Yesu , eka ne gipedho lepgi e dieng’eye mi giketoe Yesu .
To kane owuotho odhi , ne gipedhone lepgi e yo .
Yesu nochopo machiegni gi Jerusalem , kama yo lorgo kaa e got Zeituni , mi jopuonjre mang’eny nochako pako Nyasaye matek gi mor , nikech timbe madongo miwuoro mane giseneno .
Ne giwacho niya , “ Oguedh Ruoth mabiro e nying Ruoth Nyasaye ! Kue obedi e polo , kendo duong’ obedi e polo malo . ”
Eka moko kuom jo-Farisai mane nie ogandano nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Japuonj , kwer jopuonjreni mondo oling’ ! ”
To nodwokogi ni , “ Awachonu ni , ka giling’ to kara koda ka kitegi bende biro kok ! ”
Yesu nomedo chopo machiegni gi Jerusalem , kendo kane oneno dalano , ne oywage ,
kowacho niya , “ Yaye , mad ne bed ni ing’eyo tinendeni gima dikelni kue ! To kata kamano ogeng’ore ni wang’i .
Ndalo nobi ma wasiki notimnie ageng’a koni gi koni kakunyoni bur alwora .
Ginitieki kaachiel gi jogi duto , kendo ok giniwe kata kidi achiel kochung’ ewi wadgi , nikech ne ok ing’eyo kinde mane Nyasaye obiroe iri mondo olimi ! ”
Yesu nodonjo e Hekalu , mi ochako riembo joohala ,
kowachonigi niya , “ Ondiki e Muma ni , ‘ Oda nobed od lemo’ , to un useloke od jomecho . ”
Ne opuonjo e Hekalu pile , to jodolo madongo gi jopuonj Chik kod jodong oganda ne dwaro nege .
To ne ok ginyal yudo yo mar timo kamano , nikech ji duto nosiko kawinjo puonjne , ka ok gidwar ni mondo kata mana wach achiel okadh mak owinjo .
Chieng’ moro kane Yesu puonjo ji e Hekalu , kendo lando Wach Maber , jodolo madongo gi jopuonj Chik , kaachiel gi jodong oganda , ne jobiro ire ,
mopenje niya , “ Nyiswa ane ! Ere teko ma in-go , momiyo itimo gik ma kamagi ? Koso ng’ama omiyi teko mar timogi ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Weuru ane bende apenjue gimoro achiel . Nyasauru ane !
Teko ma Johana batisogo ji noa kuom Nyasaye koso kuom dhano ? ”
Eka jogo nochako wuoyo e kindgi giwegi , ka gipenjore ni , “ Ere kaka dwadwoke ? Ka wawacho ni teko Johana noa kuom Nyasaye , to obiro penjowa gima omiyo ne ok wayie wach Johana .
To ka wawacho ni noa kuom dhano , to ji duto man kagi biro chieliwa gi kite , nikech giyie ni Johana ne janabi . ”
Kuom mano ne gidwoko ni ok ging’eyo kuma ne teko Johana oaye .
Eka Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Ka kamano , to an bende ok anyal nyisou kuma ayudoe teko ma atimogo gigi . ”
Bang’e Yesu nogoyo ni ji ngero niya , “ Ng’at moro noloso puoth mzabibu . Eka ne oweye e lwet jopur , mi owuok odhi wuoth e piny moro mabor kuom ndalo mang’eny .
To kane kinde ma olemo chieki ochopo , ne ooro jatichme ir jopurgo mondo oomne pokne kuom gik monyak e puodho . To jopurgo nogoyo ng’atno , moriembo gi lwete nono .
Kuom mano wuon puodho nochako ooro jatich machielo , to en bende jogo ne ogoye , kendo otimone marach , mi oriembe nono .
Eka nooro jatich mar adek , to mano bende ne gigoyo , mi giriembo .
Bang’ mano , wuon puodho nopenjore kawacho ni , ‘ Koro ere gima koro datim ? Ee , ang’eyo gima abiro timo , abiro oro wuoda awuon , nimar kamoro dipo ka gimiye luor . ’ .
To kane jopurgo oneno wuodeno , ne giwacho e kindgi giwegi niya , ‘ Ma eri e wuod wuon lowo . Wanegeuru mondo lopeni odong’nwa ! ’
Omiyo ne gidhire oko e tok puodho mi ginege . ” Eka Yesu nopenjogi ni , “ Koro uparo ni wuon puodho biro timo jopurgo nadi ?
Donge obiro biro , mi oneg jogo , kendo okaw puodho mi omi jopur moko nono ? ” To kane ji owinjo kamano , ne giwacho ni , “ Ngang’ ! Mano ok nyalre ! ”
Yesu norangogi , mopenjogi niya , “ To kara , ere tiend weche mondiki e Muma ma wacho ni , Kidi mane jogedo odagi , ema koro osedoko kidi motegno moriwo kor ot’ ?
Ng’ato ang’ata mopodho kuom kidino notur matindotindo , to ka kidino ema opodho kuom ng’ato to norege ka buru ! ”
Jopuonj Chik kod jodolo madongo notemo mondo omak Yesu gikanyono , nikech ne ging’eyo ni osegoyo ngerono mana kuomgi , to kata kamano ne giluoro ji mane ni kanyo .
Omiyo ne girito mondo giyud thuolo maber . Ne gioro jombetre mane owuondore ni joma kare , mondo omake kowinjo kowacho gimoro marach , kendo okete e lwet ruoth .
Jombetrego nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Japuonj , wang’eyo ni gima iwacho kendo ipuonjo en adier . Bende wang’eyo ni ok iluoro wang’ ng’ato , kata dabed ni en ng’ama nadi , to ipuonjo yor Nyasaye gi adiera .
To koro , nyiswa ane ka Chikwa oyie mondo wagol osuru ni Kaisar , kata kik wagol ? ”
To Yesu noneno kaka gichikone obadho . Omiyo nowacho nigi ni ,
“ Nyisauru ane siling’ mondo ane . ” Kane gisekelone siling’ , nopenjogi niya , “ Kidoni gi nying’ man kuom siling’ni gin mag ng’a ? ” Ne gidwoke ni , “ Gin mag Kaisar . ”
Eka Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Kara chiwuru ni Kaisar gi Kaisar to gi Nyasaye chiwuru ni Nyasaye ! ”
Kamano ne ok ginyal make kata gi wach achiel e nyim ji kanyo , omiyo ne giling’ thi , ka giwuoro dwokone !
Jo-Sadukai moko nobiro ir Yesu . ( Gin e joma wacho ni chier ongee ) Ne giwachone niya ,
“ Japuonj ! Musa nondikonwa Chik ni ni ka ng’ato otho , mi oweyo chiege ka onge nyathi , to owadgi nyaka kaw chiegeno , mondo onywolnego nyithindo .
To koro ne nitie owete abiriyo . Wuowi maduong’ nokendo dhako , to otho ka ok onywolo nyathi .
Eka owadgi maluwe notero chiegeno ,
kendo mar adek bende . Mano e gima notimore ni owete abiriyogo duto , to giduto ne githo ka ok ginywolo nyithindo .
Bang’e dhakono bende notho .
To koro , chieng’ chier , to dhakono nobed chi ng’a kuomgi , ka ji abiriyogo duto nokende kamano ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Chwo gi mon mae pinyni kendore ,
to chwo gi mon moyier mondo ochopi e piny mabiro , kendo ochier kuom joma otho , ok kendre .
Adier ok ginyal tho kendo , nikech gichal gi malaika , kendo gin nyithind Nyasaye , nimar gin joma osechier .
To kata mana Musa bende onyiso maler ni joma otho chier , nikech kusomo wach bungu maliel , to ubiro neno ni oluongo Ruoth Nyasaye ni Nyasach Ibrahim , gi Nyasach Isaka , kod Nyasach Jakobo .
To wang’eyo ni ok en Nyasach joma otho , to en Nyasach joma ngima , nikech e nyim Nyasaye , ji duto ngima . ”
Eka jopuonj Chik moko nowacho niya , “ Idwoko maber , japuonj . ”
Ne giwacho kamano nikech ne ok ginyal hedhore penje weche moko kendo !
Yesu nopenjogi niya , “ Ere kaka ji wacho ni Mesia nobed nyakwar Daudi ,
ka Daudi owuon to owacho e kitap Zaburi niya , ‘ Ruoth Nyasaye nowacho ni Ruodha ni , “ Bed e bada korachwich ka ,
nyaka chop aket wasiki obed raten tiendi . ” ’
Kamano waneno ni Daudi ema luongo Mesia ni Ruoth . Koro ere kaka Mesia dibed nyakwar Daudi ? ”
Kane oyudo ji duto winjo weche Yesu , nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya ,
“ Beduru motang’ ni jopuonj Chik , ma ohero wuotho gi lewni maboyo , kendo mohero mondo ji omosgi kamiyogi duong’ kuonde ma ji ochokoree , bende mohero kombe ma nyime e ut lemo , kendo mohero kuonde moyiedhi e sewni .
Gin joma yako ut mond liete , ka giriasore gi lemo moyware . Gininwang’ kum marach moloyo ! ”
Yesu noting’o wang’e , moneno ka jomwandu bolo chiwogi e sandug sadaka mar Hekalu ,
to bende noneno chi liel moro modhier ka golo ndururu ariyo .
Eka nowacho niya , “ adier awachonu ni chi liel modhierni osegolo chiwo maduong’ moloyo ji mamoko duto ,
nimar ji mamoko osechiwo mana gik ma gigolo kuom mwandugi . En to , kata obedo ni odhier kamano , to osechiwo duto ma dokonyrego . ”
Jomoko ne wuoyo kuom Hekalu , kawuoro kaka olose gi kite mabeyo kendo kaka mich michiwoe ni Nyasaye long’o . To Yesu nowachonigi niya ,
“ Ndalo biro ma onge kata mana kidi achiel kuom gik munenogi duto ma nodong’ kochung’ ewi wadgi , to giduto nowitgi piny . ”
To ne gipenjo niya , “ Japuonj , gigo notimre karang’o ? Koso ang’o ma notimre manyisowa ni kindeno chiegni ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Beduru motang’ , mondo kik wuondu , nikech ji mang’eny nobi gi nyinga , kawacho ni , ‘ An e en , ’ kendo ni , ‘ Ndalo chiegni . ’ . To kik uluwgi !
Bende kik ubed maluor kuwinjo humb lwenje gi koko , nikech gik ma kamago nyaka kwong timre , to mano ok onyiso ni giko mar piny chiegni . ”
Nodhi nyime kowacho ni , “ Ogendini noked gi ogendini wetegi , kendo ruodhi bende nomonj ruodhi wetegi .
Piny noyiengni matek , kendo kech gi tuoche nobedie kuonde mopogore opogore . Gik malich mabwogo ji , kod honni madongodongo bende notimre e polo mondo obed ranyisi .
“ To kapok gigo duto otimore , to nomaku , mi sandu , kendo noteru mondo oyalu e nyim jodong ut lemo , mi ketu e jela . Bende giniteru e nyim ruodhi kod jodongo nikech an .
Mano e thuolo ma unuyudi mar hulo gik museneno .
Emomiyo keturu chunyu mondo ung’e ni ka kindeno ochopo , to ok unuchandru kuom paro gima dudwoki ,
nikech an ema namiu weche kod rieko ma onge wasiku kata achiel ma nosir kata nokwer .
Kata mana jonywolu gi oweteu gi wedeu kod osiepeu nondhogu , kendo ginichiw jomoko kuomu mondo onegi .
Bende ji duto nobed mamon kodu nikech an .
To kata kamano , onge kata yie wiu achiel ma nolal .
Omiyo timuru kinda , nimar mano e kaka unuyud ngima maradier .
“ Ka uneno ka ogend lweny olworo Jerusalem , to ng’euru ni kinde mikethee osechopo !
Kuom mano , joma nie piny Judea nyaka ring dhi pondi e gode , kendo joma ni Jerusalem nyaka wuog oko , bende jogo man oko kik duog Jerusalem ,
nimar mago nobed ndalo ma Nyasaye kumoe joge , mondo weche duto mondiki e Muma otimre .
Mano kaka nobed malit e ndalogo ni mon mayach kod mon man gi nyithindo mapod dhoth , nikech chandruok maduong’ nobed e piny , kendo jo-Israel noyud kum malit .
Moko kuomgi noneg e lweny , to moko nomaki mi ter e pinje mamoko duto , kendo ogendini ma ok jo-Yahudi nonyon Jerusalem nyaka chop ndalo lochgi rum .
“ Ranyisi nobedi e wang’chieng’ gi due kod sulue , kendo ogendini mae piny nobed kodhier nono , kendo ka luor , nikech nam nowuo , kendo apaka nogore madongodongo .
Luoro nomi chuny ji ling’re nikech gik mabiro timore e piny , kendo teko momako sulue e polo bende noyiengni .
Eka Wuod Dhano nothinyre , kabiro e bor polo gi teko malich kod duong’ maler .
Ka gigo ochako timore , to chung’uru tir , kendo ting’uru wiu , nikech warruok maru okayo machiegni . ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nogoyonigi ngero niya , “ Par ane uru yadh ng’owo kod yien mamoko .
Ka uneno ka bedegi chako loth , to ung’eyo mak ng’ato onyisou , ni ndalo chwiri chiegni .
Kamano bende , ka uneno ka gik ma asewachonugo timore , to unung’e ni Loch Nyasaye ochopo machiegni .
To nyako ung’e ni gigo duto notimre kapok tieng’ ma kawuononi otho duto .
Polo gi piny norum . Wechena to ok norum .
“ Ritreuru mondo kik utim anjawo , kata kik ubed jomer kata joma parore kuom gik manie pinyni , nono to chieng’no biro poyou mana ka obadho ,
nimar enopo ji duto modak e piny .
Omiyo beduru motang’ kulemo pile mondo uyud teko mar tony e gik mabiro timore duto , kendo uchung’ e nyim Wuod Dhano . ”
Pile Yesu ne puonjo e Hekalu godiechieng’ , to gotieno ne odhi onindo e got miluongo ni got Zeituni .
Ji duto ne mondo e Hekalu gokinyi mang’ich mondo owinj puonjne .
Koro Sap Makati ma ok ketie Thowi , miluongo ni Pasaka , ne chiegni .
To jodolo madongo kod jopuonj Chik ne dwaro yo ma digineggo Yesu ling’ling’ , nimar ne giluoro ji .
Bang’e Satan nodonjo kuom Judas miluongo ni Iskariot , mane acheil kuom jopuonjre Yesu apar gariyo .
Omiyo nodhi opimo wach gi jodolo madongo kod jotend jorit Hekalu , kaka doket Yesu e lwetgi .
Ne gimor ahinya , kendo ne giwinjore kode ni ginimiye pesa .
Judas noyie , kendo nochako dwaro rieko ma doketgo Yesu e lwetgi ka ji ok ong’eyo .
Chieng’ Sap Makati ma ok ketie Thowi , ma inegoe nyarombo Pasaka , nochopo .
Yesu nooro Petro kod Johana , kowachonigi ni , “ Dhiuru ulosnwa Pasaka mondo wabi wacham . ”
To ne gipenje ni , “ Ere kama idwaro ni mondo walosee ? ”
Nowachonigi niya , “ Ka usedonjo Jerusalem , to ubiro romo gi ng’aat moting’o dapi . Luweuru nyaka ot modonjoe ,
kendo nyisuru wuon odno ni , ‘ Japuonj penji ni , ere ot moikne , mobiro chamoe Sap Pasaka gi jopuonjrene ? ’
Eka obiro nyisou ot malach moiki e gorofa malo . Kanyo ema mondo uikie gik moko duto . ”
Kamano ne gidhi , kendo ne ginwang’o gik moko duto mana kaka Yesu nosenyisogi , mi giiko Pasaka kuno .
Kane sa ochopo , Yesu nobet e mesa kod jootene .
Nowachonigi niya , “ Asegombo ahinya mondo acham Pasakani kodu kapok osanda ,
nimar awachonu ni ok nachak achame ngang’ nyaka chop time mogik e Piny Ruoth Polo . ”
Eka nokawo kikombe , mi ogoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano . Bang’e nowacho niya , “ Kawuru ma , mondo upogru ,
nimar awachonu ni chakre kawuono ok nachak amadh divai nyaka chop Loch Nyasaye bi . ”
Eka nokawo makati , kendo kosegoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano , nong’ingo makatino , kowacho ni , “ Ma e ringra mochiw nikech un . Timuru kamano mondo uparago . ”
Kamano bende nokawo kikombe bang’ chiemo , kowacho niya , “ Kikombe ni e remba , mochwer nikech un , kitimonugo Winjruok Manyien gi Nyasaye .
To ng’euru ni ng’at mondhoga ni koda e mesa ka !
Wuod Dhano biro tho mana kaka Nyasaye nochano . To mano kaka nobed malit ni ng’at mondhoge ! ”
Eka ne gichako penjore kendgi ni en ng’a kuomgi ma ditim gima kamano .
Mbaka nowuok e kind jopuonjre ka gipenjore ni en ng’a ma kwano ka ng’ama duong’ moloyo kuomgi .
Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Ruodhi mag pinyni nigi teko kuom jogi , kendo jotelo dwaro ni mondo ji oluonggi ni , ‘ Osiepe ji’ .
To un ok uchal kamano . Ng’at maduong’ie moloyo kuomu nyaka bed ka ng’ama tinie moloyo , kendo jatelo nyaka bed ka jatich .
Kuom ji ariyogi , ere ng’ama duong’ie moloyo wadgi ? Jal ma obet kachiemo , koso jal matiyone ? Donge en jal ma obet kachiemo ? To an , an e kindu ka ng’at matiyo .
Un e joma osesiko koda e masichena duto ,
kendo kaka Wuora osechano mondo omiya teko mar loch , e kaka un bende asechano mondo uyud loch .
Unuchiem kendo unumethi koda e pinya , kendo unubed e kombe ruodhi , kung’ado bura ni dhoudi apar gariyo mag Israel . ”
Eka Yesu nodhi nyime ni , “ Simon , Simon , winji ! Satan oseyudo thuolo mondo opiedhu mana kaka dhako piedho cham .
To in aselemoni mondo yieni kik lal , kendo ka iselokori , miduogo ira , to nyaka ijiw oweteni . ”
Petro nodwoke ni , “ Ruoth , aikora dhi kodi e jela kata mana kar tho bende . ”
To Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Petro awachoni ni thwon gweno ok ang’ nokog tinende kapok ikweda didek ni ok ing’eya . ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nopenjogi ni , “ E ndalo mane aorou ka uonge gi ofuko mar pesa , kata sandug wuoth , kata gi wuoche , ne uchando gimoro koso ? ” Ne gidwoke ni , “ Onge gima ne wachando . ”
Eka nowachonigi niya , “ To koro akonu ni ng’at man gi ofuko mar pesa , kata sandug wuoth , mondo okaw , bende ng’at ma onge gi ligangla mondo olok lawe , ong’iewgo ligangla ,
nimar awachonu ni gima Muma wacho ni , ‘ Ne okwane kod joketho’ , nyaka timre kuoma , nikech gik ma ondik kuoma koro chiegni timore . ”
Jopuonjrene nowachone ni , “ Ruoth , ligengni ariyo eki ni ka . ” En to nokwerogi ni , “ Weuru wuoyo kamano ! ”
Yesu nowuok , modhi e got Zeituni kaka ne otimo pile , kendo jopuonjrene bende nodhi kode .
Kane ochopo kanyo , nowachonigi niya , “ Lemuru mondo kik udonj e tem . ”
Eka noweyogi modhi kuma ochwalore ma dirom diro kidi , mi nogoyo chonge piny , kendo olemo ,
kowacho niya , “ Wuora kiyie to gol kikombe mar masirani oa kuoma , to ok kaka an ema adwaro , to gima idwaro ema mondo otimre . ” [
Eka malaika moa e polo nofwenyorene , mi omiye teko .
Chunye nochandore malit ahinya , mi nomedo lemo matek , kendo luya nochotne maton piny mana ka remo . ]
Kane oa malo bang’ lemo , ne odok ir jopuonjrene , mi onwang’o ka nindo oterogi , nikech chunye ne lit .
Nowachonigi ni , “ Ang’o momiyo unindo ? Auru malo ulem , mondo kik udonj e tem . ”
Kane pod owuoyo , ji moko mang’eny notucho , ka jal miluongo ni Judas otelonigi . Ne en achiel kuom joote apar gariyo . Nosudo ir Yesu mondo onyodhi .
To Yesu nopenje niya , “ Judas , indhogo Wuod Dhano mana gi nyoth koso ? ”
Kane jopuonjre Yesu oneno gima dwaro timore , ne gipenje niya , “ Ruoth , waked gi ligangla koso ? ”
Eka ng’at achiel kuomgi nong’ado it jatich jadolo maduong’ ma korachwich oko .
To Yesu nokwere ni , “ We timo kamano ! ” Eka nomulo it ng’atno , mochango .
Bang’ mano Yesu nowacho ni jodolo madongo gi jotend jorit Hekalu , kod jodongo mane obiro mondo omake niya , “ Ere gimomiyo ubirona gi ligengni kod arunge , mana ka gima an jamecho ?
Pile ne an kodu e Hekalu , to ne ok umaka . To koro ma e sa maru , ka teko mar mudho tiyo . ”
Ne gimako Yesu , mi gitero e od jadolo maduong’ , to Petro noluwo bang’gi gi chien .
Kane gisemoko mach e laru , mi gibet piny kanyo , Petro nobiro mobet kodgi .
To nyako moro ma jatich nonene ka mach liel , morango wang’e tir , kendo owacho niya , “ Jali bende ne ni kode ! ”
To Petro nokwer ni , “ Nyako ! Ok ang’eye . ”
Bang’e matin , ng’at moro bende nonene mowachone niya , “ In bende in achiel kuomgi ! ” To Petro nodwoke ni , “ Omera , ok an ! ”
Bang’e kinde ma dirom sa achiel , ng’at machielo nojiwo wach matek , ni , “ Adier , jali bende ne ni kode , nikech en ja-Galili . ”
To Petro nokwer , kawacho niya , “ Omera , ok ang’eyo gima iwacho ! ” Gikanyono , kapod owuoyo , thwon gweno nokok .
Eka Ruoth Yesu nolokore mong’iyo Petro , mi Petro noparo wach mane osewachone ni , “ Tinendeni , kapok thwon gweno okok , to ang’ nikweda didek . ”
Mano omiyo Petro nowuok oko , moywak malit .
Joma ne rito Yesu nojare , kendo ogoye .
Ne giumo wang’e mi gipenje ni , “ Hul ane ng’ama ogoyi . ”
Bende ne giyanye gi weche mang’eny maricho .
Kane piny oyawore , jodong jo-Yahudi gi jodolo madongo kod jopuonj Chik nochokore , mi oter Yesu e buchgi .
Ne giwachone ni , “ Ka in e Mesia adier , to nyiswa ane . ” En to nokonigi ni , “ Ka anyisou , to ok ubi yie ,
to bende ka apenjou gimoro , to ok ubi dwoka .
To chakre kawuono , Wuod Dhano biro bet e bat korachwich mar Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto ! ”
Eka ne gipenje giduto ni , “ To kara , in e Wuod Nyasaye ? ” Nodwokogi ni , “ Uwacho adier ni an e en . ”
Bang’ mano , ne giwacho ni , “ Koro pod wadwaro joneno nang’o , to wan wawegi wasewinjo dhoge owuon ? ”
Eka joburano duto nochung’ motero Yesu e nyim Pilato ,
mi gichako donjone kuno , ka giwacho niya , “ Ne wanwang’o jali kapuonjo jowa marach , kokwerogi ni kik gigol osuru ni Kaisar , kendo kowacho ni en owuon en Mesia , tiende ni ruoth . ”
Eka Pilato nopenjo Yesu ni , “ In e ruodh jo-Yahudi koso ? ” To en nodwoko ni , “ In ema isewacho kamano . ”
Bang’ mano , Pilato nowacho ni jodolo madongo kod joma nochokore duto ni , “ Ok ayudo jali gi ketho . ”
To ne gijiwo wach matek niya , “ Oketho ji , kopuonjo e Judea duto . Ne ochako Galili , kendo koro osechopo ka . ”
Kane Pilato owinjo kamano , nopenjo ka Yesu en ja-Galili .
To kane osenyise ni oa kuno , notere ir Herode ma bende noyudo ni Jerusalem e ndalogo .
Herode nodoko mamor ahinya koneno Yesu , nikech nosewinjo humbe , omiyo nogombo ahinya mondo onene , kendo oneye hono moro motimo .
Ne openjo Yesu weche mang’eny , to Yesu ne ok odwoke kata wach achiel .
Jodolo madongo kod jopuonj Chik nobiro , mondonjone matek ahinya .
Herode kaachiel gi askechene nojare , kendo nonyiere . Eka Herode nogolo chik , morwakne kandhu maber , bang’e odwoke ir Pilato .
Chieng’ onogo , Herode gi Pilato ne jomako osiep , nikech noyudo gisebedo ka gimonre chon .
Pilato noluongo jodolo madongo gi jodongo kod ji duto ,
mi owachonigi niya , “ Nende ukelona jali ni en ng’at maketho oganda , to asenone e nyimu , kendo ok ayudo ni en gi ketho mudonjonegogi .
To kata mana Herode bende ok oyude gi ketho , nimar osedwokonwago . Onge gima ng’atni osetimo mowinjore gi buch tho .
Emomiyo abiro golo chik mondo odhi . ” [
Nowacho kamano nikech higa ka higa e Sawo mar Pasaka ne nyaka ogony ni ji ng’at achiel motue . ]
To oganda ji duto nokok ni , “ Neg ng’atni , to gonynwa Baraba ! ” (
Baraba en ng’at mane oseket e jela nikech wach koko mane otimore Jerusalem , kendo nikech nek . )
Pilato ne dwaro gonyo Yesu , omiyo nochako owuoyo gi ji kendo .
To ne gikok ni , “ Gure e msalaba ! Gure e msalaba ! ”
Eka nochako openjogi mar adek ni , “ To ere gima rach mosetimo ? Ok wanwang’o ketho kuome mowinjore gi tho . Omiyo abiro chwade , to aweye odhi . ”
To ne gisiko ka gikok matek moloyo ni mondo ogur Yesu e msalaba , nyaka kokogi
nomiyo Pilato oyie ng’ado bura kaka gidwaro .
Ne ogonyo jal mane gikwayo , mane oyudo otue nikech koko kendo nikech nek . Yesu to noketo e lwetgi mondo gitimne kaka gidwaro .
Kane gigolo Ysu kanyo mondo gidhi ginegi , ne gimako ng’at moro ma nyinge Simon ja-Kurene mane oyudo biro Jerusalem koa e gweng’ moro . Ne giyieyone msalaba mondo oting’ , koluwo bang’ Yesu .
Oganda maduong’ noluwo Yesu , ka mon goyo nduru malit , kaywage .
To Yesu nolokore , mowachonigi niya , “ Un nyi Jerusalem , weuru ywaga , to ywagreuru mana un uwegi , kendo ywaguru nyithindu ,
nikech ndalo biro ma ji nowachie ni , ‘ Mano kaka mon maonge nyithindo gin johawi ! Adier , mon ma ok onywol , kendo ma thundegi ok odhodhi gin johawi ! ’
Bende giniwach ni gode niya , ‘ Ruombreuru kuomwa ! ’
Ka gik ma kamagi timore ni an , ma achalo gi yath manumu , to ang’o ma notimrenu , un muchalo gi yath motwo ? ”
Ji ariyo mamoko ma joketho bende ne gidhigo mondo gigur gi Yesu .
Kane gichopo kama iluongo ni , ‘ Hanga Wich’ , ne giguro Yesu e msalaba , kaachiel gi joketho ariyogo , achiel e bathe korachwich , to machielo e bathe koracham .
Yesu nowacho niya , “ Wuora , wenigi , nikech gikia gima gitimo . ” Askeche to nokawo lepe , mi gipogore gi ombulu .
To ji mang’eny ne ni kanyo , kaneno gima timore , kendo jodong jo-Yahudi nonyiere , kawacho ni , “ Noreso jomoko , omiyo ka en e Mesia ma Nyasaye oseyiero adier , to mondo oresre ane ! ”
Askeche bende ne ojare . Ne gibiro ire , mi gimiye kong andwayo ,
ka giwachone ni , “ Ka in e ruodh jo-Yahudi to resri ane ! ”
Bende ewi msalaba malo nondiki ni , “ JALI E RUODH JO-YAHUDI . ”
Achiel kuom joketho mane ogur kanyogo nogoyo ni Yesu siboi , kawachone ni , “ Donge in e Mesia ? Ara , resri ane , kendo ireswa wan bende ! ”
To ng’at machielo nokwero jalo ni , “ Ok iluoro kata mana Nyasaye ? Donge ineno ka wanie kum achiel kode ?
To wan okumwa kare , nikech wayudo gima owinjore gi timwa . Jali to onge gima rach mosetimo . ”
Eka nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Para , chieng’ miyudoe lochni . ”
Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Adier awachoni ni , tinende ang’ nibed koda e Paradis . ”
Koro ne en kar sa auchiel mar odiechieng’ , to wang’chieng’ noimore , mi piny duto otimo mudho nyaka sa ochiko .
Nanga mane ogeng’o Kama Ler mar Hekalu noriedore diere ariyo .
Eka Yesu nokok matek niya , “ Wuora , aketo chunya e lweti . ” To kane osewacho kamano , chunye nochot .
Kane jaduong’ lweny oneno gima otimore , nomiyo Nyasaye duong’ , kowacho ni , “ Adier jali ne en ng’at makare ! ”
Ji duto mane ochokore kanyo mondo one wachno noneno gik ma notimore , kendo ne gidok miechgi ka gikino wigi .
To osiepe Yesu duto , kod mon mane oseluwe koa Galili , nochung’ gi chien kaneno gigo .
Ne nitie ng’at moro ma nyinge Josef , mane oa e dala jo-Yahudi miluongo ni Arimathaya . Ne en ng’at makare kendo mogen , kendo ne ogeno ni none Loch Nyasaye .
Kata obedo ni ne en achiel kuom jobuch jo-Yahudi kamano , to ne ok oyie gi dwarogi kata gi gima gitimo .
Nodhi ir Pilato , mokwayo mondo omiye ringre Yesu .
Kamano noloro ringre Yesu piny , moboyo gi nanga maber , eka nokete e bur mane osekuny ariwa e kor lwanda . Ne en bur manyien , mapok oyikie ng’ato .
Chieng’no ne chieng’ Ikruok , tiende ni tich abich , kendo Sabato ne okayo machiegni .
