Mon mane oseluwo Yesu koa Galili , nodhi gi Josef moneno burno , kendo oneno kaka ne oketie ringre Yesu .
Bang’e ne gidok Jerusalem , mi giloso mo mang’ue ng’ar kod yath madum mamit . Chieng’ Sabato to ne giyueyo kaka Chik Musa dwaro .
Gokinyi mang’ich , chieng’ Jumapil , mon-go nodhi e liel , koting’o gik mang’ue ng’ar mane giseloso .
Ne giyudo kidi mane odin-go dho bur koseng’iel ,
to kane gidonjo to ne ok ginwang’o ringre Ruoth Yesu .
Kane pod gichung’ kanyo , ka gihum nono kuom wachno , ni gipo ka ji ariyo morwako lewni mang’ang’ni ochung’ butgi .
Mon-go nobwok ahinya , mosiko mana ka okulo wigi piny . To jogo nopenjogi niya , “ Marang’o umanyo ng’at mangima e kind joma otho ?
Osechier ! Oonge ka . Paruru gima ne owachonu kane pod en Galili , ni
‘ Wuod Dhano nyaka ket e lwet joricho , mi gur e msalaba , to chieng’ mar adek enochier . ’ . ”
Mon-go noparo wachno ,
kendo kane gidok gia e liel , ne ginyiso joote apar gachiel kod ji mamoko duto wechego .
Mon-go ne Maria nyar Magdala , gi Joana , gi Maria min Jakobo , kod mon moko mane ni kodgi . Gin ema ne gitero wechego duto ni joote .
To joote nokawo wechegigo koyuma , mi odagi yiego . [
Petro to noa malo , moringo odhi e liel , kendo kane okulore morango liel , ne ok oneno gimoro mak mana lewni kende . Eka ne odok Jerusalem , kowuoro gima otimore . ]
Chieng’ onogo , jopuonjre ariyo ne dhi e dala moro miluongo ni Emau , ma en kama dirom wuodh seche ariyo , kia Jerusalem .
Ne giwuoyo kuom gik mane otimore ,
to kane oyudo giwuoyo kamano , Yesu owuon nobiro mosudo butgi , kendo ne giwuotho kaachiel .
To ne ok ginyal ng’eye .
Nopenjogi niya , “ Wach ang’o muwacho kendu kuwuothoni ? ” Eka ne gichung’ , ka gimieno wang’gi .
To achiel kuomgi ma nyinge Kleopa nodwoke , kapenje niya , “ In kendi e wendo Jerusalem ma ok ong’eyo gik mosetimore kuno e ndalogi koso ? ”
Nopenjogi ni , “ En ang’o mosetimore ? ” Eka ne gidwoke ni , “ Yesu ja-Nazareth ne janabi ma wechene gi timbene ne nigi teko e nyim Nyasaye kod ji duto .
To jodolowa madongo kod jodongo nondhoge mondo ong’adne buch tho , mi nogure e msalaba .
To wan ne wageno ni en ema dores Israel ! Bende koro en ndalo adek nyaka gigo timre .
To mon moko manie kanyakla marwa nende obwogowa gi wach . Nende gimondo e liel ,
to ne ok ginwang’o ringre Yesu . To kane giduogo , ne ginyisowa ni malaika moko ne ofwenyorenigi , monyisogi ni ongima .
Eka jowa moko nodhi e liel , monwang’o mana kaka ne mon-go onyisowa . Yesu owuon to ne ok gineno . ”
Kane gisetieko wuoyo kamano , Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Yaye un joma ofuwo ! Mano kaka ung’ulni kuom yie gik moko duto mane jonabi owacho !
Donge ne owinjore ni nyaka Mesia ne masichegi kapok oyudo duong’ne maler koso ? ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nonyisogi weche mane jonabi duto ondiko .
Ne gichopo machiegni gi dala mane gidhiye , to Yesu ne nenore ni pod dwaro dhi nyime .
To ne gigeng’e , ka giwachone ni , “ Yie wadhi kodi ka , nimar sa koro oniang’ , kendo piny chiegni yuso . ” Kuom mano , nodhi kodgi .
Kane oyudo obet piny kodgi mondo gichiem , nokawo makati , moguedho , kendo ong’ingo , momiyogi .
Eka wang’gi noyepo , mi ging’eye , to ne gipo ka olal nono e wang’gi !
Bang’e ne giwacho e kindgi giwegi niya , “ Donge ne chunywa mor , kowuoyo kodwa e yo , kendo konyisowa tiend weche mondiki e Muma ? ”
Gikanyono ne gia malo , mi gidok Jerusalem . Ne giyudo joote apar gachiel , kochokore gi joma ne gin-go ,
kawacho niya , “ Ruoth osechier adier , kendo osefwenyore ni Simon ! ”
Eka jopuonjre ariyogo bende nohulo gima ne osetimore e yo , kendo kaka ne ging’eyo Ruoth kong’ingo makati .
Kane pod giwacho wechego ne gipo ka Ruoth owuon ochung’ e diergi , kawachonigi ni , “ Okueuru ! ”
To ne gibwok , kendo ne gidoko maluor ngang’ , ka giparo ni gineno jachien .
Nopenjogi niya , “ Ang’o momiyo chunyu parore ? Koso marang’o uriwo gi kiawa ?
Neuru luetena gi tiendena , mondo ung’e ni en mana an ! Mulauru , mondo une , nikech jachien onge gi ringruok kaka uneno an-goni ! ”
Kane osewacho kamano , nonyisogi luetene gi tiendene .
To ne pod ok ginyal yie , nikech pod ne giwuoro kendo gimor , omiyo nopenjogi niya , “ Bende un gi chiemo kaeri ? ”
Ne gimiye rech motedi ,
mi okawo , kendo ochamo mana e nyimgi kanyo .
Nowacho nigi niya , “ Magi e gik mane awachonu kapod an kodu , kane anyisou ni gik moko duto mondik kuoma e Chik Musa gi Kitepe Jonabi kod Zaburi nyaka timre . ”
Eka nomiyogi rieko mar winjo tiend weche mondiki e Muma ,
kendo nowachonigi niya , “ Ondiki e Muma ni Mesia nyaka sandi , mi chier kuom joma otho chieng’ mar adek ,
mondo wach loko chuny olandi ni ogendini duto , chakre Jerusalem , mondo owenigi richogi e nyinge .
Un muneno wechegi ema nyaka unyis ji mamoko .
To bende ng’euru ni abiro oronu mich mane Wuora osingore ni nomiu , to beduru abeda Jerusalem nyaka chop uyud teko moa malo . ”
Eka nogologi Jerusalem , moterogi machiegni gi Bethania , mi noting’o lwete moguedhogi .
To kane oyudo oguedhogi kamano , ne opogore kodgi , kendo noting’e malo odhi e polo .
Ne gilame , to bang’e ne gidok Jerusalem ka gimor ahinya ,
kendo ne gisiko e Hekalu pile ka gidendo Nyasaye .
Kar chakruok , Wach ne nitie . Wach ne ni kod Nyasaye , kendo Wach ne en Nyasaye .
Kamano , nyaka a chakruok , Wach ne ni kod Nyasaye ,
kendo en ema nomiyo ochue gik moko duto . Onge gimoro kata achiel mane ochue maonge en .
Gimoro amora mane ochue noyudo ngima kuome , kendo ngimano nokelo ni ji ler .
Lerno rieny e mudho , to mudho pok oime .
Nyasaye nooro ng’at moro ma nyinge Johana .
Nobiro nyiso ji wach ler , mondo ji duto oyie nikech wachne .
En ne ok en lerno , to nobiro mana ni mondo onyis ji wach lerno .
Wach ne en ler maradier marieny ni ji duto , kendo ne oyudo obiro e piny e kindeno ,
to kata obedo ni en ema nomiyo ochue piny , to piny ne ok ong’eye .
Nobiro e pinye , to joge ne ok orwake .
To ji duto mane orwake , mi oyie kuome , nomiyo teko mar doko nyithind Nyasaye .
Ne onywolgi kuom Nyasaye , to ok kuom anywola , kata kuom gombo mar ringruok , kata kuom dwaro mar dhano .
Wach nodoko dhano , mi odak kodwa , kende ne waneno duong’ne maler . En duong’ machalo gi duong’ mar Wuowi ma miderma , mopong’ gi ng’wono kod adiera .
Johana nonyiso ji wach kuome , kakok niya , “ Jali ema yande awuoyo kuome , ka awachonu ni ng’at moro biro bang’a , man gi duong’ moloya , nikech kane pok abetie , en to ne entie . ”
Waduto waseyudo gueth mathoth moa kuom ng’wonone mogundho ,
nikech kata obedo ni Musa ema nokelonwa Chik , to Yesu Kristo ema nokelonwa ng’wono gi adiera .
Onge ng’ama oseneno Nyasaye , to Wuowi ma miderma , machiegni gi Wuoro moloyo , ema osemiyo wang’eye .
Jo-Yahudi man Jerusalem nooro jodolo gi jo-Lawi ir Johana , mopenje ni , “ In ng’a ? ”
Johana nohulonigi ratiro , mak opando gimoro , niya , “ An ok an Mesia . ”
Eka ne gichako gipenje ni , “ To in e Elija koso ? ” To Johana nokwerogi ni , “ Ooyo , ok an Elija . ” Ne gichako gipenje ni , “ In e janabi mwageno ni biro biro ? ” Nodwokogi ni , “ Ooyo . ”
Kuom mano , ne giwachone ni , “ To ara , nyiswa ni in ng’a , nikech nyaka wayud wach mwadoko ni joma oorowa . In iwuon iwacho ni in ng’a ? ”
Eka Johana nodwokogi gi wach mane Isaya janabi okoro niya , “ An e ng’at makok e thim ni , ‘ Losuru ni Ruoth yo moriere tir . ’ . ”
Jomoko kuom joma ne oorgo ne jo-Farisai .
Ne gipenjo Johana ni , “ Ka ok in Mesia , kata Elija , kata janabi mwageno ni biro birono , to ang’o momiyo ibatiso ji ? ”
Johana nodwokogi ni , “ An abatiso ji gi pi . To ng’at moro ochung’e dieru ka , ma pok ung’eyo .
En jal mane awacho ni biro bang’a , ma ok awinjora gonyo tond wuochene . ”
Gigo duto notimore Bethania , yo wuokchieng’ mar aora Jordan , kuma ne Johana batisoe ji .
Kinyne , Johana noneno Yesu kabiro ire , mowacho ni , “ Neuru ! Jalcha e Nyarombo Nyasaye , magolo richo mag piny !
En e jal ma yande awuoyo kuome kawacho ni , ng’ato biro bang’a maduong’ moloya , nikech kane pok abetie , en to ne entie .
Kata mana an awuon ne ok ang’eyo ni nobed ng’a , to nabiro ka abatiso ji gi pi mondo jo-Israel ong’eye . ”
Bende Johana nomedo nyiso ji gima noseneno , kowacho niya , “ Naneno Roho machalo gi akuru kalor a e polo , mobet kuome .
Koro aseneno mano katimore , kendo anyisou ni en e Wuod Nyasaye . ”
Kinywe kendo , Johana ne oyudo ochung’ kanyo gi jopuonjrene ariyo .
Noneno Yesu ka wuotho , mowacho niya , “ Neuru ! Jalcha e Nyarombo mar Nyasaye ! ”
Jopuonjrene ariyogo nowinjo wachneno , moluwo bang’ Yesu .
Kane Yesu olokore , moneno ka giluwe kamano , nopenjogi niya , “ Ere gima udwaro ? ” To ne gidwoke ka gipenje ni , “ Rabi , idak kanye ? ” ( Rabi en dho Hibrania , ma tiende ni japuonj . )
Nowachonigi ni , “ Biuru mondo une . ” Kamano ne gidhi kode , mi gineno kama odakie , kendo ne gibet kode chieng’no duto . Ne en kar sa apar mar odhiambo .
Ng’at achiel kuom ji ariyo mane owinjo ka Johana wuoyo , ne Andrea , owadgi Simon Petro .
Gikanyono Andrea nodhi oyudo Simon owadgi , mowachone niya , “ Wasenwang’o Mesia ! ” ( Tiende ni Kristo . )
Eka nokelo Simon ir Yesu . Yesu nong’iyo Simon , mowachone ni , “ In Simon wuod Johana , to chieng’ moro noluongi ni Kefa . ” ( Kefa en Petro gi dho Grik , tiende ni Lwanda . )
Kinyne Yesu ne dwaro dhi e piny Galili . Noyudo Filipo , mi owachone niya , “ Luwa ! ”
Filipo ne ja-Bethsaida , dala mane Andrea gi Petro odakie
Filipo noyudo Nathaniel , mowachone niya , “ Wasenwang’o jal mane Musa ondiko kuome e Kitap Chik , kendo mane jonabi bende ondiko kuome . En Yesu , wuod Josef , ja-Nazareth . ”
To Nathaniel nopenjo ni , “ Bende gimoro maber diwuog Nazareth adier . ” Filipo to nodwoke ni , “ Bi mondo ine . ”
Kane Yesu oneno Nathaniel kabiro ire , nowacho ni , “ Neuru ! Ja-Israel hie e cha biro . En ng’ama kare , ma onge miganga . ”
To Nathaniel nopenje ni , “ Ing’eya nadi ? ” Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Kane inie tiend ng’owo cha , kapok Filipo oluongi , to ne aseneni . ”
Nathaniel nodwoke ni , “ Japuonj , in e Wuod Nyasaye ! In e Ruodh Israel ! ”
To Yesu nopenje niya , “ Donge iyie mana nikech awacho ni ne aneni e tiend ng’owo ? To ibiro neno gik madongo moloyo mano ! ”
Eka nowachone kendo ni , “ Awachonu adier ni unune polo koyawore , kendo ka malaika mag Nyasaye idho malo kendo lor piny kuom Wuod Dhano ka raidhi . ”
Bang’ ndalo adek , ne nitie kisera e dala mar Kana piny Galili . Min Yesu ne ni kuno ,
kendo Yesu bende noluongi e kiserano gi jopuonjrene .
To divai norumo , omiyo min Yesu nowachone ni , “ Jogi koro onge gi divai . ”
To Yesu nowacho ni min niya , “ Mama , ere gimomiyo ikelona wachni ? Kindena pok ochopo . ”
Eka min mare nowacho ni jotich ni , “ Timuru gimoro amora mowachonu . ”
Degi auchiel mag kite nochung kanyo , mondo ji ologie e yo ma Chik jo-Yahudi dwaro . Dak ka dak ne nyalo ting’o pi moromo depe ariyo .
Yesu nowacho ni jotich niya , “ Pong’uru degigi gi pi . ” Mi ne gipong’ogi thich .
Eka nowachonigi ni , “ Koro twomuru pi moko , uter ni jaduong’ kisera . ” Ne gitimo kamano ,
to kane jaduong’ kisera obilo pi mane koro oselokore divai , ne ok ong’eyo kuma oaye , to mak mana jotich mane otuomo pigno ema nong’eyo . Eka jaduong’ kisera noluongo wuon kisera , mowachone niya ,
“ Ji mang’eny kuongpo kelo divai maber , eka bang’e ka welo osemer , to gikelo divai ma ok ber . Into isekano divai maber nyaka sani ! ”
Yesu notimo hono Kana e piny Galili . En e ranyisi mane okwongo timo . Kamano nonyiso duong’ne maler , mi jopuonjrene noyie kuome .
Bang’ mano , Yesu gi min mare gi owetene kod jopuonjrene nodhi Kapernaum , mobet kuno kuom ndalo moko manok .
Sap jo-Yahudi miluongo ni Pasaka nochopo machiegni , omiyo Yesu nodhi Jerusalem .
Kane odonjo e Hekalu , noyudo johand dhok gi rombe kod akuche , kaachiel gi jowil pesa kobet kanyo .
Nokawo tworo , olosogo del , mi oriembogo jogo duto oko e Hekalu , kaachiel gi jambgi . Nopuko pesa jowil pesa , kendo ogoyo mesnigi piny .
Nowacho ni johand akuche niya , “ Goluru gigi ka ! Kik ulok od Wuora kar loko ohala ! ”
Mano nomiyo jopuonjrene oparo wach mondiki e Muma ni , “ A Nyasaye , hera ma aherogo Hekalu mari wang’o chunya ka mach . ”
Jodong jo-Yahudi nopenjo Yesu ni , “ Ere gima nyalo nyisowa ni in gi teko mar timo gima isetimono ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Mukuru Hekalu ni to abiro gere kendo gi ndalo adek . ”
To ne gimedo penje ni , “ Gero Hekaluni osekawo higni piero ang’wen gauchiel ! In to ere kaka dichak igere gi ndalo adek ? ”
To Hekalu mane Yesu wuoyo kuome ne mana ringre owuon ,
kendo bang’e , kane ochier oa kuom joma otho , jopuonjrene noparo ni kara mano e gima ne owacho . Kuom mano , ne giyie ni Muma wacho adier , kendo ne giyie ni weche Yesu bende gin adier .
Kane Yesu ni Jerusalem , e Sap Pasaka , ji mathoth noyie kuome , nimar ne gineno honni motimo .
Yesu to ne ok oketore e luetgi , nikech nong’eyo kit dhano kaka chal .
Omiyo ne ok odwar mondo ng’ato onyise gimoro kuom dhano , nimar nong’eyo gik manie chuny dhano .
Chieng , moro ja-Farisai moro ma nyinge Nikodemo mane jaduong’ jo-Yahudi ,
nodhi ir Yesu gotieno , mowachone niya , “ Rabi , wang’eyo ni in japuonj moa ka Nyasaye , nikech onge ng’at manyalo timo honni mitimogi , mak mana ka Nyasaye ni kode . ”
To Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Adier , adier , awachoni ni ka ok onywol ng’ato nywol manyien , to ok onyal neno Loch Nyasaye . ”
Nikodemo nopenje ni , “ Ere kaka dichak nywol ng’ato kosedoko ng’ama duong’ ? Dodog ei min , kendo chak nywole ? ”
To Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Adier , adier awachoni ni , ka ng’ato ok onywol gi pi kendo gi Roho , to ok onyal donjo e Piny Ruoth Nyasaye .
Gima ringruok onywolo en mar ringruok , kendo gima Roho onyuolo en mar Roho .
Omiyo kik ibwogi ka awachoni ni nyaka nywolu nywol manyien .
Yamo kudho kuma ohero , kendo iwinjo dwonde , to ikia kuma oaye , kata kuma odhiye . Gima kamano bende ema timore ni ji duto ma Roho onywolo . ”
Nikodemo nopenje ni , “ Ere kaka gik ma kamago nyalo timore ? ”
To Yesu nodwoke kapenje ni , “ Ere kaka inyalo bet japuonj e Israel , to ikia gik ma kamago ?
Awachoni adier ni wawacho gik ma wang’eyo , kendo wanyiso ji gik ma waseneno , to onge ng’ato kuomu moyie ni gik mwawacho gin adier .
Ka gik manie piny ka ema anyisou , to ok uyie , koro ere kaka duyie ka anyisou gik polo ?
Onge ng’at mosedhi e polo , mak mana Wuod Dhano , mane olor oa e polo .
“ Kaka ne Musa ochungo thuond mula e thim , e kaka ibiro chungo Wuod Dhano bende ,
mondo ng’ama oyie kuome to oyud ngima ma nyaka chieng’ kuome .
Nyasaye nohero piny ahinya kama , omiyo nochiwo Wuode ma miderma mondo ng’ama oyie kuome kik lal , to obed gi ngima ma nyaka chieng’ .
Nyasaye ne ok ooro Wuowi ni obi e piny mondo ong’ad ni piny bura , to noore ni mondo piny onwang’ warruok kuome .
Ng’ama oyie kuom Wuowi onge gi bura , to ng’ama ok oyie kuome to bura oseloyo nikech ok oyie kuom Wuowi ma miderma mar Nyasaye .
“ Burano chalo kama : ler osedonjo e piny , to ji ohero mudho moloyo ler nikech timbegi richo .
Ji duto ma timbegi richo ok dwar ler , kendo ok dwar dhi e ler , nikech ok gidwar mondo timbegi maricho ofwenyre .
Ng’at ma timbene kare to dhiyo e ler mondo timbene ong’ere e lela ni otimogi koluoro Nyasaye . ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nodhi e piny Judea gi jopuonjrene , mi obet kodgi kuno ka obatiso ji .
Johana bende ne batiso ji Aenon , machiegni gi Salim , nikech pi ne ng’eny kuno . Ji ne dhi ire , kendo nobatisogi .
Mago notimore kapok otueye e jela .
Mbaka nowuok e kind jopuonjre Johana gi ja-Yahudi moro kuom wach puodhruok .
Kuom mano , ne gidhi ir Johana , mi giwachone ni , “ Japuonj ! Ng’at mane ni kodi loka aora Jordan , kendo mane iwuoyo kuome cha , koro batiso ji , kendo ji duto dhi ire . ”
To Johana nodwokogi niya , “ Onge ng’at manyalo bedo gi gimoro mak mana ka Nyasaye ema omiye .
Un donge nuwinjo ka akwer ni ok an Mesia , to an mana jal mane oor mondo otel nyim Mesia ?
Ng’at man gi miaha e wuon kisera , to osiep wuon kisera mochung’ kanyo bedo mamor kowinjo dwond wuon kisera . Mor ma kamano ema an bende an-go , kendo koro oroma chuth .
En nyaka odongi , to an adog piny . ”
Jal moa malo duong’ moloyo ji duto . Ng’at monywol e piny en mar piny , kendo owacho weche mag piny . Jal moa e polo to duong’ moloyo ji duto .
Owacho gik moseneno , kendo mosewinjo , to onge ng’ama oyie ni gima owacho en adier .
To ka ng’ato oyie ni gima Jalo wacho en adier , to obiro ng’eyo malong’o ni Nyasaye en jaadiera .
Jal mane Nyasaye ooro wacho mana weche Nyasaye , nimar Nyasaye chiwo Roho mogundho , ma ok ong’wonyo lwete .
Wuoro ohero Wuowi , kendo oseketo gik moko duto e lwete .
Ng’at moyie kuom Wuowi nigi ngima ma nyaka chieng’ . To ng’at ma ok owinjo Wuowi ok none ngimano ngang’ , to mirimb Nyasaye osiko kuome .
Jo-Farisai nowinjo ni joma Yesu oseloko jopuonjrene , kendo obatiso , ng’eny moloyo jopuonjre Johana .
( To chutho Yesu owuon ne ok batiso ji , to jopuonjrene ema ne timo kamano . )
Kane Yesu owinjo gima ji wacho , noa judea mondo odog Galili .
Nonego okadh e piny Samaria ,
omiyo nochopo e dala Samaria moro miluongo ni Sukar , machiegni gi puodho mane Jakobo omiyo Josef wuode .
Kanyo ema soko Jakobo bende ne nitie . To kaka ne wuoth koro oolo Yesu , nobet e dir sokono ka ojony . Koro ne en kar sa auchiel mar odiechieng’ .
Chi Samaria moro nobiro umbo pi . Yesu nowachone ni , “ Miyae pi amodhi . ”
( Sechego noyudo ka jopuonjrene osedhi Sukar ng’iewo chiemo . )
To chi Samariano nodwoke ni , “ Ere gimomiyo ikwaya pi , to in ja-Yahudi , to an to an chi Samaria ? ”
Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Ka da ing’eye mich mar Nyasaye , kendo ing’e jal makwayi pi mondo omodhini , to in ema da ikwaye pi , mi da omiyi pi mangima . ”
Dhakono nowacho niya , “ Jaduong’ , ionge gi gir tuombo , to soko bende tut . Koro pi mangima to diyud kanye ?
Koso iparo ni iduong’ moloyo Jakobo kwarwa , mane omiyowa sokoni , kendo omodhoe , kaachiel gi nyithinde kod jambe ? ”
Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Ng’ama omodho pigni , riyo biro loyo kendo ,
to ng’ama omodho pi ma anamiye , riyo ok nolo nyaka chieng’ . Pi ma anamiye nodok soko e iye , ma pige bubni , kendo kelo ngima ma nyaka chieng’ . ”
Dhakono nowachone niya , “ Jaduong’ , miya pigno mondo kik riyo chak loya , kendo kik achak abi aumb pi kuma bor kama . ”
Yesu nowachone ni , “ Dhi iluong chwori , eka ubi ka . ”
Dhakono nodwoke ni , “ An aonge gi dichwo . ” Yesu nodwoke ni , “ In kare kiwacho ni ionge gi dichwo ,
nikech isebedo gi chwo abich , to jal ma koro in godono bende ok chwori ! Omiyo gima iwachono en adier ! ”
Dhakono nowachone ni , “ Jaduong’ , aneno ni in janabi .
To kwerewa ne lemo e wi godni , to un jo-Yahudi uwacho ni Jerusalem e kama ji onego olemie . ”
Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Nyarwa , ng’eni ndalo biro ma ji ok nolam Wuoro e godni , kata e Jerusalem .
Un jo-Samaria ulamo gima ok ung’eyo . To wan jo-Yahudi walamo gima wang’eyo , nikech warruok oa kuom jo-Yahudi .
To ndalo biro , kendo ose mana chopo , ma jolemo maradier biro lamoe Wuoro e yo ma Roho dwaro , kendo gi adiera , nikech joma kamago ema Ruoth Nyasaye dwaro mondo obed joma lame .
Nyasaye en Roho , kendo joma lame nyaka lame mana e yo ma Roho dwaro kendo gi adiera . ”
To dhakono nowachone niya , “ Ang’eyo ni Mesia , miluongo ni Kristo , biro biro , kendo ka obiro to obiro nyisowa gik moko duto . ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ An mawuoyo kodini e En ! ”
E sano jopuonjre Yesu nodwogo , kendo ne giwuoro ka gineno kowuoyo gi ng’ama dhako . To onge ng’ama nopenje gima odwaro kuom dhakono , kata gima omiyo owuoyo kode .
Dhakono noweyo dapige kanyo , modok dala , odhi wacho ni joma chwo niya ,
“ Biuru uneye ng’at mosehulona gik moko duto ma asetimo ! Bende dobed Kristo adier ? ”
Kuom mano jogo nowuok e dala , modhi neno Yesu .
E sa mane dhakono odhi omoe joma chwogo , jopuonjre Yesu ne sayo Yesu ni , “ Japuonj , chamie gimoro . ”
To ne odwokogi ni , “ An gi chiemo ma un ok ung’eyo . ”
Omiyo jopuonjre nochako penjore kendgi ni , “ Ng’ato osekelone chiemo koso ? ”
Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Chiemba en timo gima Jal mane oora dwaro , kendo tieko tich mane omiya .
Donge uwacho ni pod dueye ang’wen eka cham chiegi ? Anto awachonu ni , ng’iuru puothe maber , mondo une kaka cham osechiek moromo keyo !
Kata mana sani jokeyo yudo pokgi , kendo choko cham ni ngima ma nyaka chieng’ . Kamano jochuoyo kod jokeyo bedo mamor kanyakla ,
mana kaka ngero wacho , ni , ‘ Ng’at achiel chuoyo , to ng’at machielo keyo . ’ . Ngerono en adier ,
nikech aseorou mondo uka cham mane luchu ok ochuerie . Jomoko nono ema notiyo matek , to un ema koro uchamo luchgi . ”
Jo-Samaria mang’eny mane nitie dalano noyie kuom Yesu nikech wach mane dhakono osewachonigi ni , “ Nohulona gik moko duto ma asetimo . ”
Kuom mano , kane jo-Samaria odhi ir Yesu , ne gikwaye mondo oyie obed kodgi , mi noyie , mobet kodgi kuom ndalo ariyo .
Ji mang’eny moko bende koro noyie , ka giwinjo weche mane Yesu wacho owuon .
Omiyo ne giwacho niya , “ Koro wayie , to ok nikech gima nyocha iwacho , to mana nikech wasewinje gi itwa wawegi , kendo koro wang’eyo ni en Jawar mar piny . ”
Kane Yesu osetieko ndalo ariyo kanyo , noa modhi Galili ,
nikech en owuon nosewacho niya , “ Janabi ok mi duong’ e gweng’gi . ”
Kane ochopo Galili , to jo-Galili norwake gi mor nikech ne giseneno gik moko duto mane otimo Jerusalem e ndalo Sap Pasaka , nimar gin bende ne gidhi e sawo .
Yesu ne ochako odok Kana e piny Galili , kuma ne olokoe pi divai . To jaduong’ moro ne ni kuno mane wuode tuo Kapernaum .
Kane ng’atno owinjo ni Yesu osea Judea mi obiro Galili , nodhi ire mokwaye mondo odhi ochangne wuode mane chiegni tho .
Yesu nowachone niya , “ Un , ka ok uneno ranyisi gi honni , to ok unyal bedo gi yie . ”
To jaduong’no nowachone niya , “ Jaduong’ , yie ibi kapok nyathina otho . ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Dhiyo , wuodi ngima ! ” Ng’atno noyie wach Yesu , modhi .
Kane pod en e yo odhi , jotichne noromone gi wach ni wuode osekwo .
Nopenjogi sa mane ochako bedoe mangima , mi gidwoke ni , “ Midhusu nyoro oweye sa abiriyo mar odiechieng’ . ”
Eka wuon nyathi nong’eyo ni mano e sa onogo ma nyoro Yesu owachone ni , “ Wuodi ngima . ” Kuom mano , en owuon kaachiel gi joode , ne giyie kuom Yesu .
Mano e hono mar ariyo mane Yesu otimo kosea Judea odhi Galili .
Bang’ mano , Yesu nodhi Jerusalem , nikech nitimo Sap jo-Yahudi moro kuno .
E Jerusalem kuno , e bath rangach miluongo ni Ranga Rombe , ne nitie yawo moro miluongo gi dho Yahudi ni Bethesda . Yawono ne nigi agolni abich .
Ji mang’eny matuo , kaka muofni , gi rang’onde , kod pudhe , ne nindo e agolnigo [ Ne girito mondo pi otugre ,
nimar kinde moko malaika ne lor e yawono , kendo tugo pi . To bang’ tugruok pi kamano , ng’at matuo mokwongo donjo e pi ne chango kuom tuo moro amora ma en go . ]
To ng’at moro ne ni kanyo , mane osebedo matuo kuom higni piero adek gaboro .
Yesu nonene konindo kanyo , mi ong’eyo ni osetieko ndalo mang’eny , omiyo nopenje niya , “ Idwaro mondo ochangi koso ? ”
To ng’at matuono nodwoke ni , “ Jaduong’ , aonge gi ng’at ma diketa e yawo ka pi otugore , nikech an , kadwaro dhi , to ng’at machielo kwongona akwonga , ”
Yesu nowachone niya , “ Chungi , ikaw pieni , iwuothi ! ”
Gikanyono ng’atno nochango , mokawo piene , kendo owuotho . To chieng’no ne en chieng’ Sabato .
Mano omiyo jodong jo-Yahudi nowacho ni ng’at mane osechangono niya , “ Kawuono en chieng’ Sabato , omiyo Chikwa ok oyie mondo iting’ pieni kamano . ”
To ng’atno nodwokogi ni , “ Jal ma nende ochanga ema nowachona mondo ating’ piena awuothi . ”
Eka ne gipenje ni , “ En ng’a , ma nende owachoni ni mondo iting’ pieni iwuothi ? ” To ng’at mane osechangono ne ok ong’eyo nying ng’at mane ochange ,
nimar Yesu nosea , nikech ji ne thoth kanyo ahinya .
Bang’e Yesu noyudo ng’atno e Hekalu , mowachone niya , “ Winji ! Kaka koro osechangi , koro we timo richo , nono to dipo ka gimoro marach moloyo otimi . ”
Eka ng’atno nodhi , monyiso jo-Yahudi ni ng’at mane ochange iluongo ni Yesu .
Kuom mano , jo-Yahudi nochalo himo Yesu , nikech notimo gik ma kamago chieng’ Sabato .
To Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Wuora pod tiyo nyaka chil kawuono , kendo an bende atiyo mana kamano . ”
Mano nomiyo jo-Yahudi oramo ni nyaka nege . To ne ok gidwar nege nikech ketho Sabato kende , to ne gidwaro nege bede nikech nopiemore gi Nyasaye , koluongo Nyasaye ni Wuon mare .
To Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Adier , adier awachonu ni , Wuowi ok nyal timo gimoro kende owuon , to otimo mana gima oneno ka Wuoro timo , nikech gima Wuoro timo , ema Wuowi bende timo .
Wuoro ohero Wuowi , kendo onyise gik moko duto ma en owuon otimo , to bende enonyise timbe madongo moloyo magi , mi unuwuor !
Kaka Wuoro chiero joma otho , komiyo ngima , e kaka Wuowi bende yiero joma odwaro , kendo omiyo ngima .
To bende Wuoro ok ng’ad ni ji bura , to oseketo teko mar ng’ado bura e lwet Wuowi ,
mondo ji duto omi Wuowi duong’ mana kaka gimiyo Wuoro . Ng’at ma ok mi Wuowi duong’ , to ok mi Wuoro mane ooro Wuowi duong’ .
Adier awachonu ni ng’ama owinjo wachna , mi oyie kuom Jal mane oora , nigi ngimaa ma nyaka chieng’ , ng’at ma kamano ok ter e bura , to osea e tho , odonjo e ngima .
“ Adier , adier , awachonu ni , kinde biro ma joma otho nowinjie duond Wuod Nyasaye , kendo ji duto ma owinjo dwolno nodok mangima . Adier , kindeno ose mana chopo .
Kaka Wuoro owuon nigi teko mar miyo ji ngima , e kaka osemiyo Wuowi bende teko mar miyo ji ngima .
To bende osemiye teko mar ng’ado bura , nikech en Wuod Dhano .
Wachno kik bwogu nikech ndalo biro ma kata mana joma otho manie bur nowinj dwonde ,
mi wuog oko . Joma timbegi beyo nochier , mi yud ngima , to joma timbegi richo nochier e bura .
“ An ok anyal timo gimoro gi tekona awuon . Ang’ado bura mana kaka Nyasaye onyisa , kendo bura mang’ado en bura makare , nikech ok adwar timo gima an ema adwaro , to atimo mana gima Jal mane oora dwaro .
Ka awuoyo kuoma awuon to weche ma awacho ok nyal kwan ka adier .
To nitie ng’at machielo mawuoyo kuoma , kendo ang’eyo ni gima owacho kuoma en adier .
Ne uoro joote ir Johana , mi ne onyisou weche ma adier .
Ok awach kamano nikech atenora kuom gima dhano ema wacho , to awacho kamano mana ni mondo ukwo .
Johana ne en taya marieny maler , kendo kuom kinde moko ne uyie mondo lerno omiu mor .
Adier , Johana nowuoyo kuoma kanyiso ni Wuora noora , to koro tich ma atiyo , mane Wuoro omiya mondo ati , nyiso malong’o ni Wuoro noora , moloyo kaka ne Johana onyiso .
To Wuoro owuon , mane oora , bende osewuoyo kuoma . Un to pok uwinjo dwonde , kata wang’e bende pok uneno .
Wachne ok bedi e chunyu , nikech ok uyie kuom Jal mane ooro .
“ Uketo chunyu kuom somo Muma , ka uparo ni Muma nyalo miyo uyud ngima ma nyaka chieng’ . Adier , Muma ema wuoyo kuoma ,
to kata kamano udagi biro ira mondo uyud ngima .
An ok adwar mondo ji omiya duong’ .
Un to ang’eyo ni ok un kamano , nikech ang’eyo malong’o ni ok uhero Nyasaye kata matin !
An asebiro e nying Wuora , to ok userwaka . To ka ng’ato obiro e nyinge owuon to ubiro rwake arwaka !
To ere kaka unyalo bedo gi yie , kuhero mondo ng’ato ka ng’ato oyud pak kuom wadgi , to ok utem mondo uyud pak moa kuom Nyasaye ma achiel kende .
Kik upar ni an ema nadonjnu e nyim Wuoro . Ng’at ma nodonjnu en mana Musa , ma useketo genou kuome !
Ka da uyie wach Musa , to da uyie gima awacho , nikech an ema ne ondiko kuoma .
To ka ok uyie weche mane Musa ondiko , to ere kaka duyie wachna ? ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nowuok modhi loka nam Galili , ma bende iluongo ni nam Tiberia .
Oganda maduong’ noluwe , nikech ne gineno honni mane otimo kochango joma tuo .
Eka Yesu noidho got moro , mobet piny kuno gi jopuonjrene .
To Sap Pasaka , ma en sawo mar jo-Yahudi , koro ne chiegni .
Yesu noting’o wang’e , moneno ka oganda maduong’ biro ire , omiyo nopenjo Filipo niya , “ Ere kuma wanyalo ng’iewoe makati ma dwami jogi ocham ? ”
Nowacho kamano kotemo go Filipo , nimar en owuon nong’eyo gima obiro timo .
To Filipo nodwoke niya , “ Siling’ mia ang’wen ok ding’iew makati moromo ng’ato ka ng’ato kawo matintin . ”
Japuonjrene moro machielo , ma nyinge Andrea , owadgi Simon Petro , nowachone niya ,
“ Rawera moro ni ka , man gi makati abich mag shairi , kod rech mothol ariyo . To magi dinyal ang’o kuom joma ng’enygi ? ”
To Yesu nokone ni , “ Nyisuru ji obed piny . ” Kamano ji nobet piny . To kanyo noyudo nitie lum mang’eny . Kuom ji duto mane obet piny kanyo ne nitie joma chwo ma dirom alufu abich .
Bang’ mano , Yesu nokawo makati , mi ogoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano . Eka nopogogi ni ji ka obet piny kamano . Rech bende nopogo , kendo ng’ato ka ng’ato nochiemo kaka odwaro .
Ka ne giseyieng’ giduto , Yesu nowacho ni jopuonjrene niya , “ Chokuru ng’injo modong’ mondo kik gimoro lal . ”
Kuom mano ne gichoko ng’injo mag makati abich mane ji ochamogo , mi opong’o aditini apar gariyo .
Kane ji oneno hono mane Yesu otimono , ne giwacho ni , “ Nyaka bed ni jali e janabi mane onego bi e piny ka . ”
Yesu nong’eyo ni ji dwaro make , kendo chune mondo obed ruoth , omiyo nopondo modhi e got kar kende .
Kane piny ochopo odhiambo , jopuonjrene nodhi e dhonam ,
moidho yie moro mondo ong’ad nam odog loka Kapernaum . Piny koro nosechido , to Yesu ne pok ochopo irgi .
E kindeno ahiti maduong’ ne kudho , omiyo nam noloko marach ahinya .
Kane gisekiewo yie kama bor ma dirom kilomita abich kata auchiel , ne gineno Yesu kawuotho ewi pi , biro irgi e yie . Luoro nomakogi ahinya ,
to Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Kik uluor ! En mana an . ”
Eka ne gikwaye mondo odonj irgi e yie , kendo gikanyono yie nogowo e dhowath mane gidwaro dhiye .
Kinyne , oganda mane odong’ loka machielo noparo ni yie achiel kende ema ne ni kanyo , kendo ne ging’eyo ni Yesu ne ok oidho e yieno kod jopuonjrene , to jopuonjrene nodhi mana kendgi .
To yiedhi moko moa Tiberia nobiro , mogowo machiegni gi kama ne ji ochamoe makati mane Yesu oguedho .
Omiyo kane ji oneno ni Yesu onge kanyo , kendo ni jopuonjrene bende onge , ne giidho yiedhigo , mi gidhi Kapernaum , manyo Yesu .
Kane jogo oyudo Yesu loka machielo , ne gipenje niya , “ Japuonj , ichopo ka karang’o ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Awachonu adier ni , udwara mana nikech makati ma nyoro uchamo , muyieng’ , to ok nikech honni museneno .
Kik uti ni chiemo makethore , to tiuru mana ni chiemo mosiko , kendo makelo ngima ma nyaka chieng’ . Wuod Dhano ema nomiu chiemono , nikech en ema Nyasaye Wuoro oseketo kido mare kuome , manyiso ni oyie kode . ”
Eka ne gipenje ni , “ Ang’o monego watim , eka wabed joma tiyo tich Nyasaye ? ”
To Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Tich ma Nyasaye dwaro mondo uti en ni mondo uyie kuom Jal mane ooro . ”
Kuom mano ne gichako gipenje niya , “ To ere ranyisi minyalo timo mondo wane , eka wayie gima iwacho ? Ang’o minyalo timo ?
Kwerewa ne ochamo chiemo miluongo ni Manna e thim , kaka ondiki e Muma ni , ‘ Nomiyogi chiemo moa e polo mondo gicham . ’ . ”
Eka Yesu nomedo wachonigi niya , “ Adier , adier , awachonu ni , Musa ne ok omiyou kuon maradier moa e polo , to Wuora ema miyou kuon maradier moa e polo ,
nikech kuon ma Nyasaye chiwo en mana jal molor oa e polo , kendo ochiwo ngima ni piny . ”
Kane giwinjo wachno ne gikwaye ni , “ Jaduong’ yie imiwa kuonno pile . ”
To Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ An e kuon mar ngima , kendo ng’ama obiro ira ok nowinj kech nyaka chieng’ , bende ng’at moyie kuoma riyo ok nochak olo ngang’ .
To asewachonu ni , kata obedo ni usenena , to ok uyie kuoma .
Ji duto ma Wuoro omiya nobi ira , kendo ng’ato ang’ata mobiro ira ok nariemb ngang’ ,
nikech ok aselor aa e polo mondo atim gik ma Jal mane oora dwaro .
Jal mane oora dwaro ni kik awit kata ng’at achiel kuom joma ne omiya , to ni mondo achiergi duto chieng’ giko piny .
Adier , Wuora dwaro ni mondo ng’ato ang’ata moneno Wuowi , mi oyie kuome , oyud ngima ma nyaka chieng’ ; kendo anachiere chieng’ giko piny . ”
Jo-Yahudi nochako ng’ur kane giwinjo ka Yesu owacho ni en e kuon moa e polo .
To ne gipenjore ni , “ Jali ok e Yesu wuod Josef koso ? Donge wang’eyo wuon mare ? To ere kaka onyalo wacho ni olor oa e polo ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Weuru ng’ur .
Onge ng’ama nyalo biro ira mak mana ka Wuoro mane oora ema okele ; kendo anachiere chieng’ giko piny .
Ondik e Kitap jonabi ni , ‘ Nyasaye nopuonj ji duto . ’ . Omiyo ng’ato ka ng’ato ma owinjo dwond Wuoro mi opuonjore kuome , to biro mana ira .
Ok awach ni nitie ng’at moro moseneno Wuoro , to mak mana Jal mane oa ka Nyasaye kende ema osenene .
Awachonu adier ni , ng’at moyie ema nigi ngima ma nyaka chieng’ .
An e kuon mar ngima .
Kwereu nochamo Manna e thim , to kata kamano ne githo .
Anto awuoyo kuom kuon moa e polo , ma ka ng’ato ochamo to ok nyal tho ngang’ .
An e kuon mangima mane olor oa e polo . Ng’at mochamo kuonni nobed mangima nyaka chieng’ . To bende kuon ma abiro chiwo mondo piny oyud ngima en ringra . ”
Jo-Yahudi nochako dhawo kendgi niya , “ Ere kaka jali dimiwa ringre mondo wacham ? ”
Yesu nowacho nigi ni , “ Awachonu adier ni , ka ok uchamo ringre Wuod Dhano kendo umadho rembe , to uonge gi ngima e iu .
Ng’at ma ochamo ringra , kendo omadho remba , nigi ngima ma nyaka chieng’ , kendo anachiere chieng’ giko piny .
Ringra e chiemo madieri , kendo remba e math adieri .
Kamano ng’at ma ochamo ringra , kendo omadho remba , ema osiko kuoma , kendo an bende asiko kuome .
Kaka Wuoro mangima noora , kendo angima nikech en , e kaka ng’at mochamo ringra bende nobed mangima nikech an .
Ma e kuon mane olor oa e polo . Ok ochal gi gima ne kwereu ochamo to bang’e otho . Ng’at ma ochamo kuonni to nobed mangima nyaka chieng’ ”
Yesu nowacho wechego kapuonjo e od lemo Kapernaum .
Jopuonjre Yesu mang’eny mane owinjo wechego nowacho niya , “ Ma puonj matek manadi ! Ng’ano ma dichikne ite ? ”
Yesu nong’eyo ni jopuonjrene ng’ur kuom puonjneno , omiyo nopenjogi ni , “ Wachni obwogou koso ?
Ka kamano , to kara dubwogi machal nadi , ka uneno Wuod Dhano kaidho dok malo kama ne oaye ?
Roho ema kelo ngima ; dhano to ok nyal gimoro . Weche ma asewachonu gin roho kod ngima ,
to ji moko kuomu pod ok oyie . ” Yesu nowacho kamano nikech nyaka a chakruok noseng’eyo joma oyie , kod ng’at mane biro ndhoge .
Eka nomedo wacho niya , “ Mano ema omiyo ne awachonu ni ng’ato ok nyal biro ira ka ok Wuora ema omiyo obiro . ”
Chakre kanyo ng’eny jopuonjrene nodok chien , mi oweyo luwe .
Omiyo nopenjo joote apar gariyo ni , “ Un bende udwaro weya koso ? ”
To Simon Petro nodwoke ni , “ Ruoth , ere ng’ama dwadhi ire , to in ema in gi weche makelo ngima ma nyaka chieng’ ?
Wan koro waseyie , kendo wang’eyo ni in e Ng’ama Ler mar Nyasaye . ”
To Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Un ji apar gariyo , donge ne ayierou uduto ? To kata kamano ng’at achiel kuomu en jachien . ”
Nowuoyo mana kuom Judas wuod Simon Iskariot , nikech kata obedo mana ni Judas ne achiel kuom joote apar gariyogo , to en ema nobiro ndhogo Yesu .
Bang’ mano , Yesu nowuotho koni gi koni ka puonjo e piny Galili . Ne ok odwa dhi Judea nikech jodong jo-Yahudi ne dwaro nege .
Sap jo-Yahudi miluongo ni Sap Kiche ne chiegni ,
omiyo owetene nowachone ni , “ A ka , idhi Judea mondo jopuonjreni one honni mitimo .
Ka ng’ato dwaro mondo ji ong’eye , to ok onyal tiyo kama opondo . Ka en adier ni itimo gik ma kamagi , to ara nyisri e nyim piny . ”
Ne giwachone kamano nikech kata gin ma gin owetene ne ok giyie kuome .
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Kindena pok ochopo , to un , kindeu nitie ndalo duto .
Un piny ok nyal mon kodu to an omon koda nikech kinde duto asiko kanyise ni timbene richo .
Un , dhiuru adhiya e sawono . An to ok adhi , nikech kindena pok ochopo . ”
Kane osewacho kamano , nodong’ Galili .
To kane owete Yesu osedhi e sawo , en bende nodhi . To ne ok odhi ratiro , to nodhi mana ling’ling’ .
Jodong jo-Yahudi nomanye e sawo , ka penjo kuma entie .
Ji mang’eny mane odhi e sawono ne wuoyo kuom Yesu , ka moko wacho ni , “ Ooyo , owuondo ogandawa . ”
To kata kamano onge ng’ama noloso kuome ratiro , nikech ne giluoro jodong jo-Yahudi .
To chieng’ mane ndalo sawo ochopo e diere , Yesu nodhi e Hekalu , mochako puonjo ji .
Jodong jo-Yahudi nowuoro , kawacho ni , “ Ere kuma ng’atni oyudoe rieko makama , to ok osomo ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Gik ma apuonjo ok gin maga awuon , to gin mag Jal mane oora .
Ng’at moyie timo gima Nyasaye dwaro , to biro ng’eyo kata ka weche ma apuonjo oa ka Nyasaye , kata ka apuonjo mana wechena awuon .
Ng’at ma loso gi tekone owuon en ng’at madwaro mondo oyud duong’ , to ng’at madwaro mondo ng’at mane oore oyud duong’ en jaadiera , kendo oonge gi miganga kata matin .
Donge Musa nomiyou Chik , to onge kata ng’at achiel kuomu morito ? Ka ok kamano , to ang’o momiyo udwaro nega ? ”
Ji nodwoke ni , “ Jachien ni kodi ! Ng’ano madwaro negi ? ”
Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Ne atimo gimoro achiel kende chieng’ Sabato , mi ubwok uduto .
Paruru ni Musa nomiyou chik mar tero nyangu . ( To chutho Musa ok ema nokelo chikno , to kwereu ema nochake . ) Chikno omiyo utero yawuotu nyangu chieng’ Sabato .
To ka un utero nyathi nyangu chieng’ Sabato , mondo kik uketh Chik Musa , to marang’o ukecho koda kuom chango ng’ato chieng’ Sabato , mi dende duto bed mangima ?
Mano omiyo kik ung’ad bura kurango mana gik ma oko , to ng’aduru bura mana gi adiera . ”
Jo-Jerusalem moko nopenjore niya , “ Donge ma e jal ma gidwaro nego cha ?
To winjuru kaka opuonjo ji mana e lela , to onge ng’ama wachone gimoro . Koso dibed ni jodongwa ong’eyo ni en Mesia ?
To mano ok nyal bet kamano , nikech waduto wang’eyo kuma jali oaye . Mesia to kabiro , to onge ng’ama nong’e kuma oaye . ”
Mano nomiyo Yesu owacho gi dwol maduong’ , kopuonjo e Hekalu niya , “ En adier ni ung’eya , kendo en adier ni ung’eyo kuma aaye , to kata kamano ok asebiro gi tekona awuon . Jal mane oora e wuon adiera , to un ok ung’eye .
An to ang’eye , nikech aa ire , kendo en ema noora . ”
Eka ne gitemo make , to ne ok ginyal , nikech kindene ne pok ochopo .
To ji mang’eny noyie kuome , kapenjore ni , “ Ka Mesia obiro , dotim honni mang’eny moloyo ma jali timo koso ? ”
Jo-Farisai nowinjo ka ji kuodho wechego kuom Yesu , omiyo ne giriwo wach gi jodolo madongo , mi gioro askeche mondo omake .
To Yesu nowacho ni , “ Pod abiro medo bet kodu kuom kinde moko , eka bang’e nadog ir Jal mane oora .
Unumanya , to ok unuyuda , nikech kama abiro betie ok unyal biroe . ”
Jodong jo-Yahudi nopenjore kendgi niya , “ Kanye modwaro dhiye ma ok wanyal nwang’ee ? Koso odwaro dhi kuom jo-Yahudi modak e pinje joma ok jo-Yahudi mondo opuonj joma ok jo-Yahudi ?
Ere tiend wach mowachoni , wanamanye to ok wanayude , kendo ni , kuma obiro betie wan ok wanyal dhiye ? ”
Chieng’ mogik mar sawo , mane en odiechieng’ maduong’ ahinya , Yesu nochung’ mowacho gi dwol maduong’ niya , “ Ng’at ma riyo oloyo mondo obi ira , omodhi .
En mana kaka Muma wacho ni , ‘ Aore mag pi mangima nomol kawuok kuome . ’ . ”
To Yesu ne oloso kuom Roho , ma ji duto moyie kuome ne biro yudo . To e kindeno Roho ne pok obiro , nikech Yesu ne pok oyudo duong’ne .
Jomoko kuom joma ne owinjo wechego nowacho niya , “ Nyaka bed ni jali e Janabi mwasebedo kwageno ni biro biro . ”
Jomoko to nowacho ni , “ En e Mesia . ” To ji moko nokwer ni , “ Mesia ok nyal wuok Galili !
Donge Muma wacho ni Mesia nobed nyakwar Daudi , kendo ni nonywole Bethlehem , dala Daudi ? ”
Kamano ji nopogore kuom wachne .
Jomoko kuomgi ne dwaro make , to onge ng’at mane otimo kamano .
Kane askeche odwogo , jodolo gi jo-Farisai nopenjo gi ni , “ Ang’o momiyo ok usekele ka ? ”
To ne gidwoko niya , “ Pok wanenoe ng’at mawuoyo ka ng’atni ! ”
Eka jo-Farisai nopenjogi ni , “ Kara un bende osewuondou .
Bende usenenoe jatendwa moro , kata ja-Farisai moro , moyie kuome ?
To ji ajia ma ok ong’eyo Chik , gin joma okuong’ ! ”
Ng’at achiel kuom jodongogo ne Nikodemo , mane oyudo osedhi ir Yesu . En nowachonigi ni ,
“ Donge Chikwa okwer ni kik ng’ad ni ng’ato bura ka pok oyale , mi owinj wechene ? ”
To ne gipenje ni , “ In bende in ja-Galili koso ? Som Muma , to ibiro yudo ni onge janabi manyalo wuok Galili ! ”
[ Eka ji duto noa , modok miechgi .
Yesu noa kanyo , modhi e got Zeituni .
Kinyne gokinyi mang’ich , noduogo modonjo e Hekalu , kendo ji duto nochokore bute . Nobet piny , mochako puonjogi .
To jopuonj Chik gi jo-Farisai nokelo dhako moro mane ojuk ka terore . Ne gikete ochung’ e diergi ,
mi giwacho ni Yesu niya , “ Japuonj , dhakoni ojuk rando , ka terore !
To Chik mane Musa omiyowa wacho ni dhako ma kamano nyaka go gi kite , mi tho . In to iwacho ang’o ? ”
Ne giwacho kamano nikech ne gidwaro wach moro ma digidonjne go . To Yesu nolung’ore piny , mondiko e lowo gi lith lwete .
To kane jogo omedo penje wachno , noting’o wiye , modwokogi niya , “ Ng’ato kuomu ma pok otimo richo ema mondo okwong ogoye gi kidi ! ”
Eka nochako olung’ore , mondiko e lowo .
To kane giwinjo gima owacho , ne gia kanyo achiel achiel chakre joma dongo nyaka joma tindo , mi Yesu kende ema nodong’ , ka dhakono ochung’ bute .
Yesu noting’o wiye , mopenjo dhakono niya , “ Nyarwa , ekegi ? Onge kata achiel modong’ mondo ong’adni bura ? ”
Dhakono nodwoke ni , “ Ooyo , Jaduong’ onge ng’ato modong’ . ” Eka Yesu nokone ni , “ Kata an bende ok ang’adni bura . Dhiyo , to kik ichak itim richo kendo . ” ]
Yesu nomedo puonjo ji , kowacho ni , “ An e ler mar piny . Ng’at moluwa ok nowuoth e mudho , to nobed gi ler mar ngima . ”
To jo-Farisai nowachone niya , “ Iwuoyo mana kuomi iwuon , omiyo ok wanyal yie ni gik miwacho gin adier . ”
To Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Kata obedo ni awuoyo kuoma awuon , to gik ma awacho gin adier , nikech ang’eyo kuma ne aaye , kendo ang’eyo kuma adhiye , to un ukia kuma naaye kata kuma adhiye .
Un ung’ado bura gi rieko mar dhano , to an ok ang’ad ni ng’ato bura .
To kata ka ang’ado bura , to bura ma ang’ado en adier , nikech ok ang’ad bura kenda , to Jal mane oora ema konya .
E Chiku bende ondikie ni , ka ji ariyo owinjore e wachgi , to wach ma giwacho ikwano ka adier .
An ema awuoyo kuoma awuon , kendo Wuora mane oora osiro wachna . ”
Mano omiyo ne gipenje niya , “ Ere Wuoru nogo ? ” To Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Ok ung’eya , kata Wuora bende ok ung’eyo . Ka da bed ni ung’eya , to Wuora bende da ung’eyo . ”
Yesu nowacho wechego duto kopuonjo ji e Hekalu , ei ot mane oketie sanduge mag sadaka . Kata kamano onge ng’ama nomake , nikech kindene ne pok ochopo .
Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ An to adhi , kendo unudwara , to unutho mana e richou . Ok unyal dhi kuma adhiye . ”
Mano omiyo jo-Yahudi nowacho ni , “ Ng’atni wacho ni ok wanyal dhi kuma odhiye ! Mano nyiso ni obiro dere koso ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Un ua mwalo to an aa malo . Un , un jopinyni , anto ok an japinyni .
Mano emomiyo awachonu ni unutho e richou , nikech ka udagi yie ni an e En , to adier unutho mana e richou . ”
Eka ne gipenje niya , “ To in e ng’ano ? ” Yesu to nodwokogo ni , “ An mana ng’ama asebedo ka awachonu ni e an .
Nitie gik mang’eny ma adwaro wacho kuomu , kendo ma adwaro ng’adonugo bura . Jal mane oora en jaadiera kendo wach ma ayudo kuome ema anyiso piny . ”
To ne ok ging’eyo ni Yesu loso kodgi kuom Wuoro .
Omiyo Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Ka useting’o Wuod Dhano malo , eka unung’e ni an e En . Bende unung’e ni onge gima atimo gi tekona awuon , to weche duto ma awacho , Wuora ema osepuonja .
Jal mane oora ni koda . Pod ok oweya kenda , nikech pile atimo mana gik malong’one . ”
To kane owacho wechego , ji mang’eny noyie kuome .
Yesu nowachoni jo-Yahudi mane oyie wachne niya , “ Ka umako puonjna , to eka un jopuonjrena adier .
Bende ubiro ng’eyo adiera , kendo adiera nomi ubed thuolo . ”
To ne giwachone niya , “ Wan koth Ibrahim , kendo pok wabedo wasumb ng’ato nyaka nene . Koro ere gima omiyo iwacho ni wanabed thuolo ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Adier , adier , awachonu ni , ng’at matimo richo en misumba richo .
Misumba ok luong ni wuod dala ndalo duto , to wuod wuon dala ema iluongo kamano ndalo duto .
Kuom mano , ka Wuowi ema omiyo ubedo thuolo , to unubed thuolo chutho chutho .
Ang’eyo ni un koth Ibrahim , kata kamano udwaro nega nikech puonjna ok nyal donjonu .
An awachonu gik ma aseneno kuom Wuora , to un utimo gik ma useneno kuom wuoru ! ”
Ne gidwoke niya , “ Ibrahim e wuonwa . ” To Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Ka dabed ni un nyithind Ibrahim adier , to dikoro utimo mana gik machal gi gik mane Ibrahim otimo .
To kar timo kamano , to udwaro mana nega nikech asebedo ka anyisou adiera mane ayudo kuom Nyasaye . Ibrahim to ne ok nyal timo gima chal kamano .
Un to utimo mana gima wuonu timo . ” To ne gidwoke ni , “ Wan ok wan kimirwa ! Wan gi wuonwa achiel kende ma en Nyasaye . ”
Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Ka dabed ni Nyasaye e wuonu adier , to da uhera , nikech an ne aa ka Nyasaye , kendo koro an kodu ka . Ne ok abiro gi tekona awuon , to En ema noora .
Gik ma awacho ok nyal donjonu , kendo ok unyal winjo tiendgi nikech ok uhero wach ma akelonu .
Un nyithind wuonu ma en Satan , kendo uhero timo gik ma en ema odwaro . Nyaka a chakruok en osebedo mana janek , kendo ok odwar adiera nikech adiera onge e iye . Ka owacho miriambo , to oluwo mana kite owuon , nikech en jamriambo , kendo en e wuon miriambo duto .
An to awacho adiera , kendo mano emomiyo ok uyie wachna .
Ere ng’ato kuomu ma nyalo ng’eng’a ni an jaricho ? To ka awacho adiera , ang’o momonou yie wachna ?
Ng’at Nyasaye winjo wach Nyasaye , to un ok uwinj wach Nyasaye nikech ok un jo Nyasaye . ”
Eka jo-Yahudi nowacho ni Yesu ni , “ Donge wan kare kwawacho ni in ja-Samaria , kendo ni jachien ni kodi ? ”
To Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Aonge gi jachien , to Wuora ema amiyo duong’ . Un to uchaya .
An ok adwar mondo umiya duong’ , to nitie Jal madwaro mondo ayud duong’ , kendo en ema nong’ad bura .
Awachonu adier ni , ka ng’ato omako wachna , to ok notho nyaka chieng’ . ”
Eka jo-Yahudi nowachone ni , “ Koro wang’eyo adier ni jachien ni kodi . Ibrahim ne otho , kendo kata mana jonabi bende notho , to eka pod iwacho ni ng’at mowinjo wachni ok notho nyaka chieng’ !
Koso iparo ni iduong’ moloyo wuonwa Ibrahim mane otho ? Jonabi bende notho ! In to iparo ni in ng’a ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Ka amiyora duong’ awuon , to duong’na onge tich . Wuora ma uluongo ni Nyasachuno ema miya duong’ .
To eka un ok ung’eye , an to ang’eye . Ka anyalo wacho ni ok ang’eye , to dabed jamriambo mana ka un . To ang’eye adier , kendo pile amako wachne .
Kwaru Ibrahim ne mor koneno ndalona . Adier , nonene mobedo mamor . ”
Jo-Yahudi nokwero Yesu niya , “ In pok hiki oromo kata mana higni piero abich ! Ere kaka inyalo wacho ni iseneno Ibrahim ? ”
To Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Adier , adier , awachonu ni , kane pok onywol Ibrahim to ne antie . ”
Kane giwinjo kamano , ne gikwanyo kite mondo gigoyego , to nopondo , mi owuok e Hekalu .
Kane Yesu wuotho , noneno ng’at moro mane onywol muofu .
Jopuonjrene nopenje ni , “ Japuonj , ng’atni nonywol muofu nikech richone owuon koso nikech richo mag jonywolne ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Jali ne ok onywol muofu nikech richone owuon , kata nikech richo mag jonywolne , to nonywole muofu mana ni mondo ji one teko mar Nyasaye kichange .
Nyaka wati tije mag Jal mane oora kapod piny odiechieng’ , nikech otieno biro chopo ma ng’ato ok nyal tiyoe .
Kapod anie piny , to an e ler mar piny . ”
Kane Yesu osewacho kamano , nong’ulo olawo piny , mi olosogo lowo , owirogo wang’ ng’atno .
Eka nowachone ni , “ Dhi ilwok wang’i e yawo mar Siloam . ” ( Tiend nying yawono en ‘ Ote’ . ) Kuom mano ng’atno nodhi olwoko wang’e mi odwogo ka oneno .
Jodalagi , kod joma ne osenene ka okwecho , nopenjore niya , “ Donge jali ema yandi bet kakuecho cha ? ”
Jomoko kuomgi noyie ni mano en , to moko nokwer ni , “ Ooyo , ok en , to ochal mana kode . ” Ng’atno owuon to nowachonigi ni , “ En mana an . ”
Eka ne gipenje ni , “ To ere kaka wang’i oyawore ? ”
Nodwokogi ni , “ Ng’at moro ma nyinge Yesu noloso lowo mi owirogo wang’a , bende onyisa mondo adhi alwok wang’e e yawo mar Siloam . Omiyo ne adhi malwoko wang’a mi wang’a oyawore . ”
Eka ne gipenje ni , “ Ng’at onogo ni kanye ? ” To nodwoko ni , “ Ok ang’eyo . ”
Bang’e ne gitero ng’at ma yandi muofuno ir jo-Farisai .
To chieng’ mane Yesu olosoe lowo kendo ochangoe wang’ muofuno , ne en chieng’ Sabato .
Kuom mano jo-Farisai bende nopenjo muofuno kaka ne wang’e ochango . Nodwokogi ni , “ Ng’atno nowiro wang’a gi chuodho , eka ne aluoko , kendo koro aneno ! ”
Jo-Farisai moko nowacho ni , “ Ng’at mane otimo kamano ok nyal bet ng’at Nyasaye , nikech ok orito Chik Sabato . ” To moko nowacho ni , “ Bende ng’at ma jaricho ditim honni ma kamagi adier ? ” Kamano ne gipogore kuom wachno chutho .
Omiyo ne gichako gipenjo muofuno niya , “ In to koro ang’o miwacho kuome , kaka oseyawo wang’i ni ? ” Ne odwokogi ni , “ En janabi . ”
Jodong jo-Yahudi ne ok nyal yie ni ng’atno ne en muofu to koro oneno . Omiyo ne giluongo jonywolne ,
mi gipenjo ni , “ Ma en wuodu koso ? Uwachoni nonywole ka en muofu adier ? Ka kamano , to koro ere kaka oneno ? ”
Jonywol ng’atno nodwokogi ni , “ Wang’eyo ni en nyathiwa , kendo nonywole muofu .
To kata kamano ok wang’eyo kaka koro oneno , to bende ok wang’eyo ng’at moyawo wang’e . To en ng’at maduong’ , omiyo penje uru , nikech onyalo dwokou kende owuon . ”
Jonywolne nodwoko kamano nikech ne giluoro jodong jo-Yahudi . Ne oyudo jodong jo-Yahudi osewinjore kendgi ni ng’ato ang’ata moyie ni Yesu e Mesia , to nyaka tam mondo kik dhi e od lemo .
Mano e momiyo jonywol ng’atno nowacho ni , “ En ng’at maduong’ , penjeuru owuon . ”
Eka jodongo nochako oluongo ng’at mane onywol muofuno irgi , mi giwachone niya , “ Kuongri gi nying Nyasaye ni ibiro wacho adiera . Wan wang’eyo ni jali en jaricho . ”
To ng’atno nodwokogi ni , “ An ok ang’eyo kata en jaricho , to wach achiel mang’eyo en mana ni yande an muofu to koro aneno ! ”
Eka ne gipenje ni , “ Ang’o mane otimoni moyawo wang’i ? ”
Ne odwokogi niya , “ Donge asenyisou , to udagi winjo ? Ang’o momiyo udwaro ni mondo achak awachnu kendo ? Koso un bende udwaro doko jopuonjrene ? ”
Bang’ mano ne gijare , ka giwachone ni , “ In ema in japuonjrene , wan to wan jopuonjre Musa .
Wang’eyo ni Nyasaye nowuoyo gi Musa . Ng’atni to wakia kuma oaye ! ”
Eka ng’atno nowacho niya , “ Kara ma en wach miwuoro ! Un uwacho ni ukia kuma oaye , to en ema oseyawo wang’a !
Wang’eyo ni Nyasaye ok winj wach joricho , to ng’at moluore , kendo matimo gik ma odwaro , ema owinjo .
Nyaka nene pok owinjie ng’at moyawo wang’ ng’at mane onywol muofu .
Ka da bed ni ng’atni ok en ng’at Nyasaye , to da ok obedo gi teko mar timo kamano . ”
To ne giwachone ni , “ In nonywoli e chuny richo , to koro ere kaka dipuonjwa ? ” Eka ne giriembe oko e od lemo .
Yesu nowinjo ni oseriemb ng’atno e od lemo , omiyo kane oyude , nopenje ni , “ Bende iyie kuom Wuod Dhano koso ? ”
To ng’atno nodwoke ni , “ Jaduong’ , Wuod Dhano en ng’a mondo ayie kuome ? ”
Yesu nowachone ni , “ Isenene , kendo en ema oloso kodi ni ! ”
Eka ng’atno nogoyo chonge piny e nyim Yesu , kowachone ni , “ Jaduong’ , ayie ! ”
Bang’ mano , Yesu nowacho ni , “ Asebiro e piny mondo akel bura , mondo joma muofni onen , to joma neno odok muofni . ”
Jo-Farisai moko mane ni kanyo nowinjo gima owacho , mi openje ni , “ Iparo ni wan bende wan muofni koso ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Ka da bed ni un muofni , to da ubedo ma onge gi ketho , to kaka koro uwacho ni uneno , omiyo kethou osiko . ”
Yesu nodhi nyime kowacho niya , “ Adier , adier , awachonu ni , ng’at ma ok oluwo dhorangach ka donjo e duond rombe , to donjo mana gi kamoro nono , en jakuo kendo jamecho .
Jakwadh rombe to donjo mana gi e dhorangach .
En ema jarit rangach yawone . Rombe bende winjo duonde koluongogi achiel achiel gi nyinggi kogologi oko .
Kosegologi duto to otelonigi , kendo giluwe , nikech ging’eyo duonde .
Ok ginyal luwo ng’ama gikia nikech ok ging’eyo duonde , omiyo giringo aringa . ”
Kata obedo ni Yesu nogoyonigi ngerono , to ne ok giwinjo tiende .
Emomiyo nowachonigi niya , “ Adier , adier , awachonu ni an e dhoranga duond rombe .
Ji duto mane obiro mokwongona ne jokuo kendo jomecho , kendo rombe ne ok odewogi .
An to an e dhorangach . Ng’at mokadho kuoma ema nokwo . Ng’atno nodonj kendo nowuog oko , mi nonwang’ lek maber mokwayoe .
Jakuo biro mana ni mondo okwel , kendo oneki , kendo oketh gik moko . Anto asebiro ni mondo ji oyud ngima kendo obed ngima moromo chuth .
“ An e jakwath maber . To ung’eyo ni jakwath maber chiwo ngimane nikech rombe .
Jakwath mondiki , ma ok jakwath ma wuon rombe , to ringo weyo rombe koneno ka ondiek biro . Kuom mano ondiek gore kuom rombe kendo keyogi .
Ng’atno ringo nikech ondike andika , omiyo ok odew rombe .
An to , an jakwath maber . Ang’eyo rombena , kendo gin bende ging’eya ,
mana kaka Wuora ong’eya , kendo an bende ang’eyo Wuora . Mano emomiyo ayie chiwo ngimana nikech romba .
To bende an gi rombe moko ma ok ni e duondni . Gin bende nyaka akelgi , kendo giniwinj duonda , eka rombe duto nobed kueth achiel man gi jakwath achiel .
“ Wuora ohera nikech ayie chiwo ngimana mondo chieng’ moro achak ayude kendo .
Onge ng’at manyalo mayago , to an ema ayie chiwe , nikech mano ema ahero timo . An gi teko mar chiwe , bende an gi teko mar kawe kendo . Wuora ema osenyisa mondo atim kamano . ”
Wechego nomedo kelo pogruok e kind jo-Yahudi giwegi .
Ji mang’eny kuomgi nowacho ni , “ Jachien ni kode , kendo ojaneko ! Ang’o momiyo uchiko itu ne wechene ? ”
Jomoko to nowacho ni , “ Onge ng’at man gi jachien manyalo wacho weche ma kamagi . Bende uparo ni jachien diyaw wang’ ng’at mamuofu ? ”
Noyudo ndalo mar Sap Pwodho Hekalu ochopo , kendo ne en ndalo chwiri .
To Yesu nonwang’o wuotho e Hekalu e agola miluongo ni Agoch Solomon .
Eka jo-Yahudi nochokore molwore , mi openje ni , “ Ibiro miyo wariwo gi kiawa nyaka karang’o ? Ka in e Mesia to nyiswa ane malongo ! ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Asenyisou , to utamoru yie . Gik ma atimo e nying Wuora ema wuoyonu kuoma .
To un ok uyie , nikech ok un e kueth romba .
Romba ong’eyo dwonda , kendo an bende ang’eyogi , kendo giluwo bang’a .
Amiyogi ngima ma nyaka chieng’ , kendo ok ginilal ngang’ , bende onge ng’at manyalo gologi e lweta .
Wuora mane omiyagi duong’ moloyo gik moko duto kendo onge ng’at manyalo gologo e lwete .
Wan gi Wuora wan gimoro achiel . ”
Kane jo-Yahudi owinjo wachno , ne gichako gikwanyo kite kendo mondo gigogo Yesu .
Omiyo Yesu nopenjo gi ni , “ Asenyisou gik mabeyo mang’eny ma asetimo gi teko mar Wuora . To kuom tijena go duto , ere ma omiyo odwaro goya gi kite ? ”
To jo-Yahudi nodwoke ni , “ Ok wadwar goyi nikech gimoro maber misetimo , to wagoyi mana nikech ipiem gi Nyasaye , nimar in mana dhano , to eka iwacho ni in Nyasaye ! ”
Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Donge ondiki e Kitap Chiku ni Nyasaye owacho ni , un nyiseche ?
To wang’eyo malong’o ni wach Nyasaye ok nyal lokore .
Kane Nyasaye oluongo joma ne wachne obironigi ni , ‘ Nyiseche’ kamano , koro ere gima omiyo uwacho ni apiem gi Nyasaye , ka awacho ni an Wuod Nyasaye ? To an ema Nyasaye ne oyiera , mi oora e piny ka !
Ka uneno ni ok ati tich Wuora , to kik uyie koda .
To ka atiyo tichne , to kata ka ok unyal yie koda , to onego uyie gi tich matiyo , mondo ung’e chutho ni an ei Wuora kendo Wuora ni eiya . ”
Kane giwinjo wachno , ne gitemo make kendo , to nopondo motony .
Bang’ mano , Yesu nong’ado aora Jordan modhi loka kuma ne Johana obatisoe ji mokwongo , mi nodak kuno .
Ji mang’eny ne obiro ire , mowacho niya , “ Johana ne ok otimo honni , to gik moko duto mane owacho kuom jali gin adiera chutho . ”
Kamano ji mang’eny , ne oyie kuom Yesu kuno .
Ng’at moro ma nyinge Lazaro , mane odak Bethania , ne tuo . Bethania e dala mane Maria odakie kod Maritha nyamin mare
Maria ema ne owiro Ruoth Yesu gi mo mang’ue ng’ar , kendo oyweyo tiendene gi yie wiye . Ne en nyamin Lazaro , mane tuo .
Nyimine Lazaro nooro ni Yesu wach niya , “ Ruoth , osiepni mihero tuo . ”
To kane Yesu owinjo wachno , nowacho ni , “ Tuono ok en mar tho , to osebiro mana ni mondo Wuod Nyasaye bende oyud duong’ . ”
Yesu nohero Maritha gi nyamin mare kod Lazaro .
To kata kamano ne otieko ndalo ariyo kuma ne entie bang’ winjo ni Lazaro tuo .
Eka nowacho ni jopuonjrene ni , “ Wadoguru Judea . ”
To jopuonjrene nowachone niya , “ Japuonj , donge jo-Yahudi yandi dwaro goyi gi kite ? Ang’o momiyo pod idwaro dok kuno ? ”
Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Donge odiechieng’ achiel nigi seche apar gariyo ? Ka ng’ato wuotho godiechieng’ , to ok onyal chwanyore , nikech oneno ler mar pinyni .
To ka owuotho gotieno , to ochwanyore nikech ler ongene . ”
Bang’ mano Yesu nomedo wacho niya , “ Lazaro osiepwa nindo otero , to adhi mondo achiewe . ”
Jopuonjrene nowachone ni , “ Ruoth , ka nindo osetere , to kara obiro kwo . ”
Ne giwacho kamano nikech ne gigalo ni Yesu loso kuom nindo mar yueyo , to chutho noloso mana kuom tho mar Lazaro .
Mano omiyo koro nowachonigi ratiro ni , “ Lazaro osetho .
To amor ni yandi ok an kuno , nikech mano biro konyou , mi uyie . Omiyo wadhiuru ire . ”
Eka Thoma mane onywol rude , nowacho ni jopuonjre wetene niya , “ Wan bende wadhiuru mondo watho kode . ”
Kane Yesu ochopo , noyudo ni Lazaro osetieko ndalo ang’wen e bur .
Bethania ne chiegni gi Jerusalem ma dirom kilomita adek ,
omiyo jo-Yahudi mang’eny nobiro duogo chuny Maritha gi Maria kuom tho owadgi .
Kane Maritha owinjo ni Yesu biro , nowuok mondo oromne , to Maria nodong’ e ot .
Maritha nowacho ni Yesu niya , “ Ruoth , ka da bed ni nyocha in ka , to owadwa ok dotho .
To kata kamano sani , ang’eyo ni Nyasaye biro timoni gimoro mikwaye . ”
Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Owadu biro chier . ”
To Maritha nowachone ni , “ Ang’eyo ni nochier chieng’ giko piny . ”
Yesu nowachone niya , “ An e chier , kendo an e ngima . Ng’ato ang’ata moyie kuoma nodok mangima , kata obedo ni osetho ,
kendo ng’at mangima moyie kuoma ok notho nyaka chieng’ . Bende iyie wachni koso ? ”
Maritha nodwoke ni , “ Ee , Ruoth , ayie ni in e Mesia , Wuod Nyasaye , mane onego bi e piny . ”
Kane Maritha osewacho wechego , nodhi oluongo Maria nyamin mare ling’ling’ , mowachone niya , “ Japuonj ni ka , kendo oluongi . ”
Kane Maria owinjo kamano , noa malo piyo , mi odhi ir Yesu .
Noyudo ka Yesu pok odonjo e dala , to ne pod ochung’ mana kama ne Maritha oromonee .
Jo-Yahudi mane ni kod Maria e ot ka duogo chunye , nonene kochung’ piyopiyo , mowuok oko . Omiyo ne giluwe , ka giparo ni odhi ywak e liel .
Kane Maria ochopo kama Yesu nitie , monene , nogoyo chonge piny e nyime , mowachone niya , “ Ruoth , ka da bed ni nyocha in ka , to owadwa ok dotho ! ”
Yesu noneno Maria gi jo-Yahudi mane ni kode kaywak , mi mirima nomake , kendo noneno malit .
Eka nopenjo ni , “ Uyike kanye ? ” Ne gidwoke ni , “ Jaduong’ , bi ine . ”
Pi wang’ Yesu nochuer .
Omiyo jo-Yahudigo nowacho ni , “ Neyeuru kaka yandi ohero Lazaro ! ”
To moko kuomgi nowacho niya , “ Jali noyawo wang’ muofu ! Donge ne onyalo geng’o tho monego Lazaroni ? ”
Mirima nochako omako Yesu kendo , mi odhi but liel , mane en bur mokuny ariwa e lak got , moket kidi e dhoge .
Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Goluru kidi oko e dho liel . ” To Maritha , ma nyamin jal motho , nowachone ni , “ Ruoth , koro osetieko ndalo ang’wen e bur , omiyo nyaka bed ni koro odum . ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Donge nende awachoni ni ka in gi yie , to ibiro neno duong’ mar Nyasaye ? ”
Kuom mano ne ging’ielo kidi oko . Yesu nong’iyo malo , mowacho niya , “ Wuora , agoyoni erokamano nikech isewinja .
An ang’eyo ni iwinja ndalo duto , to asewacho wechegi mondo oganda mochung’ ka ong’e ni in ema niora . ”
Kane osewacho kamano , nokok matek niya , “ Lazaro , wuog oko ! ”
Eka jal mothono nowuok , ka tiendene gi luetene obo gi nanga mar yik , kendo ka wang’e bende obo gi kitamba . Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Gonyeuru mondo odhi . ”
Jo-Yahudi mang’eny mane obiro duogo chuny Maria noneno gima Yesu otimo , mi giyie kuome .
To moko kuomgi nodok ir jo-Farisai , mohulonigi gima Yesu osetimo .
Omiyo jo-Farisai kod jodolo madongo noluongo buchgi maduong’ , mi openjore ni , “ Ng’atni timo timbe madongo mang’eny ! Wan to watimo ang’o ?
Ka waweye odhi nyimekamano , to ji duto biro yie kuome , kendo jo-Rumi dibi , mi keth Hekaluwa , kendo tiek jowa duto . ”
To ng’at achiel kuomgi , ma nyinge Kaiafa , mane jadolo maduong’ e higano , nowachonigi ni , “ Un ok ung’eyo gima onego utim !
Donge ber ka ng’at achiel otho , moloyo ka ogandawa duto orumo ? ”
Ne ok owacho kamano gi riekone owuon , to kaka ne en jadolo maduong’ e higano , ne okoro wach ni Yesu biro tho ni oganda jo-Yahudi .
To ne ok okoro ni Yesu biro tho mana ne jo-Yahudi kende , to ni obiro tho mondo ochok nyithind Nyasaye obed e kanyakla achiel .
Chakre chieng’no ne gichako chano kaka digineg Yesu .
Kuom mano , Yesu koro ne ok wuoth ratiro kama jo-Yahudi nitie , to noa kuno modhi e dala moro miluongo ni Efraim , mane nitie gweng’ moro momanyore gi thim , mi obet kuno gi jopuonjrene .
Sap jo-Yahudi mar Pasaka koro ne chiegni , omiyo ji mang’eny moa e gwenge mopogore opogore ne dhi Jerusalem mondo opwodhre , obed moikore ni sawono .
Ne gimanyo Yesu , kendo kane ginie Hekalu ne gipenjore ni , “ Uparo nadi ? Bende dobi e sawoni adier ? ”
Ne giwacho kamano nikech noyudo jodolo madongo gi jo-Farisai osegolo chik ni ka ng’ato ong’eyo kama Yesu nitie , to nyaka ohul , mondo omake .
Kane pod ndalo auchiel , to chop Sap Pasaka , Yesu nodhi Bethania , dala gi Lazaro mane osechiero .
Ne giselosone chiemo kuno , kendo Maritha ema notiyonigi , to Lazaro ne achiel kuom joma ne chiemo gi Yesu .
Eka Maria nokawo mo mang’ue ng’ar ma nengone tek ahinya , ma dirom nus kilo . Nowiro tiend Yesu gi morno , mi oyweyo gi yie wiye , mi tik mo mang’ue ng’arno opong’o ot .
Achiel kuom jopuonjre Yesu ma nyinge Judas Iskariot , jal mane biro ndhoge , nopenjo ni ,
“ Ere gimomiyo morni ok olok siling’ mia adek , mondo opog joma odhier ? ”
To ne ok owach kamano nikech ne oparo joma odhier adier , to nowacho kamano mana nikech ne en jakuo , kendo kaka ne en jakeno mar jopuonjre , nothoro kawo pesa morito .
To Yesu nowacho ni , “ Weyeuru okane nyaka chieng’ yikna .
Nimar joma odhier un-go ndalo duto . Anto ok un koda ndalo duto . ”
Jo-Yahudi mathoth nowinjo ni Yesu ni kuno , omiyo ne gibiro mondo ginene . To ok Yesu kende ema nokelonigi neno , to bende ne gibiro mondo gine Lazaro , mane Yesu osechiero oa kuom joma otho .
Mano omiyo jodolo madongo nochano mondo oneg Lazaro bende ,
nikech en ema ne omiyo jo-Yahudi mang’eny weyogi , kendo yie kuom Yesu .
Kinyne , oganda maduong’ mane osebiro e Sawo nowinjo ni Yesu biro Jerusalem .
Ne gijako bede othidhe , mi gidhi romone , ka gikok niya , “ Opak Nyasaye ! Oguedh ng’ama biro e nying Ruoth ! Adier Nyasaye mondo ogwedh Ruodh Israel ! ”
Yesu noyudo kanyna , mi oidho mana kaka Muma wacho ni ,
“ Un jo-Sayun , kik ubed maluor . Neuru ! Ruodhu biro iru , koidho nyathi kanyna . ”
E kindeno jopuonjrene ne ok ong’eyo tiend wachno , to achien , kane Yesu oseyudo duong’ne maler , eka ne giparo ni ji osetimone kamano ,
Oganda mane ni kod Yesu kane oluongo Lazaro owuok e liel , mi ochiero oa kuom joma otho , nonyiso ji gima ne giseneno .
Mano emomiyo ji nodhi romone , nikech ne gisewinjo ni otimo hono maduong’no .
Kuom mano jo-Farisai nowacho kendgi niya , “ Uneno kaka ok unyal gimoro ! Neyeuru , piny duto luwo bang’e ! ”
Ne nitie jo-Grik moko kuom joma ne odhi lemo e Sawono .
Ne gidhi ir Filipo , mane odak Bethsaida e piny Galili , mi gikwaye ni , “ Jaduong’ , wadwaro neno Yesu . ”
Omiyo Filipo nodhi mowacho ni Andrea . Eka ne gidhi giduto ji ariyo , mi ginyiso Yesu wachno .
To Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Sa koro osechopo ma Wuod Dhano yudoe duong’ne maler .
Adier , adier , awachonu ni ka koth cham ok olwar e lowo , mi otho , to osiko mana kodhi achiel kende . To ka otho , to onyago kodhi mang’eny .
Ng’ama ohero ngimane , ngimane nolalne , to ng’ama ochayo ngimane , kendo nobed gi ngima ma nyaka chieng’ .
Ka ng’ato tiyona , to nyaka oluwa , kendo kama antie ema jatichna bende nobedie . Ka ng’ato tiyona , to Wuora nomiye duong’ .
“ Koro chunya parore , to dawach ang’o ? Dakwa Wuora mondo oresa kuom gima dwaro tima sanini ? Ooyo , ok kamano , nikech mano e gimomiyo abiro e sani .
Wuora , mi nyingi duong’ ! ” Eka dwol noa e polo , mawacho niya , “ Asemiye duong’ , kendo abiro chako amiye duong’ . ”
Ji mane ochung’ kanyo nowinjo dwolno , mi owacho ni polo ema omor . Moko to nowacho ni malaika ema owuoyo kode .
To Yesu nowachonigi ni , “ Dwolno ok obiro nikech an , to obiro mana nikech un .
Koro ing’ado bura ni pinyni , kendo jatende ibiro riemb oko .
An to , ka oting’a malo , to anaywa ji duto ira . ”
Nowuoyo kamano konyisogo kit tho mane obiro thogo .
To ji nodwoke niya , “ Chikwa osepuonjowa ni Mesia nobedie nyaka chieng’ . Koro ere kaka inyalo wacho ni nyaka ting’ Wuod Dhano malo ? Wuod Dhano to en ng’a ? ”
To Yesu nodwokogi ni , “ Pod odong’ kinde matin ma abiro betgo e kindu , ka amiyou ler . Wuothuru kapod un gi ler , mondo mudho kik juku . Ng’at mawuotho e mudho kia kuma dhiye .
Kapod un gi ler , to yieuru kuom ler , mondo ubed nyithind ler . ” Kane Yesu osewacho wechego , nodhi mi opondonigi kar kende .
To kata obedo ni nosetimonigi honni mang’eny kamano , to ne ok giyie kuome .
Mano nobet kamano mondo gima ne Isaya janabi okoro otimre . Isaya nosewacho niya , “ Ruoth , ere ng’ama oseyie wach mwalando ? Koso ere ng’ama Ruoth Nyasaye osenyiso tekone ? ”
Ok ne ginyal yie , nikech Isaya nowacho bende ni ,
“ Nyasaye oseimo wang’gi , kendo osemiyo wigi odoko mapek Ka dine ok otimo kamano , to dikoro gineno gi wengegi , kendo dikoro giparo gi wigi , mi gilokre mondo ochanggi . ”
Isaya nowuoyo kamano nikech noneno duong’ maler mar Yesu , kendo noloso kuom Yesu .
To kata kamano , ji mang’eny , koda ka jodongo , noyie kuome , to ne giluoro jo-Farisai , omiyo ne ok gidwar hulo wachno , nikech ne dipo ka oriembgi e ut lemo ,
nimar ne gihero pak mar dhano moloyo pak mar Nyasaye .
Yesu nowuoyo gi duol maduong’ , kawacho niya , “ Ngama oyie kuoma ok oyie mana kuoma kende , to oyie mana kuom Jal mane oora bende ,
kendo ng’ama nena , neno Jal mane oora .
An e ler , kendo asebiro e piny mondo ng’at moyie kuoma kik sik e mudho .
Ka ng’ato owinjo wechena , to ok oritogi , to ok an ema nang’adne bura , nimar ne ok abiro mondo ang’ad ni piny bura , to nabiro mana ni mondo ares piny .
To ng’at modaga , kendo ma ok oyie wechena , nigi jang’adne bura . Wach ma asewacho ema nong’adne bura chieng’ giko piny ,
nimar ok asewache gi tekona awuon , to Wuora mane oora ema osenyisa gima onego ahul kendo awachi .
Ang’eyo ni chikne ema kelo ngima ma nyaka chieng’ . Awacho mana gik ma Wuora onyiso mondo awachi . ”
Koro Sap Pasaka ne chiegni ahinya , kendo Yesu nong’eyo ni kindene osechopo moago e pinyni , odok ir Wuoro . Nosehero joge owuon manie piny , to koro obiro nyiso kaka oherogi chuth nyaka giko .
Yesu gi jopuonjrene ne koro chiemo . To noyudo Satan oseketo paro e chuny Judas wuod Simon Iskariot ni mondo ondhoge .
Kata obedo ni Yesu nong’eyo ni Wuoro oseketo gik moko duto e lwete , kendo ni ne osea ir Nyasaye , kendo koro odok ire ,
nochung’ oweyo chiemo . Nolonyo lepe , moketo tenge , eka nokawo taulo , otueyo e nungone .
Noolo pi e karaya , mi ochako lwokogo tiend jopuonjrene , kendo oyweyo gi taulo mane osetweyo e nungone .
Kane ochopo ir Simon Petro , Petro nopenje ni , “ Ruoth , in ema idwaro lwoko tienda adier ? ”
To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Sani ok inyal ng’eyo tiend gima atimo , to ibiro ng’eyo bang’e . ”
Petro nokwere ni , “ Ok nilwok tienda ngang’ ! ” To Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Ka ok alwoko tiendi , to ok in e kanyakla achiel koda . ”
Eka Petro nowachone ni , “ Ruoth , kara kik ilwok mana tienda kende , to lwok koda ka lweta gi wiya bende ! ”
To Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Ng’at mlosewokore ok dwar lwokruok kendo , mak mana tiende kende ema olwoko , nimar dende duto ler . Omiyo un uler , to ok un uduto . ”
Nong’eyo ng’at mane biro ndhoge , kendo mano emomiyo nowacho ni , “ Ok uler uduto . ”
Kane oselwokonigi tiendgi kamano , norwako lepe , mi ochako obet piny . Eka nopenjogi ni , “ Bende ung’eyo tiend gima asetimonuno ? ”
Un uluonga ni ‘ Japuonj’ , kendo ni ‘ Ruoth’ , to mano uluonga kare , nikech mano e an .
To ka an , ma an Ruodhu kendo Japuonju ema aselwoko tiendeu , koro un bende onego ulwok tiende oweteu .
Gima asetimonu en ranyisi , omiyo un bende timuru mana kaka asetimonuno .
Adier , adier , awachonu ni misumba ok duong’ moloyo ruodhe , kendo ng’at moor ok duong’ moloyo jal moore .
Ka ung’eyo wachno , to un johawi kutiyo kode .
“ To ok awuo kuomu uduto , nimar ang’eyo joma aseyiero . To Muma wacho niya , ‘ Ng’at machiemo koda oselokore jasika’ , kendo wachno nyaka timre .
Koro anyisou wachno kapok otimore , mondo ka otimore to uyie ni an e En
Adier , awachonu ni ng’at morwako ng’at ma aoro , to orwako mana an , kendo ng’at morwaka , to orwako mana Jal mane oora . ”
Kane Yesu osewacho kamano , chunye nochandore malit , mi ohulo ratiro niya , “ Adier , adier awachonu ni achiel kuomu biro ndhoga . ”
Jopuonjrene nong’iyore kendgi , ka gidhier nono ni oloso kuom ng’a .
To noyudo ka japuonjre Yesu moro mohero obet bute .
Simon Petro nogwelo japuonjreno , monyise mondo openj Yesu ng’at ma owuoyo kuome .
Omiyo japuonjreno nomedo sudo machiegni gi Yesu , mopenje ni , “ Ruoth , en ng’a miwuoyo kuome ? ”
Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Abiro luto kuon e tawo , to jal ma amiyo e en . ” Eka noluto kuon e tawo , momiyo Judas iskariot ,
To kane Judas ochamo kuonno , Satan nodonjo kuome . Eka Yesu nowachone ni , “ Gima ibiro timo , tim piyo . ”
To kuom joma nobet kanyo , onge ng’at mane ong’eyo gimomiyo Yesu wuoyone kamano .
To kaka Judas ema ne jakeno , jopuonjrene moko ne paro ni Yesu onyise mondo odhi ong’iew gik mane gidwaro konyorego e sawo , kata ni mondo opog pesa ni joma odhier .
To kane Judas osekawo kuonno , nowuok oko mana gikanyono . Koro ne en otieno .
Kane Judas osewuok oko , Yesu nowacho niya , “ Wuod Dhano koro yudo duong’ . Nyasaye bende yudo duong’ nikech en .
Ka Nyasaye oyudo duong’ kuome kamano , to Nyasaye bende nomiye duong’ kama entie , kendo enotim kamano piyopiyo .
Nyithinda , pod an kodu kuom kinde matin kende . Bang’e unudwara , to anyisou , mana kaka ne anyiso jo-Yahudi , ni kuma adhiye ok unyal biroe .
Amiyou chik manyien ni mondo uherru . Kaka aseherou e kaka ng’ato ka ng’ato mondo oher wadgi .
Ka uheroru kamano , to ji duto biro ng’eyo ni un jopuonjrena adier . ”
Simon Petro nopenjo Yesu ni , “ Ruoth , idhi kanye ? ” Yesu nodwoke ni , “ Kuma adhiye ok inyal luwae sani , to ibiro luwa bang’e . ”
Petro nochako openje ni , “ Ruoth , ere gimomiyo ok anyal luwi sani . Ayie tho nikech in ! ”
To Yesu nodwoke ka penje ni , “ Bende diyie tho nikech an adier ? Adier , adier , awachonu ni , ibiro kweda nyadidek , kapok thwon gweno okok . ”
Bang’ mano Yesu nowachonigi niya , “ Kik chunyu parre . Yieuru kuom Nyasaye , to kuoma bende yieuru .
E dala Wuora nitie udi mang’eny , to ka da ni ok kamano , to dikoro asenyisou , to adhi mondo alosnu kar dak .
Ka asedhi mi alosonu kar dak , to anaduog omou , mondo un bende ubi udag koda kama antie .
To adier ung’eyo yo madhi kuma adhiye . ”
Thoma nopenje ni , “ Ruoth , wakia kuma idhiye , omiyo ere kaka dwang’e yo materowa kuno ? ”
Yesu nodwoke niya , “ An e yo , kendo an e adiera . Onge ng’ama dhi ka Wuora mak okadho kuoma .
Ka ung’eya , to Wuora bende ubiro ng’eyo . Chakre kawuono ung’eye , kendo usenene . ”
Eka Filipo nowachone ni , “ Ruoth , nyiswa Wuoro , to mano biro romowa . ”
To Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Filipo , asebedo kodu ndalo mang’eny , to kara in pok ing’eya ? Ng’at ma osenena , to oseneno Wuoro . Kuom mano , ere kaka iwacho ni mondo anyisu Wuoro ?
Donge uyie ni an ei Wuora , kendo Wuora ni e iya ? Gik ma awachonu ok awach mana gi tekona awuon , to Wuora modak e iya ema tiyo tijene .
Yieuru koda ni an ei Wuora , kendo Wuora ni e iya . To ka ok unyal yie wechena , to yieuru nikech tijenego .
Awachonu adier ni ng’at moyie kuoma notim tije ma atimo . Bende enotim koda ka timbe madongo moloyo mago , nikech adhi ka Wuora .
Kendo gimoro amora mukwayo e nyinga natim , mondo wuoro oyud duong’ kuom Wuowi .
Adier , gimoro amora mukwayo e nyinga , natim .
“ Ka uhera to unumak chikena .
Anakwa Wuoro , mi nomiu Jakony machielo mondo osik kodu nyaka chieng’ .
Jakonyno en Roho Maler adiera , ma pinyni ok nyal rwako , nimar piny ok nene , kendo ok ong’eye . Un to ung’eye , nimar osiko kodu , kendo odak e iu .
“ Ok anaweu ka nyithi kiye , to anaduog iru .
Bang’ kinde matin , piny ok nochak onena kendo . Un to ununena . Anabed mangima , omiyo un bende unubed mangima .
Chieg’no unung’e ni an ei Wuoro , kendo ni un e iya , bende ni an e iu .
Ng’at mong’eyo chikena , kendo orito , ema ohera . Ng’at mohera , ema Wuora bende noher . An bende anahere , mi afwenyrane . ”
Juda , ma ok Iskariot , nopenjo Yesu niya , “ Ruoth , ere kaka wan ema ibiro fwenyorinwa , to ok ifwenyri ni piny ? ”
Yesu nodwoke niya , “ Ng’at mohera norit wachna . Wuora bende nohere , mi wanabi ire , kendo wadag kode .
Ng’at ma ok ohera , to ok rit wachna . To wach ma uwinjo ok mara , to en mana mar Wuora mane oora .
“ Asewachonu wechegi kapod an kodu ,
to Jakony , ma en Roho Maler ma Wuoro biro ooro e nyinga , nopuonju gik moko duto , kendo nomi upar weche duto ma asewachonu .
Kue ema koro aweyonu . Adier , kue mara awuon ema amiyou . En kue ma pinyni ok nyal chiwo . Kik chunyu parre , kendo kik ubed maluor .
Usewinjo ka awachonu ni adhi , to kata kamano abiro duogo iru . Ka da bed ni uhera , to da ubedo mamor ni adhi ir Wuoro , nikech Wuoro nigi duong’ moloya .
To bende asenyisou kapok gigi otimore , ni mondo ka gitimore , to uyie .
Koro okabi wuoyo kodu mathoth , nikech jatend pinyni okayo machiegni . To oonge gi tyeko kuoma !
Gigo duto nyaka timre kamano mondo piny ong’e ni ahero Wuora , kendo ni atimo mana gik ma Wuora nyisa mondo atim . “ Koro chung’uru mondo wawuog wadhi !
“ An e mzabibu maradier , kendo Wuora e japur mzabibuno .
Bedena duto ma ok nyag olemo , ong’ado oko , to bede duto ma nyago olemo olwero maler mondo omed nyak .
Un koro osedoko maler nikech wach ma asewachonu .
Beduru e iya kaka an bende abet e iu . Kaka bad mzabibu ok nyal nyago olemo kende , ka ok en kuom yath mzabibu , e kaka un bende ok unyal nyago gimoro , kapok ubet e iya .
“ An e mzabibu , to un , un bedene . Ng’at mobet kuoma , kaka abet kuomu , nyago olemo mang’eny , nikech ka upogoru koda , to ok unyal gimoro .
Ka ng’ato ok obet kuoma to iwite oko , mana kaka iwito bad yath , mi two . Bede ma kamago ichoko , kendo iwito e mach , mi wang’ .
Ka ubet kuoma , kendo wachna obet kuomu , to gimoro amora mukwayo notimnu .
Ka unyago olemo mang’eny , to umiyo Wuora duong’ . Kamano unyiso ni un jopuonjrena .
Kaka Wuora osehera , e kaka an bende aseherou . Sikuru e herana .
Ka urito chikna , to eka usiko e herana , mana kaka an bende aserito chik Wuora , kendo asiko e herane .
“ Awachonu wechegi mondo un bende ubed gi mor ma an-go , kendo mondo mor ma un-gono obed moromo chuth .
Chik ma amiyou e ma : herreuru mana kaka aherou .
Onge hera maduong’ ma ng’ato nyalo herogo osiepne , moloyo chiwonigi ngimane .
Ka utimo gik ma achikou , to eka un osiepena .
Chakre kawuono ok nachak aluongu kendo ni wasumbini , nikech misumba ok ong’eyo gima ruodhe timo . To aluongou ni osiepena , asenyisou gik moko duto ma Wuora osenyisa .
Un ne ok uyiera , to an ema ne ayierou , mi awalou mondo udhi unyag olemo , kendo mondo olemo munyagono osiki , mondo Wuora omiu gimoro amora mukwaye e nyinga .
To chik ma amiyou en ni , herreuru e kindu uwegi .
“ Ka piny mon kodu , to nyaka ung’e ni nomon koda chon , kane pok omon kodu .
Ka da bed ni un mag pinyni , to da piny ohero gire owuon . To piny mon kodu nikech aseyierou kuom piny , omiyo koro ok un mag piny .
Paruru gima nawachonu ni , ‘ Misumba ok duong’ moloyo ruodhe . ’ . Ka an ema gisanda , to un bende nyaka gisandu , to ka girito wachna , to wachu bende giniriti .
To ginitimnu kamano mana nikech an , nimar gikia Jal mane oora .
Ka dine ok abiro mi awuoyo kodgi , to da ok gibedo joketho . Koro to onge kaka digiriasre .
Ng’at mamon koda , to mon gi Wuora bende .
Ka dine ok atimonigi honni ma ng’ato pok otimo , to da ok gibedo joketho . To giseneno gik matimo , to pod gimon amona koda kaachiel gi Wuora bende .
Mago duto nyaka timre mondo ochop weche mondiki e Chikgi ni , ‘ Ne gimon koda kayiem nono . ’ .
“ Abiro oronu Jakony koa kuom Wuoro . En Roho mar adiera moa kuom Wuoro . Ka osebiro to enonyisu wach kuoma .
Un bende ununyis ji wach kuoma , nikech usebet koda nyaka ne achak tija .
“ Asewachonu wechego mondo kik uchwanyru uwe yie kuom Nyasaye .
Ji biro riembou e ut lemo . Adier , ndalo biro ma ka ng’ato onegou , to nopar mana ni otimo gima Nyasaye morgo .
Ginitim kamano nikech ok ging’eyo Wuoro , kata an .
To asenyisou gigi chon , mondo ka kinde ochopo ma gitimoree , to upar ni ne asiemou ni gibiro timore , mondo utang’ . “ Ne ok anyisou mokwongo , nikech ne pod an kodu .
Koro to adhi ir Jal mane oora , to onge ng’ato kuomu mapenja kuma adhiye ,
to chunyu opong’ gi kuyo nikech asewachonu wechego .
To kata kamano awachonu adier ni ber ka adhi , nikech ka ok adhi , to Jakony ok nobinu . To ka adhi to anaore iru ,
kendo ka osebiro , to enonyis piny tiend richo , gi tiend tim makare , kod tiend ng’ado bura , mondo ji ong’e kaka gin joricho .
“ To enonyisgi ni tamruok yie kuoma en richo .
Bende ka adok ir Wuora mi ok uchako unena , to mano nonyisgi ni an ng’at makare .
To bende abiro nyisogi ni bura osechakore , ka gineno ni oseng’ad bura ni jatend pinyni .
“ Pod an gi weche mathoth mowinjore awachnu , to pod ok unyal winjogi .
To ka Roho mar adiera osebiro , to enopuonju adiera duto . Ok enowach mana wachne owuon , to enowach mana gima owinjo , kendo enonyisu tiend gik mabiro timore .
Enomiya duong’ , nikech gik ma enowachnu nogol mana kuoma .
Gik moko duto ma Wuora nigo gin maga . Mano emomiyo asewachonu ni gik moko duto ma Roho nonyisu nogol kuoma .
“ Bang’ kinde matin , ok ubi nena . Eka achien bang’ kinde matin unuchak unena . ”
Jopuonjrene moko nopenjore kendgi ni , “ Ere tiend gima owachonwa ni , bang’ kinde matin ok wabi nene , eka achien bang’ kinde matin wanachak wanene , kowacho ni mano biro timore nikech odhi ka Wuoro ?
Ere gima oparo ka owacho ni , ‘ Kinde matin’ ? Ok wang’eyo gima owacho ! ”
To Yesu nong’eyo ni gidwaro penje wachno , omiyo nowachonigi niya , “ Ang’o ma upenjoru ? Koso en gima awachonu ni , bang’ kinde matin ok ubi nena , eka achien bang’ kinde matin unuchak unena kendo ?
Adier , adier , awachonu ni , unuywag kendo unuku , to piny nobed abeda mamor . Unuku , to kuyou nolokre mor .
Ka dhako muoch kayo to en gi rem malit kod kuyo , nikech kinde mar nyuol osechopo , . To ka osenywolo nyathi , to koro ok opar rem gi kuyo mane engo nikech koro omor ni osenywolo dhano e piny .
Kamano e kaka un bende koro un gi kuyo , to anachak aneu kendo , mi unudok mamor , kendo onge ng’ama nomau mor ma un-gono .
Chieng’no ok unupenja wach moro , nimar anawachnu adier ni gimoro amora mukwayo e nyinga , to Wuora nomiu .
Nyaka chop koroni , pok ukwayo gimoro e nyinga , to koro kwauru , to unuyudi , mondo mor ma un-go obed moromo chuth .
“ Asenyisou wechegi gi ngeche . To kinde biro ma ok nachak awuoe kodu gi ngeche kamano , to ananyisu wach Wuora mana malong’o ratiro .
E ndalogo unukwa Wuoro gima udwaro e nyinga , to ok awachi ni anakwanu Wuoro ,
nimar Wuoro owuon oherou , nikech uhera , kendo uyie ni ne aa ire .
Adier ne aa ir Wuoro , mi abiro e piny , to koro aa e piny , adok ir Wuoro . ”
Eka jopuonjrene nowachone ni , “ Koro iwuoyo malongo’ , nikech ok iwuo gi ngeche .
Koro wasefwenyo ni ing’eyo gik moko duto , kendo onge tiende mondo ng’ato openji gimoro . Mano omiyo wayie ni ia ir Nyasaye . ”
Yesu nodwokogi niya , “ Kara koro uyie ?
To winjuru ! Ndalo biro , kendo ose mana chopo , ma nokeue , mi ng’ato ka ng’ato dhi e dalane owuon , mi uweya kenda . To chutho ok an kenda , nikech Wuora ni koda .
Asenyisou wechegi duto mondo kubedo kuoma , to uyud kue . Unune malit e piny , to beduru modhil , nimar an aseloyo piny ! ”
Kane Yesu osetieko wacho wechego , nong’iyo polo , mowacho niya , “ Wuora , sana koro osechopo . Mi wuodi duong’ .
Isemiye teko kuom ji duto , mondo en bende ochiw ngima ma nyaka chieng’ ni ji duto misemiye .
Ka ng’ato ong’eyi , in Nyasaye ma achiel kende , kendo ong’eyo Jal mane ioro , ma en Yesu Kristo , to en gi ngima ma nyaka chieng’ .
Asemiyi duong’ e pinyka kuom tieko tich mane imiya mondo ati .
A Wuora , koro miya duong’ kabedo kama intie . Ee , miya duong’ mane an-go kodi kane piny pok obetie .
“ Asemiyo joma ne igolo e piny ong’eyo kaka ichal . Ne gin jogi , kendo in ema nimiyagi . Giserito wachni ,
kendo koro ging’eyo ni gik moko duto misemiya wuok mana kuomi .
Asehulonigi wach mane imiya , mi girwako , kendo giseng’eyo maonge kiawa ni ne aa iri adier , bende giseyie ni in ema ne iora .
“ Koro gin ema akwayonigi . Ok akwa ni piny , to akwayo mana ni joma ne imiya , nikech gin jogi .
