To chakre ndalo mar Adam nyaka ndalo mar Musa , tho noloyo ji duto , koda ka joma ok oketho kaka Adam noketho , kotamore rito chik mane Nyasaye omiye . Adam ne en ranyisi mar Jal mane onego obi .
To ng’wono mane Nyasaye otimo opogore mabor gi richo mane Adam otimo , nikech richo mar ng’ato achiel nokelo ni ji duto tho , to ng’wono mar Nyasaye , kod chiwo mane ng’at achiel ma en Yesu Kristo okelo nomiyo ji duto gweth mogundho .
Mich Nyasayeno opogore mabor gi richo mar ng’at achielno , nimar richo achiel nokelo ni ji duto bura , to richo mang’eny nokelo mich mang’won mane omiyo ji duto obet e winjruok gi Nyasaye .
Ka ketho mar ng’ato achiel ema nomiyo tho olocho , to mano kaka joma yudo ng’wono mogundho mar Nyasaye gi michne ma miyo gibedo e winjruok kode nobed gi ngima kendo nolochi nikech ng’at achiel ma en Yesu Kristo !
Kaka ketho achiel nomiyo bura oloyo ji duto , kamano bende e kaka tim makare achiel miyo ji duto bedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye , kendo miyogi ngima .
Bende kaka ji duto nodoko joketho nikech ng’at achiel notamore winjo wach , e kaka ji duto nobed e winjruok gi Nyasaye nikech ng’at achiel nowinjo wach .
Chik nobiro , mi ketho omedore . To kama richo nomedoree , ng’wono nomedoree moloyo ,
ni mondo kaka richo nolocho kamiyo ji duto tho , e kaka mondo ng’wono olochi , ka Nyasaye miyo ji bedo e winjruok kode , kendo miyogi ngima ma nyaka chieng’ kuom Yesu Kristo Ruodhwa .
To koro ere gima dwawachi ? Dwawachi ni ber kwasiko watimo richo mondo ng’wono mar Nyasaye omedre koso ?
Ngang’ ! Ok kamano ! Korka wach richo to wan mana joma otho . Koro ere kaka dwadhi nyime kwadak e richo ?
Donge ung’eyo ni kane obatiswa , mi wariwore gi Yesu , to batisono nomiyo wariwore kode e thone ?
Mano onyiso ni kane obatiswa mi wariwore gi Yesu e thone , to ne oyikwa kode bende , mondo kaka ne Kristo ochier oa kuom joma otho kuom teko maduong’ mar Wuoro , e kaka wan bende wabed gi ngima manyien .
Ka waseriwore kode e thone , to wanariwre kode e chierne bende .
Wang’eyo ni ngimawa machon nogur kode e msalape ni mondo kitwa mar richo orum , kendo ni mondo kik wamed bedo wasumb richo ,
nikech ka ng’ato osetho to osegonye oa e richo .
Ka wasetho gi Kristo to wayie ni wanabed mangima kode bende ,
nikech wang’eyo ni Kristo osechier oa kuom joma otho , kendo ok nochak otho nimar tho koro onge gi teko kuome .
Tho mane othogo , notho ni richo dichiel kende , to koro kaka ongima , ongima ni mondo oti ni Nyasaye .
Kamano e kaka onego ukwanru ni usetho ni richo , to ungima ni mondo uti ni Nyasaye kuom Yesu Kristo .
Mano emomiyo kik uwe richo bed gi loch e ringreu matho , mondo kik uluw gombo mag ringruok .
Kik ng’ato kuomu yie mondo fuonde moro amora obed gima itimogo richo , to chiwreuru ni Nyasaye ka joma otho mochako ochier . Adier , chiwneuru ringreu duto mondo obed gik ma itimogo gik makare ,
nimar richo ok nochak obed gi loch kuomu , nikech koro ok un e bwo Chik , to un e bwo ng’wono mar Nyasaye .
To koro nadi ? Dwatim atima richo nikech koro ok wan e bwo Chik to wan e bwo ng’wono koso ? Ngang ! Ok kamano !
Donge ung’eyo malong’o ni ka uchiworu ni ng’ato ka wasumbe , mi urito chikene , to chutho un wasumb ng’atno ? Kamano bende ka un wasumb richo to tho ema ochomou , to ka un wasumb winjo wach to Nyasaye biro miyo ubed e winjruok kode .
To wagoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano nikech kata obedo ni yande un wasumb richo , to koro urito puonj mane omiu gi chunyu duto .
Ne ogonyu e tuech richo , mi udoko wasumb tim makare .
Awuoyonu gi weche mayot winjo nikech parou mar dhano thanythany . Kaka ne uchiwo ringreu obed wasumb dwanyruok gi tim ma ok kare , mutimo atima richo , e kaka koro chiwuru ringreu obed wasumb tim makare mondo udok joma ler .
Kane un wasumb richo , to ne ok uneno ni onego uluw tim makare .
To ere ohala mane uyudo kuom timo gik ma koro miyou wichkuotgi ? Giko mar gigo en mana tho .
To koro osegonyu e tuech richo , mi udoko wasumb Nyasaye , omiyo ohala muyudo en ngima maler , kendo gikone en ngima ma nyaka chieng’ .
Misach richo en tho , to mich Nyasaye en ngima mochwere kuom Yesu Kristo Ruodhwa !
Owetena , un joma ong’eyo kaka chik tiyo , omiyo ung’eyo ni chik otueyo ng’ato mana ka pod ongima .
Wakawuru dhako man gi chwore kaka ranyisi : Chik kend otueye kuom chwore ka pod chwore ngima . To ka chwore otho , to ogonye kuom chik mane otueye kuom chwore .
To ka odhi odak gi dichwo moro ka chwore pod ngima , to iluonge ni dhako materore . To ka chwore otho to chik ok otueye . En thuolo omiyo ka ng’at machielo koro okende , to ok en dhako materore .
Owetena , un bende uchalo kamano . Ne udoko fuond ringre Kristo , omiyo Chik onge gi teko kuomu , nikech uchalo joma otho . Mano notimore mondo ubed jo-ng’at machielo , ma en Jal mane ochier oa kuom joma otho , mondo wan duto wanyag olemo ni Nyasaye .
E ndalo mane pod waluwo timbe mag dhano , Chik nomiyo gombo otiyo e ngimawa , mi onywolo mana tho .
To koro osegonywa kuom Chik mane otueyowa , nikech wachalo joma osetho . Koro ok wati ni Nyasaye e yo machon , kwaluwo mana Chik mondiki , to watiyone ka wan gi ngima manyien ma Roho kelo .
Koro ere gima dwawachi ? Dwawach ni Chik en richo koso ? Ngang ! Ayie ni ka da Chik onge , to ok dang’eyo ni richo en ang’o . Ka da ni Chik ok owacho ni ‘ Kik igombi , ’ to da ok ang’eyo ni gombo en ang’o .
Chikno nomiyo richo thuolo , mi okelo gombo duto mopogore opogore e chunya . Ka da onge Chik , to richo dobedo gima otho .
Chon ne ok ang’eyo wach Chik , to ne angima angima . To kane ang’eyo Chik , richo nodoko mangima , mi an to atho .
Kamano chik mane oketi mondo okel ngima , nokelona mana tho ,
nikech richo noyudo thuolo ma Chik okelo , mi owuonda , kendo onega .
Kuom mano , Chik Musa en gima ler , kendo chike moting’o bende ler , kendo kare , kendo beyo .
Kara dwawachi ni gima ber ema nomiyo atho koso ? Ngang’ ! Richo notiyo gi gima ber , mi onega , mondo richo ong’ere malong’o ni en ang’o . Kamano chik nyiso ni richo en gima rach moloyo .
Wang’eyo malong’o ni Chik Musa ber , nikech oa kuom Nyasaye . An to an mana dhano matho , moseng’iew modoko misumba richo .
Gik ma atimo odhiera , nikech ok atim gik ma adwaro ni mondo atim , to atimo mana gik ma ok adwar .
To ka atimo gik ma ok adwar timo kamano to mano nyiso ni ayie ni Chik ber .
To chutho ok an ema atim gigo , to richo modak e chunya ema timogi .
Ang’eyo ni an kaka dhano , onge gima ber man kuoma , nikech kata obedo ni adwaro timo gima ber , to ok anyal .
Gima ber ma adwaro timo ok atim , to gima rach ma ok adwar ema atimo .
To ka atimo gima ok adwar timo kamano to mano nyiso ni ok an ema atim gino , to richo modak kuoma ema time .
Koro gima asefwenyo en ni , ka adwaro timo gimoro maber , to richo kende ema arodhnogo .
E chunya maiye to amor gi Chik Nyasaye ,
to e ringra anwang’oe chik machielo makedo gi chik ma chunya oyiego . Chikno omiyo abedo misumba richo modak e ringra .
Yaye ! Mano kaka an ng’at machandore ! Ng’ano ma biro resa e ringruok mar thoni ?
Agoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano , nikech Yesu Kristo Ruodhwa ema biro resa ! Kuom mano , aneno ni an awuon arito Chik Nyasaye mana gi parona kende , to e ngimana mar dhano to aluwo mana chik mar richo .
Mano emomiyo koro onge bura kuom jogo man kuom Kristo Yesu ,
nikech ka ng’ato ni kuom Kristo , to chik mar Roho makelo ngima osegonye kuom chik makelo richo kod tho .
Gima Chik Musa ne ok nyal timo nikech nyawo mar dhano e gima Nyasaye notimo kane ooro Wuode e kido mar ringruok machal mana gi ringrewa matimo richo , mondo obed misango magolo richo . Kamano , kane en e ringruokno , nomiyo bura oloyo richo ,
mondo tim makare ma Chik dwaro ochop kare kuomwa , wan ma koro wawuotho kaka Roho dwaro , to ok kaka ngima mar dhano dwaro .
Joma timo gik ma ngima mar dhano dwaro , paro mana weche mag dhano , kendo mano kelo tho ,
to joma timo gik ma Roho dwaro , paro mana weche mag Roho , kendo mano kelo ngima kod kue .
Ng’at ma paro mana weche mag dhano mon gi Nyasaye , nikech ok orito Chik Nyasaye . Adier , ok onyal rite .
Chutho , joma timo mana gik ma ngima mar dhano dwaro ok nyal bedo malong’o ni Nyasaye .
Ka Roho mar Nyasaye odak e iu , to ok unyal timo gik ma ngima mar dhano dwaro , to utimo mana gik ma Roho dwaro , kendo ka ng’ato onge gi Roho mar Kristo , to ok en ng’ate .
To ka Kristo nie iu , to kata obed ni ringreu otho nikech richo , chunyu to ngima nikech Nyasaye osemiyo ubet e winjruok kode .
To bende ka Roho ma Jal mane ochiero Yesu oa kuom joma otho odak e iu , to en mane ochiero Kristo oa kuom joma otho nomi ringreu matho bedo mangima bende , nikech Roho modak e iu .
Emomiyo owetewa , wan jogowi , to ok jogop dwaro mar dhano , mondo watim gik ma ngima mar dhano dwaro ,
nikech kutimo gi ma ngima mar dhano dwaro to ubiro tho . To ka unego timbeu maricho kuom teko mar Roho , to unubed mangima .
Ji duto ma Roho mar Nyasaye otelonigi gin nyithind Nyasaye .
To Roho ma useyudo ok loku wasumbini mondo uchak ubed maluor . Ooyo , Rohono lokowa nyithind Nyasaye , omiyo ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomwa ywak ni Nyasaye , ka luonge ni , “ Baba ! Wuora ! ”
Roho owuon oriwore gi chunywa kanyisowa ni wan nyithind Nyasaye .
To ka wan nyithind Nyasaye kamano , to wayudo mich ma osesingorenwa bende . Adier , wayudo michgo kaachiel gi Kristo ! Chutho , ka wayie neno masira kode , to wanayud duong’ kode bende .
To aneno ni masira mwaneno ndalogi tin , kipimo gi duong’ mapok oel mwabiro yudo .
Gik moko duto mochue rito kogeno ahinya mondo Nyasaye omi nyithinde ofwenyre .
Nyasaye nomiyo gik moko duto mochue obedo kayiem nono , ok nikech dwarogi giwegi , to nikech dwarone owuon . To ne nitie geno ni
chieng’ moro nogony gik moko duto mochue , mondo kik gibed gik matow , to giyud thuolo maduong’ ma nyithind Nyasaye nigo .
Wang’eyo ni nyaka chil kawuono gik mochue duto chur , kendo neno rem mana ka dhako ma muoch kayo .
Ok mago kende , to wan bende wachur e iwa wawegi , ka warito mondo Nyasaye olokwa nyithinde , komiyowa thuolo chutho . Wachur kamano kata obedo ni Nyasaye osemiyowa Roho kaka mich mokwongo mar gueth ma wabiro yudo achien .
Adier genono ema ne oreswago . Ka waseyudo gima wageno yudo , to koro ok wanyal wacho ni wan gi geno , nikech ere kaka ng’ato nyalo geno yudo gima oseyudo ?
To ka wageno yudo gima pok waneno , to rit ma waritegono nyiso ni wan jokinda .
Mano e kaka Roho bende konyowa e nyawowa , nikech ok wang’eyo kaka owinjore walem . To Roho owuon kwayonwa Nyasaye , kachur gi chur ma weche dhano ok nyal wacho ,
kendo Nyasaye ma nono chuny dhano ong’eyo gima Roho kwayo , nikech okwayo ni jo-Nyasaye e yo ma Nyasaye oyiego .
Wang’eyo ni Nyasaye omiyo gik moko duto tiyo kaachiel mondo joma ohere oyud gueth . Jogo gin joma oseluongo kaka odwaro .
Gin e joma noyiero chon , mi oketo obedo gi kido machal gi kit Wuode , mondo Wuode obed wuowi maduong’ e kind owetene mang’eny .
Joma ne Nyasaye oyierogo ema noluongo , kendo joma noluongogo nomiyo obet e winjruok kode , bende joma osemiyo obet e winjruok kodego ema opogonigi duong’ne maler .
To koro dwawach ang’o kuom wechego duto ? Ka Nyasaye ni kodwa , to ere gima dwaluor , kata ka ng’ato obedo jasikwa ?
Nyasaye ne ok otimo migundia kuom Wuode owuon , to ne ochiwe mi otho nikech wan duto . To kane ochiwo Wuode kamano , to ere kaka dotamre miyowa gik moko duto mogundho ?
Ng’ano ma didonj ni joma Nyasaye oseyiero , ka Nyasaye ema osemiyo gibet e winjruok kode ?
Koso ere ng’ama ding’adnwa bura , ka Kristo Yesu ema ne othonwa ? To ok tho ema nothonwa kende , to bende ne ochier , mi obet e bat korachwich mar Nyasaye , kendo en ema okwayonwa !
Ang’o ma dipogwa gi hera ma Kristo oherowago ? Dobed masira , koso chandruok , koso sand , koso kech , koso duk , koso himruok , koso tho ?
Adier , mago timorenwa mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Inegowa seche duto nikech in , kendo wachalo mana gi rombe midwaro yang’o . ”
To kata kamano , waloyo gigo duto chutho , nikech teko mar Jal mane oherowa ,
nimar ang’eyo malong’o ni onge gima nyalo pogowa gi hera ma oherowago , bed ni en tho kata ngima , kata malaika kata joloch mag polo ,
kata gik manie wiwa malo kata gik manie bwowa piny , kata gimoro amora manadi mochue . Adier , onge gima nyalo pogowa gi hera mar Nyasaye , moherowago kuom Kristo Yesu Ruodhwa .
Kaka an ja-Kristo , gima koro adwaro wacho en adier chutho . Ang’eyo e chunya ni ok ariambi ,
kendo Roho Maler bende nyisa ni awacho adier . An gi kuyo maduong’ , kendo chunya lit pile nikech wach jowetena ma jo-Israel , ma gin joogandana kuom anywola .
Dayie mondo an awuon Nyasaye okweda , mi gola kuom Kristo , kapo ni mano dikonygi .
Jo-Israel gin joma Nyasaye oseyiero mondo obed nyithinde . Ne onyisogi duong’ne maler , kendo ne otimo kodgi singruok madongo . Nomiyogi Chik Musa kendo nonyisogi kaka onego gilame e Hekalu . Bende nosingorenigi ni obiro guedhogi .
Gin e nyikwa kwerewa madongo machon , kendo korka anywola , to Mesia ne oa e ogandagi . Opak Nyasaye Moloyo Gik Moko Duto nyaka chieng’ ! Amin .
To kik ugal ni gima Nyasaye nosingore ok osechopo , nikech jo-Israel duto ok gin joma Nyasaye oseyiero .
To bende nyikwa Ibrahim duto ok gin nyithind Nyasaye , nimar Nyasaye nowacho ni Ibrahim niya , “ Joka Isaka kende ema noluong ni nyikwai . ”
Mano nyiso ni nyithindo duto mane Ibrahim onywolo ok gin nyithind Nyasaye , to mana mago monywol kaluwore gi singruok mar Nyasaye ema ikwano ka nyithind Nyasaye adier ,
nikech mano e gima Nyasaye nosingore niya , “ Ka kinde ochopo kare , to anaduogi , kendo nanwang’ ka Sara osenywolo nyathi mawuowi . ”
To ok mano kende . Kwarwa Isaka nonywolo nyithindo ariyo gi Rebeka chiege .
To kane pok onywolgi , tiende ni kane pok gitimo gimoro maber kata marach ,
Mano bende e kaka Muma wacho ni , “ Ne ahero Jakobo , Esau to ne asin-go . ”
To koro dwawach ang’o ? Dwawach ni Nyasaye ok ni kare koso ? Ooyo ! Ok nyal bet kamano ,
nikech Nyasaye nowacho ni Musa niya , “ Anakech jogo ma adwaro kecho , kendo anabed mang’won ni joma adwaro bedonigi mang’won . ”
Emomiyo ok en wach gima ng’ato dwaro kata gima ng’ato timo momiyo Nyasaye yiere , to en mana wach ng’wono mar Nyasaye owuon .
Nyasaye wacho ni Farao e Muma niya , “ Ne aketi ruoth mana ni mondo gima atimoni omi ji ong’e kaka tekona duong’ , kendo mondo humba olandre e piny ngima . ”
Kuom mano waneno ni ka Nyasaye dwaro timo ni ng’ato ng’wono , to otimo atima . Bende ka odwaro ni mondo omi chuny ng’ato odok matek , to otimo atima kamano .
To ang’eyo ni ng’ato kuomu biro penja niya , “ Ka onge ng’ama nyalo geng’o gima Nyasaye dwaro kamano , to ere gima omiyo Nyasaye pod dhaw gi ji ? ”
To an adwoke ni , in dhano adhanani , in ng’a , ma dipenj Nyasaye wach ?
Donge jachuech nigi teko mar timo atima gima ohero gi lowo ? Koso donge lowo achiel onyalo chueyogo agulni ariyo , ma achiel itiyogo tich mogen , to machielo itiyogo tich aticha ?
To mano bende e gima Nyasaye osetimo . Kata obedo ni ne odwaro nyiso ji mirimbe , mondo ging’e tekone , to ne ohore mos gi ng’wono maduong’ , mi ok otieko joma okechogo mane owinjore otieki .
To bende notimo kamano mondo omigo ji ong’e duong’ne kaka lich . En duong’ ma omiyo joma otimonigi ng’wono , ma gin joma ne oseloso chon mondo oyud duong’ kamano .
Jogo e wan , ma moko Nyasaye oluongo kuom jo-Yahudi , to moko oseluongo kuom joma ok jo-Yahudi bende .
Mano oluwore gi gima Nyasaye owacho e kitap Hosea niya , “ Ji mane ok joga , analuong ni joga . Adier , oganda mane ok ahero , analuong ni joma ahero ,
kendo kama ne okwergie chon ni , ‘ Ok un joga , ’ e kama noluonggie ni , nyithind Nyasaye Mangima . ”
Isaya bende nowuoyo kuom jo-Israel kama : “ Kata ka jo-Israel ng’eny mana ka kuoyo manie dhonam , to ji manok kuomgi kende ema nokwo ,
nikech Ruoth Nyasaye nong’ad bura e piny piyopiyo , mana kaka nowacho ni notim . ”
Mano oluore gi gima Isaya nosewacho chon niya , “ Ka dine Ruoth Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto ok oweyonwa joma chungo wiwa , to dine warumo mana ka Sodom gi Gomora . ”
Koro wanawach ang’o ? Onego wawach ni joma ok jo-Yahudi , mane ok otemo mondo obed e winjruok gi Nyasaye , ema koro osebet e winjruok kode kuom yie ,
to jo-Israel , mane temo dwaro yor Chik ma dimi gibed e winjruok gi Nyasaye , ne ok oyudo chik ma kamano .
To ang’o ma omiyo ne ok ginyal yude ? Ne ok ginyal yude nikech ne ok gitemo mondo gibed e winjruok gi Nyasaye kuom yie , to mana kuom gik ma gitimo . Ne gichwanyore e kidi machwanyo ji .
En kidi ma Muma wuoyo kuome niya , “ Winjuru ! Aketo kidi mabiro chwanyo ji e dala Sayun . En lwanda ma nomi gipodhi . To ng’at moyie kuom Jal ma kidino ochung’ kare , to ok noywag ang’e . ”
Owetena , alamo Nyasaye matek mondo jo-Israel okwo , nikech mano ema chunya dwaro ahinya .
Ayie ni giketo chunygi kuom tiyo ni Nyasaye , to gikia yo ma onego gitinego ,
nikech pok ging’eyo yo ma Nyasaye miyogo ji bet e winjruok kode , to gise mana temo loso yorgi giwegi . Kamano ne ok giyie luwo yo ma Nyasaye miyogo ji bet e winjruok kode .
To koro Kristo osemiyo Chik obedo maonge gi tich , komiyo ji duto moyie kuome , bet e winjruok gi Nyasaye .
Gima ne Musa ondiko kuom wach bedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye kuom mako Chik wacho kama : “ Ng’at ma omako Chik , Chik nomi obed mangima . ”
To kuom wach bedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye kuom yie , to owachoe niya , “ Kik ipenjri e chunyi ni , ‘ Ng’ano ma didhi malo e polo ? ’ ” tiende ni , ng’ano ma didhi kwa Kristo obi e piny ?
“ Kata kik ipenjri ni , ‘ Ng’ano ma dilor mwalo e Piny Joma Otho ? ’ ” tiende ni , ng’ano ma digol Kristo a kuom joma otho ?
Ooyo Muma wacho kama : “ Wach Nyasaye chiegni kodi ; en mana e dhogi kendo e chunyi . ” En e wach mar yie mwalando niya ,
Ka iwacho gi dhogi e lela ni Yesu e Ruoth , kendo iyie e chunyi ni Nyasaye ne ochiere oa kuom joma otho , to noresi .
En kamano nikech ng’ato nyaka yie gi chunye mondo obed e winjruok gi Nyasaye , kendo nyaka owuo e lela gi dhoge mondo orese .
Muma wacho niya , “ Ng’at moyie kuome ok noywag ang’e . ”
Mano oriwo ji duto nikech onge pogruok e kind jo-Yahudi gi joma ok jo-Yahudi , to giduto gin gi Ruoth achiel man gi mwandu mang’eny mopogo ni ji duto malame .
Muma wacho ni , “ Ng’ato ka ng’ato malamo Ruoth noresi . ”
To ere kaka ji nyalo lame , ka ok giyie kuome ? Koso ere kaka digiyie kuom Jal ma pok giwinjo wachne ? Koso digiwinj ni entie nadi , ka ng’at malandonigi wach onge ?
Koso ere kaka ji nyalo lando Wach Maber ka ok oorgi ? En mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Mano kaka ji mor ka gineno joma kelo nigi Wach Maber ! ”
To ok en ni ji duto ne oyie Wach Maberno , to obet mana kaka Isaya wacho niya , “ Ruoth , ere ng’ama oseyie wach mwalando ? ”
Kuom mano yie a kuom winjo . To gima iwinjo en Wach Maber mawuoyo kuom Kristo .
To koro apenjo niya , “ Bende nyalo bet ni jo-Israel ne ok owinjo Wach ? ” Ooyo ! Ne gisewinjo , mana kaka Muma wacho ni , “ Dwond joland wach osewinji e piny duto . Adier , wechegi osetundo e tung’ piny gi tung’ piny . ”
Apenjo kendo niya , “ Bende nyalo bet ni jo-Israel ne ok owinjo tiend wach ? ” To akwongo adwoko penjono kanyisou gima ne Musa owacho ni , “ Anami nyiego maku kod joma ok oromo luong ni oganda . Adier , anami mirima maku kod oganda ma onge rieko . ”
To Isaya wuoyo gi chir niya , “ Joma ne ok manya ema ne onwang’a . Adier , afwenyora ni joma ne ok penja . ”
Kuom jo-Israel to owuoyoe niya , “ Odiechieng’ duto narieyo bada , ka ahombo oganda ma wigi tek kendo ma piem koda , mondo oduog ira . ”
To bende apenjo niya , “ Nyasaye osewito joge koso ? ” Ooyo ! Ok nyal bet kamano , nikech an awuon an ja-Israel ma nyakwar Ibrahim , kendo ma jadhood Benjamin .
Nyasaye ok osewito joge mane ong’eyo chon ! Koso ukia gima Muma wacho kuom Elija ? Donge owacho ni Elija noywagore ni Nyasaye kuom gima jo-Israel no timo , kowacho niya ,
“ Ruoth , gisenego jonabi magi , kendo gisemuko kendeni mag misango . An kenda ema adong’ to kata an bende gidwaro nega . ”
To Nyasaye nodwoke niya , “ An gi ji alufu abiriyo ma pok ogoyo chonggi piny mondo olam Baal . ”
Kamano ndalogi bende nitie joma odong’ ma Nyasaye oyiero kuom ng’wonone .
Oseyierogi kuom ng’wono to ok kuom gik ma gisetimo , nimar ka da bed ni oseyierogi kuom gik ma gisetimo , to ng’wono ok dobedo ng’wono adier .
To koro nadi ? Waneno ni gima jo-Israel osebedo ka dwaro , pok giyudo , to joma nok kuomgi mane oyier ema oseyude . Jomoko duto to ne omi chunygi odoko matek mondo kik winj gima Nyasaye dwaro ,
mana kaka Muma wacho ni , “ Nyasaye osemiyogi chuny ma nindo otero . Kamano wang’gi ok nen , kendo itgi ok winj wach , nyaka chil kawuono . ”
Daudi bende nowacho niya , “ Sewni maggi mondo obed obadho kod amoso , kamiyo gipodho kendo ikumogi .
Wang’gi mondo oimre kik ginen , kendo chandruok obembgi abemba nyaka chieng’ . ”
To koro apenjo niya , “ Kane jo-Yahudi ochwanyore , ne gipodho mi gilal chuth koso ? ” Ooyo , ok kamano . Ketho mane jo-Yahudi okethogo nomiyo warruok obiro ni joma ok jo-Yahudi , mondo omi jo-Yahudi obed gi nyiego kodgi .
To ka ketho mag jo-Yahudi nokelo mwandu ni piny , kendo ka lal margi nokelo mwandu ni joma ok jo-Yahudi , to mano kaka dwokogi ir Nyasaye chuth dikel mwandu miwuoro !
To koro adwaro wuoyo kodu un joma ok jo-Yahudi . Kaka oseketa jaote ni joma ok jo-Yahudi , akwano tijano ka gima duong’ ahinya ,
katemo matek mondo ami jo-Yahudi wetena obed gi nyiego kodu , mondo ami moko kuomgi okwo .
Kane Nyasaye owitogi , to mano e yo mane okelogo winjruok e kinde kod ji . To ka mano en adier , to donge ung’eyo ni korwakogi kendo , to mano nobed mana ka chier a kuom joma otho ?
Ka makati mokwong tedo ochiw ni Nyasaye , to mano miyo makati duto bet maler , kendo ka tiend yath ler , to mano nyiso ni bedene duto ler .
En adier ni Nyasaye oserwakou un joma ok jo-Yahudi , mi ubedo joge , kendo uyudo gueth kaachiel gi jo-Yahudi . To rwakuno chalo mana gi bede yadh zeituni mong’ad oko , eka ochom bad yadh zeituni ma thim kargi , ma koro yudo chiembe koa e tiend yath kaachiel gi bede mamoko .
To kik upakru ni miti uloyo bede mamokogo ! To paruru ni un ok uting’o tiend yath , to tiend yath ema oting’ou .
Kamoro ubiro wacho niya , “ Bede moko nong’ad oko mondo ochomwa kargi . ” Ee , mano en adier ,
to ne ong’adgi oko nikech ne ok giyie , to un koro usiko asika kuom yath nikech uyie . To mano kik mi usungru , to beduru gi luoro e nyim Nyasaye .
Ka jo-Yahudi , machalo bede yath hie ema ne Nyasaye ok okecho , un to dokechu nadi ?
Neuru ni Nyasaye ng’won kendo ger . Oger ni joma oselal , to ong’won ni un , to mana kusiko kuyie ng’wonone . Ka ok utimo kamano to un bende ibiro ng’adou oko .
To bende ka jo-Yahudi ok osiko kotamore yie , to nochak ochomgi e yath , nikech Nyasaye nigi teko mar chomogi kendo .
Un joma ok jo-Yahudi uchalo bad yath mane ong’ad oko kuom zeituni mae thim , mi ochom e yadh zeituni mopidhi . Jo-Yahudi to chalo gi bede yath hie , omiyo mano kaka chako chomogi kendo e yadhgi giwegi yot !
Owetena , wach moro mopondo nitie e wachni ma adwaro mondo ung’e , nikech dipo ka uparo ni uriek . Wachno chalo kama : Bath jo-Israel konchiel chunygi osedoko matek , to mano biro dhi nyime nyaka kar romb joma ok jo-Yahudi ma Nyasaye dwaro , yud warruok .
Mano e kaka jo-Israel duto nokwo , mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Jawar nobi koa Sayun . Enogol richo duto mag nyikwa Jakobo
Mano e singruok ma anatim kodgi ka agolo richogi . ”
Kane ilando ni jo-Yahudi Injili , to ne gidoko wasik Nyasaye , to mano nokelonu konyruok , un joma ok jo-Yahudi . To kata kamano Nyasaye noseyierogi , kendo pod oherogi , nikech oparo kweregi .
Ka Nyasaye oyiero ng’ato kendo oguedho , to ok olok parone kuom ng’atno .
Un joma ok jo-Yahudi , chon ne utamoru winjo wach Nyasaye , to koro useyudo ng’wono mar Nyasaye nikech jo-Yahudi otamore winjo wach .
Kamano koro jo-Yahudi otamore winjo wach nikech gineno ni useyudo ng’wono , to mano otimore mana ni mondo koro gin bende giyud ng’wono .
Nyasaye nomiyo ji duto obedo joma otamore winjo wach kamano mondo ong’wonnigi giduto .
Mano kaka mwandu mag Nyasaye dongo ! Riekone kod ng’eyone tut manadi ! Ere ng’ama nyalo ng’eyo tiend gik moparo ? Koso ere ng’ama nyalo ng’eyo yorene ?
En mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Ere ng’ama oseng’eyo paro mar Ruoth Nyasaye , kata ere ng’ama osebet jang’adne rieko ?
Koso ere ng’ama osemiye gimoro , ma dimi obed gi gope ? ”
En ema ne ochueyo gik moko duto , kendo ema omiyo gisiko gintie , bende en ema omiyogi gima omiyo gintie . Duong’ obedne nyaka chieng’ ! Amin .
Emomiyo owetena , asayou kuom ng’wono mar Nyasaye mondo uchiw ringreu obed misango mangima kendo maler ma Nyasaye nyalo yiego , nikech mano e yo maradier mar lemo monego uluw .
Kik uluw timbe mag pinyni , to lokreuru mondo parou odok manyien , eka ubiro ng’eyo gik ma Nyasaye dwaro . Gin gik mabeyo kendo malong’o ma Nyasaye oyiego .
Kaka Nyasaye osemiya mich kuom ng’wonone , anyisou ni ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu kik ketre e duong’ moongego , to mondo opar maber maromre gi yie ma Nyasaye osepogone .
Ringruok achiel nigi fuonde gi leche mang’eny ma moro ka moro nigi tichne owuon .
Kamano e kaka wan bende wang’eny , to wabedo ringruok achiel kuom Kristo , kendo waduto wan fuonde mamoko .
Wan gi mich mopogore opogore , kaka mich mane Nyasaye omiyowa kuom ng’wonone obet . Ka mich momi ng’ato en mar hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye , to mondo ohul wach maromre gi yie mopogne .
To ka michne en mar tiyo ni ji , to oket chunye e tijno . To ka ng’ato en japuonj , to mondo opuonj ji ,
kendo ka tich ng’ato en jiwo ji , to mondo otim kamano . Ka en jachiwo to mondo ochiw mabup . Ng’at momi mich mar bedo jatelo bende mondo otel ni ji katimo kinda . To ng’at makonyo ji mondo otim kamano gi mor .
Herau mondo obed maonge miganga . Beduru mosin gi gik maricho , to sikuru kuom gik mabeyo .
Herreuru kaka owete onego herre , ka ng’ato ka ng’ato miyo owadgi duong’ moloyo en owuon .
Timuru kinda maonge samuoyo , kendo keturu chunyu kuom tiyo matek ni Ruoth .
Geno ma un-go mondo omi ubed mamor . Kisandou , to timuru sinani , kendo lemuru mak uweyo .
Poguru giu ni jo-Nyasaye modhier , kendo beduru joma ohero rwako welo .
Kwauru Nyasaye mondo oguedh joma sandou . Ee , kwayeuru mondo oguedhgi aguedha , to kik okuong’gi .
Beduru mamor gi joma mor , kendo ywaguru gi joma ywak .
Beduru joma winjore , kendo kik ubed joma sungore , to beduru e achiel gi ji duto . Kik ukawru ni uriek .
Ka ng’ato otimonu marach , to kik uchulne kuor , to keturu chunyu kuom timo gik ma ji duto oyiego ni beyo .
Temuru mondo kanyalore , to udag gi ji duto gi kue .
Osiepena , kik uchul kuor , to kar chulo kuor to weuru mondo mirimb Nyasaye ema otim kamano , nikech ondiki e Muma ni Ruoth Nyasaye owacho niya , “ An ema nachul kuor . Adier , anachul maonge kiawa ! ”
Muma wacho bende niya , “ Ka jasiki odenyo , to miye chiemo , kendo ka riyo oloye to miye pi omodhi , nikech kitimo kamano , to inege gi wichkuot . ”
Kik uwe richo lou , to timuru gik mabeyo mondo ulogo richo .
Ng’ato ka ng’ato nyaka winj wach joma nigi teko mar loch , nimar teko duto wuok mana kuom Nyasaye , kendo joma nigi tekogo , Nyasaye ema oketo .
Omiyo ng’ama tamore winjo wach joma nie loch to tamore winjo mana gima Nyasaye ema oketo . Ng’ato ang’ata matimo kamano nokel kum kuome owuon ,
nikech joma nie loch ok nyal bwogo joma timo maber , to mak mana joma timo marach ema gibwogo . Donge idwaro ni mondo joma nigi loch kik bwogi ? Kara tim atima gik mabeyo , eka joma nigi loch nopaki ,
nikech gin jotich Nyasaye matiyo mondo okonyi . To ka itimo marach to gin jotich Nyasaye matoyo mirimb Nyasaye kuom joketho .
Mano emomiyo nyaka iluor joma nigi loch , ok nikech mirimb Nyasaye kende , to nikech kata e chunyi iwuon ing’eyo ni mano en gima kare .
Mano bende ema omiyo onego ugol osuru , nikech ka joma nigi loch tiyo tichgi to gitiyo ni Nyasaye .
Miuru ng’ato ka ng’ato gima onego umiye , bed ni en osuru , kata luor , kata duong . ’ .
Kik ubed gi gop ng’ato , to gowi kende ma unyalo bedogo en mana hera ma onego uhergo jowadu . Ng’at mosehero wadgi to osechopo Chik Musa duto .
Chikego e magi : Kik iterri , kik ineki , kik ikwal , kendo kik igombi . Chikego kaachiel gi chike mamoko duto , oriw e wach achiel niya , “ Her wadu kaka iherori iwuon . ”
Ka ihero wadu , to ok inyal timone marach . Mano emomiyo hera chopo chik duto .
To timuru kamano nikech ung’eyo ni kinde koro osechopo ma uchiewie ua e nindo , nikech chieng’ mibiro resowae koro chiegni moloyo ndalo mane wachakoe yie kuom Yesu .
Otieno chiegni rumo , kendo dwaro ru . Emomiyo waweuru timbe mag mudho , to wamanreuru gi gilweny mag ler .
Ngimawa mondo obed mobidhore , kaka joma wuotho e ler odiechieng’ . Waweuru dwanyruok gi mer gi terruok gi anjawo gi dhaw kod nyiego .
To rwakreuru gi Yesu Kristo kaka okumbau , kendo weuru keto chunyu kuom paro gik ma ringruok gombo .
Kata ka ng’ato nigi yie mayomyom , to rwakeuru arwaka ma ok uchande gi weche ma pod en-go kiawa .
Jomoko nigi yie motegno mamiyogi thuolo mar chamo gimoro amora ma gihero , to joma onge gi yie motegno to chamo mana alot kende .
Joma chamo kit chiemo duto kik cha joma ok tim kamano . To bende joma chamo mana alot kende kik ng’ad bura ni joma chamo kit chiemo duto , nikech Nyasaye oserwakogi .
In to in ng’a , ma diwach ni jatich ng’ato timo marach ? Kata ka ochung’ motegno , kata opodho , to obadho mana ruodhe ! To Ruoth nigi teko mar miyo ochung’ motegno !
Jomoko paro ni odiechieng’ moro duong’ moloyo odiechienge mamoko , to jomoko paro ni odiechienge duto romre . Kuom weche ma kamago , ng’ato ka ng’ato nyaka bed gi ratiro e chunye kuom gik ma okwano ni kare .
Joma paro ni odiechieng’ moro duong’ ahinya , timo kamano kamiyogo Ruoth duong’ . Joma chamo kit chiemo duto timo kamano kamiyogo Ruoth duong’ , nimar gigoyo ni Ruoth erokamano ; kendo joma kuero kit chiemo moko bende timo kamano kamiyogo Ruoth duong’ , nikech gin bende gigoyo erokamano ni Nyasaye .
Onge ng’ato kuomwa ma ngimane en mare owuon , kata ma thone en mare owuon ,
nikech ka wangima to wangima ni Ruoth , kendo ka watho to watho ni Ruoth . Emomiyo kata ka wangima kata ka watho , to wan mag Ruoth ,
nikech Kristo notho kendo ochier modoko mangima mondo obed Ruodh joma otho gi joma ngima .
Koro in to , ere gima omiyo ing’ado ni owadu bura ? Koso in , ere gima omiyo ichayo owadu ? Donge ung’eyo ni wan duto wabiro chung’ e nyim kom bura mar Nyasaye ?
Mana kaka ondiki e Muma niya , “ An Ruoth Nyasaye mangima , akuong’ora niya , ‘ Ji duto nogona chonggi piny , kendo ng’ato ka ng’ato nohul ni an e Nyasaye . ’ . ”
Omiyo ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomwa nowach mana wach man kuome owuon ni Nyasaye .
Kuom mano mondo waweuru ng’ado ni jowadwa bura . To keturu chunyu mondo une ni ok utimo gimoro manyalo miyo owadu podhi , kata ma dimi otim richo .
Ang’eyo maber chutho kaka ja-Kristo , ni onge chiemo moro ma inyalo luongo ni kuero . To ka ng’ato paro ni gimoro en gima kuero , to gino bedone mana kuero .
Ka gimoro ma in ichamo chwanyo owadu , to mano nyiso ni iseweyo wuotho e hera . Omiyo kik iwe chiemo ma ichamo keth ng’at ma Kristo nothone !
Bed kitang’ mondo gima ineno ni ber kik mi jomoko kinde mar wuoyo marach ,
nikech Loch Nyasaye ok en wach mar chiemo kata mar madho gimoro , to en mana wach tim makare gi kue kod mor ma Roho Maler kelo .
Omiyo ng’at matiyo ni Kristo e yo ma kamano ema bedo malong’o ni Nyasaye , kendo ema ji bende oyiego .
Emomiyo wadwaruru matek weche makelo kue kod weche ma ng’ato ka ng’ato dikonygo owadgi .
Kik iketh tich Nyasaye mana nikech wach chiemo . En adier ni onge chiemo moro makuero , to kichamo gimoro mamiyo ng’ato podho , to iketho .
Ber mondo iwe chamo ring’o kata madho kong’o kata timo gimoro amora manyalo miyo owadu podhi .
Paro ma in-go korka gik miyiego to bedgo mana e chunyi gi Nyasaye kende . Ng’at maonge gi kiawa moro e chunye , kotimo gima ong’eyo ni kare en jahawi !
To ng’at ma chiemo ka riwo gi kiawa , to bura oloyo , nikech gima otimo ok otim kong’eyo ni kare . Gimoro amora ma ng’ato otimo ka onge gi ratiro ni en gima kare , to en richo .
Wan joma nigi yie motegno onego wakony jogo man gi yie mayomyom , ma ok watimo mana gima wan wawegi ema wahero .
Ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomwa mondo otim gima ber kendo malong’o ni owadgi mondo okonye bet gi yie motegno .
Nyaka watim kamano nikech Kristo bende ne ok otimo mana gima en owuon ema ohero , to en mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Ayany mane ji yanyigo ema koro iyanyago . ”
Adier , weche mane ondiki chon e Muma nondiki mondo opuonjwa , kendo mondo Muma omiwa kinda kendo ohowa , mi wabed gi geno .
To Nyasaye ma wuon kinda gi hoch mondo omi ubed gi winjruok achiel kaka Yesu Kristo dwaro ,
mondo umi Nyasaye , Wuon Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo , duong’ , gi chuny achiel kod dwol achiel .
Rwakuru joweteu mana kaka Kristo bende oserakou , mondo Nyasaye oyud duong’ .
Awachonu ni Kristo nodoko jatich jo-Yahudi mondo onyis ji ni Nyasaye en jaadiera , tiende ni mondo omi gima ne Nyasaye osingore ni kwerewa otimre ,
kendo mondo joma ok jo-Yahudi opak Nyasaye nikech ng’wonone . Mano e kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Emomiyo anapaki e kind joma ok jo-Yahudi . Adier , anapak nyingi gi wer . ”
To bende owacho niya , “ Un joma ok jo-Yahudi , moruru kaachiel gi joge moyiero . ”
Owacho kendo niya , “ Un ji duto ma ok jo-Yahudi pakuru Ruoth . Ee , ogendini duto mondo opake ! ”
Isaya bende wacho niya , “ Nyakwar Jesse nobi . En ema nowuogi mondo obed ruodh joma ok jo-Yahudi , kendo en ema joma ok jo-Yahudi nogen kuome . ”
Nyasaye ma wuon geno opong’u gi mor duto kod kue nikech uyie kuome , mondo geno maru omedre mogundho kuom teko mar Roho Maler .
Owetena , an awuon ang’eyo chutho ni un joma beyo kendo mariek ahinya , bende ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu nyalo ng’ado ni wadgi rieko .
Kata kamano asendikonu gi chir e baruani ka aparonugo weche moko . Asetimo kamano nikech mich mane Nyasaye omiya kuom ng’wonone ,
mondo abed jatich Kristo Yesu , kendo mondo ati tich dolo ni joma ok jo-Yahudi . Tijano en lando Wach Maber mar Nyasaye mondo joma ok jo-Yahudi obed misango malong’o ni Nyasaye , ma Roho Maler osepwodho .
Kaka an ng’at man kuom Kristo , amor gi tich ma atiyo ni Nyasaye .
An ok dawuo kuom gimoro ma an asetimo , to dawuo mana kuom gik mane Kristo osemiyo atimo mondo joma ok jo-Yahudi oluor Nyasaye .
Notimonigi gi weche kod timbe , kendo gi teko manenore kuom ranyisi gi honni , ma en teko mar Roho . Kamano asetieko lando Wach Maber mar Kristo koni gi koni , chakre Jerusalem nyaka Iliriko .
Gima asedwaro moloyo gik moko duto en ni mondo aland Wach Maber kuonde ma nying Kristo pok ong’eree , mondo kik aged ewi mise mar ng’at machielo ,
mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Joma ne pok onyis wachne nonene , kendo joma ne pok owinjo wachne , nong’e tiende . ”
Mano emomiyo kuom ndalo mathoth ok asebedo gi thuolo mar biro iru .
To koro asetieko tija kuondegi , kendo kaka asegombo biro iru kuom higni mang’eny ,
koro adwaro ni mondo atim kamano . Abiro nenou ka akadho adhi Spania , kendo ka asebedo kodu moromo to ukonya e wuodhano .
Sani to koro adhi Jerusalem ka atero mich ni jo-Nyasaye man kuno ,
nikech kanyakla mag jo-Kristo man Makedonia gi Akaya noneno ni ber mondo gigol chiwo okony jo-Nyasaye modhier man Jerusalem .
Ne gineno ni ber mondo gitim kamano , to chutho gin jogop jogo , nikech kaka joma ok jo-Yahudi oseyudo gueth mag chuny kuom jo-Yahudi , omiyo owinjore gin bende gikony jo-Yahudi gi gik ma gichando mag pinyni .
Ka asetieko tijni , kendo amiyogi pesa duto ma osechoknigi , eka anabi iru ka adhi Spania .
Ang’eyo ni ka abiro iru to anabi gi gueth mogundho mar Kristo .
To asayou owetena , kuom Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo , kendo kuom hera mar Roho , mondo ukonya nywako tich lemo matek , kukwayona Nyasaye
mondo oresa kuom jo-Judea motamore yie , kendo mondo jo-Nyasaye man Jerusalem oyie gi tich ma atiyonigi .
Kamano ka Nyasaye oyie to anabi iru gi mor , kendo ayue kodu .
Nyasach kue mondo obed kodu uduto . Amin .
Apwoyonu nyaminwa Fibi . En jatich e kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Kenkrea .
Rwakeuru e nying Ruoth kaka jo-Nyasaye owinjore tim , kendo konyeuru e wach moro amora modwaro , nikech osekonyo ji mathoth , kaachiel gi an awuon bende .
Mosnauru Priska gi Akula ma jotich wetena kuom Kristo Yesu .
Ne gichiwo ngimagi nikech an ! Agoyonigi erokamano , to ok an kenda , to kanyakla duto mag jo-Kristo ma ok jo-Yahudi bende goyonigi erokamano .
Mosnauru kanyakla mar jo-Kristo ma lemo e odgi . Bende mosnauru Epaineto osiepna , ma en ng’at mane okwongo yie kuom Kristo e piny Asia .
Mosnauru Maria mosebedo katiyonu matek ahinya ,
kendo mosnauru bende Androniko kod Junias . Gin jo-Yahudi wetena , mane otwewago . Gin joma ogen kuom joote , bende ne gikwongona bedo jo-Kristo .
Mosnauru Ampliato osiepna kuom Ruoth ,
kendo mosnauru Urbano ma jatich wadwa kuom Kristo , kod Stefano osiepna .
Mosnauru Apele , ng’at mosetem moyud ni ja-Kristo maradier . Jood Aristobulo bende mosnauru .
Mosnauru Herodian , ma ja-Yahudi wadwa , kaachiel gi jo-Kristo ma jood Narkiso .
Mosnauru Turfena gi Trufosa , ma jotiyo tich Ruoth matek . Bende mosnauru Persi osiepna mosetiyo tich Ruoth gi chunye duto .
Rufus , jatich matek mar Kristo , bende mosnauru , kaachiel gi min mare , mosebet ka rita ka nyathine .
Mosnauru Asunkrito gi Flegon gi Herme gi Patroba gi Hermas kod owete man kodgi .
Mosnauru bende Filologo gi Julia gi Nereas kod nyamin mare , gi Olumpa kod jo-Nyasaye duto man kodgi .
Yogreuru gi mos mar jo-Nyasaye . Kanyakla duto mag joma oyie kuom Kristo omosou .
Akwayou owetena ni beduru motang’ gi joma kelo pogruok kendo miyo ji lal , ka gitamore luwo puonj mane uyudo . Ayeuru kuom joma kamago ,
nikech ok gin jotich Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo , to gitiyo mana ni gombogi giwegi . Giwuondo joma kia gi weche mamit kendo malombo ji .
Ji duto osewinjo ni umako Wach Maber ; mano emomiyo amor kodu . Adwaro ni mondo udok joma riek korka timo gima ber , to ubed joma ofuwo korka timo gima rach .
Piyopiyo nono Nyasach kue biro miyo unyon Satan gi tiendu . Ng’wono mar Ruodhwa Yesu obed kodu .
Timotheo jatich wadwa , kaachiel gi Lukio gi Jason kod Sosipatro ma jo-Yahudi wetena , jomosou .
( An Tertio , mandiko baruani , bende amosou kuom Ruoth . )
Gayo , ma an wendone , kendo ma bende jarwak jo-Kristo duto man ka e ode , omosou . Erasto ma jakeno mar dala , kod owadwa Kwarto , jomosou . [
Ng’wono mar Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo obed kodu un duto . ]
Opak Nyasaye manyalo miyo ubed gi yie motegno , kaluwore gi Wach Maber mar Yesu Kristo ma alando . Wach Maber en wach mane opondo nyaka nene .
To koro Nyasaye mochwere osechiko ni mondo oele e lela mondo ogendini duto oyie kuome kendo omak chikne , mana kaka jonabi nondiko e Muma .
Duong’ obed ni Nyasaye kuom Yesu Kristo nyaka chieng’ . En e kende ema oriek . Amen .
An Paulo , mane Nyasaye oyiero kendo oluongo mondo obed jaote Kristo Yesu , ema andiko baruani kaachiel gi owadwa Sosthene .
Wa dikonu un kanayakla mar joma oyie kuom Nyasaye man Korintho , ma un joma osewal ni Kristo Yesu , mi oluong mondo obed jo-Nyasaye kaachiel gi ji duto kuonde duto maluongo nying Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo , ma Ruodhgi kendo Ruodhwa .
Ng’wono gi kue moa kuom Nyasaye Wuonwa kod Ruoth Yesu Kristo obed kodu .
Pile agoyo ni Nyasacha erokamano nikech ng’wono mane omiyou kuom Kristo Yesu .
Bende agoyone erokamano nikech usedoko momew e yore duto kuom Kristo . Ung’eyo wuoyo maber , kendo un gi rieko duto ,
nikech usenwang’o e ngimau ni weche mane wanyisou kuom Kristo gin adier .
Omiyo onge mich moro mar chuny ma oremou kapod urito mondo Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo ofwenyore .
Bende enomi ubed motegno nyaka giko , mondo kik ubed gi bura chieng’ ma Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo biroe .
Nyasaye mane oluongou mondo ubed e achiel gi wuode Yesu Kristo Ruodhwa en jaadiera .
Owetena , asayou e nying Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo ni beduru gi winjruok uduto kuom gima uwacho , mondo kik ubed gi pogruok e kindu , to uriwru chutho kuom paro achiel kod dwaro achiel .
Akwayou kamano owetena , nikech jood Kloe moko osenyisa wachu ,
tiende ni ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu wacho mana wachne owuon . Achiel wacho ni , “ An ng’at Paulo , ” moro to wacho ni , “ An ng’at Apolo , ” kendo machielo wacho ni , “ An ng’at Petro , ” to moro bende wacho ni , “ An ng’at Kristo . ”
To Kristo dipogre tienge tienge adier ? Koso uparo ni Paulo ema ne othonu e msalaba ? Koso ne obatisu e nying Paulo ?
Agoyo erokamano ni Nyasaye ni ne ok abatiso ng’ato kuomu mak mana Krispo gi Gayo .
Omiyo onge ng’ama nyalo wacho ni ne obatisu e nyinga !
( Ee , ne abatiso Stefano bende , kaachiel gi joode , to ok apar ni ne abatiso ng’at machielo kendo . )
Yesu ne ok oora mondo abatis ji , to noora mondo aland Injili , kawuoyo gi weche maliw mondo kik tiend tho mar Yesu e msalaba go ji obindi .
Wach msalaba en mana fuwo ni joma lal , to en teko mar Nyasaye ni wan joma ireso ,
mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Anaketh rieko mar joma riek , kendo anami ng’eyo mar joma ong’eyo bed kayiem nono . ”
Koro ere ng’at mariek ? Ere japuonj Chik ? Koso ere jatwak mariek mar pinyni ? Donge Nyasaye osenyiso ji ni rieko mar pinyni en mana fuwo koso ?
To Nyasaye nochano gi riekone ni dhano ok nyal ng’eye gi riekone owuon , nikech ne odwaro ni mondo fuwo mar wach mwalando ema mondo obed yo ma owarogo joma oyie .
Jo-Yahudi to dwaro neno honni kaka ranyisi , kendo jo-Grik manyo rieko .
Wan to walando wach Kristo mane ogur e msalaba . En wach ma chwanyo chuny jo-Yahudi , to joma ok jo-Yahudi to kwane ka wach mofuwo .
To joma Nyasaye oseluongo , bed ni gin jo-Yahudi kata joma ok jo-Yahudi , to ong’eyo ni wachno en Kristo , ma en teko Nyasaye kendo riekone ,
nikech fup Nyasaye riek moloyo rieko mar dhano , kendo nyawo mar Nyasaye tek moloyo teko dhano .
Koro owetena ma Nyasaye oseluongo , parieuru kaka uchal . Ka unyalo paro kaka dhano paro , to ubiro yudo ni joma nok kuomu kende ema riek , kendo joma nok ema omew , bende joma tin kuomu kende ema wuok e miech ruodhi .
To Nyasaye noyiero gik ma piny kwano ka gik mofuwo mana kong’eyo , mondo okuodgo wi joma riek , kendo noyiero gik ma piny neno ni nyap mondo okuodgo wi joma rateke .
Bende noyiero gik ma piny obwono kendo ochayo kendo ma ok kwan ka gimoro mondo okethgo gik ma piny kwano ka gik madongo .
Notimo kamano mondo ng’ato kik sungre e nyime .
Osekelou e achiel gi Kristo Yesu , kendo osemiyo Kristo obedo riekowa . Kuom Kristo bende ema Nyasaye osemiyo wabet e winjruok kode , kendo osemiyo wabedo joge kendo wayudo warruok .
Mano emomiyo , “ Ng’at madwaro sungore to mondo osungre mana nikech gik ma Ruoth osetimo , ” mana kaka Muma wacho .
Kuom mano owetena , kane abiro iru mondo aland wach mopondo mar Nyasaye , to ne ok awuoyo gi weche mamit kata gi rieko matut ,
nimar ne aketo chunya mondo ka an kodu to kik apar gimoro amora mak mana Yesu Kristo , to moloyo wach thone e msalaba .
Kane abiro iru , to ne anyap , kendo luoro nomiyo denda duto otetni ,
bende kane alando wach to ne ok akonyora gi weche mariek maywayo ji , to teko mar Roho ema ne onyisou ni wach ma alando en adier ,
mondo yie maru kik tenre kuom rieko mar dhano to otenre mana kuom teko mar Nyasaye .
To kata kamano nitie rieko ma wapuonjogo joma yiegi otegno , to ok en rieko mar pinyni , kata mar jotend pinyni , nikech gin to lochgi osechako rumo .
To rieko ma wapuonjo en rieko mopondo mar Nyasaye mapok ofwenyre . En rieko mopand ni ji , mane Nyasaye osechanonwa chon kane pok ochue piny , mondo wayud duong’ .
Onge kata achiel kuom jotend pinyni mane ong’eyo riekono , nikech ka dine bed ni ging’eye , to dine ok giguro Ruodh duong’ e msalaba .
To riekono koro osefwenyore , mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Gik ma wang’ pok oneno , kendo ma it pok owinjo , bende mapok odonjo e chuny dhano , e gik ma Nyasaye oiko ni joma ohere . ”
To wan ema ne Nyasaye onyisowa wachne mopondo , kuom teko mar Roho , nikech Roho ofwenyo ni ji gik moko duto , kata mana weche matut mag Nyasaye .
Onge ng’ato manyalo ng’eyo paro manie chuny ng’ato machielo , to maka mana chuny ng’ato ema ong’eyo parone owuon . Kamano bende e kaka Roho mar Nyasaye kende ema ong’eyo paro mar Nyasaye .
To ne ok wayudo Roho moa kuom Nyasaye , mondo wang’e mich duto ma Nyasaye osemiyowa kuom ng’wonone .
Koro kwawuoyo kuom gigo , to ok wakonyre gi weche mag rieko ma dhano puonjo , to wakonyore mana gi weche ma Roho puonjo , kwanyiso joma nigi Roho weche mag chuny .
To ng’at maonge gi Roho ok nyal yie weche ma Roho mar Nyasaye nyise . Adier , ok onyal winjo tiendgi maber , nikech ginenore ka gik mofuwo , nimar inyalo nonogi mana gi teko mar Roho .
To ng’at man gi Roho nyalo nono gik moko duto , to en owuon onge ng’ama nyalo nono chunye .
Mano e gima Muma bende wacho ni , “ Ere ng’ama ong’eyo paro mar Ruoth , ma dimi ong’ad ni Ruoth rieko ? ” Wan to wan gi paro mar Kristo !
Kamano owetena , ne ok anyal wuoyo kodu kaka awuoyo gi joma nigi Roho . To ne nyaka awuo kodu ka gima un joma onge gi Roho , kendo mapod yom kuom Kristo .
Ne apidhou mana gi chak , to ok gi chiemo matek , nikech ne pok utegno . To kata mana kawuono , pod ok unyal chame ,
nimar pod uchalo joma onge gi Roho , nikech kapod nitie nyiego e chunyu , kendo udhaw e kindu uwegi , to adier mano nyiso ni pod uchalo gi joma onge gi Roho , kendo utimo mana timbe mag dhano .
Ka jomoko kuomu wacho ni , “ Wan jo-Paulo ” , to moko ni , “ Wan jo Apolo ” , to mano donge nyiso ni utimo mana timbe mag dhano koso ?
Un uparo ni Apolo en ng’a ? Koso Paulo to ng’a ? Donge wan mana jotich Nyasaye mane omiyo uyie kuom Kristo ? Ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomwa tiyo tich mane Ruoth omiye mondo oti .
An ne apidho kodhi , to Apolo ema ne oolo pi , to chutho Nyasaye ema ne omiyo odongo .
Kamano ng’at ma opidho yath , kata ng’at moolo pi ok kwan ni osetimo gimoro , to mak mana Nyasaye momiyo yadhno odongo ema otimo gimoro .
Onge pogruok manie e kind jal ma pidho gi jal maolo pi , to Nyasaye nomi ng’ato ka ng’ato pok mana kaka tichne owuon obet .
Waduto wan jotich Nyasaye ; un to un puoth Nyasaye , kendo un ot ma Nyasaye gero .
Kuom mich mar Nyasaye mane omiya kuom ng’wonone , ne aketo mise ka jagedo molony , kendo koro ng’at machielo gedo kuom miseno . To ng’ato ka ng’ato nyaka non maber kaka ogedo kuom miseno .
Onge mise moro nono ma ng’ato nyalo keto mak mana mise ma oseketi , ma en Yesu Kristo .
Ng’ato nyalo gedo kuom miseno gi dhahabu , kata gi fedha , kata gi kite ma nengogi tek , kata gi yien , kata gi lum , kata gi odundu ,
to tich ng’ato ka ng’ato nong’ere malong’o mana Chieng’ Giko . Chieng’no nobi gi mach , kendo mach notem tich mane ng’ato ka ng’ato otiyo .
Ka gima ne ng’ato ogero kuom miseno osiro mach , to enoyud pok ,
to ka tich ng’ato owang’ , to ok noyud pokne , to en owuon norese , to mana ka ng’ama osekadho e mach .
Donge ung’eyo ni un e Hekalu mar Nyasaye , kendo ni Roho mar Nyasaye odak e iu ?
To ka ng’ato oketho Hekalu mar Nyasaye , to Nyasaye nokethe , nimar Hekalu mar Nyasaye ler ; to un e Hekalu nogo !
Kik ng’ato wuondre owuon ! Ka ng’ato kuomu galo ni en ng’at mariek , kaka pinyni okwano rieko , to onego obed mofuwo , eka mondo obed mariek adier ,
nikech rieko mar pinyni en mana fuwo e wang’ Nyasaye . Nitie wach moro e Muma mawuoyo kuom Nyasaye kama : “ En ema omako jorieko gi riekogi giwegi . ”
To moro bende wacho niya , “ Ruoth ong’eyo ni paro jorieko gin nono . ”
Omiyo ng’ato kik pakre nikech dhano , nimar gik moko duto gin mau .
Adier , bed ni en Paulo , kata en Apolo , kata en Petro , kata en pinyni , kata en ngima , kata en tho , kata gin gik matimore ndalogi , kata gik mabiro , to duto gin mau !
Un to un mag Kristo ; Kristo to en mar Nyasaye .
Nyaka ukwanwa ka jotich Kristo , ma osemi tich rito weche mopondo mag Nyasaye .
To gima dwarore kuom jorit en ni nyaka gibed joadiera .
To an ok adew kata ka uyala , kata ka iyala e bura moro amora . To bende kata an awuon ok anyal yalora kenda .
Chutho ok ane gimoro maketho , to mano ok onyiso ni aonge gi ketho . To ng’at ma yala en Ruoth .
Omiyo kik ung’ad ni ng’ato bura ka kinde moketi pok ochopo , to rituru biro mar Ruoth , nikech en ema nogol e lela weche mopandi e mudho , kendo noel paro mag chuny dhano . Eka Nyasaye nomi ng’ato ka ng’ato pak mowinjorego .
Owetena , aketo wechegi duto kuoma , kendo kuom Apolo , kaka ranyisi ni mondo upuonjrugo tiend ngero ma wacho ni , “ Kik ukadh weche mondiki e Muma . ” Ng’ato kuomu kik sungre kachwako ng’at achiel to kwedo ng’at machielo .
Ang’o momiyo iparo ni iduong’ moloyo jomoko ? Koso ang’o ma iparo ni in-go mane Nyasaye ok ema omiyi ? Koro ere gima omiyo isungori ka gima gik ma in-go ok omiyi amiya ?
Nenore ni uparo ni useyudo gik moko duto mudwaro , kendo usedoko joma omew ! Usebedo ruodhi , to wan uweyowa oko ! Mad ubed ruodhi adier , mondo wan bende wabed ruodhi kodu !
To nenore ni Nyasaye oseketowa wan joote , ka joma odong’ chien mogik ni ji duto , kendo ka joma ong’adnigi buch tho , nikech oseketwa ka gima piny duto rango . To ok mana ji kende ema rangowa , to koda ka malaika bende !
Neuru kaka wan joma ofuwo nikech Kristo , to un , un joma riek kuom Kristo ! Wan joma nyap , to un utek . Un omiu duong’ ahinya , to wan ochawa !
Nyaka chop koroni kech kayowa , kendo riyo oloyowa . Wan duge , bende igoyowa , kendo waonge kar dak .
Watiyo matek gi lwetwa wawegi . Ka oyanywa to waguedho joma yanyowa , kendo ka isandowa , to wadhil adhila .
Bende ka ijarowa , to wadoko mamuol . Adier , nyaka chop chil kawuono , wan ji mikwano ka nono , kendo wan mana yugi mag piny !
Ok andik wechegi ni mondo akuodgo wiu , to andikogi mana ni mondo ang’adnugo rieko , kaka nyithinda ma ahero .
Kata da bed ni un gi jopuonj gana gi gana kuom Kristo , to un mana gi wuoro achiel kende , nikech kuom Yesu Kristo , an ema ne adoko wuonu , kapuonjou Injili .
Omiyo akwayou gi ng’wono ni mondo uluw mana timna .
Mano emomiyo aoronu Timotheo . En wuoda kuom Ruoth . Ahere kendo en jaadiera . Obiro paronu chike ma aluwo e ngimana kuom Kristo Yesu , kendo ma apuonjo kuonde duto , e kanyakla duto mag jo-Kristo .
Jomoko kuomu sungore kaparo ni ok nabi iru .
To abiro biro iru piyo , ka Ruoth oyie , eka anang’e an awuon teko ma joma sungorego nigo , to ka ok mana gima giwacho ,
nikech Loch Nyasaye ok obedo kuom wach , to obedo kuom teko .
Koro ere gima udwaro ? Udwaro ni abinu gi luth , koso abinu gi hera kod chuny mamuol ?
Wachore malong’o ni wach terruok nie kindu , kendo en kit terruok ma ok nwang’ kata mana e kind joma ok oyie kuom Nyasaye , nikech ng’ato terore gi chi wuon !
To eka pod usungoru asunga ! Ere gima omiyo ok useywak , mondo ng’at ma osetimo gima kamano ogol oko kuomu ?
An to , kata obedo ni ok an kodu kuno gi ringra , to chunya ni kodu , kendo aseng’ado bura ni ng’ama osetimo gima rach kamano , mana ka gima an kodu .
Chokreuru e nying Ruodhwa Yesu , ka chunya bende ni kodu ,
mondo kuom teko mar Ruodhwa Yesu wachiwuru ng’atno e lwet Satan , mondo ringre otieki , to ores chunye chieng’ Ruoth .
Sunga musungorugo ok ber ! Donge ung’eyo ngero mawacho ni , “ Thowi matin kuodo mogo duto modwal ” ?
Pukuru thowi machon mar richono mondo ubed maler chutho , eka unubed ka mogo modwal manyien , maonge thowi . To adier , kamano e kaka uchalo . To bende Kristo , ma en nyarombowa mar Pasaka , osetimnwago misango .
Emomiyo koro watimuru sawo mana gi makati ma ok ketie thowi , tiende ni makati mar chuny ler kod adiera , to ok makati moketie thowi machon mar himruok kod richo .
Ne anyisou e barupa ni kik ubedi e kanyakla mar joma terore .
To ne ok akwerou mondo kik uriwru gi joma terore ma ok oyie kuom Nyasaye , kata jogombo , kata jomecho , kata joma lamo nyiseche manono , nikech ka udwaro pogoru gi joma kamago , to kara dichunu ni mondo ua e pinyni chuth !
Ooyo , nakwerou mana ni kik uriwru kod ng’at muluongo ni owadu ka en ng’at ma terore , kata jagombo , kata ng’ama lamo nyiseche manono , kata mayanyo ji , kata jamer , kata jamecho . Ng’at ma kamano , kata mana chiemo kik uchiemgo .
Ok en tichna mondo ang’ad bura ni joma oko , to Nyasaye ema nong’adnigi bura . Donge un onego ung’ad bura mana ni joma nie kanyaklau ?
Ka ng’ato kuomu nigi wach moro kod owadgi , to ere kaka dodhi mana e buch joma ok oyie kuom Kristo , kar dhiyo e nyim jo-Nyasaye ?
Donge ung’eyo ni jo-Nyasaye ema biro yalo piny ? To ka un ema ubiro yalo piny kamano , to koro ere gima dimonu yalo weche matindo ?
Ok ung’eyo ni wanayal malaika koso ? To ka kamano , donge dwayal weche mag pinyni moloyo ?
To ka un gi buche ma kamago , to marang’o uterogi e nyim joma jo-Nyasaye ok kwan ka gimoro , mondo oyal bucheu ?
Awuoyonu kamano mondo akuodgo wiu ! Bende en adier ni onge kata ng’at achiel mariek kuomu manyalo ng’ado bura e kind ng’ato gi owadgi ,
momiyo ja-Kristo donjo ni ja-Kristo wadgi mana e nyim buch joma ok oyie kuom Kristoni ?
Buche ma un-go e kindu nyiso ni userem ! Marang’o ok uyie mondo otimnu marach ? Koso marang’o ok uyie mondo omau amaya ?
Kar timo kamano to un uwegi ema utimo marach , kendo un ema umecho , to eka utimo kamano mana ni oweteu !
Donge ung’eyo ni joketho ok noyud gueth mar Loch Nyasaye ? Kik uwuondru , to nyaka ung’e ni jochode kata joma lamo nyiseche manono , kata joma terore , kata chwo materore gi chwo wetegi ,
To kamano e kaka moko kuomu ne chalo ! To koro osepwodhu kuom richo , kendo owalu ubed jo-Nyasaye , bende osemi ubet e winjruok gi Nyasaye e nying Ruoth Yesu Kristo , kendo kuom teko mar Roho mar Nyasachwa .
Ng’ato nyalo wacho ni , “ Anyalo timo gimoro amora ma ahero . ” Ee , mano nyalo bedo adier , to kik igal ni gik moko duto mitimo gin gik mowinjore . Adier , anyalo wacho ni , “ Anyalo timo gimoro amora mahero ” , to ok anyal yie mondo gimoro amora oloka misumbane .
Ng’at machielo bende nyalo wacho ni , “ Chiemo en mar ich , kendo ich en mar chiemo . ” Ee , to Nyasaye notiek gik moko ariyogo duto . To ringruok ok ochue ni terruok , to en mar Ruoth , kendo Ruoth en mar ringruok .
Nyasaye nochiero Ruoth , kendo wan bende obiro chierowa gi tekone .
Donge ung’eyo ni ringreu gin fuond Kristo ? Koro dakaw fuond Kristo mondo alok fuond dhako ma jachode adier ? Ooyo , mano ok nyalre !
Koso ok ung’eyo ni ng’ama oriwore gi dhako ma jachode doko ringruok achiel kode ? Muma wacho niya , “ Ji ariyogo doko ringruok achiel . ”
To ng’ama oriwore gi Ruoth to doko chuny achiel kode .
Beduru mabor gi terruok . Richo moko duto ma ng’ato timo ok keth ringre . Ng’ama terore to ketho ringre owuon .
Koso ok ung’eyo ni ringreu en Hekalu mar Roho Maler modak e iu , mane Nyasaye omiyou ? Un ok un mau uwegi , to un mag Nyasaye .
Ne oseng’iewou , mochulo nengou , omiyo miyeuru duong’ gi ringreu .
To koro adwaro dwokou kuom weche mane undiko . Nupenja ka en gima ber mondo ng’ama dichwo kik bed gi dhako .
To adwokou kama : Kaka tem mar terruok ng’eny ahinya , ber mondo ng’ato obed gi chiege owuon , kendo dhako bende obed gi chwore owuon .
Dichwo nyaka tim ni chiege gik moko duto kaka owinjore otimne , kendo dhako bende nyaka tim ni chwore kamano .
Dhako ok oloyo ringre owuon , to mak mana chwore ema oloyo . Kamano , dichwo bende ok oloyo ringre owuon , to mak mana chiege ema oloyo .
Kik utuonru gima owinjore , mak mana ka uwinjoru e kindu uwegi kuom kinde matin mondo uyud thuolo mar lemo . Eka bang’e uchak ubed kaachiel , nono to Satan otemou nikech ok unyal ritoru .
Awachonu kamano mana ka aketonu parona to ok amiu chik .
To agombo ni ji duto da obedo kaka an , to kata kamano ng’ato ka ng’ato nigi michne owuon moa kuom Nyasaye , achiel e yorni , kendo moro e yo machielo .
To awacho ni joma ok okendo gi joma ok okendi kod mond liete ni ber ka gibet abeta ka an .
To ka ok ginyal ritore , to ber mondo gikendi kata okendgi , nikech kend ber moloyo owruok gi gombo .
To agolo chik kuom joma okendo gi joma okendi , to gima awacho ok en chikna awuon , to en chik Ruoth mawacho ni , “ Dhako ok onego owe chwore ,
kendo dichwo bende ok onego riemb chiege . ” To ka dhako oweyo chwore to onego osik mak okende , kata mondo odog ni chwore .
To kuom jomoko duto modong’ , to Ruoth ok wuoye , to an ema awuoyoe kama : Ka owadwa moro nigi dhako , ma ok oyie kuom Kristo , kendo dhakono oyie dak kode , to kik oriembe .
Kamano bende , ka dhako moyie kuom Kristo nigi dichwo ma ok oyie , to dichwogno oyie dak kode , to kik dhakono weye .
Mano en kamano nikech dichwo ma ok oyie owal ni Nyasaye nikech chiege ma oyieno , kendo dhako ma ok oyie kuom Kristo bende owal ni Nyasaye nikech chwore moyieno . Ka da ni ok kamano , to nyithindu da ok obedo mag Nyasaye .
To ka jal ma ok oyie ema dwaro pogore gi jaode , to jaode mondo oweye aweya oa . Wach ma kamano ok otueyo owadwa kata nyaminwa . To Nyasaye oseluongou , un joma oyie , mondo udag e kue .
In dhako moyie , ing’eyo nadi kata dires chwori ? Koso in dichwo moyie , ing’eyo nadi kata dires chiegi ?
Ber mondo ng’ato oti gi mich mane Nyasaye opogone , kendo obed mana kaka ne en kane Nyasaye oluonge . Mano e gima apuonjo e kanyakla duto mar jo-Kristo .
Kapo ni Nyasaye noluongo ng’ato kosetere nyangu , to kik odwar mondo obed ka ng’at ma ok oter nyangu . Kamano bende ng’at mane oluongi ka ok oter nyangu kik dwar mondo otere nyangu ,
nikech koda oter ng’ato nyangu , koda ok oter , to mano chalre , to gima duong’ en mana rito chik Nyasaye .
Ng’ato ka ng’ato onego obed mana kaka ne en kane Nyasaye oluonge .
Ne in misumba kane Nyasaye oluongi koso ? Mano kik chandi , to kinyalo yudo kinde mar bedo thuolo , to ber mondo itim kamano .
Ng’ama Ruoth oluongo ka misumba en ng’at Ruoth , ma osemiyo thuolo . Kamano bende e kaka ng’at ma Kristo ka ni thuolo en misumba Kristo .
Nyasaye nong’iewou mochulo nengou , omiyo kik ubed wasumb ji .
Owetena , ng’ato ka ng’ato onego bed gi Nyasaye mana kaka ne en kane Nyasaye oluonge .
To kuom joma ok okendo gi joma ok okendi to awachoe kama : Aonge gi chik ma Ruoth omiya mondo aketnigi , to anyisou mana parona kaka ng’ama ng’wono mar Ruoth osetimo ng’ama ogen .
Aparo ni kaka chandruok nitie e kindeni , ber mondo ng’ato osik kaka en .
In gi dhako koso ? Ka kamano , to kik uweru kode . To ka ionge gi dhako , to kik idwar mondo ibedgo .
To kata kamano , ka ikendo to ok iketho , kendo nyako bende ka okendi , to ok oketho . To joma kamago none masira e pinyni , kendo daher resou kuom mano .
Owetena , awachonu kamano nikech ndalo modong’ nok , omiyo chakre kawuono , joma nigi mon mondo obed ka joma ongego ,
kendo joma ywak mondo obed ka joma ok ywagi . Joma nigi mor bende obed ka joma ok nigi mor , kendo joma ng’iewo gik moko mondo obed ka joma ok gin weg ma giseng’iewogo .
Bende joma konyore gi mwandu mag piny mondo obed ka joma ok konyrego , nikech pinyni kadho , kaachiel gi gige duto .
Adwaro ni mondo ubed maonge gi parruok . Ng’at ma ok okendo osiko paro mana wach Ruoth , kaka dobed malong’o ni Ruoth .
Ng’at mokendo to paro mana wach piny , kaka dobed malong’o ni chiege ,
omiyo parone opogore ariyo . Nyako ma ok okendi paro mana wach Ruoth . Odwaro ni mondo obed ng’at Ruoth gi ringre kod chunye bende . Dhako mokendi to paro mana weche piny , nimar odwaro bedo malong’o ni chwore .
Awachonu wechegi nimar adwaro konyou . Ok atem ketonu chik matek , to adwaro mana ni mondo utim gik mabeyo kendo mowinjore , kutiyo ni Ruoth gi chunyu achiel ma ok uparo gima chielo .
Kapo ni ng’ato oneno ni otimo marach ni nyako mowinjorego ni odwaro kendo , nikech ok onyal ritore , to ber mondo okend nyakono . Ok oketho kotimo kamano .
To ka oketo chunye motegno , maonge gima ochune , to otimo maber moloyo ka ok okendo nyakono .
Emomiyo ng’ama okendo nyako mane giwinjorego otimo maber , to ng’ama ok okendo nyako mane giwinjorego otimo gima ber moloyo .
Chik otueyo dhako ndalo duto ma chwore pod ngima , to ka chwore osetho , to en gi thuolo mondo ng’ama ohero okende . To ng’ama okendono nyaka bed ja-Kristo .
To aparo ni dobed gi mor moloyo kosiko mak okende . Mano e parona , kendo aparo ni an bende an gi Roho mar Nyasaye .
Koro adwaro wuoyonu kuom chiemo motimgo misango ni nyiseche manono . Uwacho niya , “ Wang’eyo ni wan duto wan gi rieko . ” To rieko ma kamano kelo sunga , to hera to emamiyo ji dongo .
Ka ng’ato paro ni ong’eyo gimoro , to mano nyiso ni pok ong’eyo gimoro kaka onego ong’e .
To ka ng’ato ohero Nyasaye to mano nyiso ni Nyasaye ong’eye .
To koro korka wach chamo chiemo motimgo misango ni nyiseche manono , wang’eyo ni , “ nyasaye manono en ranyisi mar gimoro ma onge chuth ” , kendo ni , “ nitie mana Nyasaye achiel kende ” , mana kaka uwacho .
To kata ka nitie gik miluongo ni nyiseche e polo kata e piny , kendo kata obedo ni nyiseche ma kamago kod ruodhi ng’eny ,
wan to wan mana gi Nyasaye achiel , ma en Wuoro , kendo ma gik moko duto a kuome . Wantie mana ni mondo watine . Bende nitie Ruoth achiel kende , ma omiyo gik moko duto nitie , koda ka wan bende .
To ji duto ok ong’ieyo wachno , nikech jomoko ngimagi ong’yo gi nyiseche manono kendo kata mana sani gichamo chiemogo ka giparo ni adier otimgo misango ni nyiseche manonogo , kendo kaka chunygi nyap , giparo ni chiemogo osemiyo gidonjo e richo .
To chiemo ok nyal miyo Nyasaye yie kodwa . Kata ka ok wachiemo , to onge gima wawito , to bende kata ka wachiemo , to onge ohala ma wayudo .
To ritreuru mondo gik mutimo kik mi joma chunygi nyap donji e richo .
Ka ng’at ma chunye nyap oneni , in ma in gi rieko , kibet ichiemo e hekalu mar nyasaye manono , donge dimi obed gi chir , mi ocham chiemo motimgo misango ni nyiseche manono ?
Kamano riekoni miyo wadu ma chunye nyap , mane Kristo othone , lal chuth .
To kutimo richo kamano ni oweteu , kendo uketho chunygi , to utimo richo mana ni Kristo !
Omiyo ka wach chiemo ema miyo owadwa donjo e richo , to kara ok nachak acham ring’o mondo kik ami owadwa lal .
Donge an ng’at man thuolo ? Koso donge an jaote mar Kristo ? Donge aseneno Yesu Ruodhwa ? Koso ok un e ranyisi mar tich ma atiyo ni Ruoth ?
Kata ka jomoko ok kwana ka jaote , un to ung’eyo malong’o ni an jaote adier , nikech un e ranyisi mar otena kuom Ruoth .
Joma ok oyie koda to adwoko kama :
Donge wan gi ratiro mar yudo chiemo kod gik ma wamadho ?
Koso donge wan gi ratiro mar wuotho gi mondewa ma jo-Kristo , kaka joote mamoko gi omine Ruoth kod Petro jotimo ?
Koso wan gi Barnaba kende ema nyaka wati mondo wayud gik ma wakonyorego ?
Ere jalweny ma dikonyre gi pesane owuon , to ok chule msara ? Koso en jakwath mane , ma ok madh chak monyiedho kuom jambe ?
Kamoro uparo ni ranyisi ma achiwogo gin mana paro mag dhano , to donge Muma bende wacho mana kamano ?
Ondiki e Chik Musa ni , “ Kik itue dho dhiang’ ka ywayo lodi madiemo cham . ” To uparo ni Nyasaye wuoyo kuom dhok adier ?
Donge wan ema owuoyo kuomwa ? Adier , Chikno nondiki mana nikech wan , nimar jachwoyo kod jakeyo tiyo tijegi mana ka gigeno yudo pokgi mar cham .
Ka wan ema ne wachuoyo kodhi mag chuny , koro ere gima omiyo ubwok ka wanwang’o kuomu gik moko mag piny ma wakonyorego ?
Ka jomoko to nigi thuolo mar yudo gigo kuomu , koro wan donge wan gi thuolo moloyo ? Kata kamano ok wasekonyore gi thuolono , to wadhil gi chandruok duto , mondo kik watim gimoro ma dimon Wach Maber man kuom Kristo landre .
Donge ung’eyo ni joma tiyo tich Hekalu chamo gik mochiw e Hekalu , kendo ni joma tiyo e kendo-mar-misango bende nwang’o pokgi kuom gik motimgo misango ?
Kamano bende e kaka Ruoth osegolo chik ni mondo joma lando Injili oyud pokgi kuom lando Injili .
To an , kata obedo ni an gi ratiro mar yudo gik ma kamago , to ok asekonyora kodgi , to bende ok andik wechegi ni mondo ayudgi , nikech diber ka atho , moloyo ka ng’ato oloko gima asungoragoni odoko gima nono .
To chutho ok anyal sungora kuom lando Injili , nimar ochuna ni nyaka aland Injili , kendo dane malit ahinya ka ok alando Injili .
Ka dabed ni atiyo tijni kuom dwarona awuon , to da ayudo pok . To kaka ok atiye gi dwarona awuon , mano nyiso ni en mana tich ma Nyasaye osemiya mondo ati .
To koro pokna en ang’o ? En mor mar lando Injili ka ok chula gimoro . Tiende ni , ratiro ma an-go mar yudo pok kuom lando Injili , ok akonyrago .
Kata obedo ni ok an misumba ng’ato , to asetimora misumba ji duto , mondo alok ji mang’eny kkaka nyalore oyie kuom Kristo .
Ka an e kind jo-Yahudi , to aluwo tim jo-Yahudi , mondo alok jo-Yahudi . Tiende ni kata obedo ni an , Chik Musa ok omaka , to ka atiyo e kind joma nie bwo Chik , to atimora ka gima Chik omaka , mondo alokgi .
Kamano bende ka an e kind joma ok jo-Yahudi , to atimora ka ng’ama ok ja-Yahudi ma Chik jo-Yahudi ok omako , mondo alok joma ok jo-Yahudi . To mano ok onyiso ni ok arito chik Nyasaye , nikech chutho an e bwo chik Kristo .
Ne adoko ng’ama chunye nyap e kind joma chunygi nyap , mana ka gima an achiel kuomgi , mondo alok joma chunygi nyap . Adier , ne alokora gik moko duto ni ji duto , mondo ares moko kuomgi e yo moro amora ma anyalo .
Mago atimo nikech Injili , mondo ayud pok miyudo kuom Injili .
Donge ung’eyo ni jong’uech duto ringo e pap , to achiel kende ema yudo pok ? Un bende ringuru mondo uyombi .
Bende ji duto madwaro piem e tugo , ritore kuom chike duto . Gin gitimo kamano mondo giyud osimbo makethore . Wan to waritore mondo wayud osimbo ma ok kethre .
Mano emomiyo aringo ka ang’eyo kuma achomo . Achalo jangum ma ok dir ngum adira kayiem .
Adier , asando ringra kendo amiyo owinjo wachna , mondo kik bed ni an ma asepuonjo jomoko , yud ka an awuon arem .
Owetena , adwaro ni mondo ung’e tiend gima notimore ni kwerewa : Bor polo notelo nigi giduto ka nie wigi malo , kendo giduto ne ging’ado Nam Makwar .
Bedo e bwo bor polono , kendo ng’ado nam kamano ema ne okwan ka batiso mane omiyo giduto gibedo e achiel gi Musa .
Giduto ne gichamo chiemo achiel mar chuny ,
kendo ne gimodho pi achiel mar chuny , nikech ne gimodho e lwanda mar chuny mane wuotho kodgi . Lwandano ne Kristo owuon .
To kata kamano , wang’eyo ni ji mathoth kuomgi ne ok long’o ni Nyasaye , nikech ringregi nodong’ koke kuonde duto e thim .
Gigo duto notimore mondo obednwa ranyisi ni mondo wan kik wagomb gik maricho kaka ne gigombo .
Kik ulam nyiseche manono , kaka moko kuomgi nolamo , kaka wasomo e Muma ni , “ Jo-Israel nobet piny mondo ocham kendo omadh gik ma otimgo misango , bang’e ne gia malo mondo gitug tugo maricho . ”
Wan kik watim timbe terruok , kaka moko kuomgi notimo , mi ji alufu piero ariyo gadek kuomgi otho chieng’ achiel .
Bende kik watem Ruoth , kaka jomoko kuomgi noteme , mi thuonde onego !
Kata kik ung’ur kaka jomoko kuomgi nong’ur , mi Malaika ma Janek onego .
Gigo duto notimorenigi kaka ranyisi , kendo ne ondikgi ni mondo watang’ , wan mwadak e ndalo ma piny rumoeni .
Emomiyo , ng’at ma paro ni ochung’ motegno mondo otang’ kik opodhi .
Onge tem ma useyudo mopogore gi tem ma ji duto yudo . Nyasaye en jaadiera , omiyo ok noyie mondo uyud tem mohingo tekreu , to nomiu yo ma uwuokgo e tem moro amora , kendo nomiu teko mar dhil gi tem go .
Kuom mano , owetena ma ahero , kik ulam nyiseche manono .
Akwayou kaka joma nigi rieko ni , par ane uru gima awacho .
Ka wamadho kikombe mar gueth , ma wagoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano kuome , to donge waduto wan e achiel kuom remb Kristo ?
Kaka nitie mana makati achiel kende , mano nyiso ni kata obedo ni wan ji mang’eny kamano , to wan mana ringruok achiel , nikech waduto wariwore e chamo makati achielno .
Paruru ane kit lemo mar jo-Yahudi kod timgi . Donge jogo machamo gik motimgo ni Nyasaye misango bedo e achiel gi Nyasaye motimne misangono ?
To ka awacho kamano , to uparo ni awacho ni chiemo motimgo misango ni nyasaye manono en chiemo mopogore gi chiemo mamoko koso ? Koso uparo ni awacho ni nyasaye manono en gima adier ?
Ooyo , awacho ni misango ma joma ok oyie kuom Nyasachwa ema otimo , gitimo ni jochiende , to ok ni Nyasaye . Ok adwar mondo ubedi e achiel gi jochiende !
Ok unyal madho kikombe mar Ruoth , kendo uchak umadh kikombe mar jochiende .
Wadwaro miyo Ruoth mirima koso ? Koso waparo ni watek moloye ?
Uwacho niya , “ Ng’ato nigi thuolo mar timo gimoro amora . ” Ee , mano adier , to kata kamano gik moko duto ok konywa . Ee , wan thuolo mar timo gimoro amora , to gik moko duto ok kelnwa dongruok .
Kik ng’ato dwar mana gik makonye en owuon to ng’ato ka ng’ato mondo odwar gik makonyo jomoko .
Chamuru ring’o duto ma ung’iewo e chiro , ma ok uchich gi weche moko e chunyu ,
nikech Muma wacho niya , “ Ruoth e wuon piny ngima , kaachiel gi gik moko duto manie iye . ”
Ka ng’ato ma ok oyie kuom Kristo oluongi e chiemo , kendo ihero dhi , to cham gimoro amora momiyi , mak chunyi ochich gi wach moro .
To ka ng’ato owachoni ni , chiemono otimgo misango ni nyasaye manono , to kik icham chiemono , nikech dipo ka ichwanyo chuny ng’at monyisino .
To winji , awacho mana chuny ng’at monyisino , to ok chunyi iwuon . To kamoro ibiro penja ni , “ Ere gima omiyo paro manie chuny ng’ato machielo ema mona timo gima aneno ni an gi thuolo mar timo ?
Ka agoyo erokamano kuom chiemo ma achamo , to marang’o ng’ato neno ni atimo marach kuom chamo chiemono ? ”
To adwoko penjono ni , ka uchiemo kata umetho kata utimo gimoro amora , to timuru kamano mana ni mondo omi Nyasaye duong’ .
Kik ubed joma kelo chwanyruok ni jo-Yahudi , kata ni joma ok jo-Yahudi kata ni kanyakla mar joma oyie kuom Nyasaye ,
to timuru mana kaka atimo . Atemo bedo malong’o ni ji duto e yore duto , ka ok apar mana gima dikonya , to aparo mana gima dikony ji duto , mondo oresgi .
Luwuru timna kaka an bende aluwo tim Kristo .
Apuoyou nikech upara pile , kendo nikech umako puonj mane amiyou matek .
To adwaro ni mondo ung’e ni wi dichwo ka dichwo en Kristo , kendo wi dhako en dichwo , to wi Kristo en Nyasaye .
Kuom mano dichwo malemo kata mahulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye , koumo wiye , ochayo Kristo , ma en wiye .
To bende dhako malemo kata mahulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye ka ok oumo wiye , to ochayo chwore , ma en wiye nimar ochalre gi dhako moliel wiye .
Ka dhako ok oumo wiye , to ber mondo ong’ad yie wiye . To ka ng’ado yie wich kata lielo wich kuodo wi dhako , to ber mondo oum wiye .
Dichwo to ok owinjore um wiye , nimar ne ochweye e kido mar Nyasaye , kendo en e ranyisi mar duong’ mar Nyasaye . Dhako to en ranyisi mar duong’ mar dichwo .
Dichwo ne ok oa kuom dhako , to dhako noa kuom dichwo .
Bende dichwo ne ok ochue ni dhako , to dhako ema nochue ni dichwo .
Mano emomiyo dhako onego um wiye kaka ranyisi ni en e bwo loch chwore , nikech malaika .
To kata kamano , kuom Ruoth , dhako ok gimoro ka dichwo onge , mana kaka dichwo bende ok en gimoro ka dhako onge ,
nimar kaka dhako noa kuom dichwo , e kaka dichwo bende koro dhako onywolo , to gik moko duto a kuom Nyasaye .
Paruru ane un uwegi . Bende en gima owinjore ka dhako lamo Nyasaye e nyim ji ka ok oumo wiye ?
Donge en gima ong’ere e piny ngima ni ka dichwo nigi yie wich maboyo , to mano kelone wichkuot ?
Dhako to ka nigi yie wich maboyo to mano kelone duong’ . Osemiye yie wich maboyo mondo odok raum wiye .
To ka ng’ato dwaro goyo mbaka kuom wachni , to gima dawachi en mana ni , wan waonge gi tim moro machielo mar lemo , to kata mana kanyakla mag joma oyie kuom Nyasaye bende ongego .
Kapod apuonjou wach lemo kama , to an gi wach moro monego akweru : Ka uchokoru to chokruoku ok kel ber , to kelo mana rach .
Mokuongo , awinjo ni kuchokoru e lemo to pogruok nie kindu , kendo aparo ni wachno en adier ,
nikech pogruok nyaka bed e kindu , mondo joma ogen ong’ere ratiro !
Ka uchokoru kaachiel , to gima uchamo ok en Sap Ruoth ,
nikech ng’ato ka ng’ato rikni mondo ocham chiembe owuon , omiyo jomoko denyo , ka jomoko to mer !
Donge un gi mier munyalo chiemoe ? Koso uchayo jo-Nyasaye , momiyo ukuodo wi joma odhier ? Uparo ni dawach ang’o kuom wachni ? Uparo ni dapaku ? Ooyo , ok dapaku !
Puonj mane ayudo kuom Ruoth , mi amiyou chal kama : Ruoth Yesu nokawo makati e otieno nogo mane ondhogee ,
mogoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano , eka ong’ingo makatino , kowacho niya , “ Ma e ringra , mochiw nikech un . Timuru kamano mondo uparago . ”
Kamano bende , bang’ chiemo , nokawo kikombe kowacho niya , “ Kikombeni e remba , motimgo Winjruok Manyien gi Nyasaye . E kinde ka kinde mumadhee , to timuru kamano mondo uparago . ”
Kamano e kinde ka kinde ma uchamoe makatino , kendo umetho e kikombeno , to tho Ruoth ema uhulo nyaka chop obi .
Emomiyo ka ng’ato chamo makati mar Ruoth , kata ometho e kikombene e yo ma ok owinjore , to en gi bura kuom ringre Ruoth kod remb Ruoth .
Kuom mano ng’ato nyaka nonre mondi , eka ocham makatino kendo omethi e kikombeno ,
nikech ng’at mochamo makatino kendo ometho e kikombeno ka ok odewo ni gin ringre Ruoth , to okelo bura kuome owuon , kuom chiemo kendo metho kamano .
Mano emomiyo joma ng’eny kuomu tuo kendo nigi midekre , kendo moko osetho .
Ka da wanonre wawegi mokwongo , to ok dwayud bura .
To ka Ruoth kumowa kamano , opuonjowa mondo kik wayud bura kaachiel gi jopinyni .
Emomiyo owetena , kuchokoru kaachiel mondo uchiem , to rituru joweteu .
To ka ng’ato odenyo , to ber mondo ochiem e dala , mondo chokruok kik kelnu bura . Weche modong’ to nanyisu ka abiro .
Koro owetena , adwaro ni mondo ubed ka ung’eyo adiera man kuom mich ma Roho chiwo .
Ung’eyo ni kane pok uyie kuom Kristo , ne iterou ir nyiseche manono mamomni , mi ulal .
Mano emomiyo adwaro nyisou mondo ung’e ni , onge ng’ama nigi Roho mar Nyasaye manyalo wacho ni , “ Okuong’ Yesu ” . To bende onge ng’ama nyalo wacho ni , “ Yesu en Ruoth ” mak mana ka en gi Roho Maler .
Nitie mich mag Roho mopogore opogore , to Roho achiel ema chiwogi .
Bende nitie tije mopogore opogore , to Ruoth achiel ema itiyone .
Nitie yore mopogore opogore ma teko Nyasaye tiyoe kuom ji , to Nyasaye achiel ema tiyo e yorego duto .
Ng’ato ka ng’ato yudo mich ma Roho chiwo e yo mopogore opogore mondo otigo tich maber .
Ng’at moro omi rieko mar wuoyo , kuom teko mar Roho . Machielo omi teko mar puonjo weche matut , kuom teko mar Roho nogono .
To Roho achielno miyo ng’at moro yie , to machielo to omiyo teko mar chango ji .
Bende ng’at moro Roho omiyo teko mar timo honni , to ng’at machielo to omiyo teko mar hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye , to eka moro to omiyo teko mar pogo mich moa kuom Roho kod mago ma ok oa kuom Roho . Ng’at machielo to omiyo teko mar dhumo dhok mayoreyore , eka moro to omiyo teko mar loko tiend weche midhumogo .
To mago duto gin mana tich mar Roho achiel . Opogo michgo ni ng’ato ka ng’ato kaka ohero .
Kristo en kaka ringruok achiel man gi fuonni mang’eny . To kata obedo ni en gi fuonni mang’eny kamano , to en mana ringruok achiel .
Kamano bende e kaka wan duto , bed ni wan jo-Yahudi kata joma ok jo-Yahudi , kata wasumbini kata joma ni thuolo , to osebatiswa e ringruok achiel kuom Roho achiel , kendo wan duto osemiwa Roho achielno mondo wamadhi .
Ringruok ok olos mana gi fuoni achiel kende , to olose gi fuonni mang’eny .
Kata ka da bed ni tielo nyalo wacho ni , “ Ok an lwedo , omiyo ok an mar ringruok ” , to pod en mana mar ringruok .
Bende kata da bed ni it nyalo wacho ni , “ Ok an wang’ , omiyo ok an mar ringruok ” , to pod en mana mar ringruok .
Ka da ringruok duto bed mana wang’ , to ere kaka dowinj wach ? Kata da bed mana it kende , ere kaka dong’ue gik moko ?
To Nyasaye noketo fuonni duto achiel ka achiel e ringruok mana kaka noneno ni ber .
To wang’eyo ni nitie fuonni mang’eny , to giloso mana ringruok achiel .
Kuom mano wang’ ok nyal wacho ni lwedo ni , “ Aonge kodi gi tich . ” Kamano wich bende ok nyal wacho ni tielo ni , “ Aonge kodi gi tich ” .
Ooyo , mano ok kamano , to fuonni manenore ni nyap , ema dwarore moloyo ,
kendo mago manenore ni onge gi duong’ ema wamiyo duong’ moloyo . Kamano fuondwa ma ok long’o wageng’o maber moloyo ,
to fuondwa manenore mabeyo to ok dwar geng’o kamano . Nyasaye oseloso ringruok kaachiel komiyo fuonni mochando duong’ bedo gi duong’ moloyo ,
mondo ringruok kik pogre , to fuonni duto obed ka konyore kaachiel .
Ka fuonni achiel lit , to fuoni duto lit , kendo ka fuonni achiel omi duong’ , to fuoni duto bedo mamor kaachiel kode .
Emomiyo un duto un ringre Kristo , kendo ng’ato ka ng’ato en fuonni mar ringruokno .
Nyasaye oseketo ji e kanisane ma en kanyakla mar jo-Kristo duto , kama : mokwongo joote , mar ariyo johul wach moa kuom Nyasaye , mar adek jopuonj , eka joma timo honni , bang’e joma omi teko mar chango ji , gi joma konyo ji , gi joma omi tich telo ni ji , kod madhumo dhok mayoreyore .
Uparo ni giduto gin joote koso ? Kata ni giduto gin johul wach ? Koso giduto gin jopuonj ? Giduto gin gi teko mar timo honni ?
Koso giduto gin gi teko mar chango ji ? Giduto gidhumo dhok mayoreyore ? Koso giduto giloko tiend weche midhumogo ?
Ooyo ! To kata kamano , mich madongo moloyo ema mondo uket chunyu uyudi . To nitie yo moro moloyo ma adwaro nyisou .
Kata dabed ni awuoyo gi dhok mag ji , kata mana gi dho malaika , to aonge gi hera , to achalo mana okot maywak , kata olang’ migoyo .
Kata da bed ni an gi mich mar hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye , kendo ang’eyo midhierni kod rieko duto , kendo kata da abed gi yie mogik ma anyalo gologo gode kuonde ma gintie , to aonge gi hera , to ok an gimoro ngang’ !
Kata da bed ni apogo giga duto ni joma odhier , kendo kata da achiwo ringra mondo owang’ , to aonge gi hera , to mano ok konya kata matin .
Hera timo kinda , kendo ong’won . Ok otim nyiego , kendo ok osungre , bende ok opakre .
Hera ok tim gima kuodo wich , ok odwar mare kende , iye ok wang’ , bende ok omak sadha .
Ok omor gi tim ma ok kare , to omor gi adiera .
Hera odhil e weche duto , kendo kata ang’o ema otimore , to pod en gi yie , gi geno , kod kinda .
Hera ok rem . Tich hulo wach to norum , kendo dhum gi dhok mayoreyore nowe , bende rieko notieki ,
nikech rieko ma wan-go orem , kendo tich hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye bende orem ,
to ka gima ogik kare obiro , to mano morem norum .
Kane an nyathi , ne awuoyo kaka nyathi , kendo riekona ne mar nyathi , bende ne aparo kaka nyathi . To koro kaka asedoko ng’ama duong’ , aseweyo timbe mag nyithindo .
Koro waneno mana kido matiptip ka joma neno e rang’i marachrach , to chieng’no wananen malong’o . Rieko ma an-go sani en rieko morem , to chieng’no anang’e Nyasaye chuth , mana kaka Nyasaye ong’eya .
To gik moko adek ema osiko . Gin yie , gi geno , kod hera ; to gima duong’ moloyo kuomgi en hera .
Hera ema nyaka ubediego moloyo gik moko duto , to mich mag Roho bende nyaka udwar , to moloyo dwaruru mich mar hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye .
Ng’at madhum gi dhok mayoreyore ok wuo gi ji , to owuoyo mana gi Nyasaye , nikech onge ng’ama winjo weche mowacho . Owacho weche mopondo , kuom teko mar Roho .
To ng’ama hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye wuoyo gi ji , kokonyogi kendo ojiwogi kendo odwogo chunygi .
Ng’at madhum gi dhok mayoreyore to konyo mana en owuon , to ng’ama hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye to tego kanyakla mar jo-Kristo .
Daher mondo un duto udhum gi dhok mayoreyore , to moloyo adwaro mondo uhul wach moa kuom Nyasaye , nikech ng’ama hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye nigi tich maduong’ moloyo ng’ama dhum gi dhok mayoreyore , mak mana ka nitie jalok wach manyalo hulo tiend gima ng’at madhumo owacho , mondo jo-Kristo duto oyud konyruok .
Emomiyo owetene , ka abiro iru , mi adhum gi dhok mayoreyore , to ere kaka dakonyu , ka ok anyisou wach moro ma Nyasaye oelona e fweny , kata ka ok akelonu weche mag rieko , kata ahulonu weche mag puonj ?
To kata mana gik maonge gi ngima kaka asili kod thum bende puonjowa ni mano en adier , nikech ere kaka ng’ato ding’e puch migoyo , ka puye duto ogo mana rat ?
Kata kapo ni tung’ mar lweny ok oywak maliw , to ere ng’ama diikre ni lweny ?
Kamano bende , ka wach midhumo gi dhok mayoreyore ok winjre malong’o , to ere kaka ng’ato diwinj gima iwacho ? Wecheni dilal mana e kor yamo !
Nitie dhok matrhoth mopogore opogore e piny , to aparo ka onge moro ma ok winjre .
Omiyo ka ng’ato wacho dhok ma ok awinji , to ng’at ma wacho dhokno chalna jamwa , kendo an bende achalone jamwa .
Kamano un bende , kaka ugombo ahinya nwang’o mich mag Roho , dwaruru matek mondo uti gi mich manyalo tego jo-Kristo .
Emomiyo ng’at madhum gi dhok mayoreyore mondo olem , oyud teko mar loko weche modhumo ,
nimar ka alemo ka adhum , to chunya kende ema lemo , to parona ok tim gimoro .
Koro ere gima onego atim ? Abiro lemo gi chunya , to kendo abiro lemo gi parona bende . Abiro wero wende pak gi chunya , to bende abiro werogi gi parona bende .
Ka igoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano mana gi chunyi , ka idhum gi Roho , to ere kaka ng’ato ang’ata mobet e chokruokno diwach ni , ‘ Amin’ , bang’ erokamano migoyono , ka ok ong’eyo tiend gima iwacho ?
Kata dabed ni igoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano maber manadi , to mano ok kony ng’at machielono .
Agoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano nikech adhum gi dhok mayoreyore moloyou uduto ,
to ka an e chokruok mar jo-Kristo , to ahero wacho weche abich gi parona awuon mondo apuonjgo jomoko bende , moloyo dhumo weche gana gi gana gi dhok mayoreyore .
Owetena , kik ubed gi paro machalo paro nyithindo . Beduru ka nyithindo e weche mag richo , to nyaka ubed joma dongo gi parou .
