Muma wacho e kitap Chik niya , “ Ruoth Nyasaye owacho ni , ‘ Abiro wuoyo gi ogandani gi dho joma dhumo dhok mayoreyore . Ee , abiro wuoyokodgi gi dho jomoko nono , to kata kamano , ok giniwinja . ’ . ”
Omiyo unyalo neno ni , dhum gi dhok mayoreyore en ranyisi ni joma ok oyie , to ok ni joma oyie . To mich mar hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye en ranyisi ni joma oyie , to ok ni joma ok oyie .
Emomiyo ka jo-Kristo duto ochokore , kendo giduto gidhum gi dhok mayoreyore , mi ji moko makia , kata ma ok oyie , obiro e chokruokuno , donge digiwach ni neko omakou ?
To ka ji duto hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye , mi ng’at moro makia , kata ma ok oyie , obiro , to weche duto mowinjo chwowo chunye , kendo miyo bura loye ,
Eka paro maling’ling’ manie chunye elore e lela , mi opodho piny auma , kolamo Nyasaye kendo ohulo niya , “ Adier , Nyasaye ni kodu ! ”
Koro owetena , ere gima ber monego utim ? E chokruoku duto , ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu mondo obed gi wer , kata gi puonj , kata gi fweny , kata gi wach midhumo , kata gi loko wach midhumono ; to mago duto onego obed makonyo chokruok .
Ka nitie joma nigi mich mar dhum gi dhok mayoreyore , to ji ariyo kata adek kende ema mondo owuo , ka giluwore achiel achiel , kendo jalok wach bende nyaka bedie .
To ka jalok wach onge , to ng’ama dwaro dhum gi dhok mayoreyore nyaka ling’ e chokruok , to owuo mana e chunye owuon kende gi Nyasaye .
To kuom jogo mahulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye , ji ariyo kata adek ema mondo olosi . Ji mamoko to mondo opim ane wechegigo .
To ka wach moro ofwenyore ni ng’ato mobet piny , ka pod ng’at machielo wuoyo , to ng’at moyudo ka wuoyono mondo oling’ ,
nikech uduto unyalo hulo wach Nyasaye kuluworu achiel achiel , mondo ji duto oyud puonj kendo oyud jip .
Ng’atno nyalo ling’ kamano , nikech mich mar hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye nie teko mar jahul wach owuon ,
nimar Nyasaye ok en Nyasach koko , to en Nyasach kue .
Mon to mondo oling’ e chokruok mana kaka obet e chokruok duto mag jo-Kristo . Ok oyienigi wuoyo , mana kaka Chik Musa bende wacho .
To ka gidwaro penjo wach moro , to onego gipenj chwogi e mier , nikech en wich kuot ka dhako wuoyo e chokruok !
Koso uparo ni wach Nyasaye nochakore kuomu , kendo ni nobiro mana ni un kende ? Ooyo , ok kamano !
Ka ng’ato paro ni en jahul wach moa kuom Nyasaye , kata ni en gi mich moro mar Roho , to onego ong’e ni gima andikonu en chik moa kuom Ruoth .
To ka ok odewo wachni , to en bende kik udewe .
Emomiyo owetena , dwaruru matek mondo ubed gi mich mar hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye , to kik utam ji dhum gi dhok mayoreyore ,
to weuru gik moko duto otimre maber kendo makare .
To koro owetena , adwaro paronu Wach Maber mane apuonjou , mondo anyisu tiende . Ne urwake , kendo yie maru ochung’ kuome motegno ,
bende en ema uyudo resruok kuome , to mana ka usiko uyie gi gima ne apuonjou , kapo ni ok uyie kayiem nono .
Wach maduong’ie moloyo akelonu , kendo ma an bende nokelna , en ni : Kristo notho nikech richowa , kaka Muma wacho .
Noyike , kendo nochier oa kuom joma otho chieng’ mar adek , bende kaka Muma wacho .
Nofwenyore ni Petro , kendo ni joote apar gariyo .
Bang’ mano nofwenyore kaachiel ni jopuonjre ma kwan-gi oloyo mia abich , ma ng’enygi pod nitie nyaka chil kawuono , to moko osetho .
Bende nofwenyore ni Jakobo , eka kendo ofwenyore ni joote duto .
Bang’e mogik , an bende nofwenyorena apoya , mana ka nyathi monywol apoya .
An ema atinie moloyo kuom joote duto . Ok owinjore luonga ni jaote , nikech nasando kanyakla mar joma oyie kuom Nyasaye .
To ng’wono mar Nyasaye ema osemiyo abedo kaka achaloni , kendo ng’wono mane omiya ok osebet kayiem nono . Chutho asetiyo matek moloyo joote mamoko duto , to ok gi tekra awuon , to ng’wono mar Nyasaye ema notiyo kuoma .
Emomiyo kata bed ni wach noa kuoma kata kuomgi , to mano e gima waduto wapuonjo , kendo ema ne uyie .
Koro kaka wapuonjo ni Kristo osechier oa kuom joma otho , ere kaka jomoko kuomu wacho ni joma otho ok nochier ?
To ka chier onge , to kara kata mana Kristo bende ne ok ochier .
To ka Kristo ne ok ochier , to kara wach mwalando onge tiende , kendo un bende gima uyie onge tiende .
To bende wanenore ka joma riambo kuom Nyasaye , nikech wasebedo kwawacho ni ne ochiero Yesu oa kuom joma otho . To kara ne ok ochiere ka en adier ni joma otho ok chier ,
nimar ka joma otho ok chier , to kara kata mana Kristo bende ne ok ochier .
To ka Kristo ne ok ochier adier , to kara yie maru en kayiem nono , kendo pod un mana e richou .
Bende mano dinyis ni joma osetho ma oyie kuom Kristo , kara olal !
Ka wageno kuom Kristo mana e ngimani kende , to kara wan e joma odhierie moloyo ji duto e piny !
To en adier ni Kristo ne ochier oa kuom joma otho ! En ema nokwongo chier mana ka gir singo ni joma otho biro chier .
Tiende ni , kaka dhano nokelo tho e piny , e kaka dhano bende nokelo chier kuom tho .
Kaka ji duto tho kuom Adam , e kaka ji duto nodok mangima kuom Kristo ,
to ginibi ka ng’ato ka ng’ato ni kare owuon . Tiende ni Kristo ema nokwongo chier kaka gir singo , eka chieng’ ma Kristo oduogo , to joge nochier .
Bang’ mano chieng’ giko nochopi , ma Kristo nochiwie loch ni Nyasaye Wuoro , kosetieko loch duto , gi teko duto kod nyalo duto ,
nimar Kristo nyaka bed gi loch nyaka chop Nyasaye ket wasike duto e bwo tiende .
To jasigu ma notiek mogik en tho ,
nimar Muma wacho niya , “ Nyasaye noketo gik moko duto e bwo tiende . ” To ka Muma wacho ni , “ gik moko duto ” , to nyaka ung’e ni mano ok oting’o koda Nyasaye , nikech Nyasaye ema noketo gik moko duto e bwo Kristo .
To ka gik moko duto oseketi e bwo loch Wuowi , bang’e en bende enobed e bwo loch Nyasaye mane oketo gik moko duto e bwoye , mondo Nyasaye obed gi loch kuom gik moko duto .
Koro ka chier onge , to ere ohala ma joma ibatiso nikech joma otho biro yudo ? Ere gimomiyo ibatisogi nikech joma otho , ka joma otho ok chier ngang’ ?
Koso wan to ere gima omiyo wayie bedo e masira seche duto ?
Owetena , awachonu adier nikech mor ma an-go kodu kuom Kristo Yesu Ruodhwa ni , tho ochoma pile .
Ka an mana dhano ma ok chier , to ere ber mane ayudo kuom kedo gi ondiegi Efeso ? Ka en adier ni joma otho ok chier , to kara wachiemuru , kendo wamethuru , nikech kiny wanatho , mana kaka Muma wacho .
Kik wuondu ! Osiepe maricho ketho timbe mabeyo .
Beduru gi rieko mondo uwe timo richo . Jomoko kuomu kia Nyasaye . Awacho kamano mondo akuodgo wiu !
Ng’ato nyalo penjo ni , “ Ere kaka ichiero joma otho ? Koso ringruok manadi ma ginibedgo ? ”
To mano penjo mofuwo manadi ! Donge kodhi ma in iwuon ichwoyo kwongo tho , eka bet mangima ?
Bende gima ichwoyo ok en cham hie mabiro wuok bang’e , to en mana kodhi kende . Onyalo bedo mar ngano kata mar cham moro amora .
To Nyasaye miyogo kido kaka oneno ni long’one . Kamano kodhi ka kodhi nigi kite owuon .
To bende ring’o mag gik moko ok en kit ring’o achiel , to nitie ring dhano , gi mar le , gi mar winyo , kod mar rech .
Nitie gik polo , kod mag piny . To gik polo nigi duong’ moro , kendo mag piny bende nigi duong’ machielo .
Nitie duong’ mar wang’chieng’ , kod duong’ mar due , kod duong’ mar sulue . To chutho sulue achiel rieny matek moloyo machielo .
Mano e kaka chier mar joma otho bende chalo . Ringruok miyiko e lowo en gima tow , to ichiere ka gima ok tow .
Ka oyike , to oonge gi duong’ , to ka ochiere to en gi duong’ . Iyike ka onyap , to ichiere ka en gi teko .
Bende iyike ka en gi ringruok mar pinyni , to ichiere ka en gi ringruok mar polo . Nitie ringruok mar pinyni , to bende nitie ringruok mar polo .
Mano emomiyo Muma wacho niya , “ Adam , dhano mokwongo , nodoko ng’at man gi ngima , to Adam ma achien nodoko Roho machiwo ngima . ”
To ringruok mar polo ok ema ne okwongo betie , to ringruok mar piny ema ne okwongo , eka bang’e mano mar polo nobetie .
Dhano mokwongo nochue gi lowo mar piny , to dhano mar ariyo noa e polo .
Jogo mochue gi lowo chalo gi jal mane ochue gi lowo cha , to jogo mag polo chalo gi Jal mane oa e polo .
Kaka wasebedo gi kido mar dhano mar lowo , e kaka wanabed gi kido mar Jal mane oa e polo cha .
To owetena , gima awacho e ma : Joma pod nigi ringruok mar pinyni ok nyal yudo gueth mar Loch Nyasaye , bende gima tow ok nyal bedo wuon gik ma ok tow .
To winjuru mondo awachnue wach moro mopondo : Ok wanatho waduto , to nolokwa
ahucha ka diemo wang’ , ka tung’ mogik oywak , nimar ka oywak to joma otho nochier gi ringruok ma ok tow , kendo wan bende nolokwa ,
nikech ringruok matowni nyaka rwakre gi ringruok ma ok tow . Adier , gima tho nyaka rwakre gi gima ok tho .
Kuom mano , ka ringruok matow oserwakore gi ringruok ma ok tow , kendo ka gima tho oserwakore gi gima ok tho , eka weche mondiki e Muma nochop kare niya , “ Tho oselo , motiek chuth !
In tho , ere lochni ? In tho , ere lit mikelo ? ”
Lit mar tho en richo , kendo richo yudo teko kuom Chik .
Wagouru erokamano ni Nyasaye , mamiyo walocho kuom Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo .
Emomiyo owetena mahero , chung’uru motegno ma ok ung’ingni , kutiyo matek pile e tich Ruoth , kendo kung’eyo ni tich mutiyo kuom Ruoth ok nobed kayiem nono .
To kuom wach solro mitimo ni jo-Nyasaye , un bende timuru kaka nanyiso kanyakala mag jo-Kristo manie piny Galatia mondo otim .
Chieng’ Jumapil ka Jumapil , ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu mondo opog moko kuom gik ma Nyasaye osekonyego , oket tenge mondo solro kik tim ka abiro .
Yieruru jomoko kuomu , kendo ka abiro , to anaorgi gi barupe mondo giter chiwou Jerusalem ,
kendo ka owinjore ni an bende onego adhi , to anadhi kodgi .
Anabi iru ka aselando Wach Maber e piny Makedonia ,
kendo dipo ka abedo kodu , mi kamoro datiek ndalo chwiri kodu , mondo ukowa maber kamoro amora ma adhiye .
Anatim kamano nikech ok adwar nenou mana ka akadho , to ageno bedo kodu kuom ndalo moko , ka Ruoth oyie .
To pod abiro bet Efeso ka , nyaka chop chieng’ Pentekost ,
nikech oyawna dhoot malach kaeri mar tiyo tich maduong’ makelo konyruok , to bende nitie wasigu mang’eny .
To ka Timotheo obiro iru , to neuru ni obedo kodu koonge luoro , nikech otiyo ni Ruoth mana kaka an .
Omiyo kik ng’ato chaye , to ukowe gi kue mondo obi ira . Eri warite , wan kod owete .
To koro adwaro nyisou wach owadwa Apolo . Asejiwe ahinya mondo obi iru kod owete , to pod ok oyie maber mondo obi e ndaloni , to obiro biro ka oyudo thuolo .
Beduru motang’ , kendo chung’uru motegno kuom yieu . Beduru gi chir kendo gi jing’o .
Bende gik moko duto mutimo , timuru gi hera .
Owetena , donge ung’eyo Stefano kod joodgi ? Gin e joma okwongo doko jo-Kristo ee piny Akaya , kendo gisechiwore mondo giti ni jo-Nyasaye .
Koro akwayou owetena , ni mondo uyie bet e bwo joma kamago , kendo e bwo ng’ato ka ng’ato ma bende tiyo tich Nyasaye matek .
Amor ahinya nikech Stefano gi Fortunato kod Akaiko josebiro , nimar gisekonya karu ,
kendo giseduogo chunya , mana kaka aparo ni giseduogo chunyu bende . Onego uyie joma kamago .
Kanyakla mag jo-Kristo manie piny Asia ooronu mos , kendo Akula gi Priska kod kanyakla mar jo-Kristo malemo e odgi bende omosou ahinya kuom Ruoth .
Owete duto omosou . Yogreuru gi mos maler .
An Paulo ema koro andikonu mosni gi lweta awuon .
Ka ng’ato ok ohero Ruoth , to mondo okuong’re ! Ruodhwa bi !
Ng’wono mar Ruoth Yesu obed kodu .
Herane obed kodu kuom Kristo Yesu .
An Paulo , jaote Yesu Kristo kuom dwaro mar Nyasaye , ema andiko baruani kaachiel gi owadwa Timotheo . Wandikonu un kanyakla mar joma oyie kuom Nyasaye man Korintho , kendo ni jo-Nyasaye duto manie piny Akaya .
Ng’wono gi kue moa kuom Nyasaye kod ruodhwa Yesu Kristo obed kodu .
Duong’ obed ni Nyasaye ma wuon Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo . En e wuon ng’wono kendo makonyowa e yore duto .
Okonyowa e masichewa duto mondo wan bende wakony joma nigi masira moro amora , ka wanyisogi kaka Nyasaye osekonyowa .
Kaka masiche moko mag sand mang’eny mane Kristo oneno koro bironwa mogundho e kaka kony mang’eny ma wayudo kuom Kristo bende koro bironwa mogundho .
Ka isandowa , to en mana ni mondo okonyu , kendu uyud warruok . To ka ikonyowa , to en bende mana ni mondo Nyasaye okonyu , ka udhil gi sand ma wan bende wayudo ,
kendo geno mwagenougo ogurore nikech wang’eyo ni kaka uyudo sand kodwa e kaka uyudo kony kodwa bende .
Owetewa , wadwaro nyisou chandruok mane wayudo e piny Asia , ne omiwa ting’ mapek mohewo tekrewa , mi chunywa oa ni ok wanachak wabed mangima .
Chutho , ne wagalo ni oseng’adnwa buch tho . To mano notimore mondo kik wagen kuomwa wawegi , to wagen mana kuom Nyasaye machiero joma otho .
Noresowa e masiche malich mag tho kamano , kendo nochak oreswa . En ema waketo genowa kuome ni obiro medo resowa ,
ka un bende ukonyowa kulemonwa . Kamano , kaka ji mang’eny bende nobed ka goyo ni Nyasaye erokamano nikech mich momiyowa kuom ng’wonone .
To gimoro achiel mamiyowa mor en ni : wang’eyo malong’o e chunywa ni adier mar Nyasaye ema osetelonwa e kindwa gi ji , to moloyo to wasebet kamano mana kuom ng’wono mar Nyasaye , to ok kuom rieko mar dhano .
Weche mwandikonugi onge gi tiendgi moko mopondo , to mak mana mago ma unyalo somo , mi uwinji . Kata obedo ni sani pod ung’eyowa mana matin kende ,
Ne an gi geno ahinya kuom wachno , omiyo ne achano mokwongo mondo abi iru , uyud gueth diriyo ,
nikech ne achano mondo aneu ka akadho adhi Makedonia , kendo anachak aneu ka aduogo aa kuno , mondo ukowa ka adhi Judea .
To uparo ni kane achano kamano to ne an jahubagabaga koso ? Koso uparo ni achano yorena mana kaka dhano chano , ka weche ariyo , ma “ Ee ” gi “ Ooyo ” okikore e chunya ?
Chutho , kaka Nyasaye en jaadiera , wach ma wawacho ok oting’o “ Ee ” kaachiel gi “ Ooyo ” ,
nikech Yesu Kristo wuod Nyasaye , ma wan gi Sila kod Timotheo ne walandonu wachne , ok en “ Ee ” gi “ Ooyo ” . To en e “ Ee ” mogik ma Nyasaye wacho ,
nimar en ema singruok Nyasaye duto chopo kare kuome . Mano emomiyo kwamiyo Nyasaye duong’ to wawacho ni , “ Amin ” kuom Yesu Kristo .
Jal mamiyo wan kod un wabedo gi ratiro ni wan kuom Kristo en Nyasaye . En ema osewirowa ,
kendo oketo kido mare kuomwa , kendo omiyowa Roho mondo odag e chunywa kaka mich mokwongo mar gueth ma wabiro yudo achien .
To aluongo Nyasaye obed janenona ka aramo ni ne akechou emomiyo ne ok achako aduogo Korintho .
Ok wan gi teko kuom yieu ni nyaka uyie gima wawacho , nikech un joma nigi yie motegno . To watiyo kaachiel kodu mana ni mondo ubed mamor .
Mano emomiyo naneno ni ber mondo kik achak alimu kendo , ka limbenano dimiu chuny lit ,
nikech ka amiyou chuny lit , to koro ere ng’ama dimiya mor , ka ok mana un ma asemiyo chuny litgo ?
Mano emomiyo nandikonu baruano . Ne ok adwar biro iru mondo ayud chuny lit kuom joma onego miya mor , nimar ang’eyo malong’o ni ka amor to un bende umor uduto .
Ne andikonu ka chunya okuyo kendo chandore ahinya , kendo ka pi wang’a chuer mang’eny , to ok ni mondo amiu chuny lit , to mana ni mondo ung’e hera maduong’ ma aherougo .
Ng’at moro osekelo chuny lit , to ok an ema osemiya chuny litno , to mana machiegni un duto ema osemiyou chuny lit , ka ok adwar jimbo wach .
To kum ma jou mathoth osemiyo ng’atno oseromo ,
omiyo koro onego uwene kethone , kendo uduog chunye , nono to kuyo malit ohewe .
Emomiyo akwayou mondo unyise ni uhere .
Mano emomiyo ne omiyo andikonu , mondo atemugo , ang’e ka un joma oyie winjo wach .
Ka uweyo ni ng’ato kethone , to an bende aweyone kethone , nikech kapo ni aweyo ni ng’ato kethone , to aweyone mana nikech un , kendo e nyim Kristo ,
mondo Satan kik lowa , nikech wang’eyo riekone !
Kane achopo Troa mondo aland Wach Maber mar Kristo , ne ayudo ka dhoot oyaworena malach mondo ati ni Ruoth .
To chunya ne onge gi kue , nikech ne ok anwang’o owadwa Tito . Omiyo nagoyo oriti ni jokuno , mi achweyo Makedonia .
To wagouru ni Nyasaye erokamano nikech wan ma wan kuom Kristo , otelonwa pile koselocho , kendo komiyo walando wach man kuom Kristo kuonde duto , mana ka tik mang’ue ng’ar .
Wachalo gi ubani mang’ue ng’ar mar misango ma Kristo ochiwo ni Nyasaye , malandore e kind joma ireso kod joma lal .
Kuom joma lal en tik mar tho makelo tho , to kuom joma ireso to en tik mar ngima . Koro ere ng’ama nyalo gik ma kamago ?
Wan ok wachal gi ji mathoth makonyore gi Wach Nyasaye e yo ma ok kare , mondo oyudgo ohala . Ooyo , wan joma Nyasaye oseoro , omiyo wawuoyo e nyim Nyasaye gi adiera ka joma ni kuom Kristo .
Koro mano nenore ka gima wachako wapakore kendwa koso ? Wan ok wadwar barupe mag pak ma wabirogo iru , kata ma waago kuomu , kaka jomoko kuomu dwaro .
Un e barupwa mondiki e chunywa ma ng’ato ka ng’ato nyalo neno , kendo somo .
Nenore ratiro ni un e barua moa kuom Kristo , mane wakelo . Ok en barua mondik gi wino , to ondiki gi Roho mar Nyasaye Mangima . Bende ok ondike e kite mopa , to ondike e chuny dhano .
Wawacho kamano nikech wan gi geno e nyim Nyasaye kuom Kristo .
Wan to waonge gi teko moro kuomwa wawegi mamiyo wawacho ni wanyalo timo gimoro , to gima wan-go a mana kuom Nyasaye ,
kendo en ema ne otimowa jotich Winjruok Manyien . Ok en Winjruok mar chik mondiki , to en mar Roho . Chik mondiki kelo tho , Roho to kelo ngima .
Chik mane ogor e kite nukta ka nukta osebet kakelo tho , to kata kamano nobiro gi ler maduong’ mane omono jo-Israel ng’iyo wang’ Musa tir , kata obedo ni lerno ne rumo kamano .
Koro gima Roho kelo donge nyaka bed gi ler maduong’ moloyo koso ?
Ka gima kelo bura ema ne obiro gi ler maduong’ machalo kamano , koro gima Roho kelo , mamiyo wabedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye donge dibed gi ler maduong’ moloyo ?
Adier , ler mane nigi duong’ , koro ok nigi duong’ ngang’ , nikech ler maduong’ moloye osebiro .
Ka gima rumo ema nigi ler ma kamano , koro gima dak mosiko to dibed gi ler maduong’ machal nade !
Wawuoyo gi chir nikech geno ma kamano ma wan-go .
Wan ok watim kaka Musa , mane umo wang’e gi rageng’ mondo jo-Israel kik ne ler ka duono kendo rumo .
To chutho chuny jo-Israel nodinore , nikech nyaka chil kawuono chunygi pod oum gi rageng’no ka isomo Muma Machon , nimar rageng’no igolo mana ka ng’ato ni kuom Kristo .
Kata mana ndalogi , ka isomo Chik Musa to rageng’no pod oumo auma chunygi .
To Muma wacho ni , ka ng’ato olokore ni Ruoth to rageng’no igolo .
To Ruoth nogono e Roho kendo , kama Roho mar Ruoth tinie , to thuolo tinie .
Wan duto , ma waonge rageng’ e wang’wa , to wachalo gi rang’i , kendo wamiyo ler mar Ruoth nenore , kendo lerno medore ameda pile , ka kitwa medo lokore machal kode . Mano en tich Ruoth ma en Roho .
Kaka Nyasaye ema osemiyowa tijni kuom ng’wonone , omiyo ok wanyal nyosore .
Wasekwedo timbe mag mudho kendo makuodo wich . Ok wawuoth gi miganga , bende ok wagaj Wach Nyasaye , to wawacho mana adiera e lela e nyim Nyasaye , kwanyiso wawegi ni wan kare , kendo wamiyo ji duto yie kodwa .
Watimo kamano nikech ka Wach Maber mwalando ogeng’ore , to ogeng’ore mana ni joma lal .
Gin joma ok yie , ma nyasach pinyni osedino chunygi , mondo kik gine ler ma Wach Maber manyiso ji duong’ maler mar Kristo , ma en owuon e kido mar Nyasaye .
Ok waland wach kuomwa wan wawegi , to walando mana wach ni , Kristo Yesu en Ruoth , kendo ni wan mana jotichu nikech Kristo .
Watimo kamano nimar Nyasaye achiel mane owacho ni mondo ler orieny e chunywa mondo okelnwa ler mar ng’eyo duong’ mar Nyasaye mineno e wang’ Yesu Kristo .
To wan ma wan gi mwandu mar chuny , wachalo mana agulini mag lowo , mondo onenre ni teko maduong’ ahinyano oa kuom Nyasaye , to ok oa kuomwa wawegi .
Pile idiyowa koni gi koni , to kata kamano ok dinnwa . Wadhier nono , to chunywa ok a .
Isandowa , to ok jwang’wa , bende igoyowa piny , to ok negwa .
Pile wating’o tho mane Yesu othogo e ringrewa ,
nimar kata obedo ni wangima , to pile iterowa kar tho nikech Yesu , mondo ngima mar Yesu bende onenre e ringrewa matho .
Kamano tho tiyo kuomwa , to un , ngima tiyo kuomu .
Wan gi yie machalo gi mano ma Muma wuoyo kuome ni , “ Ne ayie , emomiyo nawuoyo . ” Kamano wan bende wayie , emomiyo wawuoyo .
Wang’eyo ni Nyasaye , mane ochiero Ruoth Yesu oa kuom joma otho , nochierwa wan bende kaachiel gi Yesu , mi terwa e nyime kaachiel gi un bende .
Mago duto obetie nikech un , mondo kaka ji mayudo ng’wono mogundho mar Nyasaye medore , e kaka erokamano mimiyogo Nyasaye duong’ bende omedore .
Kuom mano , chunywa ok nyosre . Kata obedo ni ringrewa rumo , to chunywa iloso manyien pile ka pile ,
nimar thagruok matin mwayudoni rumo piyo , to obiro kelonwa duong’ miwuoro kendo mosiko ,
nikech ok waketo parowa e gik mineno , to mana e gik ma ok ne . Gik mineno rumo , to gik ma ok ne osiko mochwere .
Wang’eyo ni ka ringrewa , ma en kiru mwadakie e pinykani , omuki , to wan gi ot ma Nyasaye osegeronwa e polo . En ot mosiko nyaka chieng’ , ma ok oger gi lwet dhano .
Adier , ka pod wan e kiru ma wan-go e pinykani , to wachur kwagombo mondo warwakre gi odwa manie polo ,
nikech kwarwakore kode to ok noyudwa ka wan duge .
Ka pod wan e kiru mae pinyni to wachur ka ting ohewowa . To mano ok onyiso ni wadwaro lonyo ringrewa mar pinyni oko . Ooyo , wadwaro mana rwako ringrewa manyien manie polo , mondo ngima mochwere omwony mano matho .
Mano e gima omiyo Nyasaye nochweyowa , kendo osemiyowa Roho kaka mich mokwongo mar gueth mwabiro yudo achien .
Kuom mano , wan gi chir pile , nikech wang’eyo ni , kapod wadak e ringruok e pinyni , to ok wadak kanyachiel gi Ruoth .
Yie ema telonwa , to wengewa ok telnwa .
Awacho ni wan gi chir , kendo daber kwaweyo dak e ringruok , mi wadhi wadak gi Ruoth .
Emomiyo , kata ka wan ka , kata ka waonge , to waketo chunywa kuom bedo malong’one ,
nikech waduto nyaka wachung’ e nyim kom bura mar Kristo , mondo ng’ato ka ng’ato oyud pok moromo gi gik mabeyo kata maricho mane otimo kapod en e ringruok .
Wang’eyo ni tiend luoro Ruoth en ang’o , emomiyo wayuayo ji . Nyasaye ong’eyo chutho ngimawa kaka chal , kendo ageno ni un bende ung’eyowa maber e chunyu maiye kaka wachal .
Ok watem mondo wachak wapakrenu kendo , to wamiyou thuolo mondo ubed gi mor nikech wan , kendo mondo ubed gi gima unyalo dwokogo jogo mapakore nikech gik moko , to ok nikech gik mag chuny .
Ka neko omakowa , to en nikech Nyasaye , to ka parowa ni kare , to en nikech un ,
nimar hera mar Kristo oloyowa chuth . Waseng’eyo malong’o ni ng’at achiel notho ni ji duto , omiyo ji duto bende ne otho .
Ne otho ni ji duto mondo ji mangima kik bed mangima kagiparo mana gin giwegi , to gibed mangima mana ka gitiyo ni Jal mane othonigi kendo ochier nikech gin .
Omiyo koro ok wanon tim ng’ato e yo ma dhano nonoe . Kata obedo ni ne wang’eyo Kristo e yorno , to koro ok wang’eye kamano .
Ka ng’ato obedo kuom Kristo to ochueye ng’ama nyien . Gik moko duto machon osekadho , kendo gik manyien osechopo .
Mago duto a kuom Nyasaye . En owuon ema ne omiyo wawinjore kode kuom Kristo , kendo nomiyowa tich mar kelo winjruok e kinde gi ji mamoko bende ,
kwanyisogi ni Nyasaye nomiyo piny owinjore kode kuom Kristo , ka ok okwan ni ji richogi . Wan ema ne Nyasaye omiyowa wach winjruokni .
Omiyo wan joote Kristo , kendo Nyasaye owuon ema wuoyonu gi dhowa . Wasayou e nying Kristo ni mondo uwinjru gi Nyasaye .
Kristo ne onge gi richo kata matin , to Nyasaye notime richo nikech wan , mondo kuom en wabed joma kare kaka Nyasaye .
Kaka joma tiyo kaachiel gi Nyasaye , wamedo sayou ni kik uwe ng’wono mar Nyasaye museyudo bed kayiem nono ,
nikech Nyasaye wacho niya , “ Ne awinji e kinde mowinjore . Adier , ne akonyi e ndalo warruok . ” Koro neuru , ma e kinde mowinjore ahinya ! Winjuru , ma e ndalo mar warruok .
Ok wadwar timo gimoro ma dichwany ng’ato , nikech dipo ka tichwa oyudo achaye .
To wanyiso ni wan jotich Nyasaye , e weche duto , kwatimo kinda ahinya e sand , e chandruok , e masira ,
e chwat , e twech , e koko , kendo e thagruok , ma ok wanindi kendo ok wachiem .
Wanyisore kuom timbewa makare , kendo kuom rieko , gi timo kinda , gi ng’wono , gi Roho Maler , gi hera maradier ,
gi lando wach adiera , kendo gi teko mar Nyasaye . Wamako tim makare ka gilweny mwamonjogo wasigu , kendo mwaritorego .
Wayudo duong’ , kendo wayudo achaye , bende iketho nyingwa , kendo ipakowa . Ikwanowa gi jomriambo , kata obedo ni wawacho adieri ,
bende wan ka joma ok ong’e , kata obedo ni ong’ewa maber , kendo wan ka joma tho , to kara pod wangima , bende kata ikumowa , to ok negwa .
Kata obedo ni wan gi kuyo maduong’ , to wamor pile , kendo kata obedo ni wan kaka jochan , to wamiyo ji mathoth mwandu . Bende wan kaka joma onge gimoro , to kara wan gi gik moko duto .
Un jo-Korintho , wawuoyonu gi chuny moyawore chutho .
Wan , chunywa ni thuolo kodu , to un ema udich e chunyu .
Koro un bende yanwauru chunyu , nikech awuoyonu kaka wuoro wuoyo ni nyithinde .
Kik uriwru gi joma ok oyie . Ere kaka tim makare diriwre gi tim marach ? Koso ler diriwre nadi gi mudho ?
Ere kaka Kristo diriwre gi jachien ? Koso ere winjruok manyalo bet e kind ng’ama oyie gi ng’ama ok oyie ?
Ere winjruok ma Hekalu mar Nyasaye nigo gi nyiseche manono ? Apenjou kamano nikech wan e Hekalu mar Nyasaye Mangima , mana kaka Nyasaye nowacho niya , “ Abiro dak kodgi , kendo anawuoth kuomgi . Anabed Nyasachgi , kendo ginibed joga . ”
Emomiyo Ruoth owacho ni , “ Auru kuomgi , kendo pogreuru kodgi . Kik umul gimoro mogak , mi narwaku .
Kutimo kamano to eka anabed wuonu , kendo unubed yawuota gi nyiga . An Ruoth Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto ema awacho kamano . ”
Osiepewa , mago e singruok ma osemiwa . Kuom mano , nyaka wapuodhre kuom gik moko duto mamiyo ringruok kod chuny doko mochido , mondo wadok joma ler chuth , kwabedo joma oluoro Nyasaye .
Yawnwauru chunyu . Onge ng’ama wasetimone marach , bende onge ng’ama wasemiyo olal , kata onge ng’ama wasemayo e yor wuond .
Ok awach kamano mondo ang’adnugo bura , nikech asewacho ni waketou e chunywa maiye , kendo wariwore kodu kaachiel pile , bed ni wangima kata watho .
Chunya ni thuolo ka aloso kodu kendo an gi mor maduong’ nikech un ! Kata obedo ni chandruokwa ng’eny kamano , to achung’ motegno , kendo amor mokadho !
En adier ni kata ka ne wachopo Makedonia to ne ok wayudo yueyo . Ne wayudo mana chandruok kuonde duto : dhaw ne oluorowa oko , kendo chunywa ne opong’ gi luoro .
To Nyasaye majiwo joma okuyo , nojiwowa kuom biro mar Tito .
Ok birone kende ema nojiwowa , to jip mane oyudo kuomu , bende nojiwowa . Ne onyisowa kaka un gi siso ahinya mar nena , kendo kaka uywak , kendo kaka usiro wechena . Mano nomiyo amedo doko mamor moloyo .
Kata obedo ni barua mane andikonu nomiyou kuyo , to ok ayuag ang’e ni ne andike . Adier , ne aywago ang’e , to koro aneno ni baruano nomiyou kuyo mana kuom kinde manok kende ,
To koro amor , to ok nikech ne amiyou kuyo , to mana nikech kuyono nomiyo uloko chunyu . Ne ubedo mokuyo e yo ma Nyasaye dwaro , omiyo onge yo moro mane wahinyougo kata matin .
Kuyo ma ng’ato bedogo e yo ma Nyasaye dwaro , miyo olokore , kendo kelone warruok maonge ywago ang’e . Kuyo mar piny to kelo tho .
Neyeuru gik ma kuyo e yo ma Nyasaye dwaro osetimonu . Mano kaka osemiyo ubedo joma paro matut , kuketo chunyu kuom nyiso ni ne ok uketho , bende osemiyo ubedo gi mirima kod luor , kendo ugombo nena . Unyiso ni utimo kinda , kendo udwaro ng’ado bura kare . Adier , usenyiso e yore duto ni uonge gi ketho e wachno .
Omiyo kata obedo ni ne andikonu kamano , to ne ok andiko nikech ng’at mane otimo marach , kata nikech ng’at mane otimne marach , to nandiko mana ni mondo un uwegi une kinda mutimo nikech wan , kendo mondo kindano onenre e nyim Nyasaye bende .
Mano ema omiyo waseyudo jip .
To komedore gi jip mane wan wawegi wayudo , ne wadoko mamor moloyo nikech mor mane Tito oduogogo . Ne uduogo chunye un uduto .
Kapo ni ne apakoune , to ok usemiyo wiya okuot . Pile kaka wasebedo mana ka wawachonu adiera kende , kamano bende e kaka pak mane wapakougo medore ameda , koparo kaka uduto ne umako wach , kendo kaka ne urwake gi luoro kod kibaji .
Mano kaka amor , nikech koro anyalo geno kuomu e weche duto !
Owetewa , wadwaro mondo ung’e gueth ma Nyasaye osemiyo kanyakla mag jo-Kristo man Makedonia kuom ng’wonone .
Ne gineno masiche malich kitemogigo , to kata kamano ne gin gi mor mogundho , omiyo kata ne gidhier ahinya , to ne gigolo chiwo maonge migundia .
Awachonu adier ni ne gigolo chiwo kaka ginyalo , mi gichiwo moloyo koda kaka ne ginyalo , kendo ne gitimo kamano maonge achune .
To bende ne gihombowa mondo gikonywa nywako tich ng’wono mar konyo jo-Nyasaye man Judea .
Ne gitimo moloyo kaka ne waparo . Mokwongo ne gichiwore ni Ruoth , eka kuom dwaro mar Nyasaye , ne gichiwore ni wan bende .
Mano emomiyo ne wakwayo Tito , mane ochako tich ng’wono , mondo olimu kendo , kendo okonyu tieke .
Ugundho gi gik moko duto , kaka yie , gi wach , gi rieko , gi kinda duto , kod hera ma uherowago . Kamano bende e kaka mondo ugol chiwo mogundho e tich ng’wonono .
Ok aketnu chik , to anyisou mana hera ma jomoko nono nigo , mondo ane ane ka herau en hera maradier .
Ung’eyo ng’wono mar Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo , ni kata ne en gi mwandu mogundho kamano , to nodoko jachan nikech un , mondo un ubed jomwandu kuom chan mare .
Kuom mano , parona kuom wachno chal kama : koro ber mondo utiek tich mane uchako higa cha . Un e joma nokwongo ni jomoko e tijni . Ok nukwongonigi keto chunyu kuom time kende , to ne ukwongonigi keto chunyu kuom time bende .
Emomiyo koro tiekuru tijno . Keturu chunyu kuom tieke kaka unyalo , mana kaka ne uketo chunyu kuchako .
Ka uketo chunyu kuom chiwo , to Nyasaye biro yie mana gi gima uchiwo , to ok odwar mondo uchiw gima uongego .
Ok adwar mondo ukony jomoko , to un udong’ gi ting’ mapek , to ber mondo gik moko obed maromre .
Kaka un gi gik mathoth e kindeni , ber mondo ukony jogo mochando . Bang’e chieng’ moro gin bende ginikonyu ka gin-go mathoth , to un uchando . Kamano mondo gik moko obed maromre ,
mana kaka Muma wacho ni , “ Ng’at mane ochoko mang’eny ne ok nigi mathoth mohinge , kendo ng’at mane ochoko matin , ne ok nigi manok moreme . ”
Wagoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano kuom miyo chuny Tito kinda mar konyou kaka wan !
Ne wakwaye mondo obi iru , mi oyie , to bende en owuon ne oikore gi chunye duto mondo obi iru .
Ero waore gi owadwa moro ma kanyakla duto mag jo-Kristo pako kuom tichne mar lando Injili .
Ok mano kende , to kanyakla mag jo-Kristo oseyiere bende mondo owuoth kodwa e tich ng’wono ma watiyo mondo Nyasaye oyud duong’ , kendo mondo onyisu ni waketo chunywa e tijni .
Watemo ritore mondo ng’ato kik bed gi ng’ur kuom tichwa maduong’ mar chiwoni ,
nikech wadwaro timo mana gima long’o , ok e nyim Ruoth kende , to e nyim ji bende .
Kuom mano , waorogi kod owadwa moro ma pile waseneno ka oketo chunye kuom gimoro amora motimo , to koro oketo chunye e tijni moloyo , nikech ogenou ahinya .
Tito to en jawuodha , kendo jatich wadwa e tich mwatiyonu . To owete mamoko ariyogo to gin joote mag kanyakla mag jo-Kristo , kendo gin joma kelo ni Kristo duong’ .
Omiyo nyisgiuru herau , kendo nyisgiuru gima omiyo wapakounigi , mondo kanyakla duto mag jo-Kristo ong’e .
Ok onego amed ndikonu kuom wach chiwo mioro ni jo-Nyasaye man Judea .
Ang’eyo kaka uikoru mar konyo , kendo asepuoyou e nyim jo-Makedonia kuom wachno , ka awachonigi ni un jo-Akaya usebedo kuikoru mar konyo , chakre higa cha . Kamano kinda maru osejiwo jogi mathoth .
Koro aoro owetegi mondo pwoch mane wapuoyougo kuom wachno kik bed wach awacha . To adwaro ni mondo ubed moikore mana kaka asewacho ,
nikech kwabiro gi jo-Makedonia moko , mi wayudo ka ok uikoru , to mano dikuod wiwa kod wiu bende , bang’ pak mwasepakougo ahinya !
Mano emomiyo aseneno ni ber mondo aor owetego obi iru mokwongo , olos chon chiwo mane usesingoru ni ubiro golo . Kamano ka abiro to anayud ka oikore , kendo mano nonyis ni uchiwe maonge achune .
Ng’euru ni , ng’ama chwoyo manok , kayo manok , to ng’ama chwoyo mang’eny , kayo mang’eny .
Ng’ato ka ng’ato mondo ochiw kaka oseparo e chunye , ma ok ochune , kendo ma ok oywago ang’e , nikech jachiwo mamor ema Nyasaye ohero .
Nyasaye nyalo miyou gik moko duto mudwaro , kendo mokadho kanyo , mondo kinde duto ubed gi gik moromou , kod mago munyalo konyogo tije mabeyo duto ,
mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Ochiwo gige mabup , kopogo ni jochan . Ng’wonone osiko nyaka chieng’ . ”
Jal mamiyo jachwoyo kodhi , kendo chiwo chiemo michamo , biro miyou kodhi michwoyo , bende nomi gidongi , kendo nomed nyak mar timu mang’won .
Enomi udok jomwandu ahinya e gik moko duto , mondo ubed jong’wono ndalo duto , kendo mano nomi ji mang’eny goni Nyasaye erokamano nikech chiwou ma wamiyogi .
Tich ma watiyoni ok kel mana gik moko duto ma jo-Nyasaye dwaro kende , to obiro miyo ji medo goyo ni Nyasaye erokamano bende .
Chiwouni biro nyiso ni umako chik Nyasaye , kendo ni uhulo Wach Maber man kuom Kristo gi adiera , omiyo gibiro miyo Nyasaye duong’ , kendo ginipake nikech ng’wono ma utimonigi , kendo ni ji duto .
Kuom mano , gibiro neno kaka Nyasaye osebedonu mang’won ahinya , kendo gibiro lemonu gi hera maduong’ .
Wago ni Nyasaye erokamano kuom mich mare modhiero ji wacho !
An Paulo koro akwayou kuom muolo kod ng’wono mar Kristo mondo uwinja . An ma uwacho ni amuol ka an kodu , to ager ka an mabor kodu ,
akwayou ni kik umi abed mager kodu , ka abiro , nikech an gi adiera ni anyalo bedo mager ni joma paro ni watimo mana gik moko mag piny !
Adier wadak e pinyni , to lweny mwakedo ok en mar piny .
Bende gilweny ma wakedogo ok gin mag piny , to gin gilweny motegno mag Nyasaye , ma wamukogo kuonde mochiel motegno . Tiende ni , waketho mbaka manono ,
kod sunga mamon gi rieko mar Nyasaye . Waketo paro duto mag dhano e tuech mondo owinj Kristo .
Bende ka uselokoru chuth , to waikore kumo ji duto ma osetamore winjo wach .
Paruru ane gik ma osetimore . Ka ng’ato paro ni en ng’at Kristo , to mano ber , to kata kamano nyaka ong’e ni wan bende wan jo-Kristo mana kaka en .
Nyalo bet ni apakora moloyo kaka owinjore , kuom teko mane Ruoth omiyowa . To Ruoth nomiyowa tekono mondo wagerugo , to ok ni mondo wakethugo , omiyo ok ane wichkuot kuom timo kamano .
Kik upar ni atemo mana buogou gi barupena .
Ng’ato nyalo wacho niya , “ Paulo ndiko barupe mager , kendo ma oting’o weche mapek , to en owuon ka en kodwa to oyomyom , kendo ok ong’eyo wuoyo . ”
To joma wacho kamano nyaka par ni , kaka awacho e barupena ka aonge kodu , e kaka anatim ka an kodu !
Ok dwahedhre pimore gi joma ting’ore malo , kata wacho ni wachopo e rang’iny ma gintie . Joma pakore kendgi , kendo nyisore kendgi , gin joma onge gi rieko .
To wan ok wanyal pakore mokadho tong’wa . En tong’ mane Nyasaye owuon ema oketonwa , kendo un bende un ei tong’no ,
omiyo kwabiro iru Korintho , to ok wakadho tong’ , nikech wan ema ne wakwongo biro iru kwakelo Wach Maber man kuom Kristo .
Ok onego wapakre kuom tich ma jomoko osetiyo kuonde mokadho tong’wa , to wageno ni kaka yie maru medo bedo motegno , duong’ mwayudo e kindu bende biro medore ahinya , mak wakadho tong’wa .
Kamano wanyalo lando Wach Maber e pinje maboyo moyombo thuru , ka ok wapakore kuom gima osetim ei tong’ mar ng’at machielo .
Muma wacho niya , “ Ng’at madwaro sungore , to mondo osungre , mana nikech gik ma Ruoth osetimo . ”
Ng’at ma Ruoth pako ema iyiego . Ng’at ma pakore kende to onge tich .
Yieuru uhore mos , nikech adwaro bedo mofuo matin ! To ang’eyo ni useyie koda .
An gi nyiego kuomu , to en mana nyiek Nyasaye . Ne amiyo umako osiep gi Kristo , kendo ne adwaro terou ire kaka ng’ato tero nyako ngili ir chwore .
To aluor ni kaka thuol nowuondo Hawa gi riekone parou bende kamoro inyalo wuondo mi uwe hero Kristo kende gi chunyu duto .
Awacho kamano nikech ka ng’ato obiro ma lando wach Nyasaye machielo , ma ok Yesu mane walando wachne , kata ka oyudo roho machielo mopogore gi Roho mane uyudo , kata Wach Maber machielo gi mano mane uyudo , to mano kaka uyiego mana mapiyopiyo !
To ok apar ni an chien kata matin kuom joote muparo ni dongogo !
Nyalo bet ni ok alony kuom wuoyo , to rieko to an-go ! Mano e gima wasenyisou kinde duto e nyim ji duto .
Kane alandonu Wach Maber mar Nyasaye , ne ok akwayo chudo moro , to adok piny mondo ating’u malo . Koro kane atimo kamano to ne atimonu marach koso ?
Ooyo , kane an kodu katiyonu ne akwayo chudo kuom kanyakla mamoko mag jo-Kristo mana ka gima amayogi !
Bende kane achando gimoro ka an kodu , to ne ok akwayo ng’ato kuomu mondo okonya , to owete mane oa Makedonia nokelona gik moko duto mane achando . Ne aritora mondo kik achandu , kendo pod abiro ritora mana kamano .
Kaka an gi adiera mar Kristo , onge gima dimona pakora kuom wachni e piny Akaya duto .
Koso uparo ni ka awuoyo kamano , to mano nyiso ni ok aherou ? Ngang’ ! Nyasaye ong’eyo ni aherou .
To abiro dhi nyime ka atimo mana gima atimo sani , mondo kik awe thuolo ni joma dwaro pakore ni gin bende gin joote kaka wan .
Joma kamago gin joote mag miriambo , kendo jotich mawuondo ji kariasore ni gin joote mag Kristo .
To mano ok en gima bwogo ng’ato , nikech kata mana Satan bende riasore ni en malaika mar ler .
Omiyo ok en wach mabwogo ji ka jotichne bende oriasore ni jotich tim makare . To e giko giniyud gima owinjore gi timgi !
Awacho kendo ni kik ng’ato gal ni afuwo , to ka ugalo kamano , to ara kawauru ka ng’ama ofuwo , mondo an bende apakra matin nono .
To ng’euru ni ka apakora kama , to ok awuo ka ja-Kristo , to awuoyo mana ka gima an ng’ama ofuwo .
Ji mathoth pakore kuom gik ma gisetimo e piny ka , koro an to ang’o ma dimona pakora kamano ?
Un uwegi un joma riek , omiyo uyie ayiea gi weche joma ofuwo !
Ka ng’ato lokou wasumbe , kata chamou , kata yakou , kata kaworenu , kata thalo lembu , to uyie ayiea !
Ayie gi achaya ma uchayowago ni wan to wasebedo manyap , ma ok watimonu gik ma kamago ! Koro awuoyo ka ng’ama ofuwo , to ka ng’ato dwaro pakore nikech wach moro , ka an bende anyalo pakora .
Gipakore ni gin jo-Hibrania koso ? To donge an ja-Hibrania mana kaka gin ? Bende gipakore ni gin jo-Israel , to an ok an ja-Israel koso ? Kendo giwacho ni gin nyikwa Ibrahim , to an bende ok an nyakwar Ibrahim ?
Koso donge gipakore ni gin jotich Kristo ? An to an jatich Kristo moloyo gi . ( Ka awacho kamano , to awuoyo ka janeko ! ) Asetiyo tich matek , kendo asebedo e od tuech , bende osechwada , kendo aseneno masiche mag tho moloyo chandruok moro amora ma gin giseneno .
Jo-Yahudi nochwada kiboko piero adek gochiko , nyadibich .
Bende jo-Rumi nogoya gi ludhe didek , kendo ne ogoya gi kite dichiel . Yie nobarorena e nam nyadidek , kendo ne ariyo e chuny nam odiechieng’ gotieno .
E wuodhena mang’eny pile ne aneno masiche e aore , kendo nayudo thagruok kuom jomecho , kendo kuom jo-Yahudi wetena kod kuom joma ok jo-Yahudi . Bende ne aneno masiche e mier , gi thim , gi nembe , kendo kuomowete mag miriambo .
Ne atiyo matek , kendo ne achandora ma ok anyal nindo kuom kinde moko , bende kech ne okaya , kendo riyo ne oloya . Kuom ndalo mang’eny ne ok ayud chiemo , kendo koyo ne chama ka achando lewni ma arwaki .
To ewi mago duto , nitie ting’ mapek ma an-go pile mar paro kanyakla duto mag jo-Kristo .
Ka ng’ato nyap , to donge an bende abedo manyap kode , kendo ka ng’ato opodho modonjo e richo , to donge litna ?
Ka ochuna ni nyaka apakra to abiro pakora nikech weche manyiso nyawona .
Nyasaye ma Wuon Ruoth Yesu ma ipako nyaka chieng’ ema ong’eyo ni ok ariambi .
Neuru ! Kane an Damaski , jatelo manie bwo ruoth Aretas ne oketo jorit e dhoranga dala mondo omaka ,
to ne awuok gie otuch manie kor ohinga , kilora piny gi osera , mi atony e lwete !
Ochuna ni nyaka apakra , kata obedo ni ok kony gimoro kamano . To koro abiro wuoyo kuom fweny maseneno kod weche mopondo ma Ruoth oseelona .
Ang’eyo ja-Kristo moro mane oter e polo mar adek , higni apar gang’wen mokadho . ( Ok ang’eyo ka ringre ema ne oter kuno , kata ne oneno mana fweny . )
Awacho kendo ni ang’eyo ni ng’atno noter e Paradis . ( To ok ang’eyo kata gino notimore adier , kata ne en mana fweny . Nyasaye kende ema ong’eyo . )
Ng’at ma kamano ema nyalo miyo apakra , to ok abi pakora nikech an awuon , to mak mana ni abiro pakora kuom nyawona
To ka dabed ni adwaro pakora , to ok dabedo ng’ama ofuwo , nikech dawacho mana adiera . To ok anyal pakora , nimar ok adwar ni mondo ng’ato opaka moloyo gima oseneno katimo , kata ma owinjo ka awacho .
Emomiyo ne omiya kudho machwowo ringra , ma en jaote mar Satan , mondo omonja kik asungra , kata kik ating’ra malo nikech duong’ miwuoro mar gik mane Nyasaye ofwenyona .
Ne asayo Ruoth didek mondo ogol wachni kuoma ,
to nowachona niya , “ Mich ma amiyi kuom ng’wonona oromi , nikech kama nyawo nitie ema teko tiyoe moloo . ” Emomiyo amor ahinya pakora nikech nyawona , mondo teko mar Kristo odag kuoma .
Mano omiyo ayie nyawo , kata achaya , kata chandruok , kata sand , kata thagruok , nikech Kristo , nimar ka wanyap , to eka watek .
Atimora ka ng’ama ofuwo , to un ema usemiyo abedo kamano . Ne onego upwoya , nimar kata obedo ni ok an gimoro , to joote muparo ni dongogo ok oloya kata matin .
Ne anyisou ni an jaote maradier katimonu ranyisi gi honni kod tije madongodongo , ka adhil gi chandruok kod masiche .
Koro ere yo mane kanyakla mamoko mag jo-Kristo oloyougo , mak mana ni an awuon ema ne ok akwayou mondo ukonya ? Ka uneno ni mano en ketho , to ara yieuru ung’wonna kuom kethonano !
Koro aikora mondo abi iru e limbena mar adek , to pod ok nadwar mondo ukonya , nikech ok mwanduu ema adwaro , to adwaro mana un uwegi . Nyithindo ok onego ken ni jonywolgi , to jonywol ema keno ni nyithindgi .
An to ayie chiworanu gi mor , katiyonu gi tekra duto . To ka an aherou ahinya kamano , koro mano dimi uhera mana matin koso ?
Ung’eyo ni ne ok akwayou mondo ukonya , to pod ubiro wacho ni ne ahoyou , mi amakou gi rieko .
To joma ne aoro iru ne amiyo omayou gimoro koso ?
Adier , ne akwayo Tito mondo obi iru , kendo ne aore gi owadwa machielo cha . To Tito nomayou gimoro koso ? Donge wan gi Tito ne wawuotho gi Roho achiel , kendo e yo achiel ?
Kamoro uparo ni watemo doko joma beyo e nyimu kwandikonu wechegi duto ! Ooyo , wawuoyo mana e nyim Nyasaye , ka wan kuom Kristo . Osiepena , gik moko duto mwatimo , watimo mana ni mondo wagergo chunyu .
Aluor ni ka abiro to dipo ka anwang’o ka ok uchal kaka adwaro , kendo un bende dipo ka unwang’o ni ok achal kaka udwaro ! Aluor ni dhaw gi nyiego gi mirima gi ichlit gi ajara gi kuoth gi sunga kod koko nyalo betie .
Bende aluor ni ka abiro to Nyasacha dipo ka omiya bedo gi wichkuot e nyimu , mi dabed gi kuyo nikech joma thoth mane oketho , to otamore lokore kuom tim ma ok ler mane gisebedo ka gitimo , kaka terruok kod anjawo .
Koro abiro iru e limbena mar adek . Muma wacho ni weche duto nyaka ng’ere e nyim joneno adek kata ariyo .
E limbena mar ariyo kane an kodu , ne asiemo jogo mane osetimo richo , kendo ne asiemo ji mamoko bende . To koro anwoyonigi wachno ka aonge kodu , ni , ka abiro , to ok nawe mak akumogi .
Eka unung’e adier ni Kristo ema miya teko mar wuoyo . En ok onyap ka otiyo e kindu , to otiyo gi teko kuomu .
Adier ne oyie bedo manyap kigure , to koro ongima kuom teko mar Nyasaye . Wan bende wayie bedo manyap kode , to teko mar Nyasaye nomi wabed mangima kode mondo watinu .
Nonreuru pile mondo une ane ka un gi yie . Adier , ng’ireuru uwegi ! Donge ung’eyo ni Yesu Kristo nie iu , mak mana ka un joma orem ?
To ageno ni ung’eyo ni wan to ok warem .
Walamo Nyasaye ni mondo kik udonji e richo . To ok walem kamano ni mondo wanyisgo ni wan kare , to mana ni mondo utim gik mabeyo , kata obedo ni wachalo joma orem kamano .
Ok wanyal timo gimoro ma digeng’ adiera , to mana makonyo adiera .
To wamor ka wanyap , to un utek . Chutho gima walemone en ni mondo ubed joma kare e yore duto .
Mano emomiyo andiko wechegi ka aonge kodu , ni mondo ka abiro , to kik abed mager katiyo gi teko mane Ruoth omiya , ma en teko mar gerou , to ok mar kethou .
Koro oritu owetena ! Temuru mondo ubed joma kare , kuwinjo wechena . Beduru gi winjruok , kendo gi kue , eka Nyasach hera kod kue nobed kodu .
Yogreuru gi mos mar jo-Nyasaye . Jo-Nyasaye duto omosou .
Ng’wono mar Ruoth Yesu Kristo , gi hera mar Nyasaye , gi achiel ma wan-go kuom Roho Maler obed kodu uduto .
An Paulo kaachiel gi owete duto ma wan-go wandikonu un kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Galatia . An Paulo , andiko kaka jaote ma ok teko mar dhano ema oketo , nikech onge ng’ama ne oketa jaote , to mana Yesu Kristo , gi Nyasaye Wuoro mane ochiere oa kuom joma otho ema ne oketa .
Ng’wono gi kue moa kuom Nyasaye wuoro gi Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo obed kodu .
Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo ema ne ochiwore owuon nikech richowa , mondo oreswa e piny marach ma kawuononi , koyie timo kaka Nyasaye Wuonwa dwaro .
Duong’ obed ni Nyasaye nyaka chieng’ . Amin .
Awuoro kaka uselokoru piyopiyo uweyo Nyasaye mane oluongou kuom ng’wono mar Kristo , kendo koro uluwo Wach Maber machielo mopogore .
To chutho onge Wach Maber moro machielo , to nitie jomoko machandou katemo loko Wach Maber mar Kristo obed gimoro nono .
To kata ka ng’ato dipuonju Wach Maber machielo ma ok mano mane wapuonjou , bed ni en wan , kata mana malaika mar polo , to Nyasaye mondo okuong’e .
Kaka ne wawacho chon , e kaka amedo wacho ni , ka ng’ato opuonjou Wach Maber machielo mopogore gi mane uyudo , to Nyasaye mondo okuong’e .
Koso uparo ni mano nenore ka gima adwaro ni mondo abed malong’o e nyim dhano ? Ooyo , adwaro bedo malong’o e nyim Nyasaye ! Koso uparo ni adwaro mondo dhano ema obed mamor koda ? To ka da bed ni pod atemo timo kamano , to da ok abedo jatich Kristo .
Owetena , adwaro ni mondo ung’e ni Wach Maber ma alando ok owuok kuom dhano .
Adier , ne ok ayude kuom dhano , bende onge ng’ama ne opuonjago , to Yesu Kristo owuon ema ne ofwenyonago .
Nyaka bed ni usewinjo kaka timna ne chalo kane pod aluwo dini mar jo-Yahudi . Ung’eyo kaka ne asando kanyakla mar joma oyie kuom Nyasaye malit , katemo matek mondo atiekgi chuth ,
kendo kaka ne aloyo mbesena mathoth ma jo-Yahudi e tich dini mar jo-Yahudi , kaketo chunya e tich kwerewa .
To Nyasaye , mane owala kane pok onywola , ne oluonga kuom ng’wonone mondo atine . Kuom mano , e kinde mane oneno ni ber
mondo ofwenyna Wuode aland Wachne Maber ni joma ok jo-Yahudi , to ne ok apenjo dhano gima onego atim .
Bende ne ok adhi kata mana Jerusalem ir jogo mane okwongona bedo joote , to mokwongo ne adhi e piny Arabia , eka bang’e nadok Damaski .
To kata bang’ higni adek , kane adhi Jerusalem mondo ane Petro , mi abet kode kuom ndalo apar gabich ,
to ne ok aneno joote mamoko , mak mana ong’Jakobo ma owadgi Ruoth .
Akuong’ora e nyim Nyasaye , ni weche ma andikonugi gin adier !
Bang’e ne adhi e gwenge moko mag Siria gi Kilikia .
E ndalogo kanyakla mag jo-Kristo man Judea ne pok ong’eya gi kita ,
to ne giwinjo mana ka ji wacho ni , “ Jal mane sandowa , tinde lando Wach Maber mane otemo mondo otieki ! ”
Kuom mano ne gimiyo Nyasaye duong’ nikech an .
Bang’ higni apar gang’wen , ne achako adok Jerusalem , ka wan gi Barnaba , kendo Tito bende ne wadhigo .
Ne adhi nikech Nyasaye nonyisa ni mondo adhi , mi achokora gi jodong kanyakla mar jo-Kristo kar kendgi , kendo nanyisogi Wach Maber ma alando ni joma ok jo-Yahudi , nimar ne ok adwar ni mondo tich mane asebedo ka atiyo , kata mapod atiyo , obed kayiem nono .
To kata mana Tito mane jawuodha ne ok ochun mondo oter nyangu , kata obedo ni ne ok en ja-Yahudi kamano .
To mak mana jomoko mane obiro kanyo kawuondore ni gin owete , ema ne dwaro ni mondo otere nyangu . Jogo ne obiro ling’ling’ mondo ocher ane ni thuolo manade ma wan-go kuom bedo jo-Kristo , nikech ne gidwaro lokowa wasumbni .
To ne ok wayie winjo wachgi kata matin , mondo adiera mar Injili kik lalnu .
To jogo mane onenore ka jotelo ne ok omiya wach moro manyien . ( Awacho ni ne ginenore ka jotelo , nikech ok adewo gima gin , nimar Nyasaye ok odewo nenruok maoko mar dhano . )
Kar kelo wach moro manyien , to ne gineno ni Nyasaye osemiya tich lando Injili ni joma ok jo-Yahudi , mana kaka nomiyo Petro tich lando Injili ni jo-Yahudi .
Ne giyie ni Nyasaye mane omiyo Petro teko mar bedo jaote ni jo-Yahudi , ema bende ne omiya teko mar bedo jaote ni joma ok jo-Yahudi .
Kuom mano , Jakobo gi Petro kod Johana , ma ji oyiego ni jotelo mag kanyakla mar jo-Kristo , nong’eyo mich mane Nyasaye osemiya kuom ng’wonone , mi gimako lwet Barnaba kod lweta kaka ranyisi ni wariwore kodgi e tich . Ne wawinjore waduto ni wan wadhi ir joma ok jo-Yahudi to gin gidhi ir jo-Yahudi .
To ne gidwaro mana ni mondo wapar jochan , ma en gima an bende ne aseketo chunya ahinya mondo atim .
To kane Petro obiro Antiokia , ne akwere mana e wang’e , nikech kethone ne nenore ratiro .
Ne othoro chiemo gi owete ma ok jo-Yahudi , kane pok jomoko moa kuom Jakobo obiro , to kane jogo obiro , to nong’wony moweyogi , nikech noluoro joma ne dwaro mondo oter joma ok jo-Yahudi nyangu .
Jo-Yahudi moko mane ni kuno bende noriwore kode e ndhogruok ma kamano , mi kata mana Barnaba bende ne ndhogruokgino oywayo !
To kane aneno ni timgino ok oluwore gi adiera mar Injili , ne awacho ni Petro e nyimgi duto niya , “ In , in ja-Yahudi , to iluwo tim joma ok jo-Yahudi , koro marang’o ichuno joma ok jo-Yahudi mondo olu tim jo-Yahudi ? ”
Chutho , wan wawegi nonywolwa jo-Yahudi , kendo ok wan joogendini mamoko ma joricho .
To kata kamano , wang’eyo ni mako Chik Musa ok nyal miyo ng’ato bed e winjruok gi Nyasaye , to mana yie kuom Yesu Kristo ema miyo ng’ato bedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye . Wan bende waseyie kuom Kristo Yesu , mondo wabed e winjruok gi Nyasaye kuom yie , to ok kuom mako Chik , nimar Muma wacho ni , “ Onge ng’ama nyalo bet e winjruok gi Nyasaye kuom mako Chik . ”
To ka wadwaro ni mondo wabed e winjruok gi Nyasaye kuom Kristo , to eka pod iyudo ni wan joricho mana kaka joma ok jo-Yahudi , koro uparo ni mano nyiso Kristo konyo tich richo koso ?
Ng’ang’ ! Ka achako luwo yor Chik ma en yo ma aseweyo chuth ni onge gi tich , to mano nyiso ni an jaketh Chik !
Korka Chik to an ng’ama otho , ma Chik owuon ema onego , mondo obed mangima ni Nyasaye . Ne ogura gi Kristo e msalape ,
mi koro ok an ema angima , to Kristo ema ngima e iya , kendo ngima ma koro an-goni , an-go mana nikech yie ma ayiego kuom Wuod Nyasaye , mane ohera , mi ochiwo ngimane nikech an .
Ok adwar miyo mich ma Nyasaye ochiwo kuom ng’wonone obed kayiem nono . To ka en adier ni mako Chik ema miyo ng’ato bedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye , to kara Kristo notho kayiem nono !
Yaye , un jo-Galatia mofuwogi ! Ng’ano moseirou , un mane onyisu wach tho Yesu ratiro , mana ka gima ogure e msalaba e wang’u kunenoni ?
Dwokauru ane wach achielni : Uparo ni ne uyudo Roho nikech ne urito Chik , koso nikech ne uyie Wach Maber mane olandnu ?
Bende en adier ni ufuwo kamano ? Ne uchako ngimau manyien kuom Roho mar Nyasaye , to koro uparo ni unyalo miyo ngimano bedo malong’o chuth gi tekou uwegi koso ?
Gik madongo duto mane otimorenugi osebet kayiem nono koso ? Ooyo , ok apar ni mano nyalo bedo kamano !
Uparo ni Nyasaye chiwonu Rohone mogundho , kendo timo honni madongo e kindu , nikech umako Chik , koso nikech uyie Wach Maber mane uwinjo ?
Muma wacho niya , “ Ibrahim noyie kuom Nyasaye , mi yieneno ema ne omiyo Nyasaye okwane ni en ng’ama kare . ”
Kuom mano , nyaka ung’eni joma oyie e nyithind Ibrahim maradier .
Muma wuoyo kuom Ibrahim niya , “ Kuomi ema Nyasaye nogwedhie ogendini duto mag piny . ” Kamano ne onyise Wach Maber chon ni Nyasaye nomi joma ok jo-Yahudi bed e winjruok kode kuom yie .
Omiyo kaka Ibrahim noyie , mi oguedhe , e kaka ji duto moyie bende oguedhi .
To jogo moyiengore kuom rito Chik kaka gima miyo gibedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye nie bwo kuong’ , nikech Muma wacho niya , “ Okuong’ ng’ato ang’ata ma ok osiko omako weche duto mondiki e kitap Chik ! ”
Ong’ere malong’o ni onge ng’ama Chik miyo obet e winjruok gi Nyasaye , nimar Muma wacho bende ni , “ Ng’at ma obedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye nikech oyie ema nobed mangima . ”
To Chik ok otenore kuom yie ngang’ , nikech Muma wacho niya , “ Ng’ama otimo gik ma Chik dwaro ema nobed mangima kuom Chik . ”
To Kristo nowarowa kuom kuong’ ma Chik kelo , kane odoko ng’ama okuong’ nikech wan , nimar Muma wacho niya , “ Okuong’ ng’ato ang’ata ma olier e yath . ”
Gigo notimore kamano mondo gueth mane Nyasaye osingore ni Ibrahim obi ni joma ok jo-Yahudi kuom Kristo Yesu , kendo mondo wayud Roho mane Nyasaye osingore ni nochiw ni joma oyie .
Owetena , weuru amiue ranyisi mar gima timore pilepile . Ka ji ariyo otimo winjruok mi osingore , to onge ng’ama nyalo ketho winjruokgino , kata medoe wach moro , kata obedo ni en mana winjruok mae kind dhano gi dhano kamano .
To Muma wacho ni Nyasaye notimo singruok gi Ibrahim kendo gi nyakware . Ok owacho ni , gi nyikwaye , tiende ni , ji mang’eny , to owacho ni , gi nyakware , tiende ni , ng’at achiel kende , ma en Kristo .
Tiend gima awacho e ma : Nyasaye notimo winjruok , mi osingore ni norit winjruokno . Kuom mano , Chik mane obiro bang’ higni mia ang’wen gi piero adek ok nyal ketho winjruokno , kendo mi singruok mane Nyasaye otimo bed kayiem nono ,
nikech ka gik ma Nyasaye chiwo iyudo mana kuom Chik , to kara koro ok yudgi kuom singruok . To wang’eyo ni Nyasaye nochiwo michne ni Ibrahim e yor singruok .
Koro ere gima omiyo oket Chik Musa ? Nokete mondo onyis ketho , kendo mana ni mondo obedie nyaka chop nyakwar Ibrahim mane otimne singruok bi . To bende kane Nyasaye ooro Chik Musa , nomiyo malaika mondo okel , mi malaika nokete e lwet jaote ,
to kane Nyasaye omiyo Ibrahim singruok , to notiyo kende , maonge jaote .
To Chik mon gi singruok mar Nyasaye koso ? Ooyo , ok kamano , nikech ka dine bed ni chik moro nyalo kelo ngima , to kara dhano dobet e winjruok gi Nyasaye kuom chik .
To Muma osewacho ni piny duto nie bwo loch mar richo , mondo singruok motenore kuom yie kuom Kristo omi mana joma oyie .
Kane pok ndalo mar yie obiro , to ne wasiko kotuewa e bwo Chik , nyaka chop ne oelnwa yie mane onego bino .
Kamano Chik nokelonwa jarit , nyaka Kristo nobiro mondo omi wabed e winjruok gi Nyasaye kuom yie .
To koro ka yie osebiro , to tich jarit orumo ,
nimar kuom yie uduto un nyithind Nyasaye kuom Yesu Kristo .
Kuom mano onge pogruok e kind jo-Yahudi , kata e kind wasumbini gi joma ni thuolo , kata e kind chwo gi mon , nikech uduto un achiel kuom Kristo .
To ka un jo-Kristo , to kara un nyikwa Ibrahim , kendo unuyud mich mane Nyasaye osingore .
Tiend gima awacho e ma : Wuowi nyalo bedo jacham gikeni duto mag wuon mare , to ka pod en nyathi , to oonge pogruok gi misumba ,
nikech pod en e bwo joma rite gi joma ochung’ne nyaka chop kinde mane wuon mare oketo .
Kamano wan bende , kane pod wan nyithindo , ne oketwa wasumbini mag timbe machon mag piny .
To kane ndalo mowinjore ochopo , Nyasaye nooro Wuode owuon . Wuodeno , dhako ema nonywolo , mi odak e bwo Chik Musa ,
mondo owar joma nie bwo Chik , eka wabed yawuot Nyasaye .
To Nyasaye ne dwaro nyisou ni un yawuote , omiyo nooro Roho mar Wuode e chunywa . En Roho maywak ni , “ Baba ! Wuora ! ”
Kuom mano , koro ok in misumba , to in wuowi . To kaka in wuod Nyasaye , en owuon obiro miyo ichamo gikeni mokano ni yawuote .
E kinde machon ne ok ung’eyo Nyasaye , omiyo ne un wasumbini mag gik moko ma ok nyiseche kata matin .
To koro kaka ung’eyo Nyasaye , ( to moloyo onego awachi ni koro kaka Nyasaye ong’eyou , ) ere kaka udok e timbe machon mag piny , manyap kendo modhiergo , mondo uchak ubed wasumbgi kendo ?
Ka urito ndalo gi dueye gi higni kamano ,
to umiya luoro ni mita dipo kane atiyonu kayiem nono !
Owetena , akwayou ni mondo ubed ka an , nikech an bende asebedo mana machal kodu , kendo pok utimona gimoro marach .
To ung’eyo ni e limbena mokwongo , tuo mane atuogo ema ne omiyo adong’ , mi alandonu Injili .
To kata obedo ni ne atuo kamano , to ne ok uchaya , kendo ne ok udaga , to ne urwaka mana ka gima urwako malaika , kata ka gima urwako Kristo Yesu .
Tinde to ere mor mane un-go cha ? Awacho adier ni ang’eyo ni ka dine unyalo , to dine ugolo wengeu oko mi umiya .
To koro asedoko jasiku nikech awachonu adiera koso ?
Jomokogo to hoyou ka miyou duong’ to chunyi ok ber kodu . Gidwaro mana ni mondo gipogu koda ,
mondo un bende umigi duong’ kuom wach maber , to ok mana ni ka an kodu kende .
Nyithinda , awinjo rem mana ka dhako ma muoch kayo , mondo anyuolu kendo , nyaka chop chue Kristo e iu .
Mano kaka agombo ni mondo abed kodu koro , mondo ang’e gima dawachnu , nimar adhier nono nikech un !
Adwaro penjo joma dwaro bedo e bwo Chik ka gisewinjo gima Chik wacho ?
Donge owacho ni Ibrahim ne nigi yawuowi ariyo ? Achiel ne wuod dhako ma misumba , to machielo ne wuod dhako man thuolo .
Wuod dhako ma misumbano nonywol kuom dwaro mar dhano , to wuod dhako man thuolo nonywol mondo singruok mar Nyasaye ochopi .
To wachno nigi tiende mopondo kama : Mon ariyogo ochung’ kar singruok ariyo . Hagar en dhako mane onywolo nyithinde e tich misumba , kendo ochung’ kar singruok mane otim e got Sinai ,
ma en got manie piny Arabia . Kamano Hagar ochung’ kar Jerusalem ma ndalogi , manie tich misumba gi joge duto ,
To dhako man thuolo ochung’ kar Jerusalem manie polo , kendo en e minwa ,
mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ In dhako ma migumba mane ok onywol , bed mamor ! Ting’ dwondi ikog gi mor , in mane muoch ok okayi , nikech dhako ma chwore oweyo nobed gi nyithindo mang’eny , moloyo dhako modak gi chwore . ”
Koro owetena , un nyithind Nyasaye kuom singruokne , mana kaka Isaka nobet .
E kindeno , wuowi mane onywol kuom dwaro mar dhano ne osando jal mane onywol kuom Roho mar Nyasaye , kendo kamano e kaka obet e ndalogi .
To ere gima Muma wacho ? Owacho niya , “ Riemb dhako ma misumba gi wuode , nikech wuod dhako ma misumba ok nocham mwandu gi wuod dhako man thuolo . ”
Kuom mano , owetena , ok wan nyithind dhako ma misumba , to wan nyithind dhako man thuolo .
Kristo nogonyowa mondo wabed joma ni thuolo . Omiyo chung’uru motegno , mondo kik uyie chak rwak ng’utu e jok mar bedo misumba kendo .
An Paulo awachonu ni , ka oteru nyangu , to Kristo ok nokonyu kata matin .
Achako awacho kendo ni , ng’ato ka ng’ato moter nyangu nigi gowi mar mako Chik Musa duto te .
Ka udwaro mondo ubed e winjruok gi Nyasaye kuom mako Chik , to usepogoru gi Kristo , kendo usea kuom ng’wono mar Nyasaye .
Wan to Roho ema miyo wageno ni ibiro miyo wabedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye kuom yie ,
nimar ka wan kuom Kristo Yesu , to bedo moter nyangu , kata bedo ma ok oter nyangu , ok kony gimoro , to gimoro achiel kende madwarore en mana yie matiyo kuom hera .
Ne onwang’o uchako maber . Ng’ano mane otamou mondo kik uwinj adiera ? Ere kaka ne osemou ?
Sem ma kamano ne ok oa kuom Nyasaye ma luongou !
Paruru ngero mawacho ni , thowi matin kuodo mogo duto modwal .
An gi geno kuomu kuom Ruoth ni ok nurwak paro moro mayore , to ng’ato ang’ata machando parou noyud kum kuom Nyasaye , bed ni en ng’ama nade !
Owetena , ka en adier ni pod apuonjo ni nyaka ter ji nyangu , to ere gima omiyo pod isanda ? Ka da bed ni en adier ni pod apuonjo ni nyaka ter ji nyangu , to kara puonj ma apuonjogo wach msalap Yesu da ok ochwanyo ji !
To joma chando parou onego odhi mondo orore !
To un owetena , noluongu mondo ubed thuolo , to kik uwe mondo thuolo ma un-gono mi utim gimoro amora mudwaro , to ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu mondo okony wadgi kuom hera ,
nikech chik duto ichopo e wach achiel niya , “ Her wadu kaka iherori iwuon . ”
To ka ukaru kendo ukidhoru kendu mana ka ondiegi , to nyaka utang’ , nono to utiekoru pep !
To gima awachonu e ma : Wuothuru kuom Roho , eka ok unutim gik ma ngima mar dhano gombo ,
nikech gombo mar ngima dhano kedo gi dwaro mar Roho , kendo dwaro mar Roho kedo gi gombo mar ngima dhano . Gik moko ariyogo monre , omiyo ok unyal timo gik mudwaro timo .
To ka Roho otelonu , to ok un e bwo Chik .
Timbe mag ngima dhano nenore ratiro . Gin terruok , tim ma ok ler , anjawo ,
lamo nyiseche manono , jwok , sigu , dhaw , nyiego , mirima , ichlit , miero , pogruok e kanyakla ,
gombo , mer , dwanyruok , kod gik moko machal kamago . To asiemou , kaka nasiemou chon ni , joma timo gik ma kamago ok noyud gueth mar Loch Nyasaye .
To gik ma Roho nyago gin : hera , mor , kue , horuok , ng’wono , ber , bedo jaadiera ,
muolo , kod ritruok . Onge chik makwedo gik ma kamago .
Joma oyie kuom Kristo Yesu oseguro gombo mag ngima mar dhano kod herane marach e msalaba .
Ka wabedo mangima kuom Roho , to ber mondo wawuothuru bende kuom Roho .
Waweuru wuorruok , kendo kik wakwinyre , bende kik ng’ato tim nyiego gi wadgi .
Owetena , kata ka oyud ng’ato rando katimo gimoro marach , to un ma uwuotho kuom Roho nyaka utem mondo urieye gi chuny mamuol , kuritoru mondo un bende kik udonj e tem ma kamano .
Kawuru ting’ mag jowadu , nikech kutimo kamano to uchopo chik mar Kristo .
Ka ng’ato galo ni en gimoro , ka ok en gimoro , to owuondore owuon .
To ng’ato ka ng’ato mondo onon tije owuon , ma ok odewo gima ng’ato machielo osetimo ,
nimar ng’ato ka ng’ato nigi ting’ne owuon .
Ber mondo ng’at ma ipuonjo wach Kristo okony japuonjne , kopogone gik mabeyo duto ma en-go .
Kik uwuondru , nikech ok unyal wuondo Nyasaye ! To ng’euru ni ng’ato ka ng’ato noka mana gima ochwoyo .
Ng’at ma ochuoyo kuom gombo mag ngima dhano , noka tho kuom ngima mar dhano , to ng’ama ochuoyo kuom Roho , noka ngima mochwere kuom Roho .
Kuom mano , kik waol gi timo gik mabeyo , nikech ka ok wanyosore , to wanake , ka ndalo , ka ndalo ogik .
Emomiyo , kinde moro amora mwayudoe thuolo , to ber mondo watim ni ji duto maber , to moloyo ni jogo ma owetewa kuom yie .
Neyeuru kaka andikonu awuon gi nukta madongo !
Jogo madwaro doko malong’o kapakore kuom tim ringruok , e joma temo chunou mondo oteru nyangu . To gitimo kamano mana ni mondo kik giyud sand ma digiyudo ka gilando wach msalap Kristo .
To kata mana jogo moramo ni nyaka ter ji nyangu ok mak Chik , to gidwaro ni mondo oteru nyangu mana ni mondo gipakre kuom gima otim e ringreu .
An to ok anyal pakora kuom gimoro mak mana kuom msalap Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo , mosemiyo piny ochalona ka gima ogur e msalaba , kendo ma osemiyo an bende achalo ni piny ka ng’ama ogur e msalaba .
Kata ka oter ng’ato nyangu , kata ka ok oter , to mano ok gimoro , to gima dwarore en mana ni mondo ng’ato ochue chwech manyien .
Kue gi ng’wono obed kod ji duto maluwo chikni , tiende ni jo-Israel maradier mar Nyasaye .
Nyaka a kawuono , kik ng’ato chak chanda , nimar mbelni ma an-go e ringra nyiso ni an misumba Yesu .
Owetena , ng’wono mar Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo obed kodu . Amin .
An Paulo , jaote mar Yesu Kristo kuom dwaro mar Nyasaye , andikonu un jo-Nyasaye man Efeso , ma un joma oyie kuom Kristo Yesu .
Ng’wono gi kue moa kuom Nyasaye Wuonwa gi Ruoth Yesu Kristo , obed kodu .
Wagouru erokamano ni Nyasaye ma wuon Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo , nimar oseguedhowa , wan ma wan kuom Kristo , komiyowa mich duto mag Roho moa e polo .
Kuom herane , noyierowa kuom Kristo kapok ochue piny , mondo wabed maler kendo maonge mbala e nyime .
Nowalowa chon mondo wadok yawuote kuom Yesu Kristo , nikech mano e kaka ne odwaro , kendo omorgo .
Ne otimo kamano mondo ji opak ng’wonone man gi duong’ mane otimonwa kuom Wuode mohero .
Nyasaye oseweyonwa richowa , kendo osewarowa nikech tho mar Kristo . Mano kaka mich
ma Nyasaye oseolo kuomwa kuom ng’wonone ogundho ! Kuom riekone gi ng’eyone ,
oseelonwa dwarone mopondo , tiende ni oseelonwa gik mane ochano chon kuom ng’wonone , mondo otim kuom Kristo ka ndalo ogik kare .
Osechano mondo oriw gik moko duto manie polo kod manie piny obed e achiel kuom Kristo .
Nyasaye , mochano gik moko duto mondo obed kaka odwaro nyaka a chakruok , noyierowa wan jo-Yahudi mondo wabed joge owuon kuom Kristo .
Notimo kamano mondo wan jo-Yahudi mane wakuongonu geno kuom Kristo , un joma ok jo-Yahudi , wami ji opak duong’ne maler .
Kamano e kaka un joma ok jo-Yahudi bende ne uwinjo wach mar adiera , ma en Wach Maber mane okelonu warruok , mi uyie kuom Kristo , kendo Nyasaye nomiyou Roho Maler mane osingore ni nomiu , kaka ranyisi ni un joge .
Roho e singo ma nyiso ni wananwang’ gik ma Nyasaye osesingore ni nomi joge , kendo omiyo wabedo gi adier ni Nyasaye nowar joge chuth , mondo ji opak duong’ne maler .
Mano emomiyo kane awinjo wach yie ma un-go kuom Ruoth Yesu , kod hera muherogo jo-Nyasaye duto ,
ne achako goyo ni Nyasaye erokamano nikech un , bende pok aweyo timo kamano . Alemonu
ka akwayo Wuoro ma wuon duong’ duto , kendo ma Nyasach Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo , mondo omiu Roho makelonu rieko kendo fwenyonu gik moko mondo ung’eye .
Akwayo ni chunyu oyawre mondo ung’e gima ugeno moseluongoue kendo ung’e kaka guethne mosesingore ni nomi joge ogundho ,
bende mondo ung’e teko maduong’ matiyo kuomwa , wan joma oyie kuome . Mano e teko maduong’
mane otiyogo kochiero Kristo oa kuom joma otho , mi oketo e bade korachwich e polo .
Kristo nigi loch kuno kuom ruodhi mag polo duto , kendo kuom teko duto , gi loch duto , gi duong’ duto , kod nying moro amora minyalo luongi , ok e pinyni kende , to e piny mabiro bende .
Nyasaye noketo gik moko duto e teko Kristo , kendo nomiyo Kristo obedo wi kanisa , ma en kanyakla mar ji duto moyie kuom Kristo .
Kanyakla mar joma oyie kuom Kristo en ringre Kristo , kendo ka ringruok oriwore gi wich , to Jal mamiyo gik moko duto chopo kare , bende chopo kare en owuon !
Chon ne un joma otho nikech kethou kod richou .
E ndalogo , yore richo ema ne uwuothoe , kuluwo timbe mag pinyni . Ne uwinjo wach ruodh teko mar kind polo gi piny , ma en chuny ma koro tiyo kuom joma otamore yie kuom Nyasaye .
Chutho waduto ne wachal kodgi , kane watimo gik ma ngima mar dhano gombo , kendo watimo gimoro amora ma ringrewa gi parowa dwaro . Kamano wan bende ne onego Nyasaye kumwa gi mirimbe nikech timbewa , mana kaka obiro kumo jomoko .
To Nyasaye noherowa ahinya , omiyo nonyisowa kaka ng’wonone ogundho ,
nimar kata obedo ni ne wan joma otho kamano nikech richowa , to nomiyo wadoko mangima kaachiel gi Kristo . Ng’wonone ema omiyo oseresou !
Adier , nochierowa kaachiel gi Kristo Yesu , kendo nomiyo wabedo kaachiel kode e polo .
Notimo kamano mondo onyisgo tienge duto mabiro mwandu mogundho mar ng’wonone mane omiyowa kuom hera maduong’ mane oherowago kuom Kristo Yesu .
Ne uyie kuome mi oresou mana kuom ng’wonone , to ok kuom gik mane utimo un uwegi . En mana mich mar Nyasaye !
Ne ok owaru nikech gimoro amora ma usetimo , omiyo kik ng’ato pakre .
Wan chuech manyien mar Nyasaye . Nochueyowa kuom Kristo Yesu mondo wabed joma timo timbe mabeyo , mane Nyasaye owuon oikonwa mondo watim .
Paruru ni ne un joma ok jo-Yahudi kuom anywola . Chutho , jogo mong’ere kaka joma oter nyangu nikech gima otim gi lwedo e ringregi , ne luongou ni joma ok oter nyangu .
Bende paruru ni e kindego ne uonge gi Mesia . Ne ok un e kanyakla mar oganda jo-Israel . Kamano ne ok un kuom joma Nyasaye otimogo winjruok , kosingore ni obiro guedhogi , kendo ne udak e pinyni ka uonge gi geno , kendo ka uonge gi Nyasaye .
To koro kuom Kristo Yesu , un ma yande un mabor , osekelu machiegni kuom tho mar Kristo .
Kristo owuon e kue marwa , nikech oseriwo jo-Yahudi gi joma ok jo-Yahudi odoko oganda achiel . Kuom chiwo ringre owuon , osemuko ohinga mar sigu mane opogowa ,
kendo osetieko Chik Musa gi wechene duto . Osetimo mago duto mondo oriw ogendini ariyo obed achiel kuome , mondo kue obedie .
Ne otho e msalaba mondo otiek sigu mae kindwa , kendo otimwa ringruok achiel kuom Nyasaye .
Ne obiro molando Wach Maber mar kue ni un joma ok jo-Yahudi mane ni mabor gi Nyasaye , kendo ni jo-Yahudi mane ni machiegni kode .
Kuom Kristo ema wan waduto , wanie gi thuolo mar dhiyo e nyim Wuoro kuom Roho achiel .
Emomiyo koro ok un welo kata jodak to un e oganda achiel gi jo-Nyasaye , kendo un jood Nyasaye .
Un bende osegeru ewi mise mane joote kod johul wach moa kuom Nyasaye oketo , ka Kristo owuon ema obedo kidi motegno moriwo kor ot .
Kimedo gero ot , to en ema omako ot duto , komiyo obet Hekalu maler kuom Ruoth .
Un bende igerou kuome kaachiel kodwa mondo ubed kar dak mar Nyasaye kuom Roho .
Mano emomiyo an Paulo , ng’at motue mar Kristo Yesu nikech un joma ok jo-Yahudi , agoyo chonga piny mondo alem .
Ang’eyo ni usewinjo kaka Nyasaye osemiya tich mar landonu Wach Maber kuom ng’wonone ,
kendo kaka nofwenyona wach moro mopondo mane osechano chon . ( Asendiko matin kuom wachni ,
kendo ka usomo gima asendiko , to unyalo neno ni ang’eyo wach mane opondo man kuom Kristo . )
E ndalo machon , ne ok nyis ji wach mopondono , to koro Nyasaye oseele gi teko mar Roho ni jootene maler kod johul wach .
To wach mopondono en ni , kaluwore gi Wach Maber , to joma ok jo-Yahudi , chamo gikeni kodwa wan jo-Yahudi , kendo gin ringruok achiel kodwa , bende giriwore kodwa e singruok mane Nyasaye ochopo kuom Kristo Yesu .
Nyasaye noketa jatich Wach Maber kuom mich mar ng’wonone mane omiya kuom tekone .
An e ng’ama tinie ahinya moloyo jo-Nyasaye duto , to Nyasaye notimona ng’wono , momiya tich mar lando ni joma ok jo-Yahudi Wach Maber mar mwandu mogundho mar Kristo .
Bende nomiya tich mar miyo ji duto ng’eyo kaka weche mopondo mag Nyasaye tiyo . Nyaka nene , Nyasaye ma Jachuech gik moko duto nopando wachne ni tienge machon duto ,
mondo koro kuom kanyakla mar jo-Kristo , omi joloch gi weg teko manie polo ong’e riekone mathoth mopogore opogore .
Nyasaye notimo kamano kuom Kristo Yesu Ruodhwa , kaluwore gi dwarone mane osechano nyaka nene ni notim .
Ka wan e achiel gi Kristo , kendo kwayie kuome , to wan gi thuolo mar sudo ir Nyasaye gi chir mondo walos kode .
Emomiyo akwayou mondo kik chunyu nyosre kisanda nikech un . Chutho , sandruoknano kelonu mana duong’ !
Kaka nawacho ni adwaro goyo chonga piny mondo alem , to koro agoyo chonga kalamo Wuoro ,
mamiyo dhoudi duto mae polo kod mae piny ng’eyo tiend gima bedo wuoro en .
Akwayo Nyasaye kuom duong’ne mang’ongo mondo omiu teko e chunyu maiye kuom Roho mare ,
kendo mondo Kristo olos kar dakne e chunyu kuom yie . Akwaye bende mondo umoki kendo ugurru e hera ,
mondo un , kaachiel gi jo-Nyasaye duto , ung’e hera mar Kristo , ma lachne , gi borne , kod borne modhi malo , kod tutne ok nyal ng’ere .
Adier , akwayo mondo ung’e herane modhiero rieko duto ng’eyo , mondo Nyasaye opong’ chunyu chuth gi gik moko duto momiyo ubedo kaka en .
Duong’ obed ni Nyasaye , manyalo timonwa gik moko duto moloyo kaka wakwayo kata kaka waparo , kuom tekone matiyo kuomwa .
Ee , duong’ obedne e kanyakla mar jo-Kristo , kendo kuom Kristo Yesu e tienge duto nyaka chieng’ . Amin .
Emomiyo , an ng’at motue nikech Ruoth , akwayou ni mondo uwuoth mowinjore gi luong mane Nyasaye oluongougo .
Pile kik ubed joma sungore , to beduru mamuol , kendo horeuru mos , bende nyisuru hera ma uherorugo kuom weyo ni joweteu kethogi .
Temuru kaka unyalo mondo urit winjruok ma Roho osemiyou , kuom kue moriwou kaachiel .
Nitie ringruok achiel gi Roho achiel , mana kaka nitie geno achiel ma Nyasaye oseluongoue .
Nitie Ruoth achiel , gi yie achiel , kod batiso achiel .
Nyasaye bende en achiel , ma Wuon ji duto . En ema oloyo gik moko duto , kendo otiyo kuom gik moko duto , bende en ei gik moko duto .
To kata kamano , ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomwa osemi mich mar ng’wono mowinjorego , kaka Kristo nosechano .
Mano emomiyo Muma wacho niya , “ Kane oidho malo , nodhi kotelo ni joma omako e lweny , kendo nopogo ni ji mich . ”
Koro ere tiend wach ma wacho ni , “ noidho malo ” ? Tiende en mana ni , kapok oidho , to noselor bende kuonde man mwalo e bwo piny .
Kuom mano , Jal mane olor mwalo ema bende noidho malo kuma bor moyombo polo duto , mondo opong’ kuonde duto e piny kendo e polo .
En ema nopogo mich ni ji , koyiero ji moko mondo obed joote , to moko johul wach moa kuom Nyasaye , kendo moko joland Wach Maber , to moko jotend jo-Kristo , to moko jopuonj .
Ne otimo kamano mondo omi jo-Nyasaye duto obed joma ong’eyo tich konyo ji , kendo tich gero ringre Kristo ,
nyaka chop wan duto wabed e achiel ma wayudo nikech wayie kuom Wuod Nyasaye , kendo wang’eye . Eka wanabed joma otegno chutho , kendo wanachop e rang’iny mogik mar Kristo .
Koro ok wanachak wabed ka nyithindo mayomyom , ma yamo mar puonj moro amora uko , kendo tago , ka ji maricho wuondowa gi riekogi ma gidwaro witowago .
Ooyo , wanabed joadiera , kwawuotho e hera , mondo wadogi e weche duto kuom Kristo . En e wich ,
kendo ringruok duto ochomore kuome , komakore gi leche duto ma en-go . En ema omiyo fuoni ka fuoni tiyo tichne . Kuom mano ringruok dongo kendo gerore kuom hera .
Awachonu ka aramo e nying Ruoth , ni kik uwuoth kaka joma ok ong’eyo Nyasaye , ma parogi ni nono .
Chunygi nie mudho , kendo gionge gi ngima ma Nyasaye chiwo , nikech gin joma kia , kendo tokgi tek ta .
Parogi mar pogo ber gi rach osetho , omiyo giwere mana ni anjawo , ka gitimo timbe duto ma ok ler gi chunygi duto .
To mano ok e kaka ne opuonju Wach Kristo !
Chutho ne uwinjo jo-puonjre mage , ne opuonju adiera man kuome .
Omiyo nyaka uwe kit ngimau machon , kendo ulony dhano machon mochomo tho nikech gombo ma ok ni kare .
Nyaka ulos chunyu gi parou odok manyien ,
bende nyaka urwakru gi dhano manyien , ma olos e kido machal gi mar Nyasaye , kendo maler chutho mowinjore gi adiera .
Emomiyo koro weuru miriambo ! Ng’ato ka ng’ato mondo owach ni wadgi mana adiera , nikech wan duto wan fuond ringruok achiel .
Ka mirima omako ng’ato kuomu , to kik owe mirima tere e richo , kendo kik owe chieng’ podhi ka pod en gi mirima .
Kik umi Satan thuolo ma kamano .
Ng’ama yande kwalo nyaka we kuelo , mondo ochak tich matek kendo modimbore gi lwete owuon , oyud gima dokonygo wadgi moro modhier .
Ka uwuoyo to wach moro marach kik wuog e dhou , to wachuru mana weche mabeyo kendo makonyo ji , kendo mowinjore , mondo joma winjo wecheu oyud konyruok .
Kik umi Roho Maler mar Nyasaye chuny lit , nikech Roho e kido ma Nyasaye oketonu , kaka ranyisi ni noresu chieng’ resruok .
Kuom mano , weuru kecho , gi mirima , gi ichwang’ , gi dhaw , gi ayany , kod himruok duto .
To beduru mang’won , ka ng’ato ka ng’ato kecho wadgi , kendo weyone richone , mana kaka Nyasaye oseweyonu kuom Kristo .
Kaka un nyithind Nyasaye mohero , nyaka utem mondo ubed machal kode .
Beduru gi hera , mana kaka Kristo noherowa , mi ochiwonwa ngimane obedo misango madum tik mamit ni Nyasaye .
Terruok gi tim ma ok ler moro amora , kata gombo , kik bedi e kindu , kendo kata mana wacho kik wachi nimar mano ok owinjore gi jo-Nyasaye ,
kendo tim ma kuodo wich , kata twak mofuwo , kata oyuma , bende ok owinjore . To moloyo onego ugo mana erokamano ni Nyasaye ,
nikech ung’eyo ni ng’ama terore kata ma ok ler , kata ma jagombo , ma en ng’ama lamo nyiseche manono , ok noyud gueth mar Loch Kristo gi Nyasaye .
Kik uwe ng’ato wuondu gi weche manono , nikech gik ma kamago ema miyo Nyasaye olo mirimbe kuom joma tamore winjo wachne .
Kuom mano , kik urip gi joma kamago ngang’ .
Chon ne un jomudho , to koro , kaka usedoko jo-Ruoth , un joler . Omiyo nyaka uwuoth ka joma nie ler ,
nimar ler ema kelo ber gi timbe makare kod adiera duto .
Temuru mondo ung’e gik malong’o ni Ruoth .
Beduru mabor gi joma timo timbe mag mudho maonge ohala . To moloyo umi kit timbegi ong’ere ratiro .
En wichkuot kata mana wacho gik ma gitimo ling’ling’ .
To ka gik moko duto ogol e lela , to kitgi madiera nenore ,
nikech gima kite onenore malong’o e lela , lokore ler . Mano emomiyo iwero niya , “ In ma inindo , chiew ! Chier , ia kuom joma otho , mondo Kristo orieny kuomi . ”
Emomiyo tang’uru ahinya kaka onego ubedi . Kik ubed ka joma ofuwo , to beduru ka joma riek .
Kik uketh kinde ma un-go , nikech ndalogi gin ndalo mag richo .
Kuom mano , kik ubed joma ofuwo , to temuru ng’eyo gima Ruoth dwaro .
Weuru mer , nono to ubiro ketho ngimau chuth . Kar timo kamano , to Roho ema mondo opong’u .
Weruru wende Zaburi , gi wende lemo ka un kaachiel , kendo kuwer kamano , to denduru Ruoth e chunyu .
Kamano gouru erokamano pile ni Nyasaye Wuoro kuom gik moko duto , e nying Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo .
Beduru gi winjruok e kindu , kumiyog Kristo duong’ .
Un mon luoruru chwou mana kaka uluoro Kristo ,
nikech dichwo e wi dhako , mana kaka Kristo e wi kanyakla mar joma oyie kuome , ma en ringre , kendo en jawar mare .
Kuom mano , mon nyaka winj chwogi e weche duto , mana kaka kanyakla mar jo-Kristo winjo Kristo .
Un chwo , heruru mondu mana kaka Kristo nohero kanyakla mar joma oyie kuome , mochiwo ngimane nikech en .
Ne ochiwore kamano mondo opwodhe , kolwoke gi pi kendo gi wach ,
mondo ka okawe obedo mare , to obed gi duong’ kendo maler , maonge chilo kata jowruok kata gimoro amora ma kamano .
Chwo onego oher mondgi mana kaka gihero ringregi giwegi . Ng’at mohero chiege oherore owuon .
Onge ng’ama ok dwar ringre owuon , to opidhe kendo orite , mana kaka Kristo bende rito kanyakla mar joma oyie kuome ,
nikech en ringre owuon . Wan to , wan fuond ringreno .
En mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Emomiyo , ng’ato weo wuon gi min , to padore kuom chiege , kendo ji ariyogo doko ringruok achiel . ”
Nitie adiera maduong’ mopondo e wachni , to aneno ni owuoyo kuom Kristo gi kanyakla mar joma oyie .
To un bende owuoyo kuomu kama : Ng’ato ka ng’ato mondo oher chiege kaka oherore owuon , kendo dhako ka dhako bende nyaka luor chwore .
Un nyithindo , winjuru wach jonywolu , nikech timo kamano en gima kare kuom Ruoth .
Chik mokwongo man gi singruok kuom Chik Apar e ma : “ Luor wuoru gi meru ,
eka mondo ine maber , kendo idag aming’a e piny . ”
Un wuone , kik utim ni nyithindu gik ma dimi mirima makgi , to pidhgiuru kuchikogi kendo upuonjogi e yor Kristo .
Un wasumbini , winjuru wach ruodhiu mae pinyni , kuluor kendo kutetni , kendo timuru kamano gi chuny achiel , mana kaka uwinjo Kristo .
Kik utim kamano mana ni ji oneu , ka gima udwaro bedo malong’o mana ni ji , to timuru gima Nyasaye dwaro gi chunyu duto , kaka wasumbini mag Kristo .
Tiuru tichu gi chuny maler , ka joma tiyo ni Ruoth , to ok matiyo ni ji ,
nikech ung’eyo ni Ruoth nomi ng’ato ka ng’ato pokne kuom tich maber mosetiyo , bed ni en misumba kata en thuolo .
Un ruodhi bende timuru ni wasumbini mau mana kamano . Kik ubwoggi , nikech ung’eyo ni un kaachiel kodgi , un gi Ruoth achiel kende e polo ma ok oluoro wang’ ng’ato .
To wach mogik en ni , beduru motegno kuom Ruoth , kendo kuom tekone maduong’ .
Manreuru gi gilweny duto mag Nyasaye , mondo uyud teko mar siro wuond mariek mag Satan ,
nimar wasigu mwakedogo ok gin dhano , to wakedo gi joloch gi joma nigi teko , kod ruodhi mag piny motimo mudhoni , kaachiel gi lang chuny maricho ma ok mag pinyni .
Omiyo , manreuru gi gilweny mag Nyasaye sani , mondo usir wasigu chieng’ ma lweny gerie , kendo kusetimo duto munyalo , to nonwang’ kapod uchung’ motegno .
Kuom mano , nyonuru piny motegno , kutueyo adiera ka okanda e nungou , kendo kurwako tim makare ka gilweny mag akor ,
kendo rwakuru ikruok mar lando Wach Maber mar kue ka wuocheu .
Ting’uru yie ka okumba kinde duto , mondo uneggo aserni makakni ka mach mag Ng’ama Rach .
Rwakuru warruok ka ogut lweny , kendo makuru wach Nyasaye ka ligangla ma Roho miyou .
Keturu chunyu pile kuom lemo , kukwayo Nyasaye mondo okonyu , kulemo kuom Roho kinde duto . Ritreuru kuom wachni odiechieng’ gotieno , kendo timuru kinda kukwayo ni jo-Nyasaye duto .
An bende lemnauru mondo ka awuoyo , to Nyasaye omiya wach ma onego awachi , mondo awuo gi chir , ka ahulo Wach Maber mosebedo wach mopondo ,
ma an jaotene , kata an ng’at ma otue kamano . Adier , lemnauru mondo awuo kuome gi chir kaka owinjore awuo .
Ang’eyo ni udwaro ng’eyo kaka abet . Ero , owadwa Tukiko , ma jatich modimbore kuom Ruoth , biro nyisou weche duto man kuoma .
Mano ema omiyo aore iru , mondo onyisu kaka wan duto wabet , kendo mondo oduog chunyu .
Kue gi hera kod yie moa kuom Nyasaye Wuoro gi Ruoth Yesu Kristo , obed kod owete duto .
Ng’wono obed kod ji duto mohero Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo gi hera ma ok rum .
Wan Paulo gi Timotheo ma wasumb Kristo Yesu , wandikonu un jo Nyasaye duto man Filipi man kuom Kristo Yesu , kaachiel gi jodongu kod jokonygi .
Ng’wono gi kue moa kuom Nyasaye Wuonwa kod Ruoth Yesu Kristo obed kodu .
Pile ka aparou to agoyo erokamano ni Nyasacha ,
kendo pile ka alemonu to alemo gi mor ,
nikech kony ma usekonyago e tich lando Injili , chakre chieng’ mokwongo nyaka chil kawuono .
Ang’eyo malong’o ni Nyasaye mane ochako tich maber e chunyu biro dhi kode nyime nyaka chope chieng’ ma Yesu Kristo obiroe .
En kare mondo apar kamano kuomu uduto , nikech aherou ahinya , kendo nikech uduto uriworu koda e ng’wono ma Nyasaye osemiya mar bedo e tuech , kendo mar temo siro adiera mar Injili kendo jiwo .
Nyasaye ong’eyo ni awacho adier ni hera matut ma aherougo oa mana kuom Yesu Kristo owuon .
Alemo ni mondo herau omedre mathoth ahinya kuom rieko gi ng’eyo duto ,
mondo ubed gi rieko mar yiero mana gima kare kende . Kamano unubed maler kendo maonge bura chieng ma Kristo obiroe ,
ka ngimau ogundho gi timbe mabeyo duto ma Yesu Kristo kende ema nyalo chiwo mondo Nyasaye oyud duong’ gi pak .
Owetena , adwaro mondo ung’e ni gik ma osetimorena osemiyo Injili omedo landore
nimar askeche ruoth duto , kod jomoko man kaeri , ong’eyo ratiro ni an e tuech nikech an jatich Kristo .
