Bende bedona e tuech kamano osemiyo owete mang’eny omedo bedo gi yie motegno kuom Ruoth , omiyo koro gilando wach gi chir , maonge luoro .
Ang’eyo ni jomoko lando wach Kristo ka nigi ichlit kod miero . Jomoko to lande ka chunygi ler adier .
Joma chunygi lergo timo kamano nikech gihera kendo ging’eyo ni Nyasaye osemiya tich mar kedo ni Injili .
Ji moko to lando wach Kristo ka parogi ok ler , kendo gidwaro mana ni mondo gin giwegi ema giyud duong’ . Giparo ni ka gitimo kamano to gibiro medona chandruok e tuech .
To onge wach ! Amor , nimar wach Kristo ilando e yore duto , bed ni en yor wuondruok kata yor adiera , kedo abiro medo bedo mamor ,
nikech ang’eyo ibiro resa nikech ulemona , kendo nikech Nyasaye osemiya Roho mar Yesu Kristo mondo okonya .
Kamano ageno ahinya ni ok anatim gimoro ma dikuod wiya e yo moro amora , to koro abiro wuoyo gi chir , kaka asetimo kinde duto , mondo gik moko duto ma atimo omi Kristo duong’ , kata angima kata atho .
An ka angima , to ngimana en Kristo , to ka atho , to tho kelona ohala .
To ka bet mangima e ringruok nyalo miyo ati tich moro maber , to kara ok ang’eyo gima dayier ,
nikech gik moko ariyogo beyona duto . To agombo ahinya ni aa , mondo adhi abed gi Kristo , nikech mano ema dibedna maber moloyo .
To ka amedo bedo mangima e ringruok , to mano dikonyu moloyo .
Aonge gi kiawa kuom mano , omiyo ang’eyo ni anabed mangima , kendo nasik kodu , mondo akonyu udongi kendo ubed mamor kuom yie .
Kamano , ka achako abedo kodu kendo , to unumed bedo mamor koda kaka owadu kuom Kristo Yesu .
To koro nyaka une ni ngimau mapile obedo mowinjore gi Wach Maber mar Kristo . Kata ka abiro nenou , kata ka ok abiro , to adwaro winjo ni uchung’ motegno gi chuny achiel , mondo uked ni adiera mar Wach Maber .
Kik uluor wasiku , to pile beduru gi chir , nikech mano biro nyisogi ni gin ginilal , to un noresu , nikech Nyasaye owuon ema biro nyisogi kamano !
Nyasaye onyisou ni oherou , ok mana nikech osemiyo uyie kuom Kristo kende , to nikech osemiyo uneno masira bende nikech en .
Lweny mukedoni en mana lweny achiel mane uneno ka akedo chon , kendo mapod uwinjo ni akedo .
Ka bedowa kuom Kristo nyalo kelonwa hoch , kata hera maduogo chuny , kata bedo e achiel kuom Roho , kata ng’wono kod miwafu ,
to kara beduru gi paro achiel , gi chuny achiel mondo umi chunya opong’ gi mor .
Kik ubed gi piem kata sunga , to beduru mobolore , ka ukwanoru ka joma tindoe moloyo jomoko ,
kendo kik upar mana gima konyou uwegi , to nyaka upar gima konyo jomoko bende .
Paro mae chunyu nyaka bed machal gi paro mane Kristo Yesu nigo :
Kite ne kit Nyasaye nyaka a chakruok , to ne ok otuere ni nyaka osik marom gi Nyasaye ,
to notimore gima nono . Nokawo kit misumba , mi odoko dhano mana ka wan , kendo konenore ka dhano kamano ,
to nobolore , kendo nowinjo wach nyaka tho , mana tho mar msalaba !
Mano emomiyo Nyasaye ne omiye duong’ ahinya e polo , kendo omiye nying’ moloyo nying’ duto .
Kamano gik moko duto manie polo gi manie piny kod manie bwo piny mondo ogo chonggi piny , omi nying Yesu duong’ ,
kendo ji duto mondo ohul ni Yesu Kristo e Ruoth , mondo Nyasaye Wuoro bende oyud duong’ .
Kuom mano , osiepena , kaka ne uwinjo wachna kane an kodu , koro ka an mabor kodu , to ber mondo uwinj wachna moloyo . Tiuru gi luoro kod kibaji , mondo umi warruok ochop kare ,
nikech Nyasaye owuon ema tiyo e chunyu , komiyou dwaro kendo timo gima long’one .
Gimoro amora mutimo to timuru ka ok ung’ur , kata ka ok ugoyoe mbaka .
Nyaka ubed nyithind Nyasaye maler kendo maonge wach , kubedo maonge ketho e kind tieng’ mobam kendo ma jarichoni , mondo urieny e kindgi ka sulue marieny e polo ,
kunyisogi wach ngima . Ka utimo kamano , to unumi abed mamor chieng’ ma Kristo obiroe , nikech mano nonyis ni ng’uech ma aringoni , kod tich ma atiyo , ok ne akethoe tekra kayiem nono .
Yie maru en misango muchiwo ni Nyasaye , omiyo kata ka obedo ni remba iolo kimedo e misangono , to berna , kendo adwaro mondo uduto ung’e kaka amor .
Kamano e kaka un bende onego ubed mamor , mondo wabed mamor kaachiel .
Ageno ni ka Ruoth Yesu oyie , to abiro oro Timotheo iru mapiyo , eka chunya noduogi ka awinjo wach ma kuomu .
En bende ema chunye chalo gi mara , kendo en ema oparou adier ,
nikech ji duto dwaro mana mekgi giwegi , to ok dew wach Yesu Kristo .
To uduto ung’eyo ber mar Timotheo , kendo kaka osekonya e tich mar lando Injili , mana ka wuowi makonyo wuon .
Mano emomiyo en ema ageno ore iru piyo , ka aseng’eyo kaka wachna obet .
To pod ageno ni ka Ruoth oyie , to an awuon bende abiro biro iru piyo .
Aseneno ni ber mondo aornu owadwa Epafrodito bende , ma jatich wadwa ma wasekedogo kaachiel . Osebedo jaoteu mane uoro mondo okonya e gik ma adwaro ,
to en gi siso mar nenou uduto , kendo chunye chandore nikech nuwinjo ni otuo .
Adier , notuo , mi both otho , to Nyasaye nokeche , to ok en kende ema ne okeche to an bende nokecha , mondo kik abed gi kuyo nyadiriyo .
Emomiyo adwaro ore ahinya iru , mondo ubed mamor kunene , kendo mondo kuyo ma an-go orum .
Kuom mano , rwakeuru gi mor maduong’ kaka owadu kuom Ruoth . Miuru joma chal kode kamano duong’ ,
nimar nochiwo ngimane mi both otho nikech tich Kristo , mondo okonya gi kony mane un uwegi ok unyal konyago , nikech un mabor koda .
Koro oritu owetena , kendo beduru mamor kuom Ruoth . Onge teko moro ma aneno kuom nwoyonu weche mane asendikonu mokwongo , kendo en gima biro konyou .
Beduru motang’ ni guogi ma gin joma timbegi richo , kendo moramo ni nyaka ter ji nyangu , ma en mana ketho ringruok kayiem nono .
To wan ma Roho Maler ema otelonwa kuom lamo Nyasaye , wan e joma oter nyangu adier , kendo sungawa ni kuom Kristo Yesu . To ok waketo genowa kuom tim ringruok .
To kata ka da bed ni en wach mar keto geno kuom tim ringruok to an onge gima da aluoro . Chutho , ka en mana wach keto geno kuom ringruok , to onge ng’ama diloya !
Notera nyangu chieng’ mar aboro bang’ nywolna , kaka Chik Musa dwaro , kendo an ja-Israel ma jadhood Benjamin , bende an ja-Hibrania ma wuod jo-Hibrania . Kuom wach rito Chik Musa to ne an ja-Farisai ,
kendo kinda mane an-go kuom rito chik kwerewa nomiyo asando kanyakla mar jo-Kristo . Adier , onge ng’ama diyud ketho moro kuoma , nikech narito weche duto ma Chik dwaro .
To kata kamano , gigo duto mane akwano chon ka ohala , tinde akwano ka gik manono nikech Kristo .
To moloyo mano , akwano gik moko duto ka gik manono , nimar gueth maduong’ mar ng’eyo Kristo Ruodha Yesu ohewo gimoro amora . Adier , ne aweyo gik moko duto olalna nikech en . Akwanogi duto mana ka yugi miwito oko , mondo ayud Kristo kaka pokna ,
ka ariwora kode eringruok achiel . Koro ok adwar ni mondo okwana ka ng’ama dwaro bedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye nikech rito Chik , to adwaro bedo ng’ama Nyasaye osemiyo bedo e winjruok kode nikech oyie kuom Kristo .
Gima adwaro moloyo en mana ng’eyo Kristo kod teko miyudo kuom chierne . Adwaro riwora kode e sandne , kendo doko machal kode e thone ,
ka ageno ni , kanyalore , to an bende nochiera kuom joma otho .
Ok awach ni asechopo , kata ni asebedo makare chuth , to atemo matek ka ageno ni abiro mako gima ne omiyo Kristo Yesu owuon omaka .
Adier , owetena , an ok awach ni asemake , to gima duong’ ma ang’eyo en ma : Ka wiya owil kod gik ma osekadho , to ahawo gima ni nyima ,
kendo aringo matek mondo achop kar pok , ma en ngima mae polo ma Nyasaye luongowae kuom Kristo Yesu .
Mano e chuny ma onego wabedgo , wan duto ma wan jo-Kristo motegno : To ka parou opogore e wach moro , to Nyasaye nolernu mano bende .
To wadhiuru nyime mana kwaluwo chike ma waseluwo nyaka sani .
Owetena , temuru uduto mondo uluw timna . Wasebedonu ranyisi makare , omiyo ng’iuru ane jogo ma timgi oluwore gi timwa ,
nimar kaka ne wawachonu ndalo mang’eny , koro eri achako awachonu ka pi wang’a chuer ni , nitie ji mathoth ma ngimagi miyo gidoko wasik msalap Kristo .
To notiekgi e giko , nimar igi e nyisechegi , kendo gisungore mana ni gik makelonigi wichkuot , bende giparo mana weche mag pinyni .
Wan to polo e thurwa , kendo warito Ruoth Yesu Kristo mondo oa e polo obi oreswa .
Obiro kawo ringrewa manyap kendo matho , mi olok obed machal gi ringre owuon man gi duong’ , kotiyo gi teko mamiyo oketo gik moko duto e bwo lochne .
Emomiyo owetena ma ahero , chung’uru motegno kuom Kristo . Siso oloya kodu ahinya , jowadwa . Un ema umiya mor , kendo un e osimbona , manyiso ni aselocho .
Akwayo Yuodia gi Suntuke mondo jowinjre kuom Ruoth .
To in owadwa maradier , bende akwayi mondo ikony mon-go , nikech gisetiyo koda matek kuom lando Injili , ka wan gi Klement kod jotich wetewa mamoko duto , ma nyingi ondiki e kitap ngima .
Beduru mamor pile kuom Ruoth kendo amedo wacho ni , beduru mamor .
Muolo maru mondo onenre ni ji duto . Ruoth chiegni ,
omiyo kik upar gimoro , to nyisuru Nyasaye gik moko duto muchando , kulemo kendo ka chunyu goyone erokamano .
Eka kue mar Nyasaye modhiero ji ng’eyo norit chunyu gi parou , kubedo kuom Kristo .
To wach mogik , owetena , paruru weche duto mabeyo kendo mowinjore yud pak , kaka : weche madiera , weche makelo pak , weche makare , weche maler , weche malong’o , kod weche mang’won .
Timuru gik moko duto mane apuonjou , kendo uyudo kuoma , bende ma usewinjo ka awacho kata ka atimo . Eka Nyasach kue nobed kodu .
Mano kaka an gi mor maduong’ kuom Ruoth , nikech uchako upara kendo , bang’ ndalo mang’eny ahinya ! Ang’eyo ni ne ok uweyo para , to thuolo mar timo gimoro ema ne otamou .
Ok awach kamano nikech achando gimoro , nimar asepuonjora ni gik ma an-go oroma maber .
Aseng’eyo dak kachando gimoro , kata ka an gi gik mathoth . Asepuonjora wach moro mopondo , omiyo kamoro amora ma antie , e kinde moro amora , to anyalo bedo modhil , kata ka ayieng’ , kata ka adenyo , kata ka an gi gik mathoth , kata ka an gi manok .
Anyalo chomo gik moko duto tir , kuom teko ma Kristo miya .
To kata kamano , nutimo maber ahinya kane ukonya e chandruokna .
Un jo-Filipi , ung’eyo maber ni e ndalo mane akwongo landoe Injili , kane aa piny Makedonia , onge kanyakla mar jo-Kristo kata achiel mane okonya gi chiwo mar pesa , mak mana un .
Kata kane an Thesalonika , to ne ukowona pesa , ok mana dichiel kende , to ndalo mogwarore , mondo akonyrago .
To kik upar ni mich ema adwaro . Ooyo , gima adwaro en mana ni mondo Nyasaye omednu ohala .
Koro andikonu risit ! Eri , an gi gik moko duto ma adwaro , kendo mokadho kanyo , ka koro Epafrodito osekelona chiwo mane uorona . Chiwouno en misango madum tik mang’ue mamit , ma Nyasaye oyiego , kendo long’one .
Nyasacha nomiu gik moko duto muchando , kogolo kuom mwandune man gi duong’ , kuom Kristo Yesu .
Duong’ obed ni Nyasachwa kendo Wuonwa nyaka chieng’ . Amin .
Mosuru jo-Nyasaye duto man kuom Kristo Yesu . Owete ma wan-go ka omosou .
Jo-Nyasaye duto omosou , to moloyo jogo ma jood Kaisar .
Ng’wono mar Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo obed kod chunyu .
An Paulo , jaote mar Kristo Yesu kuom dwaro mar Nyasaye , ema andiko baruani kaachiel gi owadwa Timotheo .
Wandikonu un jo-Nyasaye man Kolosai , ma un owetewa maradier kuom Kristo . Ng’wono gi kue moa kuom Nyasaye Wuonwa obed kodu .
Ndalo duto kwalemonu , to wagoyo erokamano ni Nyasaye , Wuon Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo ,
nikech wasewinjo yie ma un-go kuom Yesu Kristo , kod hera muherogo jo-Nyasaye duto .
Kane wach maradier , ma en Wach Maber obironu mokwongo , ne uwinjo wach geno ma okelo . Kuom mano , yieu kod herau owuok kuom gima ugeno ma okannu maber e polo .
Wach Maberno nyago olemo , kendo olandore e piny ngima , mana kaka oselandore e kindu , chakre chieng’ mane ukwongo winjoe wach ng’wono mar Nyasaye , mi ung’eye adier .
Epafra mane opuonjou wachno en misumba wadwa , kendo jatich Kristo maradier matiyonu karwa .
En ema nonyisowa kaka Roho osemiyou hera .
Mano emomiyo , chakre chieng’ mane onyisowae kamano , pok waweyo mak walemonu , kwakwayo ni mondo ung’e dwaro mar Nyasaye chutho , ka un gi rieko kod ng’eyo duto ma Roho chiwo .
Kamano unudag e ngima mamiyo Ruoth duong’ , kendo unutim gik malong’one e yore duto , kunyago olemo mag timbe mabeyo duto , kendo kumedo ng’eyo Nyasaye .
Walemo ni mondo otegu gi teko mar duong’ne mang’ongo , komiyo udhil , kendo uketo chunyu mos , kata ka ang’o ema timore .
Gouru erokamano gi mor ni Wuoro , ma osemiyo ubedo joma owinjore yudo gueth kaachiel gi joge owuon e piny ler .
En ema ne oresowa e Loch mudho , mi oterowa e Loch Wuode mohero ,
mane owarowa , kaweyonwa richowa .
Kristo e kido mineno mar Nyasaye ma ok ne . En gi duong’ mar wuowi makayo , kendo en gi loch kuom chuech duto ,
nikech kuome ema ne Nyasaye ochueyoe gik moko duto manie polo kendo manie piny , ok mana gik mineno kende , to koda ka gik ma ok ne bende , kaka loch , gi duong’ , gi ruodhi , kod teko . Mago duto Nyasaye nochueyo kuom Kristo , kendo ni Kristo .
Kristo ne nitie kane pok ochue gik moko duto , kendo en ema gik moko duto oriwore kuome .
En e wi kanyakla mar jo-Kristo , kendo kanyakla mar jo-Kristo e ringre . En ema ne ochako kanyakla mar jo-Kristo , kendo en ema ne okwongo chier oa kuom joma otho , mi obedo jatelo kuom gik moko duto ,
nikech Nyasaye owuon ema ne oyiero mondo en owuon odag kuom Kristo gi kite duto .
Ne oyiero mondo omi gik moko duto obed gi winjruok kode kuom Kristo , kokelo kue kuom remb Wuode mane ochuer e msalaba . Adier , Nyasaye nomiyo gik moko duto manie polo kod manie piny obedo gi winjruok kode kuom Kristo , koda ka un bende .
Chon un ne un mabor gi Nyasaye , kendo ne un wasike , nikech timbe manono mane utimo , kendo uparo .
To koro kuom tho mane Wuode othogo e ringruok , Nyasaye osemiyo ubedo gi winjruok kode mondo okelu e nyime kuler , kuonge mbala , kendo kuonge ketho .
To nyaka usik e yie ma un-gono ka uchung’ motegno e mise , ma ok uyiengni uweyo geno mane ubedogo kane uwinjo Injili . En e Wach Maber ma oselandi ni chuech duto e piny ngima , kendo an Paulo ne oketa mondo abed jatich wach maberno .
Emomiyo koro amor ka aneno masira nikech un . Mano e kaka ringra chopo gima orem kuom masiche mane Kristo oneno nikech kanyakla mar jo-Kristo ma en ringre .
Nyasaye ema ne omiyo adoko jatich kanyakla mar jo-Kristo , kendo tich maduong’ mane omiya en kelonu Wach Maber , kendo elonu tiende malong’o .
En wach mane osebedo kopandi nyaka nene ni tienge mathoth kuom higni mang’eny , to koro oseele ni jo-Nyasaye .
Nyasaye nochano mondo joge ong’e kaka wach mane osepandino nigi duong’ miwuoro kuom joma ok jo-Yahudi . To wachno en ni Kristo odak e iu , kendo miyo ugeno kuom duong’ mabiro .
Kristo ema wahulo wachne ni ji duto , kwanyisogi kendo wapuonjogi gi rieko , mondo wakelgi giduto e nyim Nyasaye ka gin jo-Kristo motegno .
Mano e gima achandora katiyone , ka teko maduong’ mar Nyasaye tiyo kuoma .
Adwaro ni mondo ung’e kaka akedonu matek , kendo ni jo-Laodikia , kaachiel gi ji duto mapok anena wang’ gi wang’ .
Atimo kamano mondo gibed gi chuny motegno ka giriwore kuom hera mondo giyud mwandu mar chuny ma ng’ato yudo ka en gi ng’eyo maradier . Kamano gining’e wach mopondo mar Nyasaye , ma en Kristo owuon .
En ema mwandu duto mag rieko kod ng’eyo opand kuome .
Awachonu kamano mondo kik uwe ng’ato wuondu gi weche mamit maywayo ji .
Kata obedo ni ok an kodu gi ringra , to an kodu gi chunya , kendo amor ahinya kaneno kaka uritoru maber , kendo kaka un gi yie motegno kuom Kristo .
Kaka userwako Kristo ka ruoth , kamano bende e kaka onego udag kuome .
Beduru kumoko kuome , kendo kugeroru kuome , kendo kumedo bedo gi yie motegno , mana kaka ne opuonju , kendo gouru erokamano mogundho .
To tang’uru mondo kik uwe ng’ato mak parou gi rieko kod wuond manono , mawuok kuom puonj dhano kod timbe machon mag piny , to ok kuom Kristo .
Nyasaye mangima gi kite duto odak kuom Kristo , tiende ni e ringre Kristo ,
omiyo ka un kuom Kristo , to un gi gik moko duto te , nikech en e jatelo moloyo jotelo duto , kendo oloyo teko duto .
Kane uyie kuom Kristo to noteru nyangu , to ok nyangu mar ringruok , to nyangu mar Kristo , ma en lonyo kit dhano machon matimo richo ,
nikech kane obatisu , to gik moko ariyo notimore : ne oyiku e liel gi Kristo , kendo ne ochieru bende gi Kristo , nikech uyie kuom teko mar Nyasaye mane ochiero Kristo oa kuom joma otho .
Kata obedo ni chon ne un joma otho gi chunyu nikech richou , kendo nikech ne un joma ok jo-Yahudi , tiende ni joma ok ter nyangu , to Nyasaye koro osemiyo udoko mangima kaachiel gi Kristo . Adier , noweyonwa richowa duto !
Norucho wach mane ondiki motueyowa ni nyaka wamak Chik . Wachno nodonjonwa kuom kethowa duto to ne ogole oko chuth , kogurogo e msalaba .
To bende e msalabano ema ne Kristo omayoe joloch kod joteko teko duto mane gin go , kendo koselocho to nomiyogi wichkuot , kosembogi e lela ka wasumbe mondo ji onegi .
Kuom mano , kik uwe ng’ato ketnu chik kuom gik ma uchamo kata gik mumadho , kata kuom wach sawo moro , kata kuom rito ndalo mag due mopor kata Sabato .
Gigo duto gin mana tipo mar gik mabiro , to adiera wuon en Kristo .
Nitie joma keto chunygi kuom sando ringregi kod lamo malaika , kendo moramo kuom gik ma gineno e fweny , kendo ting’ore malo kayiem nono kuom parogi mag dhano . Kik uwe joma kamago mau poku .
Giseweyo bedo kuom Kristo ma en Wich . Kuom Kristo , ringruok duto yudoe gik modwaro , kendo fuoni gi leche omake kaachiel , omiyo odongo kaka Nyasaye dwaro ni mondo odongi .
Ne utho gi Kristo , mi ogonyu kuom timbe machon mag piny . To koro ere gima omiyo uwuotho ka jopiny ? Ang’o momiyo umako chike mawacho ni ,
“ Kik imak gini , ” kata ni , “ Kik imul gini ” ?
To gigi duto gin mana gik makethore kosetigo , kendo wechego duto gin mana chik kod puonj mag dhano .
Adier , ginenore ka weche man gi rieko , nikech giwuoyo kuom timo kinda e lemo , kod dembruok , to ok ginyal konyo ng’ato geng’o gombo mag ringruok .
Osechieru kaachiel gi Kristo ua kuom joma otho , omiyo nyaka uket chunyu kuom gik man malo , kuma Kristo obetie e bat korachwich mar Nyasaye .
Chomuru parou kuom gik man malo , to ok kuom gik mag piny ,
nikech usetho , kendo ngimau koro osepand gi Kristo kuom Nyasaye .
Kristo e ngimau maradier , kendo ka ochako oduogo , to un bende unubi kode e duong’ne maler .
Emomiyo neguru dhano machon gi timbene duto mag piny ka , kaka terruok , gi dwanyruok , gi hera marach , gi gombo marach , kod ich lach ma en mana lamo nyiseche manono ,
nikech weche ma kamago ema miyo Nyasaye olo mirimbe kuom joma otamore yie kuome .
Un bende ne uluwo timbe ma kamago e ngimau machon .
To koro kaka jo-Kristo , nyaka uwe timbego duto , kaka : ichwang’ , gi mirima , gi himruok , gi ayany , kod weche mochido .
Kik ng’ato wuond wadgi , nimar uselonyo dhano machon gi timbene ,
mi urwako dhano manyien mamedo doko manyien pile , mondo obed machal gi kit jachwechne , mi omi ung’e Nyasaye chuth .
E ngimau manyienni , onge ja-Yahudi kata ng’ama ok ja-Yahudi ; onge ng’ama oter nyangu kata ng’ama ok oter nyangu . Kendo onge misumba kata ng’ama ni thuolo . Bende onge ng’ama ok osomo gi jamaranda . To Kristo en duto kendo kuom duto .
Emomiyo , kaka Nyasaye oseyierou mondo ubed joge owuon mohero , nyaka ubed gi miwafu , gi ng’wono , gi bolruok , gi muolo kod horuok .
Beduru jogo ma ng’wono ni joma timonigi marach , to kik ubed joma mako sadha gi jowadgi . Ruoth oseweyonu richou , omiyo un bende nyaka uwe ni joma timonu marach .
To ewi mago duto , to beduru gi hera , nikech hera ema riwo gik moko duto bedo achiel chuth .
Kue ma Kristo chiwo ema mondo obed jang’ad bura e chunyu , nikech kue nogo ema ne Nyasaye oseluongoue kaachiel e ringruok achiel . Omiyo gouru erokamano mogundho .
Wach Kristo , gi gueth duto mokelo , mondo odag e chunyu . Puonjreuru kendo jiwreuru gi rieko duto . Weruru mamit e chunyu ni Nyasaye , kugoyone erokamano gi wende Zaburi gi wende pak kod wende mag chuny .
Gimoro amora ma uwacho kata utimo onego obedi e nying Ruoth Yesu , kugoyoni Nyasaye Wuoro erokamano e nyinge .
Un mon , winjuru chwou , nimar mano e gima joma obedo kuom Ruoth onego tim .
Un chwo , heruru mondu , kendo kik ubed mager kodgi .
Un nyithindo , winjuru jonywolu e weche duto , nikech mano ema long’o ni Nyasaye , kendo en gima joma obedo kuom Kristo onego tim .
Un jonywol , kik ulwer nyithindu , nikech dipo ka chunygi ojok .
Un wasumbini bende , winjuru chutho ruodhiu mae pinyni , kendo ka utiyo , to kik uti mana ni mondo ji oneu , ka gima udwaro bedo malong’o ni ji , to keturu chunyu e tichu , nikech uluoro Ruoth
Gimoro amora mutimo , to timuru gi chunyu duto , mana ka gima utiyo ni Ruoth , to ok ni dhano ,
kung’eyo ni Ruoth ema nomiu pok mosesingore ni joge , nimar Kristo e Ruoth mutiyone .
Ng’at matimo marach kata da bed ni en ng’ama nadi , noyud pok kuom rach mosetimo , nikech Nyasaye yalo ji duto mana machalre , ka ok odewo wang’ ng’ato .
Un ruodhi , timuru ni wasumbu maber kendo mowinjore , kung’eyo ni un gi Ruoth e polo .
Timuru kinda kuom lemo , kendo kulemo kamano , to parou obed moyawore , kendo ugo ni Nyasaye erokamano .
To wan bende lemnwauru kukwayo Nyasaye mondo oyawnwa dhoot , waland wachne , ma en wach mopondo man kuom Kristo , momiyo anie tuech .
Lemnauru mondo ahul wachno maler kaka owinjore .
Ng’euru kaka utiyo gi rieko gi joma ok oyie kuom Kristo , ma ok uketho kinde ma un go kata matin .
Wecheu onego bed mang’won pile kendo man gi ndhadhu , kendo nyaka ung’e kaka udwoko ng’ato ka ng’ato .
Owadwa Tukiko , ma jatich maradier , kendo ma misumba wadwa kuom tich Ruoth , biro nyisou weche duto ma kuoma .
Mano emomiyo aore iru mondo oduog chunyu , konyisou kaka waduto wabet .
Aore gi Onesimo , owadwa maradier kendo mwahero , ma jathuru . Gibiro nyisou gik moko duto matimore ka .
Aristarko man koda e tuech omosou . Mariko ma owadgi Barnaba bende omosou . ( Usewinjo wachne , kapo ni obiro iru , to mondo urwake maber . )
Joshua ma bende iluongo ni Justo , bende ooronu mos . Ji adekgo e jo-Yahudi kende moyie kuom Kristo , ma atiyogo ni Loch Nyasaye , kendo gisekonya ahinya .
Epafra ma bende jathuru , kendo ma misumba Yesu Kristo , bende ooronu mos . Pile olemonu matek , kokwayo Nyasaye mondo omi uchung’ motegno ka jo-Kristo maradier , kuketo chunyu kuom timo gik moko duto ma Nyasaye dwaro .
Anyalo wachonu adier kaka otiyonu matek , kendo ni jo-Laodikia kod jo-Hieropoli .
Luka ma jathiethwa mwahero , kod Dema , jomosou .
Mosnwauru owete man Laodikia , kendo mosnwauru Numfa kod kanyakla mar jo-Kristo malemo e ode .
To kusesomo baruani , to nyaka une ni usome bende ni kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Laodikia . To un bende nyaka usom barupa mane andiko ni jo-Laodikia , ma gibiro oronu .
Nyisuru Arkipo ni mondo one ni otieko gima ne omiye mondo otim , nikech en tich Ruoth .
An Paulo andiko mosni gi lweta awuon niya , “ Amosou to paruru nyororo motueyago . Ng’wono mar Nyasaye obed kodu . ”
An Paulo , kaachiel gi Silvano , kod Timotheo , wandikonu un kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Thesalonika , ma un jo-Nyasaye Wuoro kod Ruoth Yesu Kristo . Ng’wono gi kue obed kodu .
Wagoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano ndalo duto nikech un , kendo waluongo nyingu pile e lemowa .
E nyim Nyasachwa kendo Wuonwa , wiwa ok nyal wil gi timbe ma usetimo nikech yie ma un-go , gi tich matek musetiyo nikech hera ma ungo , kendo gi kinda ma unyisogo ni ugeno kuom Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo .
Wang’eyo , owetewa , ni Nyasaye oherou kendo oseyierou mondo ubed joge owuon ,
nikech kane wakelonu Injili , to ne ok wakele mana gi wach mar dhok , to ne wakele gi teko mar Roho Maler , mi uyie chuth . Bende ung’eyo kaka ne wachalo ka ne wan kodu Thesalonika . Adier , ne wabet kamano mana nikech un .
Ne uluwo timwa kod tim Ruoth bende . To kata obedo ni Injili nokelonu chandruok malit kamano , to ne urwake gi mor ma Roho Maler ochiwo .
Kuom mano , ne udoko ranyisi ni joma oyie duto manie piny Makedonia , kod piny Akaya ,
nimar wach Ruoth nolandore kochakore kuomu . Ok nolandore mana e Makedonia gi Akaya kende , to wach yie ma un-go kuom Nyasaye osechopo e it ji kuonde duto . Omiyo koro onge gima onego wawachi ,
nikech jogo duto wacho giwegi kaka ne urwakowa kane walimou , kendo kaka ne ulokoru uweyo nyiseche manono mondo uti ni Nyasaye maradier kendo mangima .
Bende giwacho kaka koro urito Wuode mondo obi oa e polo . Wuodeno en Yesu , mane ochiero oa kuom joma otho , kendo moresowa kuom mirima mabiro .
Owetewa , un uwegi ung’eyo ni kane walimou , to limbewa ne ok obedo kayiem nono .
Ung’eyo kaka nosandwa kendo oyanywa malit e dala mar Filipi , kane pok wabiro iru Thesalonika . To kata kamano Nyasaye nomiyowa chir mondo walandnu Injili , kata obedo ni ji mathoth ne mon kodwa kamano .
Ok wahomb ji gi wach mar miriambo , kata mar dwanyruook , kata mar miganga ,
to wawuoyo kaka joma Nyasaye oseyiego , momiyo Injili . Ok watem bedo malong’o ni ji , to wadwaro bedo malong’o ni Nyasaye , manono chunywa .
Ung’eyo maber ni ne ok wakonyre ngang’ gi weche miwuondogo wang’ ji , kendo Nyasaye ong’eyo ni ne waonge gi gombo moro mwapando e chunywa .
Ne ok wadwar mondo ji opakwa , bed ni un ema upakowa kata ji mamoko ema pakowa .
Chutho kata obedo ni ne wanyalo miyou ting’ mapek nikech wan joote Kristo , to ne wabet mamuol e dieru kane wan kodu mana kaka min nyathi rito nyathine .
To ne waherou ahinya , omiyo ne ok wayie mana chiwore mondo wamiu Wach Maber mar Nyasaye kende , to ne wayie miyou chunywa bende , nikech hera maduong’ mane waherougo .
Owetewa , parieuru kaka ne watiyo matek kwachandore . Kane walandonu Wach Maber mar Nyasaye to ne watiyo odiechieng’ gotieno ni gik mwachando , mondo kik wami ng’at moro kuomu ting’ mapek .
Un ema ung’eyo , mana kaka Nyasaye bende ong’eyo ni kane wan kodu , to timbewa ne ler kendo kare , maonge ketho moro e nyimu un joma oyie .
Ung’eyo ni ne wabet gi ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu mana kaka wuoro bet gi nyithinde owuon .
Ne wajiwou kwahoyo chunyu kendo wasiemou mondo ubed joma bedo malong’o ni Nyasaye ma luongou e lochne man gi duong’ .
To bende wagoyo erokamano pile , nikech kane uyudo Wach Nyasaye mane wakelonu , to ne ok urwake mana ka wach dhano , to ne urwake ka Wach Nyasaye adier , matiyo e chunyu un joma oyie .
Owetewa , gik mosetimorenu chal mana gi gik mane otimore ni kanyakla mag jo-Nyasaye moyie kuom Yesu e piny Judea , nimar ne usandoru e lwet jopinyu mana kaka gin bende ne gisandore e lwet jo-Yahudi wetegi .
Jo-Yahudigo ema ne onego Ruoth Yesu kod jonabi maggi , kendo gin ema ne giriembowa oko . Ok gilong’o ni Nyasaye , bende gimon gi ji duto .
To bende gitemo koda ka sindowa mondo kik waland ni joma ok jo-Yahudi wach makelonigi warruok . Kamano gipong’o rapor mar richogi , omiyo mirimb Nyasaye koro osejukogi !
Owetewa , kane wasewere kodu , to kata obedo ni ne ok waneu kamano , to wiwa ne ok owil kodu kata matin . Bang’ kinde matin kende ne wabedo gi siso maduong’ mondo wanere kodu wang’ gi wang’ .
Kuom mano ne wachano biro iru . Adier an Paulo ne achano biro iru ndalo mang’eny , to Satan nosindowa .
Ne wadwaro timo kamano nikech , un e genowa , kendo morwa , kendo osimbowa ma wabiro pakorego e nyim Ruodhwa Yesu kobiro .
Adier , un e duong’wa gi morwa .
Emomiyo , kane ok wanyal bet mos , ne waparo ni ber mondo owewa wadong’ kendwa Athens ,
to waornu owadwa Timotheo ma watiyogo tich Nyasaye mar lando Wach Maber mar Kristo , mondo obi ojiwu ubed gi yie motegno ,
mondo kik ng’ato kuomu dog chien nikech masiche muneno . Un uwegi ung’eyo ni wan jo-Kristo nyaka wane sandruok ma kamago ,
nikech kane wan kodu ne wawachonu chon ni nyaka sandwa , kendo koro uneno ka mano ema osetimore .
Mano emomiyo , kane ok wanyal medo bet mos , to naoro Timotheo mondo awinj kaka yieu chal , nikech ne aluor ni dipo ka Satan osetemou , mi tichwa obedo kayiem nono .
To Timotheo koro oseduogo koa iru , kendo okelonwa wach ni udhi nyime maber , kendo yieu gi herau pod otegno , bende osewachonwa ni uparowa gi hera mang’won ndalo duto , kendo ni ugombo nenowa kaka wan bende wagombo nenou .
Kuom mano , owetewa , kata obedo ni wachandore e masiche mang’eny , to yie ma un-go no osehoyo chunywa ,
nikech ka uchung’ matek kuom Ruoth , to kara koro wangima maber .
Erokamano maduong’ marom nadi ma dwago ni Nyasaye nikech un , kuom mor duto mumiyo wamorgo e nyim Nyasachwa !
Walemo matek ahinya odiechieng’ gotieno ni mondo waneu wang’ gi wang’ kendo wakelnu gimoro amora ma yieu oremo .
Nyasachwa kendo Wuonwa gi Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo mondo otelnwa wabi iru .
To un , Ruoth mondo omi uherru , kendo uher ji duto gi hera mogundho mana kaka wan bende waherou .
Ruoth mondo oteg chunyu ubed joma onge bura , ka ubedo maler e nyim Nyasaye Wuonwa , chieng’ ma Ruodhwa Yesu biroe kod joge duto .
To koro mogik , owetewa , wan kod gimoro achiel monego wakwau kaka jo-Kristo wetewa . Wakwayou ni mondo ngimau obed moluwore gi puonj mane wamiyou . Ne wanyisou kaka onego uwuothi mondo ubed malong’o ni Nyasaye , kendo adier mano e kaka uwuotho , to kata kamano wajiwou mondo umed timo kamano moloyo .
Ung’eyo chik mane wamiyou moa kuom Ruoth Yesu .
Nyasaye dwaro ni mondo ubed joma ler , omiyo nyaka uwe terruok .
Ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu mondo ong’e rito ringre owuon e yo maler kendo mipako .
Kik umi gombou thuolo kaka joma ok oyie Nyasaye timo .
Kik ng’ato tim ni wadgi marach , kata wuond wadgi e wachni , nikech Ruoth nochul kuor kuom wechegi duto , mana kaka ne wawachonu chon ka wasiemou matek .
Nyasaye ok oseluongowa mondo wadag e dwanyruok , to oseluongowa mondo wabed joma ler .
Emomiyo ng’at modagi puonjni ok odagi winjo dhano , to odagi winjo mana Nyasaye , mamiyou Roho mare Maler .
Onge tiende ndikonu kanyisou kaka onego uher joweteu moyie , nikech un uwegi Nyasaye osepuonjou kaka onego uherru .
Adier , mano e kaka uhero owete duto man Makedonia , to wahombou owetewa , ni mondo umed timo kamano moloyo .
Dwaruru dak e ngima mokue , kendo tiju kende ema urangi , ka utiyo gi luetu mana kaka ne wapuonjou mokwongo .
Ka utimo kamano , to ubiro miyo joma ok jo-Kristo genou , kendo ok unuchand gimoro .
Owetewa , wadwaro ni mondo ung’e wach man kuom joma osetho , mondo kik ubed gi kuyo ka joma onge geno .
Wayie ni Yesu notho , kendo ochako ochier . Kamano bende e kaka wach joma otho koyie kuom Kristo nobedi . Nyasaye nokelgi kaachiel gi Yesu .
Koro wanyisou gimoro ma Ruoth owuon ema nowacho . Nowacho ni , wan joma pod odong’ kangima chieng’ ma Yesu biro , ok wanakwong dhi ni jogo mosetho .
Chieng’no dwol moro nogol chik , kendo dwond malaika maduong’ nowinji , kendo tung’ mar Nyasaye noywagi , kendo Ruoth owuon nolor koa e polo . Eka joma notho koyie kuom Kristo nochier mokwongo .
Bang’e , wan mapod wangima noyudhwa , mi terwa malo e boche polo kaachiel gi jogo , mondo warom ni Ruoth e kor polo . Mano e kaka Ruoth noterwa mondo wabed kode nyaka chieng’ .
Owetewa , onge tiende ndikonu kuom ndalo kata sa ma gigo notimree ,
nikech ung’eyo maber ni Chieng’ Ruoth nobi mana kaka jakuo biro gotieno ,
ji nobed kawacho ni kue nitie , kendo weche ni kare , to ka diemo wang’ nono masira nopogi , mana kaka muoch poyo dhako man gi ich , kendo ok ginitony kata matin .
To un owetewa , ok un e mudho , ma dimi odiechieng’no pou ka jakuo ,
nimar un duto un nyithind ler , kendo nyithind odiechieng’ . Ok wan mag otieno , kata mag mudho .
Omiyo kik wanindi kata ji mamoko duto nindo , to wanenuru ka waritore maber .
Joma nindo to nindo gotieno , kendo jomer bende mer gotieno .
To wan , jogo mag odiechieng’ , waritreuru ka waserwako yie gi hera kaka akor mar lweny , kendo ka waserwako geno mar warruok kaka ogut lweny .
Nyasaye ok oseketowa ni mondo okumwa , to oseketowa ni mondo wayud warruok kuom Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo .
Kristo ne othonwa ni mondo kata ka wangima , kata watho , to wabed mangima kode .
Kuom mano , jiwreuru kendo konyreuru , mana kaka koro utimoni .
To wakwayou owetewa , ni mondo uluor jogo matiyonu matek . Gin jotendu kuom Ruoth , kendo gipuonjou .
Migiuru duong’ ahinya , kendo hergiuru nikech tich ma gitiyo . Beduru gi kue e kindu uwegi .
Owetewa , wakwayou ni mondo usiem joma budho abudha nono kayiem , kendo uduog chuny joma luor , bende ukony joma yomyom , kendo uhoru mos gi ji duto .
Neuru ni onge ng’ato machulo richo kar richo , to ndalo duto temuru mondo utim maber e kindu uwegi , kendo ni ji duto .
Beduru mamor pile .
Lemuru ma ok uwe ,
kendo gouru ni Nyasaye erokamano , kata gima nade ema timore , nikech mano e gima Nyasaye dwaro ni mondo utim kaka jo-Kristo .
Kik usind Roho tiyo ,
kendo kik ucha weche mag joma hulo wach moa kuom Nyasaye .
Temuru gik ma kamago duto , kendo rituru mabeyo kuomgi ,
to weuru maricho duto .
Nyasaye owuon ma wuon kue mondo omi ubed maler chutho , kendo orit chunyu gi ngimau kod ringreu , mondo ka Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo obiro , to ubed joma onge bura chuth .
Jal maluongou en jaadiera , kendo enotim kamano .
Owetewa , wan bende lemnwauru .
Yogreuru owete duto gi mos mar jo-Nyasaye .
Achikou matek e nying Ruoth mondo usom baruani ni owete duto .
Ng’wono mar Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo mondo obed kodu .
An Paulo , kaachiel gi Silvano , kod Timotheo , wandikonu un kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Thesalonika moyie kuom Nyasaye Wuonwa kod Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo .
Ng’wono gi kue moa kuom Nyasaye Wuoro kod Ruoth Yesu Kristo obed kodu .
Owetewa , nyaka wago erokamano ni Nyasaye nikech un . Owinjore mondo watim kamano nimar yie ma un-go medore ahinya , kendo hera ma ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu oherogo wadgi bende medore moloyo .
Mano emomiyo wan wawegi wapuoyou ni kanyakla mag jo-Nyasaye , nikech udhil gi sand kod chandruok muneno , to pod uyie ayiea motegno .
Mano en gima nyiso ratiro ni bura mar Nyasaye ni kare , nimar kuseneno sand kod chandruok nikech Loch Nyasaye kamano , to e giko , mano nomi kwanu ka joma owinjore yudo gueth mar Lojno .
Adier , kaka Nyasaye en ng’ama kare , enosand joma sandou ,
to noresu un muneno sandruok , kendo wan bende noreswa . Mano notimre ka Ruoth Yesu ofwenyore , koa e polo gi malaika mage man gi teko ,
e mach maliel mondo ochul kuor ni joma ok oyie Nyasaye , kendo ni joma odagi winjo Wach Maber man kuom Ruodhwa Yesu .
Giniyud kum ma en lal ma nyaka chieng’ , koriembgi mabor gi tekone man gi duong’ .
Mano notimre chieng’ ma Ruoth obiroe mondo oyud duong’ kuom joge duto , kendo oyud luor kuom joma oyie kuome . Un bende unubed kuom jogo , nikech ne uyie wach mane wakelonu .
Mano emomiyo walemonu pile , kwakwayo ni mondo Nyasachwa omi ubed joma owinjore gi ngima moluongoue , kotiyo gi tekone mondo ochop dwaro mabeyo duto ma un-go , kendo omi tichu duto , mutiyo nikech yie ma un-go , odhi maber .
Walemo ni mondo nying Ruodhwa Yesu oyud duong’ kuomu , kendo ni mondo un bende uyud duong’ nikech un joge . Nyasachwa kod Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo mondo omi gima kamano otimre kuom ng’wonone .
To koro wadwaro wuoyo kodu kuom biro mar Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo , kendo kaka ibiro chokowa kanyakla mondo waromne .
Wakwayou mondo kik uparru , kata kik chunyu chandre , kugalo ni Chieng’ Ruoth osechopo .
Kik uyie mondo ng’ato owuondu e yo moro amora , bed ni en yor fweny , kata en wach ma ng’ato ohulo , kata barua moro muparo ni mit oa kuomwa , nimar chiengno ok nobi kapok Piem Mogik obetie , kendo kapok Ng’at Mochayo Chik othinyore . En e Jal ma gikone en mana lal .
Obiro sungore , kokwero gimoro amora miluongo ni nyasaye , kata gimoro amora milamo . Enohedhre kata mana bet e Hekalu mar Nyasaye , kohulo owuon ni en Nyasaye .
Donge unyalo paro ni kane pod an kodu , to ne anyisou wachni ?
To koro nyaka bed ni ung’eyo gima pod osinde ni mondo kik ofwenyre nyaka ndalo moketne chopi .
Teko mopondo mar tich Chayo Chik koro tiyo ling’ling’ , to ka jal ma koro sindo Ng’at Mochayo Chik ogol oko , to tekono nofwenyre .
Bang’e Ng’at Mochayo Chik nothinyre , to Ruoth Yesu nobi gi duong’ne duto , mi nonege gi muya moa e dhoge , kendo notiek tekone duto .
Biro mar Ng’at Mochayo Chikno nobed tich Satan . Notim honni duto gi ranyisi mag miriambo ,
kod wuond duto maricho miwuondogo joma olal . Jogo nolal kamano nikech gidagi hero adiera manyalo miyo gikwo .
Mano emomiyo Nyasaye ooronigi teko moro mondo owuondgi , kendo omi giyie gima ok adier .
Kamano nokum ji duto mane otamore yie adiera , to ohero mana richo .
Un owetewa ma Ruoth ohero , nyaka wago ni Nyasaye erokamano pile nikech un , nimar un ema Nyasaye noyierou nyaka a chakruok mondo uyud warruok , ka opuodhou gi Roho , kendo kuom yie ma un-go kuom adiera .
Ne oluongou mondo uyud warruokni kuom Wach Maber ma walando , kendo mondo un bende uyud duong’ mar Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo .
Emomiyo owetewa , chung’uru matek . Makuru puonj mane wapuonjou gi dhowa kod barupewa .
Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo owuon , gi Nyasaye Wuonwa moseherowa gi hera maduong’ , kendo mosejiwowa gi jip mochwere , kendo mosemiyowa geno maber , kuom ng’wonone ,
To koro owetewa , lemnwauru mondo Wach Ruoth olandre piyopiyo , kendo oyud duong’ kaka osetimore e kindu .
Lemuru bende mondo Nyasaye oreswa kuom joma okethore , kendo kuom joma timbegi richo , nikech ji duto ok gin joma oyie .
To Ruoth en jaadiera , omiyo enojiwu , kendo enoritu kuom Ng’ama Rach .
To wan , Ruoth miyo wageno ni utimo gik moko duto ma wawachonu , kendo ni ubiro medo timo kamano .
Ruoth mondo omi chunyu omed hero Nyasaye , kendo ubed gi kinda machalo gi kinda mane Kristo nigo .
To owetewa , wachikou e nying Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo ni , pogreuru kuom owete mabudho abudha kayiem nono , kendo ok luw chik mane uyudo kuomwa .
Un uwegi ung’eyo kaka onego uluw timwa , nimar kane wan kodu ne ok wabudh abudha .
Ne ok wayudo chiemo nono kuom ng’ato ma ok wachulo , to ne watiyo matek gi luchwa odiechieng’ gotieno , mondo kik wami ng’ato kuomu ting’ mapek .
Ok ne watimo kamano nikech ne waonge gi ratiro mar yudo konyruok kuomu , to ne watimo kamano mana ni mondo wabed ranyisi munyalo luwo .
Adier , kane wan kodu to ne wamiyou chik ni ka ng’ato ok dwar mondo oti , to kik ochiem .
Wawacho kamano nikech wawinjo ni nitie jomoko kuomu mabudho abudha ka ok tim gimoro , to tije jowadgi ema gikeloe weche .
E nying Ruoth Yesu Kristo wagolo chik ni joma kamago , kendo wasiemogi ni mondo giti gi kue , giyud gik ma gikonyorego .
To un owetewa , kik uol gi timo maber .
Ka ng’at moro ok oyie winjo gima wawacho e baruani , to ng’iuru ng’atno maber , kendo pogreuru kode , nikech mano dipo ka okuodo wiye .
To kik ukwane ka jasigu , to siemeuru ka owadu kuom Kristo .
Ruodh kue owuon mondo omiu kue mare pile e yore duto . Ruoth obed kodu uduto .
An Paulo andiko mosni gi lweta awuon . En kido ma aketo e barupena duto , kendo mano e kaka andiko .
Ng’wono mar Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo obed kodu uduto .
An Paulo , jaote mar Kristo Yesu kuom chik mar Nyasaye ma Jawarwa gi Kristo Yesu ma en geno marwa ,
andikoni in Timotheo , nyathina maradier kuom yie . Ng’wono gi miwafu kod kue moa kuom Nyasaye Wuonwa gi Kristo Yesu obed kodi .
Adwaro mondo imed dak Efeso mana kaka ne akwayi mondo itim , kane oyudo awuok adhi e piny Makedonia . Ji moko ni Efeso kuno mapuonjo puonj mayore , to nyaka ikwergi mondo giwe timo kamano .
Bende nyisgi mondo giwe keto chunygi kuom sigendini manono kod sigendini mag anywola , nimar mago gin mana weche makelo mbaka ma ok rum , to ok gimi ji ng’e cheno mar Nyasaye , miyudo kuom yie .
Gima omiyo ne anyisi mondo itim kamano en ni mondo hera mawuok e chuny maler maonge bura , kendo man gi yie maradier , obedie .
Ji moko oseweyo luwo mago , mi obayo yo , kendo odonjo e mbekni manono .
Chunygi dwaro mondo gibed jopuonj Chik Nyasaye , to ok ging’eyo tiend weche ma giwacho , kata mana tiend puonj ma gipuonjo ka giramo ni e adier .
Wang’eyo ni Chik ber , ka ji tiyo kode kare ,
ka ging’eyo ni Chik ok oketi ni joma beyo , to okete ni joma ketho chik maroyiem , gi joma ok oluoro Nyasaye , kod joma onjawni . Bende okete ni jonek wuonegi kata minegi kata mana jomoko nono .
Okete bende ni joma terore , kendo ni chwo materore gi chwo wetegi , kendo ni joma kwalo ji , gi jomriambo , gi joma kuong’ore gi miriasia . Chutho Chik oketi ni ng’ato ang’ata matimo gimoro amora makedo gi puonj maradier .
Puonjno owinjore kod Wach Maber mawuoyo kuom duong’ maler mar Nyasaye mipako . Wach maberno ema ne Nyasaye omiya mondo alandi .
Agoyo erokamano ni Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo kuom miya teko mondo ati tijni , nikech nokwana ka jaadiera , mi oyiera mondo atine .
Kata obedo ni ne an ng’at mayanyo nyinge , kendo ma jasand ji , kendo ma jakwinyo , to ne okecha nikech ne atimo gigo kane pok ayie , kendo ka akia gima atimo .
Bende Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo ne onyisa ng’wono mogundho ahinya , kaachiel gi yie kod hera ma wayudo ka wan kuome .
Wach maradier kendo mowinjore ji oyiego chuth en ni , “ Yesu Kristo nobiro e piny mondo owar joricho , ” To an e jaricho marachie moloyo joricho duto ,
to Yesu Kristo ne okecha mana ni mondo kuoma ema okwong onyisie ji kaka ojahore mos ahinya . Nodwaro bende mondo obed ranyisi ni joma biro yie kuome mondo oyud ngima mochwere .
Opak Ruoth mochwere ! En Ruoth ma ok tho , kendo ma ok ne . En e Nyasaye kende . Duong’ obedne ma nyaka chieng’ . Amin .
Koro Timotheo nyathina , asemiyi chikno kaluwore gi weche mane johul wach moa kuom Nyasaye okoro kuomi chon . Ked lweny maber , ka wechego jiwi ,
kendo bed gi yie motegno , kionge gi gimoro ma dimi chunyi thagi . Jomoko osetimo gik ma chunygi nyisogi ni ok kare , omiyo koro giseweyo yie mane gin-go , mi gilal .
Humenayo gi Aleksander gin ji ma kamago . Aseketogi e lwet Satan mondo gipuonjre ni kik giyany Nyasaye .
Koro wach mokwongo ma akwayo en ni mondo ji oter ywakgi ir Nyasaye ka gilemo kendo ka gisayo ni ji duto , kendo gigoyo erokamano .
Nyaka gilem ni ruodhi gi jotelo duto , mondo wadag e ngima mokue kendo moboch , kwaluoro Nyasaye , kendo ka wan joma odimbore chuth .
Lemo ma kamago en gima ber kendo malong’o ni Nyasaye Jawarwa ,
ma dwaro mondo ji duto okwo , kendo ong’e adiera .
Nyasaye en achiel , to e kinde kod ji bende nitie jagach achiel , ma en Yesu Kristo , ma bende en dhano kaka ji .
En ne ochiwore mondo owar ji duto . Kamano kane kinde mowinjore ochopo , to nonyiso ratiro ni Nyasaye dwaro waro ji duto .
Mano emomiyo noketa jaote , mondo aland wachno , kapuonjo joma ok jo-Yahudi wach mar yie maradier . Ok ariambi , to awacho adiera !
Emomiyo adwaro ni mondo kamoro amora ma ji ochokoree e lemo , to chwo ema mondo olem . To nyaka gibed joma ler , manyalo ting’o luetgi malo kaonge gi mirima kata mbaka moro e chunygi .
Mon bende onego rwakre gi lewni mowinjore , ka gibidhore kendo giritore kare . Rwakruokgi kik bed mana mar kado wich , kata mar dhahabu , kata kite mabeyo , kata lewni ma nengogi tek ,
to onego girwakre gi timbe mabeyo kaka owinjore gi mon ma wacho ni oluoro Nyasaye .
Mon mondo opuonjre koling’ , kendo koyie winjo wach .
Ok ayie mondo dhako opuonj ji kata mondo otel ni chwo , to ber mondo oling’ ,
nikech Adam ema nochue mokwongo , eka ochue Hawa .
Bende ok Adam ema ne owuondi , to Hawa ema nowuondi modoko jaketho .
To kata kamano , dhako noyud resruok e yor nywolo nyithindo , ka osiko e yie gi hera gi puodhruok kod ritruok .
En wach madieri ni ka ng’ato dwaro mondo obed jatend kanyaka mar jo-Kristo , to odwaro tich mogen .
Kuom mano jatend kanyakla mar jo-Kristo nyaka bed ng’at ma wach moro marach onge kuome , kendo mokendo dhako achiel kende , bende nyaka obed ng’at moritore , mobidhore , modimbore , mohero rwako welo , kendo ma japuonj molony .
Kik obed jakong’o , kata ng’at mohero goruok , to nyaka obed ng’at mamuol ma ok ohero dhaw , bende ma ok ohero pesa .
Nyaka obed ng’at morito dalane adimba , kendo mochiko nyithinde kaka owinjore mondo gimiye luor ,
nikech ka ng’ato kia rito dalane owuon , to ere kaka dorit kanyakla mar jo-Nyasaye ?
Kik obed ng’at mowar machiegni , dipo ka sunga omake , mi bura mane oloyo Satan oloye en bende .
Bende nyaka obed ng’at ma joma ok jo-Kristo ogeno , mondo kik ji yud thuolo mar chaye , ma dimi opodhi e obadho mar Satan .
Kamano jokony jotend kanyakla mar jo-Kristo bende nyaka bed joma odimbore , to ok joma dhogi ariyo , kata jokong’o , kata joma oowore ni yudo ohala .
Nyaka gibed joma onge ketho moro ma gipando e chunygi , kendo nyaka gibed joma omako adiera mar yie marwa matek .
To kapok gichako tich to nyaka temgi , mondo one ane ka gionge ketho moro .
Kamano mondgi bende nyaka bed gi tim makare , to kik gibed mon ma jokuoth , to gibed mon moritore , kendo ma jo adiera e weche duto .
Jokony jotend kanyakla mar jo-Kristo nyaka bed joma nigi mon achiel achiel , kendo gibed joma rito nyithindgi gi miegi maber .
Jokony jotend kanyakla mar jo-Kristo matiyo maber yudo nying’ maber , kendo gin gi ratiro mar lando wach yie ma wan-go kuom Kristo Yesu .
Andikoni baruani ka ageno biro iri mapiyo ,
to kapo ni adeko , to baruani biro nyisi kaka jood Nyasaye onego owuothi . Jood Nyasaye en kanyakla mar joma oyie kuom Nyasaye Mangima , kendo e siro kod mise ma adiera oyiengoree .
Chutho , mano kaka adiera mar yie mwapuonjo duong’ ahinya ! Owacho niya , “ Kristo nobiro e ringruok ka dhano . Roho ne onyis ni oonge gi ketho . Malaika ne onene . Ne oland nyinge e kind ogendini . Ji ne oyie kuome e piny ngima Ne otere malo e duong’ . ”
Roho wacho malong’o ni e ndalo giko , ji moko nowe yie marwa , ka gichiko itgi ni puonj mag jochiende ma miyo ji lal .
Jopuonj mag miriambo ma parogi odinore ka gima owang’ gi nyinyo maliet nowuond ji ,
ka gipuonjogi ni kik gikendi , bende ginikwergi mondo kik cham chiemo moko , ma Nyasaye ema ochweyo mondo joma oyie , kendo ong’eyo adiera , ocham gi erokamano .
To gik moko duto mane Nyasaye ochueyo beyo , kendo onge monego ji kuer , to onego chamgi kigoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano ,
nikech Wach Nyasaye gi lemo miyo gibedo maler .
Ka ipuonjo owete wechego , to inibed jatich maber mar Kristo Yesu , kendo weche mag yie kod puonj maber miseluwo nomi idongi .
To bed mabor gi sigendini manono mag pinyni maonge tiendgi . Bed kipuonjo timo timbe mowinjore gi luoro Nyasaye .
Ing’eyo ni ka ng’ato oketo chunye kuom tuke mag rieyo del , to mano konye mana e yore moko kende , to ka ng’ato oketo chunye kuom luoro Nyasaye , to mano konye e yore duto nikech okelone gueth e ngima ma sani , kendo e ngima mabiro bende .
Wachno en adier , kendo owinjore ji oyiego chuth .
Mano ema omiyo watiyo matek kendo wakedo , nikech wan gi geno kuom Nyasaye mangima , ma Jawar mar ji duto , to moloyo Jawar mar joma oyie .
Puonj ji wechego , kendo chikgi ,
ma ok iyie mondo ng’ato ochayi nikech itin . To bed ranyisi ni jo-Kristo , kuom weche miwacho , gi gik mitimo , kod hera miherogi ji , kendo kuom bedo jaadiera , bende kuom bedo ng’ama ler .
Ket chunyi kuom somo ni ji Wach Nyasaye , kendo kuom lando wach , kendo kuom puonjo ji , nyaka chieng’ moro abi .
Kik ijwang’ mich mar Roho mane iyudo kane okor wach kuomi e kinde mane jodongo oyieyoe luetgi kuomi .
Tim gigo gi chunyi duto mondo ji one kaka idongo e yore duto .
Tim kinda e wechego , kiritori iwuon , kendo kitimo gik mipuonjo . Kitimo kamano to iniresri iwuon , kendo nires joma winjo weche mipuonjo bende .
Kik idhaw ni ng’ama duong’ , to los kode mos , mana kaka dilos gi wuoru . Bende bed kod yawuowi mana ka gima gin omineni .
Mon madongo to bedgo kaka mineni , to nyiri kod mon matindo to bedgo kaka nyimineni e yo maler chutho .
Nyaka ipar mond liete modong’ kendgi chuth .
To ka chi liel moro nigi nyithinde kata nyikwaye , to ber mondo ginyis ni giluoro Nyasaye kuom gik ma gitimo e miegi , ka gikonyo jonywolgi gi jonywol jonywolgi , nikech mano ema long’o ni Nyasaye .
Chi liel hiehie en chi liel modong’ kende , maonge watne moro , en ogeno mana Nyasaye , kendo osiko kolemo , kendo osayo Nyasaye odiechieng’ gotieno .
To chi liel mohero raha to osetho , kata obedo ni ongima .
Puonj ji chikno , mondo mond liete obed ma onge bura .
Ka ng’ato ok nyal rito wedene , to moloyo ka ok onyal rito joode , to en ng’at mosekwedo yie marwa , kendo orach moloyo ng’at ma ok oyie .
Kik iyie mondo ondik nying chi liel ma hike pok oromo piero auchiel e kwan mond liete . To bende nyaka obed dhako modimbore kuom chwore achiel ,
kendo ma ji oyiego ni timbene beyo , bende moserito nyithinde maber . Bende nyaka obed dhako mohero rwako welo kendo moyie konyo jo-Nyasaye kadwokore piny e tich moro amora kaka lwoko tiend jo-Nyasaye , kendo nyaka oket chunye kuom tiyo tije mabeyo duto .
To kik iyie mondo ondik nying mond liete mapod tindo , nikech ka gombogi osegologi kuom Kristo , to gidwaro mondo okendgi .
Kamano bura loyogi , nikech giketho singruok mane gitimo mokwongo gi Kristo .
Bende ka giwuotho e mier ka gitiyo , to gipuonjore doko josamuoyo , to ok mana josamuoyo kende , to bende giting’o weche koni gi koni , kendo gidonjo e weche ma ok mekgi , ka giwacho gik ma ok owinjore giwachi .
Omiyo daher mondo okend mond liete matindo , mi ginywol nyithindo , kendo girit utgi , eka digitam jasikwa yudo thuolo mar wacho weche maricho kuomwa .
Mond liete moko osebayo yo , kendo giluwo Satan .
Ng’at moseyie , bed ni en dichwo kata dhako , man gi wedene moko ma mond liete , nyaka okonygi , ma ok oweyo ni jo-Kristo ting’ mar konyogi , eka jo-Kristo obed gi thuolo mar konyo mond liete modong’ kendgi chuth .
Jo-Kristo nyaka kwan jodongo motelo ni kanyakla mar jo-Kristo maber ka joma owinjore yud pok nyadiriyo , to moloyo onego gipar joma keto chunygi kuom tich lando wach , kendo kuom puonjo ji .
Muma wacho niya , “ Kik itwe dho dhiang’ ka ywayo lodi madiemo cham , ” kendo ni , “ Jatich ber gi pokne . ”
Kik iyie giwach ma odonjnigo jaduong’ kanyakla mar jo-Kristo moro , kaonge joneno ariyo kata adek .
Joma timo richo to ikwer mana e nyim ji ratiro , mondo jomoko bende obed maluor .
Amiyi chik matek e nyim Nyasaye kendo e nyim Kristo Yesu kod malaika maler ni , nyaka irit chikego . Kiyalo wach moro amora to kik ing’ad bura kapok iwinjo weche duto koni gi koni , kata kik idog ni ng’ato kayiem .
Kik irikni yieyo lwedo kuom ng’ato kikete e tich telo , nikech dipo ka iriwori kode e richone moro , to ritri ibed maler .
Ok onego imodh mana pi kende , to madh divai matin mondo okonyni iyi , nikech midekre ma in-go pile .
Jomoko richogi ong’ere ratiro , kendo terogi e bura , to jomoko richogi fwenyore mana bang’e achien .
Kamano bende e kaka timbe mabeyo bende nenore ratiro , to kata ka ok ginenre , to nyaka gifwenyre bang’e .
Owete manie tich misumba nyaka kwan ruodhigi ka joma onego mi luor duto , mondo kik ji cha nying Nyasaye , kod wach mwapuonjo .
To wasumbini man gi ruodhi moyie kuom Kristo kik cha ruodhigigo mana nikech gin owete , to nyaka gitinigi maber moloyo , nikech joma gitiyonigigo gin owete ma gihero . Ka ipuonjo to wechego ema nyaka ijiw malong’o .
To ka ng’ato kelo puonj mayore , kendo ma ok oluwore gi weche maradier gi mag Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo , kod puonj ma miyo ji luoro Nyasaye ,
to mano nyiso ni en ng’at ma jasunga , kendo ok ong’eyo gimoro . Oowore mana gi mino wach , kod goyo mbaka makelo nyiego , gi daw , gi hango wach , gi chich maricho mamiyo ji parruok ,
kod dondruok maonge giko . Joma timo gik ma kamago gin joma parogi okethore , kendo ma adiera oselalnigi . Giparo ni lamo Nyasaye nyalo kelonigi ohala !
To chutho , lamo Nyasaye nyalo keloni ng’ato ohala , to mana ka gik ma en-go orome .
Ne ok wakelo gimoro e pinyni , bende ok wanyal kawo gimoro waago .
Omiyo , ka wan gi chiemo kod lewni , to mago mondo oromwa .
Joma dwaro bet jomwandu podho e tem kod gombo mathoth mofuwo kendo mahinyogi . Gombo ma kamago rwako ji e kethruok , kendo miyo ji lal ,
nimar hero pesa e chakruok mar kit richo duto . Jomoko osegombo mondo oyud pesa mathoth , kendo mano osemiyo gibaro giweyo yie marwa , mi gichwowo mana chunygi giwegi gi chandruok mathoth .
To in ng’at Nyasaye , nyaka ibed mabor gi gigo duto , to dwar mondo ibed mana ng’ama kare , kendo moluoro Nyasaye , bende man gi yie kod hera , kendo motimo kinda , kendo mamuol .
Ked lweny maber mar yie kimako ngima mochwere , ma en ngima mane oluongie kane ihulo malong’o ni iyie kuom Kristo e nyim ji mang’eny .
Amiyi chik e nyim Nyasaye mamiyo gik moko duto ngima , kendo e nyim Kristo Yesu ma bende nohulo malong’o yie ma en-go e nyim Pilato .
Chikno en ni nyaka irit chik mane omiyi ma ok iketho , kendo ibed maonge bura nyaka Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo duogi .
Nyasaye mipako , ma en kende e wuon loch , nomi Kristo obi e kinde ma en owuon oseketo . En e Ruodh ruodhi , kendo en e jaloch moloyo joloch duto .
En kende ema ok otho , kendo odak e ler ma dhano ok nyal chopoe . Onge dhano mosenene , kata manyalo nene . Pak gi loch ma nyaka chieng’ obedne ! Amin .
Nyis joma nigi mwandu mag pinyni mondo kik gibed jong’anyi , kendo kik giket chunygi kuom mwandu manono , to gigen mana Nyasaye ma miyowa gik moko mogundho mondo wabedgo mamor .
Nyisgi mondo gibed joma timbegi beyo , ka timbegigo ema obedonigi mwandu mogundho , mayie pogo gik ma gin-go ni jowetegi .
Ka gitimo kamano , to ginikan mwandu ma nobednigi mise maber e ndalo mabiro , mondo giyud ngima ma en ngima maradier .
To in Timotheo , rit gima osemiyi mondo irit . Kik ichik iti ni weche manono ma onge tiendgi , kod mbekni ma ji goyo kuom gima giluongo ni rieko , to adier ok en rieko kata matin !
Jomoko mawacho ni gin kod rieko ma kamano osebayo yo mi oa kuom yie ma wan-go . Ng’wono obed kodu .
An Paulo , jaote mar Kristo Yesu kuom dwaro mar Nyasaye ,
andikoni in Timotheo , nyathina ma ahero . Nyasaye ne omiya tich mar lando ni ji wach ni osesingorenwa ni wayudo ngima kuom Kristo Yesu . Ng’wono gi miwafu kod kue moa kuom Nyasaye Wuoro gi Kristo Yesu Ruodhwa obed kodi .
Alemoni pile , odiechieng’ gotieno , kendo ka alemo to agoyo erokamano ni Nyasaye ma atiyone ka parona liw , kaka kwerena bende notiyone .
Ka aparo kaka pi wang’i nochwer to agombo neni , mondo chunya obed gi mor mogundho ,
nikech aparo yie maradier ma in-go . Yienino chalo gi yie mane Lois dani nigo mokwongo , kendo mane Yunike meru bende ni-go .
Mano emomiyo aparoni mondo ichier mich mar chuny mane Nyasaye omiyi kane ayieyo lweta kuomi .
Nyasaye ne ok omiyowa chuny mar bedo ngoche , to nomiyowa chuny mar bedo gi teko , gi hera , kod ritruok .
Omiyo kik wiyi kuodi kod nyiso ji wach Ruodhwa , kata kik wiyi kuod koda , an ng’ate motue . To kuom teko mar Nyasaye , yie mondo ine masiche kodwa nikech Injili .
Nyasaye nowarowa kendo oluongowa mondo wabed joge owuon , ok nikech gimoro maber ma wasetimo , to mana nikech mano ema nodwaro kuom ng’wonone . Nyaka nene ne omiyowa ng’wononeno kuom Kristo Yesu .
To koro oseele kuom fwenyruok mar Jawar Kristo Yesu e piny . Kristo ema nosetieko tho , kendo osenyisowa ratiro kuom Injili ni ngima ma nyaka chieng’ nitie .
Ne oyiera mondo aland Wach Maber kaka jaote kendo japuonj .
Mano ema omiyo aneno masira kama , to wiya ok nyal kuot , nikech ang’eyo Jal mane ayie kuome , kendo aonge gi kiawa ni gima asemiye , onyalo ritona nyaka chop chieng’ Bura .
Nyaka imak puonj maradier mane amiyi , obedni ranyisi . Luw puonj ka in gi yie kod hera ma wan-go kuom Kristo Yesu .
Gima ber mane omiyino rit mang’won , ka Roho Maler konyi .
Ing’eyo ni owete duto manie piny Asia , koda ka Fugelo , gi Hermogene , oseringo oweya kenda .
To Ruoth mondo oguedh jood Onesiforo , nikech noduogo chunya ndalo mang’eny , kendo wiye ne ok okuot koda kane an e jela ,
to kane ochopo Rumi nomanya ahinya nyaka oyuda .
Ing’eyo maber ahinya kaka ne okonya e yore mathoth e dala mar Efeso ! Ruoth mondo okeche chieng’ Bura .
Omiyo in nyathina , bed motegno kuom ng’wono ma wan-go kodi , ka wan kuom Kristo Yesu .
Weche duto mane iwinjo ka apuonjo e nyim joneno mang’eny , to in bende nyaka inyis joma igeno , ma bende nyalo puonjo jomoko .
Yie mondo osandi kodwa kaka jalweny maber mar Kristo Yesu .
Jalweny maber ok dwar mondo oduodre gi weche mag dala , nimar odwaro bedo malong’o ni jal mane ondike .
Jang’uech maringo kar tugo bende ok yud osimbo mar locho ka ok oringo kaka chik dwaro .
Japur motiyo matek bende ema onego kuong yud pokne kuom cham moka .
Par gima awachoni , kendo Ruoth nokonyi ng’eyo tiend weche duto .
Par ni Wach Maber ma alando en wach Yesu Kristo , ma nyakwar Daudi , mane ochier oa kuom joma otho .
Wach Maberno ema omiyo isanda kendo itueya gi nyororo ka ng’at motimo gik maricho . To wach Nyasaye ok nyal tue !
Mano emomiyo adhil e weche duto nikech joma Nyasaye oseyiero , mondo gin bende giyud warruok man kuom Kristo Yesu , kod duong’ne mochwere .
Nitie wach moro maradier mawacho niya , “ Ka wasetho gi Kristo , to wanabed mangima kode bende .
Ka watimo kinda to wanalochi kode bende , to ka wakwede , to en bende nokwedwa .
Kata ka wan ok wabedo joadiera , en to pod en mana jaadiera , nikech ok onyal loko kite . ”
Nyaka ibed kiparo ni ji wechego , kendo chikgi matek e nyim Nyasaye , ni kik gimin wach , nimar timo kamano ok kony gimoro kata matin to kelo mana kethruok ni joma winjo .
Tem matek mondo inyis ji ni in ng’at ma Nyasaye oyiego , kendo mapuonjo wach mar adiera e yo makare , kaka jatich ma tichne ok kuod wiye .
To bed mabor gi weche manono mag oyuma , nikech joma ohero weche ma kamago medo mana bedo mabor gi Nyasaye ,
kendo gik ma gipuonjo chalo mana gi adhola manyamore .
Gisebayo yor adiera , ka giwacho ni ndalo chier osekadho , mi giketho yie mar jomoko .
To Nyasaye oseketo mise motegno mochung’ kogurore , kendo ondikie niya , “ Ng’ato ka ng’ato mahulo nying Ruoth nyaka pogre gi richo . ”
Ong’ere ni e ot moro amora maduong’ nitie agulini mopogore opogore , ma moko olos gi dhahabu kata fedha , to moko bende olos gi bao kata lowo . Mokwongo itiyogo tije mogen , to mokogo itiyogo tich aticha .
Omiyo ka ng’ato opuodhore oa e yore ma ok ler , to enobed kaka agulu mitiyogo tich mogen , nikech en ng’at mochiwore ni Nyasaye , ma Ruoth nyalo konyorego kuom tiyo tich moro amora maber .
Nyaka iring ia e gombo mag yawuowi , to ibed e kanyakla mar joma sayo Ruoth gi chuny maradier , kendo madwaro bedo joadiera , kendo madwaro tim makare gi hera kod kue .
Bed mabor gi mbekni mofuwo maonge rieko , king’eyo ni gikelo miero .
Jatich Ruoth ok owinjore bed makwiny , to onego obed ng’ama ng’won gi ji duto , kendo obed japuonj molony , mahore mos ,
kendo marieyo joma dagi wachne gi muolo . Kamoro dipo ka Nyasaye nyalo miyo chunygi lokre mondo ging’e adiera ,
kendo giyud rieko , mi gitony gia e obadho mar Satan , mosemakogi mondo gitim dwarone .
To ng’e malong’o ni kinde mag chandruok nobedi e ndalo mag giko .
Ji nobed joma oherore kendgi giwegi , kendo ma ohero pesa . Ginibed joma wuorore kendo ma jong’ayi , kendo ma yanyo ji . Bende ok giniwinj jonywolgi , bende ok ginibed joma goyo erokamano , kata joma oluoro Nyasaye .
Ginibed joma ok ohero jowetegi , kendo mamako sadha . Bende ginibed joma jokuoth kendo joma oowore , kendo jomahundu , kendo joma ok ohero gik mabeyo .
Ginibed andhoke kendo joma mwomore kendo josunga , bende ginibed joma ohero raha moloyo Nyasaye .
Ginitim gik mamiyo ginenore ka joma oluoro Nyasaye , to ngimagi to nonyis ni gionge gi teko ma luoro Nyasaye kelo . In to nyaka ibed mabor gi joma kamago .
Joma kamago ema yudo thuolo mar donjo e mier , kendo hoyo mon mayomyom mogangore gi richo , kendo ma gombo mayoreyore ywayo koni gi koni .
Gin mon matemo puonjore pile , to ok nyal ng’eyo adiera chuth .
Kaka Janes gi Jambre nokedo gi Musa , e kaka joma richogo bende kedo gi adiera . Gin joma parogi okethore , kendo joma yiegi orem .
To ok ginidhi nyime , nikech fupgi nofwenyre e lela e nyim ji duto , mana kaka fup Janes gi Jambre bende ne ofwenyore .
In to iseluwo puonjna gi timna kod gik ma adwaro timo e ngimana . Iseneno yie mara , gi dhilna , gi herana , gi kindana ,
gi sand misandago , kod masiche ma aneno . Ing’eyo gik moko duto mane otimorena Antiokia gi Ikonio kod Lustra , kendo ing’eyo kaka ne adhil e sandgo duto . To Ruoth ne oresa e mago te .
Chutho , ji duto madwaro doko joma oluoro Nyasaye kodembore kuom Kristo Yesu to nyaka yud sand .
To joma richo gi joma wuondore nomed bedo joma richo moloyo , ka giwuondo ji , kendo gin bende iwuondogi .
To in nyaka isik kirito weche misepuonjori , kendo ming’eyo ni adier , king’eyo ni joma ne opuonji gin ng’a gini .
Bende ng’e ni nyaka ia e nyathi isebedo king’eyo weche manie Muma ma nyalo miyi rieko makeloni warruok , ka iyie kuom Kristo Yesu .
Weche duto manie Muma wuok kuom much Nyasaye , kendo konyo kuom puonjo ji , kendo kuom kwero gik maricho , kendo kuom rieyo ji , kendo kuom tiego ji mondo obed joma kare ,
mondo jo-Nyasaye obed molony kendo moikore chuth ni tije mabeyo duto .
E nyim Nyasaye kendo e nyim Kristo Yesu , mabiro ng’ado bura ni joma ngima gi joma otho , aparo ni Kristo biro duogo mondo olochi . Omiyo amiyi chik ni ,
land Wach Nyasaye , kendo ket chunyi kuom tijno kinde duto , kata ka piny ber kata rach . Kwer weche duto ma ok ni kare . Kendo rie weche maricho , kijiwo ji kendo ipuonjo gi kinda duto .
Ndalo biro ma ji ok noyie puonj maradier , to giniluw mana gombogi giwegi , kendo ginidwar bedo gi jopuonj mathoth mondo opuonjgi mana weche malombogi .
Ginidagi winjo adiera , to ginichik itgi mana ni sigendini manono .
In to , bed modhil kinde duto . Nyaka iyie yudo masira kitiyo tich mar lando Wach Maber , kendo chop tich duto ma omiyi .
An to , ngimana chalo gi misango miolo piny e kendo-mar-misango , kendo kinde ma aago e pinyni chiegni ,
Asekedo lweny maber , kendo asetieko ng’weya , bende aserito yie marwa .
Koro gima okanna en mana osimbo mimiyo joma kare , ma Ruoth ma jang’ad bura makare biro miya chieng’ birone . To ok an kenda ema nomiya osimbo , to nomi koda ka ji duto morito birone gi chunygi duto .
Tem matek mondo ibi ira piyo ,
nimar Dema oseringo oweya , nikech ohero pinyni , kendo osedhi Thesalonika . Kreske to osedhi e piny Galatia kendo Tito osedhi e piny Dalmatia .
Luka kende ema wadong’go ka . Ka ibiro , to kaw Mariko ubigo , nikech okonya maber .
Tukiko to aseoro Efeso .
E kinde akinda ma ibiroe to kelna law mane aweyo Karpo e dala mar Troa , kendo ikelna kitepena , to moloyo mago molos gi pien .
Aleksander ma jatheth mula notimona marach ahinya , Ruoth chieng’ nochule kuom gik mane otimona .
In bende tang’ne , nikech nokedo matek gi weche duto mane awacho .
E kinde mokwongo mane achung’ie e bura mondo awach wachna , onge ng’ato mane ochwaka , to ji duto noringo oweya . To Nyasaye mondo ong’wonnigi .
Ruoth ne ochung’ buta momiya teko mondo aland Wach Maber chuth , mondo ji duto ma ok jo-Yahudi owinj Wach Maber . Kamano ne oresa e dho sibuor .
Bende ang’eyo ni Ruoth pod biro resa kuom gimoro amora madwaro hinya , mi ochopa maber e polo kuma olochoe . Duong’ obedne nyaka chieng’ . Amin .
Mosna Priska gi Akula , kod jood Onesiforo .
Erasto ne odong’ Korintho . Trofimo to naweyo ka tuo e dala mar Mileto .
Tem matek mondo ibi ira kapok ndalo koyo ochakore . Yubulo gi Pude gi Lino kod Klaudia , kaachiel gi owete mamoko duto , jomosi .
Ruoth obed gi chunyi . Ng’wono obed kodu .
An Paulo , ma misumba Nyasaye , kendo jaote Yesu Kristo , ema andiko baruani . Nyasaye ne oora mondo ajiw yie mar joma Nyasaye oyiero obed motegno , kendo mondo apuonjgi adiera mamiyo giluoro Nyasaye ,
kuom geno yudo ngima mochwere , mane Nyasaye , ma ok riambi osesingore chon ni nomiwa .
Nyasaye ma jawarwa ema nohulo wachne malong’o e ndalo mane en owuon oketo , kendo nogolo chik ni an ema onego miya tich mar lando wachneno .
Andikoni in Tito , nyathina maradier kuom yie moriwowa kanyakla , ka akwayo mondo ng’wono gi kue moa kuom Nyasaye Wuoro gi Yesu Kristo obed kodi .
Ne aweyo idong’ e chula mar Krete mondo ilos gik mane pod orem , kendo iyier jodong kanyakla mag jo-Kristo e mier duto , kaka ne achiki .
Ka itimo kamano , to nyaka iyier mana joma onge ketho , man gi mon achiel achiel , ma nyithindgi gin joma oyie , kendo ma ji ok chichgo ni ngimagi achach , kata ni wang’gi tek .
Jatend kanyakla mar jo-Kristo en jarit tich Nyasaye , omiyo nyaka obed ng’at maonge ketho . Kik obed ng’ama jasunga , kata ma jamrima , kata ma jamer , kata ma ohero goruok , kata ng’ama ohero pesa .
To nyaka obed ng’at mohero rwako welo , kendo mohero gik malong’o . Bende nyaka obed ng’at mabidhore , kendo ma jang’ad bura kare , kendo ma timbene ler , kendo mong’eyo ritore owuon .
Nyaka oyie chuth ni wach mwapuonjo en adier , kendo nyaka omake matek , eka onyalo jiwo ji gi puonj maradier , kong’eng’o joma tamore yie puonjno .
Chutho , nitie ji mang’eny ma wang’gi tek , kendo mohero weche mag ayiem , bende ma jowuond . To moloyo gin jo-Yahudi moyie kuom Kristo .
Nyaka kwergi mondo giling’ , nikech giketho mier ka gipuonjo weche ma ok owinjore gipuonji , mana ni mondo giyud pesa .
Janabi moro ma ja Krete wadgi nowacho niya , “ Pile jo-Krete gin jomriambo . Gin ondiegi maricho , kendo jowuoro ma josamuoyo . ”
Gima nowacho en adier ! Emomiyo siemgi matek mondo gibed gi yie motegno ,
ma ok gidewo sigend jo-Yahudi , gi chik mag ji modagi adiera .
Gik moko duto ler ni joma ler , to onge gimoro kata achiel maler ni joma okethore , kendo ma ok oyie . Parogi kod chunygi okethore .
Giwacho ni ging’eyo Nyasaye , to timbegi nyiso ni gidage . Gin joma timbegi mono , kendo ma ok winj wach , kendo ma ok nyal timo gimoro maber .
To in Tito , nyaka iwach mana weche mowinjore gi puonj maradier .
Nyak inyis joma dongo mondo obed joma oritore , kendo ma ok ohero oyuma , kendo joma bidhore . Bende gibed joma nigi yie motegno , kendo man gi hera kod kinda .
Kamano bende nyaka inyis mon madongo mondo obed joma oluoro Nyasaye e ngimagi , to kik gibed jokuoth , kata joma ohero kong’o , to gibed ranyisi mabeyo ,
mondo omi mon matindo opuonjre hero chwogi kod nyithindgi ,
kendo obed joma oritore , mangimagi ler , bende ma rito utgi maber . Nyaka gibed mon mang’won kendo moluoro chwogi , mondo Wach Nyasaye kik yany .
Kamano e kaka onego jiw yawuowi bende mondo gibed joma oritore e yore duto .
In iwuon nyaka ibednigi ranyisi maber , kendo kipuonjo , to nyis ni in ng’at moriere , ma ok dwar oyuma .
To ka iwuoyo , to wach mana weche maradier ma ji ok nyal chayo ni ofuwo , mondo okuod wi jasigu , maonge gima rach mowacho kuomwa .
Nyis wasumbini mondo owinj ruodhigi e gik moko duto , kendo gitinigi maber ma ok gidwok wach .
Kik gikwel , to ginyis malong’o ni gin joma inyalo geno adier e weche duto , mondo gimi ji one kaka puonj mar Nyasaye Jawarwa ber e gik moko duto ma gitimo .
Nyaka watim kamano nikech ng’wono mar Nyasaye makelo warruok ni ji duto osefwenyore .
Ng’wonono puonjowa mondo wawe richo gi gombo mag piny , mi wabed joma oritore kendo makare , ka waluoro Nyasaye e pinyni ,
kendo warito gueth ma wageno yudo , ma en fwenyruok mar duong’ maler mar Kristo Yesu , Nyasachwa maduong’ kendo Jawar .
En ema ne ochiwore owuon nikech wan , mondo oreswa e richo duto , kendo opuodhwa wabed joge moyiero , mondo watim timbe mabeyo .
Mago e gik ma nyaka ipuonj ji , kijiwogi kendo ikwerogi gi teko duto momiyi , to kik iyie mondo ng’ato o chai .
Par ni ji mondo ochiw luor ni joma nigi loch kod joma nigi teko , ka giwinjo wachgi kendo giikore tiyo tije mabeyo duto .
Nyisgi ni kik giwuo marach kuom ng’ato , kata kik gibed joma ohero dhaw , to gibed joma dwaro kelo winjruok , ka ginyiso ji duto muolo ma gin go .
Wan wawegi chon ne waonge rieko . Ne ok wawinjo wach , kendo ne wan joma ne olal . Ne wan wasumbini mag gombo mayoreyore mag ringruok , klendo pile ne wan gi ichlit gi nyiego e chunywa . Ne wamon gi jowetewa , kendo jowetewa bende ne mon kodwa .
Kane ng’wono mar Nyasaye Jawarwa kod hera ma oherogo dhano ofwenyore ,
nowarowa . Ne ok owarowa nikech tim makare moro amora ma wan wawegi ne wasetimo , to nowarowa mana nikech ng’wonone owuon . Nowarowa gi lwok mane Roho Maler okelonwago nywol manyien kod ngima manyien .
Kuom Yesu Kristo Ruodhwa , Nyasaye noolo Roho mogundho kuomwa ,
ni mondo ka osemiyo wabedo e winjruok kode kuom ng’wonone , to wadok joma geno chamo gikeni mag ngima mochwere .
Wechego gin adier , kendo adwaro ni mondo ine ni ji owinjore , mondo joma oyie kuom Nyasaye oket chunygi kuom timo gik mabeyo . Adier , wechego beyo kendo konyo ji .
To nyaka iwe mbekni mofuwo , gi sigendini mag anywola , kod dhaw gi piem kuom weche mag Chik Musa , nikech weche ma kamago onge ohala , kendo gin weche manono .
Kisesiemo ng’at makelo pogruok diriyo , to weri kode chuth !
Nyaka ing’e ni ng’at ma kamano parone osekethore . Okethore aketha kong’eyo .
Kinde akinda ma aoroe Artema iri , kata aoro Tukiko , to reti mondo ibi ira Nikopoli , nikech kuno ema aseneno ni ber mondo abedie ndalo chwiri .
Tem matek mondo ikony Zena ma jabura kod Apolo e wuodhgi mondo kik gichand gimoro e yo .
To nyaka ine ni jowa opuonjore tiyo tije mabeyo , mondo giyud gik ma gichando . Kik gibed joma budho abudha .
Ji duto ma wan-go omosou . Mosnwa osiepewa man gi yie . Ng’wono mar Nyasaye obed kodu ndalo duto .
Kuom Filemon , osiepwa kendo jatich wadwa : An Paulo , ng’at motue nikech Yesu Kristo , ema andiko baruani gi owadwa Timotheo . Wandikoni kaachiel gi kanyakla mar jo-Kristo malemo e odi .
Bende wadikoni nyaminwa Afia kod Arkipo jalweny wadwa .
Ng’wono gi kue moa kuom Nyasaye Wuonwa gi Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo obed kodu .
Agoyo ni Nyasaye erokamano pile ka aluongo nyinge e lemona ,
nikech awinjo wach yie ma in-go kod hera ma iherogo Ruoth Yesu , kaachiel gi jo-Nyasaye duto .
Akwayo Nyasaye ni , kaka ilando ni jomoko yie ma in-go , waduto wamed ng’eyo malong’o gueth mogundho ma wan-go nikech wayie kuom Kristo .
Owadwa , kane awinjo ni hera ma iherogo jo-Nyasaye oseduogo chunygi , ne amor ahinya , kendo an bende chunya noduogo .
Kuom mano , kata obedo ni an-gi ratiro kuom Kristo mar chuni timo gima onego itim ,
to akwayi mana gi muolo nikech hera ma waherorego . An Paulo ng’at moti , bende ma koroni otue nikech Yesu Kristo ,
asayi kuom wach nyathina Onesimo , mane odoko wuoda ka an e od tuech ka .
Onesimo yandi ok konyi , to koro okonyowa ahinya , in kaachiel kod an .
Aduoge iri , kata obedo ni ochalo ringra awuon kamano !
Da ahero mondo obed koda ka okonya kaeri , e kinde ma anie tuech nikech Injili ni .
To ok adwar chuni mondo ikonya , to daher mondo ikonya mana kuom ng’wononi . Kuom mano , ok anatim gimoro ka ok iyiego .
Kamoro nyalo bet ni Onesimo nowuok kuomi kuom ndalo manok , mondo chieng’ moro oduog iri ubed kode nyaka chieng’ .
To koro ok oduog mana kaka misumba kende , to oduogo ka ng’ama oloyo misumba , nikech osedoko owadu ma ihero kuom Kristo . An owuon ahere , to in ema ibiro here moloyo , nikech ibiro here kaka dhano , kendo ibiro here kaka owadu kuom Ruoth !
Omiyo , ka ikwano ni an kod in wan e achiel kuom yie , to rwak Onesimo kaka dirwaka .
Ka osetimoni gimoro marach , kata ka en gi gopi moro to kwan mano ka gima an ema an gi gopi .
Koro andiko wechegi gi lweta awuon , ka asingora niya , “ An Paulo , abiro chuli , ” ka ok aparoni ni gopa ma in-go en mana ngimani iwuon !
Par wachno owadwa ! Adwaro ni mondo itimna ng’wono kuom Ruoth e wachni . Duog chunya kaka ja-Kristo wadwa .
Andikoni ka ang’eyo ni ibiro timo gima asewacho , kata moloyo mano .
To bende , ikna kar bet , nimar ageno ni Nyasaye biro winjo kwayou uduto , mi oduoga iru .
Epafra , motuewago nikech Kristo Yesu , omosi .
Mariko gi Aristarko gi Dema kod Luka , ma gin jotich wetena , bende jomosi .
Ng’wono mar Ruoth Yesu Kristo obed kodu .
Chon Nyasaye nomiyo jonabi owuoyo gi kwerewa e yore mang’eny kendo mopogore opogore ,
to e ndalo mogikgi , Wuowi owuon ema osebedonwa wach Nyasaye . En ema Nyasaye osekete wuon gik moko duto , kendo en ema osemiye chueyo gik moko duto .
En ema orieny kaka duong’ maler mar Nyasaye , kendo en e kit Nyasaye hie , kendo en ema omiyo gik moko duto osiko nikech wachne man gi teko . Kane en owuon oseloso yor pwodhruok kuom richo , nobet piny e bat korachwich mar Nyasaye manie polo .
Kaka nyinge mar Wuowi mane omiye duong’ moloyo nying malaika , e kaka obedo maduong moloyo malaika .
Onge malaika moro mane Nyasaye owachone ni , “ In e Wuoda : tinendeni asedoko Wuoru , ” kata mane owacho kuome ni , “ Anabed wuon mare , kendo enobed wuoda . ”
To bende kane Nyasaye chiegni kelo Wuode makayo e piny , to ne owacho niya , “ Malaika duto mag Nyasaye mondo olame . ”
Ka owuoyo kuom malaika to owacho niya , “ Nyasaye loko malaikane yamo . Oloko jotichne ligek mach . ”
To ka owuoyo kuom Wuowi , to owacho niya “ A Nyasaye , lochni nosik nyaka chieng’ , kendo irito piny gi adiera .
Ihero timbe makare , to imon gi timbe maricho . A Nyasaye , mano emomiyo Nyasachi oseyieri ruoth , mowiri gi mo , komiyi mor mang’eny moloyo mor mosemiyo jowadu . ”
Bende owacho niya , “ A Ruoth , kar chakruok in ema nichweyo piny , kiketo mise mare , kendo ne iseloso polo gi lueti iwuon .
Gin to ginirum , in to isiko mochwere . Giduto ginidog moti , kaka law doko moti ,
mi iniban-gi ka law abola , kendo inilokgi kaka iloko law . In to isiko mana in , kendo hiki ok norum . ”
Nyasaye pok onyiso malaikane moro ni , “ Bed e bada korachwich ka , nyaka chop aket wasiki obed raten tiendi . ”
Kamano waneno ni malaika gin mana roho matiyo ni Nyasaye . Nyasaye orogi mondo gikony joma biro yudo warruok .
Mano emomiyo nyaka waket chunywa kuom mako weche ma wasewinjo , mondo kik waba yo .
Wach Chik mane malaika okelo ne nigi teko , omiyo ng’at mane ok oluwe , kendo ok orite , noyudo kum moromo kode .
Wan to dwatony nade , ka wajwang’o warruok maduong’ makama ? Ruoth Yesu owuon ema nokwongo nyiso ji wach warruokno , eka joma nowinjo wachno nonyisowa ni en adier .
Nyasaye owuon bende nonyiso ni en adier , kuom timo ranyisi gi honni kod tije madongo mopogore opogore , kendo kuom pogonwa mich mag Roho kaka en owuon odwaro .
Wawuoyo kuom piny mabiro , to Nyasaye ne ok oketo malaika mondo obed jotend pinyno .
Nitie kamoro e Muma mawacho niya , “ Dhano en ang’o ma dipare ? Koso Wuod dhano en ang’o ma didewe ?
Ne imiyo obedo matin moloyo malaika kuom kinde manok . Bang’e ne isidhone osimbo mar duong’ kod pak ,
bende ne iketo gik moko duto e bwo tiende . ” Ka Muma wacho ni Nyasaye noketo gik moko duto e bwo tiend dhano , to mano nyiso ni onge gima odong’ ma ok oketoe tekone . To koro pod ok wane ka gik moko duto oket e teko dhano .
To gima waneno , en mana Yesu , mane Nyasaye omiyo obedo matin moloyo malaika kuom kinde manok mondo otho ni ji duto kuom ng’wonone mar Nyasaye . En ema Nyasaye nosesidhone osimbo mar duong’ kod pak , nikech rem mar tho mane oneno .
Nyasaye mane ochweyo gik moko duto mondo otine ne dwaro mondo okel nyithinde mang’eny e duong’ne maler . Omiyo noneno ni ber mondo omi jal matelonigi e warruok bed ng’ama kare chuth bang’ neno sandruok .
Jal mapwodho ji , kaachiel gi jogo mipwodho , giduto gin nyithind ng’at achiel . Mano emomiyo oluongogi ni owetene , ma ok wiye okuot ,
kowacho niya , “ Anahul nyingi ni owetena . Anapaki gi wer e dier chokruok . ”
Owacho bende niya , “ Anaket genona kuom Nyasaye . ” Kendo owacho ni , “ Eri , an ka , kaachiel gi nyithindo ma Nyasaye osemiya . ”
Emomiyo kaka nyithindogo nigi ringruok mar dhano , e kaka Yesu bende nokawo ringruok mar dhano . Notimo kamano mondo , kuom thone , oketh loch jal man gi teko mar tho , tiende ni Satan ,
kendo mondo ogony joma luoro mar tho osemiyo obedo wasumbini ndalo duto mag ngimagi .
Nenore malong’o ni ne ok obiro mana ni mondo okony malaika , to nobiro ni mondo okony nyikwa Ibrahim .
Mano emomiyo nyaka ne obed machalo gi owetene e yore duto , mondo odog jadolo maduong’ mang’won kendo maradier , matiyo e nyim Nyasaye , katimo misango migologo richo mag jo-Nyasaye .
Kaka koro en owuon osekadho e tem mar neno masira , omiyo koro onyalo konyo jogo mitemo .
Emomiyo owetena ma Nyasaye osemiyo obedo joge owuon , kendo ma bende oseluongo mondo odhi ire e polo , paruru Yesu , mane ooro mondo obed Jadolo Maduong’ mar yie ma wahulo .
Ne obedo jaadiera ni Nyasaye mane okete e tich mana kaka Musa bende nobedo jaadiera e od Nyasaye .
Kwar jodhoot moro nigi duong’ moloyo jodhoode . Mano emomiyo Yesu bende duong’ moloyo Musa .
Jodhoot ka dhoot nigi kwargi , to wuon gik moko duto en Nyasaye .
Musa nobedo jaadiera e od Nyasaye duto , to mana kaka jatich , kendo nowuoyo kuom gik ma Nyasaye nowacho e ndalo mabiro .
To Kristo en jaadiera e od Nyasaye kaka wuowi ma jatend od wuon mare . Wan e jood Nyasaye , to mana ka wasiko gi chir kod geno ma ok dog chien .
Onego watim mana gima Roho Maler wacho e Muma ni , “ Winjuru dwond Nyasaye kawuono .
Kik wiu dog matek kaka ne wi kwereu odoko matek kane ging’anyo ni Nyasaye , e kinde mane giteme e thim .
Nyasaye wacho niya , ‘ Kwereu notema kuno mondo ong’e chunya , kata obedo ni giseneno gik mane atimo kuom higni piero ang’wen .
Mano emomiyo nakecho kod tieng’ni , mi awacho niya , “ Ndalo duto gitamore winjo chikena , kendo ok ging’eyo yorena , ”
Kuom mano mirima ne omaka , mi akuong’ora ni , “ Ok ginidonj kama antie mondo giyue koda . ” ’ ”
Owetena , beduru motang’ mondo kik ng’ato kuomu bed gi chuny marach matamore yie , mamiyo oweyo Nyasaye mangima .
To moloyo , jiwreuru ng’ato gi ng’ato kapod iluongo ndalo ni ‘ Kawuono’ , mondo kik richo gal ng’ato kuomu , mi bed gi chuny matek ,
nimar ka wamako geno mane wachakogo nyaka giko matek , to wanabed jocham gikeni kaachiel gi Kristo .
Muma wachonwa wan bende niya , “ Winjuru dwond Nyasaye kawuono . Kik wiu dok matek kaka ne wi kwereu odoko matek kane ging’anyo ni Nyasaye . ”
Ng’ano giri mane ong’anyo kane owinjo dwonde ? Donge gin jogo duto mane Musa owuokgo Misri ?
To ng’ano giri mane Nyasaye okechogo kuom higni piero ang’wen ? Donge gin joma ne otimo richo , mi ringregi odong’ e thim ?
Koso ng’ano giri mane Nyasaye okuong’ore ni ok nodonj kama entie mondo oyue kode ? Ne gin joma notamore winjo wachne .
Omiyo waneno ni ne ok ginyal donjo kar yueyone nikech ne gitamore yie .
Koro Nyasaye oseweyonwa singruok ni wanyalo donjo kama entie mondo wayue kode . Omiyo watang’uru mondo ng’ato kuomwa kik par ni thuolo mar donjo e yueyono osekadhe ,
nikech Wach Maber oseyalnwa mana kaka noyal ni joma chon . To wach mane giwinjo ne ok okonyogi , nikech , kata ne giwinje gi itgi kamano , to ne ok giyie gi chunygi .
To wan mwaseyie koro wadonjo kama Nyasaye nitie mondo wayue kode . Nyasaye wacho e Muma niya “ Mirima ne omaka , mi akuong’ora ni , ok ginidonji kama antie mondo giyue koda . ” Owacho kamano , kata obedo ni tije noserumo , chakre ndalo mane otieko chueyo piny ,
mana kaka Muma wacho kamoro kuom ndalo mar abiriyo niya , “ Nyasaye noweyo tijene duto , mi oyueyo chieng’ mar abiriyo . ”
To kaka waseneno , Muma wacho bende ni , “ Ok ginidonj ngang’ kama antie , mondo giyue koda . ”
Mano nyiso malong’o ni nitie jomoko moyienigi donjo kama Nyasaye nitie mondo giyue kode . To kaka joma ne okwongo winjo Wach Maber ne otamore yie mi ok odonjo mondo oyue gi Nyasaye ,
Nyasaye oseketo kinde machielo miluongo ni , ‘ Kawuono’ . Owuoyo kuome e Muma higni mang’eny achien , komiyo Daudi wacho niya , “ Winjuru dwond Nyasaye kawuono . Kik chunyu dok matek . ”
Ka dine bed ni Joshua osemiyogi kar yueyo , to Nyasaye ok dochako owuoyo kuom kinde machielo .
Mano nyiso ni yueyo machalo gi yueyo mar chieng’ Sabato pod nitie ma jo-Nyasaye nyalo yudo ,
nimar ka ng’ato odhi yueyo gi Nyasaye to oweyo tichne owuon mi oyueyo , mana kaka Nyasaye bende noweyo tichne ni oyueyo .
Emomiyo waketuru chunywa mondo wadonji e yueyono . Kik watamre yie kaka jogo notamore , nono to walal .
Wach Nyasaye ngima kendo tiyo , bende obith moloyo ligangla ma dhoge ariyo . Opowo chuny dhano , kendo odonjo nyaka iye mogik , kama opogoe paro gi chuny , kod fuoni gi ondhudho . Bende oketo bura ni paro kod dwaro manie chuny ng’ato .
Onge gimoro amora mochue , manyalo pondo ni Nyasaye , to gik moko duto elore e lela ni Jal ma nyaka wanyis gik ma wasetimo .
Emomiyo koro wamakuru yie ma wahulo matek , nikech wan gi Jadolo Maduong’ nosedhi nyaka e nyim Nyasaye . En Yesu Wuod Nyasaye .
Wan gi Jadolo Maduong’ manyalo kecho nyawowa nikech noteme e yore duto ma wan bende itemowae , to ne ok otimo richo .
Emomiyo wasuduru gi chir e nyim kom Nyasachwa mang’won , mondo okechwa , kendo okonywa kuom ng’wonone e kinde ma wadwaroe kony .
Jodolo madongo duto iyiero kuom ji , kendo iketogi mondo giti ni ji e nyim Nyasaye , ka gichiwo mich gi misengni migologo richo .
Ginyalo dembo joma kia kod joma orwenyo , nikech gin giwegi bende nyawo obembogi e yore mang’eny .
Mano emomiyo nyaka gitim misengni ma gigologo richogi giwegi mana kaka gitimo ni ji .
Bende onge ng’ama nyalo yierore kende owuon mondo okaw tich maduong’ mar bedo jadolo maduong’ , to Nyasaye kende ema yiero ng’ato , mi ket jadolo , mana kaka noketo Harun .
Kamano bende Kristo ne ok oyierore kende owuon mondo okaw duong’ mar bedo jadolo maduong’ , to Nyasaye ema nokete jadolo maduong’ kawachone ni , “ In e Wuoda , tinendeni asedoko Wuoru , ”
Muma wacho bende kamoro machielo niya , “ In jadolo nyaka chieng’ e kit tich dolo mar Melkizedek . ”
E ndalo mane Yesu odak e pinyni ka dhano , ne olemo , kendo osayo Nyasaye mane nyalo rese e tho , ka oywak malit , kendo pi wang’e chuer . Nyasaye nowinjo ywakne nikech dembruokne .
