Kata obedo ni ne en Wuod Nyasaye kamano , to nopuonjore winjo wach kuom masiche mane oneno ,
Kendo kane osebedo ng’ama kare chuth , nodoko jakel warruok mosiko ni ji duto mawinjo wachne ,
mi Nyasaye nochake ni Jadolo Maduong’ e kit tich dolo mar Melkizedek .
Wan gi weche mathoth ma dwawachnu kuom Melkizedek , to tugo tiendgi tek , nikech itu nok .
Tinde onego ubed jopuonj , to pod udwaro mana ng’ama puonjou nonro mar wach Nyasaye . Kar chamo chiemo motegno , to chak ema pod udwaro !
To ng’at mamadho mana chak kende pod en mana nyathi makwar , ma ok ong’eyo puonj man kuom wach makare .
Joma dongo to chamo chiemo motegno , nikech gisepuonjore , mi ging’eyo pogo gik mabeyo gi gik maricho .
Omiyo koro waweuru chakruok mar wach Kristo , to wadhiuru nyime gi puonj motegno . Ok onego wachak wapuonju weche mokwongogo , ka gima wachako waketo mise kendo , nikech ung’eyo ni nyaka ulokru uwe timbe materou e tho kendo uyie kuom Nyasaye .
Wasepuonjou weche mag lwok mopogore opogore , gi yweyo lwedo kuom ji , gi chir mar joma otho , kod kum mochwere .
To koro wameduru mana dhiyo nyime , kendo mano ema wabiro timo ka Nyasaye oyie .
Joma yande ler oserieny e chunygi , mi obilo mich mar polo , kendo opognigi Roho Maler ,
kendo obilo Wach Nyasaye , mi oyudo ni mit , mi ong’eyo teko mar piny mabiro ,
to bang’e odok chien , ok nyal dwoki mi chak lokre kendo , nimar gin giwegi giguro Wuod Nyasaye e msalaba , kendo gimiyo ichaye ratiro .
Nyasaye guedho lowo mamwonyo pi koth ma chuene pile , kendo manyago cham makonyo joma pure .
To ka lowono nyago mana kudho kod buya , to ikwane ni oonge ohala . Nyasaye chiegni kuong’e , kendo mach nowang’e mi tieke !
To jowadwa , kata ka wawuoyo kodu kama , to wageno ni ubiro yudo gik mabeyo ma warruok kelo .
Nyasaye en jaadiera , kendo wiye ok nyal wil gi tichu kod hera ma usenyiso ni uherego , ka ukonyo joge , kaka usebedo kutimo kendo pod utimo ,
to wagombo ahinya mondo ng’ato ka ng’ato otim kinda nyaka giko , mondo uyud chutho gima ugeno .
Kik utim samuoyo , to beduru joma luwo ranyisi mar jogo mayudo gik ma Nyasaye nosingore ni nomigi nikech giyie kendo gitimo kinda .
Kane Nyasaye osingore ni Ibrahim , to nokuong’ore gi nyinge owuon , nikech onge ng’ama duong moloye ma dine okuong’ore gi nyinge .
Nowacho niya , “ Anaguedhi adier , mi ami nyikwayi bed mang’eny . ”
Kuom mano , bang’ timo kinda , Ibrahim noyudo gima ne Nyasaye osesingorene .
Pile ji kuong’ore gi nying ng’ama duong’ moloyogi gi duong’ , kendo kuong’ruok ema itiekogo weche duto manie kind ji , mondo kiawa moro obed maonge .
Mano emomiyo Nyasaye ne oguro singruokne kokonyore gi kuong’ruok , nikech ne odwaro ni mondo jogo mane onego oyud gik mane osingorenigi ong’e malong’o ni gima ochano timo ok nyal lokore .
Kuom mano , Nyasaye nokonyore gi gik moko ariyo ma ok nyal lokore , kendo ma ok onyal wachoe miriambo , tiende ni singruok gi kuong’ruok . To wan , joma osetony , koro wayudo jip motegno ka wamakogo geno manie nyimwa .
Genoni ema wan go . Ochalo gi loch mogur , motue chunywa kuome . Ok ong’ingni , to omoko matek ta . Okadho nanga mar rageng’ , mi odonjo kama Ler Moloyo .
Kanyo ema Yesu nodonjoe nikech wan kotelonwa , kendo nodoko jadolo maduong’ nyaka chieng’ e kit tich dolo mar Melkizedek .
Melkizedekno ne ruodh Salem , kendo ne en jadolo mar Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto . Noromo gi Ibrahim kane Ibrahim dok dala koa loyo ruodhi , mi noguedhe .
En ema ne Ibrahim omiye achiel kuom apar , mag gik moko duto mane omayo ruodhigo . To tiend nying mar Melkizedek gin ariyo : mokwongo en ni ‘ Ruoth Makare’ , to bende en ruodh Salem , tiende ni ‘ Ruodh Kue’
Onge wach moro mondiki ni en gi wuon kata min kata anywolane , kendo onge wach chakruok mar ndalone kata giko mar ngimane . En kaka Wuod Nyasaye . Osiko jadolo nyaka chieng’ .
Parieuru duong’ ma jali nigo , ka Ibrahim kwarwa ema ne omiye achiel kuom apar mag gik mabeyo mope !
To chik ochiko nyikwa Lawi , ma gin joma tiyo tich dolo , mondo ochok achiel kuom apar mag gik moko kuom ogandagi , tiende ni gigol gigo kuom jo-Israel wetegi , kata obedo ni owetegigo bende gin nyikwa Ibrahim kamano .
Melkizedek to ne ok en nyakwar Lawi , to kata kamano Ibrahim nomiye achiel kuom apar mag gik mope , mi noguedho kata mana Ibrahim , ng’at mane oyudo singruok mag Nyasaye !
Ong’ere malong’o ni ng’ama duong’ ema guedho ng’ama tin .
To korka jodolo , to waneno ni joka Lawi , ma gin joma yudo achiel kuom apar mag gik mokogo , gin joma tho . Korka Melkizedek to waneno ni ng’at mane oyudo achiel kuom apar , Muma wacho ni pod ngima .
Chutho , wanyalo wacho ni kane Ibrahim ochulo achiel kuom apar , to kata mana Lawi nyakware , ma en ng’at mane onego oyud pok mar achiel kuom apar , bende nochulo pokno ,
nimar Lawi ne pod nie ringre Ibrahim kwar mare kane Melkizedek oromo gi Ibrahim .
Chik mane omi jo-Israel notenore kuom tich dolo mar jo-Lawi . To ka dine bed ni tich dolo mar jo-Lawi ochopo tichne maonge gima orem , to onge gima dine mi jadolo moro machielo wuogi e kanyakla mar Melkizedek , to ok e kanyakla mar Harun .
To ka kit tich dolo oloki , to mano nyiso ni chik bende nyaka loki .
Awacho kamano nikech Jal mwawuoyo kuomeni , tiende ni ruodhwa , noa e dhoot moro ma ng’ato pok oaye mondo oti tich dolo kendo-mar-misango .
Ong’ere malong’o ni Ruodhwa noa e dhood Juda . To kane Musa owuoyo kuom tich jodolo ne ok omulo nying dhood Juda .
To tiend wachni medo nenore malong’o moloyo , ka jadolo machielo owuok machalo Melkizedek .
Ne ok okete e tich dolo kaka chik pinyni dwaro , to nokete kuom teko mar ngima maonge gima nyalo ketho ,
mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ In jadolo nyaka chieng’ e kit tich dolo mar Melkizedek . ”
Chik machon osegol oko nikech oonge teko kendo ok onyal konyo gimoro ,
nimar Chik ne ok ochopo gima ne oketene . To geno manyien koro osekel , mamiyo wasudo machiegni gi Nyasaye .
To bende mano ne ok otim maonge kuong’ruok . Kane oketi jo-Lawi e tich dolo , to kuong’ruok ne onge .
Yesu to ne oket jadolo gi kuong’ruok , kaka Muma wacho ni , “ Ruoth Nyasaye osekuong’ore , kendo ok nolokre ngang’ kuom wachne mawacho ni , ‘ In jadolo nyaka chieng’ . ’ . ”
Mano omiyo singruok ma Yesu osiro ber moloyo singruok machon .
Nitie wach moro machielo bende , jodolo ma jo-Lawi ne nyaka bed mang’eny , nikech kaka gin dhano matho , tho ne monogi siko e tichgi .
Yesu to nigi tich dolo ma ok we ni ng’at moro machielo , nikech osiko nyaka chieng’ .
Kuom mano en gi teko mochwere mar reso jogo makadho kuome kasudo ir Nyasaye , nikech ongima nyaka chieng’ mondo okwanigi Nyasaye .
To jadolo maduong’ ma kamano ema wadwaro , nikech oler , kendo oonge ketho ; chilo moro onge kuome , bende osepoge kuom joricho , kendo oseting’e malo moyombo polo .
Onge gima dimi otim misengni pile , kaka jodolo madongo moko kwongo timo misengni ma gipwodhogo richogi giwegi , to eka gitimo misengni mipwodhogo richo oganda . En to notimo misango dichiel kende , kane ochiwore en owuon ka misango .
Chik Musa to keto dhano adhana manyap mondo obed jodolo madongo , to weche singruok mane Nyasaye okuong’orego mane obiro achien bang’ Chik , oketo Wuowi mosedoko ng’ama kare chuth jadolo maduong’ .
To wach maduong’ kuom weche ma wasewacho e ma : Chutho wan gi jadolo maduong’ ma kamano . Obet e bat korachwich mar Kom Duong’ manie polo .
Obet kanyo ka otiyo Kama Ler maradier , ma en hema ma Nyasaye ema oguro , to ok dhano .
Jodolo madongo duto oketi mondo ochiw mich , kendo otim misengni , omiyo jadolowa maduong’ni bende nyaka bed gi gimoro mochiwo .
Ka da en e pinyka , to da ok obedo jadolo kata matin , nikech nite jodolo machiwo mich kaka Chik Musa dwaro .
Tich ma jodologo chiwo en kido gi tipo mar tich manie polo , mana kaka tich Musa bende nobet , nikech kane Musa chako tich gero Hema mar Romo gi Nyasaye , to Nyasaye nowachone niya , “ Neni iloso gik moko duto machal gi kido mane onyisi e got . ”
To tich ma Yesu oseyudo ber moloyo tich jodologo , mana kaka winjruok ma okelo ber moloyo winjruok machon , nikech en winjruok ma singruok mabeyo moloyo ema guro .
Ka dine winjruok mokwongo bed ma onge wach moro moremie , to Nyasaye ok dodwaro winjruok mar ariyo .
To Nyasaye noneno wach moro morem kuom joge , mana kaka Muma wacho ni , “ Ruoth Nyasaye owacho niya , ‘ Ndalo biro ma anatimie singruok manyien gi dhood Israel kod dhood Juda .
Ok nochal gi singruok mane atimo gi kweregi , kane atayogi , kagologi e piny Misri , nimar ne ok girito singruok mane atimo kodgino , mi an bende ne ajwang’ogi’
To Ruoth medo wacho niya , ‘ Singruok ma anatim gi dhood Israel bang’ ndalogo e ma : Anaket chikena e parogi , kendo anandikgi e chunygi . Anabed Nyasachgi , mi ginibed joga
Onge ng’ama nopuonj wadgi , kata ma nopuonj omin mare , kawachone ni , “ Ng’e Ruoth , ” nikech giduto gining’eya , chakre ng’at matinie moloyo nyaka ng’ama duong’ie moloyo .
Anang’wonnigi giduto kuom timbegi maricho , kendo ok nachak apar richogi ngang’ . ’ . ”
To ka Nyasaye wuoyo kuom singruok manyien kamano , to mano nyiso ni osemiyo singruok mokwongo odoko machon , kendo ong’ere ni gima odoko machon , kendo oti , chiegni rumo .
Singruok mokwongo ne nigi chike moko miluwo kilamo Nyasaye , to bende ne en gi kar lemo molosi e pinyka .
Ne olos hema ma ong’ad iye ariyo . Kama ikwongo donjoe iluongo ni Kama Ler . Kanyo ema ne nitie rachung taya , gi mesa moketie Makati miketo e nyim Nyasaye pile .
To tok nanga mar rageng’ mar ariyo , ne nitie Hema moro miluongo ni Kama Ler Moloyo .
Ei hemano ne nitie kendo-mar-misango molos gi dhahabu miwang’oe ubani , kod Sandug Muma , gi ludh Harun mane oloth , kod kite mopa mondikie Singruok .
To ewi Sandugno ne nitie kido mag malaika miluongo ni kerubi , manyiso duong’ maler mar Nyasaye . Buombegi noumo kama igoloe richo . To ok wanyal wuoyo matut kuom gigo sani .
Kamano e kaka ne ochan gigo . Jodolo donjo e hema maoko pile , kendo tiyo tijegi mag lemo .
Hema mar ariyo to jadolo maduong’ kende ema donjoe nyadichiel higa ka higa . To bende ok onyal donjo kanyo ka oonge gi remo ma ochiwo mondo obed misango mopwodhogo richone owuon , kendo mopwodhogo richo ma oganda otimo ka ok ong’eyo .
Kamano Roho Maler nyisowa ni ka hema maoko pod nitie , to yo midonjogo Kama Ler Moloyo pok oyaw .
Mano en ranyisi manyiso kaka gik moko chalo e kinde ma kawuono . Onyiso ni mich gi misengni ma ichiwo ni Nyasaye ok nyal miyo chuny jalemo bedo malong’o chuth ,
nimar gik mobadhe gin mana chiemo gi gik ma imadho kod tim lwok mopogore opogore . Magi gin mana chik mag tim maoko ma oketi mondo oti nyaka chop kinde ma Nyasaye losoe gik moko manyien .
To koro Kristo osebiro . En jadolo maduong’ ma wuon gik mabeyo ma koro nitie ka . Hema ma otiyoe en hema man gi duong’ moloyo kendo malong’o chuth . En hema ma ok olos gi lwedo , tiende ni ok en mar piny mochueni .
Kristo nodonjo Kama Ler dichiel kende , to ok koting’o remb diek kata emb nyiroye , to mana koting’o rembe owuon , mi oyudonwa warruok mochwere .
Ka remb diek gi remb ruedhi kod buch roya mikiro nyalo pwodho ringre joma ogak mi gidok maler ,
to koro remb Kristo dipwodh chunywa maler marom nadi ! Kuom Roho mochwere , Kristo nochiwore owuon ni Nyasaye ka misango maonge songa , mi ogolowa e timbe materowa e tho , mondo walam Nyasaye mangima .
Omiyo Kristo e jal makelo winjruok manyien , mondo jogo mane oluongi oyud mwandu mochwere mane Nyasaye osingore ni gibiro yudo . Mano nyalo timore nikech tho osebetie makelo resruok kuom richo mane otim e ndalo winjruok machon .
To ka ng’ato lamo ni ji gige , to gigego ok pogi kapok ong’ere malong’o ni osetho .
To kapod ongima to lemoneno onge gi teko kata matin .
Mano emomiyo kata mana winjruok mokwongono ne ok ochako tich ka onge remo .
Mano en adier , nikech kane Musa osehulo ni ji chike duto , nokawo remb nyiroye gi diek , kaachiel gi pi , mi okiro e kitap Chik , kendo okiro kuom ji duto , nokiro remono gi yie rombo malando kod owino ,
kowacho niya , “ Ma e remo mar singruok mane Nyasaye ochikou mondo uriti . ”
Kamano bende e kaka Musa nokiro remo e Hema mar Romo gi Nyasaye , gi gik moko duto mane itiyogo e tich lemo .
Chutho , kaluwore gi Chik Musa to chiegni ni gik moko duto ipwodho gi remo , kendo ka remo ok ochuer , to golo richo onge .
Kane owinjore ni gigo , ma gin mana kido mag gik manie polo , nyaka pwodh gi misengni ma kamago , to kara gik manie polo hie nyaka pwodh gi misengni mabeyo moloyo mago .
Awacho kamano nikech Kristo ne ok odonjo Kama Ler molos gi lwedo , ma en mana kido mar Kama Ler hie , to nodonjo e polo hie , mondo koro ochung’nwa e nyim Nyasaye .
Ok odonj mondo ochiwre pile , kaka jadolo maduong’ donjo Kama Ler higa ka higa gi remb chiayo ,
nikech ka da bed ni otimo kamano , to dine osande pile , chakre chuech piny . To e ndalo ma piny rumoeni osefwenyore mana dichiel kende , ni mondo otiek richo , kochiwore owuon ka misango .
Ng’ato ka ng’ato nyaka tho mana dichiel kende , to bang’ mano Nyasaye yale .
Mano e kaka Kristo bende ne ochiw ka misango dichiel kende , mondo oting’ richo mag ji mang’eny , to obiro fwenyore kendo mar ariyo , to ok ni mondo ogol richo , to mana ni mondo okel warruok ni jogo morite .
To Chik Musa oting’o mana kido mar gik mabeyo mabiro , to ok giting’o gigo hie . Misengni ma jodolo timo ka luwore gi Chik gitimo higa ka higa . To mano nyiso ni Chik ok nyal miyo jolemo bed kare chutho ,
nikech ka dine ni Chik nyalo timo kamano , to misengnigo dowe chuth , nimar ka osepwodh jolemo chuth , to richo ok dichak chand parogi kendo .
To kar golo richo , to misengni mitimogo paronigi mana richogi higa ka higa ,
nikech remb ruedhi gi remb diek ok nyal golo richo .
Mano emomiyo , kane Kristo biro e piny , nowacho ni Nyasaye niya , “ Ok misengni kod chiwo ema nidwaro , to ringruok ema iseikona .
Misengni miwang’o pep , gi misengni mag golo richo , bende ne ok imorgo .
Omiyo nowacho niya , ‘ Era e ! A Nyasaye , asebiro mondo atim dwaroni , mana kaka Muma wacho kuoma e Kitap Chik . ’ . ”
Waneno ni mokwongo Kristo nowacho niya , “ Misengni gi chiwo , kata misengni miwang’o pep , gi misengni mag golo richo , ne ok idwaro , bende ne ok imorgo , ” kata obedo ni Chik dwaro mondo otimgi kamano .
To eka nowacho niya , “ Era e ! A Nyasaye , asebiro mondo atim dwaroni . ” Kamano Yesu Kristo ketho yo machon mar chiwo chiayo ka misango , to okelo yo manyien ma ng’ato chiwoe ngimane owuon .
Wan to opwodhowa nikech Yesu Kristo nochiwo ringre owuon nyadichiel kende , kotimo mana gima ne Nyasaye dwaro .
Jodolo duto mag jo-Yahudi chung’ katiyo tich lemo odiechieng’ , kendo ginwoyo mana misengni ma gitimo pile , ma ok nyal golo richo kata matin .
Kristo to notimo misango achiel kende mar golo richo , moromo nyaka chieng’ , mi obet e bad Nyasaye korachwich , mana kaka Muma wacho .
Chakre kindeno orito nyaka Nyasaye ket wasike bed raten tiende .
Osemiyo joma opwodhi kamano odoko joma long’o chuth nyaka chieng’ kuom misango achiel mane otimono .
Roho Maler bende nyisowa ni mano en adier . Mokwongo owacho niya ,
“ Singruok ma anatim kodgi bang’ ndalogo e ma : Anaket chikena e chunygi , kendo anandikgi e parogi . An Ruoth Nyasaye ema awacho kamano . ”
To omedo wacho ni , “ Ok nachak apar richogi kod kethogi ngang’ . ”
To ka richo osewe , to misango mar golo richo onge gi tich .
Emomiyo owetena , koro wanyalo donjo Kama Ler Moloyo gi chir , nikech Yesu osethonwa ,
mi oyawonwa yo manyien kendo mangima kuom ringre owuon , mondo wakadh nanga mar rageng’ wadonj e nyim Nyasaye .
Kaka koro wan gi jadolo maduong’ e od Nyasaye ,
wasuduru ir Nyasaye gi chuny maradier , kendo ka wan gi yie motegno , bende ka chunywa manyisowa ni wan joketho opwodhi , kendo ka ringrewa olwoki gi pi maliw .
Wamakuru matek gik mwahulo ni wageno kuomgi , mak wamindni , nikech Nyasaye mane omiyowa singruokne en jaadiera .
Ng’ato ka ng’ato nyaka par kaka onyalo jiwo wadgi omed bedo gi hera kod timbe mabeyo .
Kik wawe mak wachokore kaachiel , kaka jomoko oseweyo timo , to nyaka wajiwreuru ng’ato gi ng’ato , to moloyo onego utim kamano kuneno ka Chieng’ Ruoth sudo machiegni .
Ka wasiko watimo richo mana mar ayiem , bang’ ng’eyo adiera , to onge misango moro mapod odong’ manyalo golo richowa .
Gima odong’ en mana kibaji , kwang’eyo ni wachomo bura , gi mirima mager ka mach , ma Nyasaye biro tiekogo joma otamore yie kuome .
Ja-Yahudi moro amora machayo Chik Musa to inego ma ok okechi , ka nitie joneno ariyo kata adek manyalo hulo ni otimo kamano .
To koro parieuru kum malit moloyo ma ng’at machayo Wuod Nyasaye onego yudi ! Ng’at ma kamano osekawo remo mar singruok mane opwodhego ka gima nono , kendo osejaro Roho mar ng’wono !
Wang’eyo Jal mane owacho niya , “ An ema nachul kuor . Adier , anachul maonge kiawa ! ” kendo mane owacho ni ni , “ Ruoth nong’ad bura ni joge . ”
En gima lich miwuoro , lwar e lwet Nyasaye mangima !
Parieuru gik mane otimorenu e ndalo mokadho , kane ler mar Nyasaye orieny e chunyu . Kata obedo ni ne un e lweny mager kendo matek , to ne utimo kinda ka udhil .
Jomoko kuomu nodoko ka joma ourore e nyim ji , kiyanyogi kendo isandogi , to moko bende ne ok oringo oweyo joma ne itimonigi kamano .
Ne usandoru kaachiel gi joma ne otue e jela , bende ne uyie mondo oyak giu , kung’eyo ni un gi mwandu maber moloyo , kendo mosiko .
Emomiyo kik uwit geno ma un-go , nikech obiro kelo pok maduong’ .
To timuru kinda mondo utim gima Nyasaye dwaro , mi uyud gima osesingore ni nomiu ,
Kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Pod odong’ mana kinde matin kende , eka jal monego bi nobi . Ok nodeki !
Yie ema nomi ng’ata makare bed mangima . To ka odok chien , to ok nabed mamor kode . ”
Wan to ok wan kuom jogo madok chien kendo lal , to wan kuom jogo moyie , kendo ma Nyasaye biro reso .
To yie en ang’o ? Yie en bedo gi adiera ni wabiro yudo gik mwageno , kendo en bedo gi ratiro maonge kiawa ni gik ma ok wanyal neno , nitie .
Yie mane kwerewa nigo nomiyo Nyasaye oyie kodgi .
Yie ema omiyo wang’eyo ni Wach Nyasaye ema nochueyo gik moko duto manie polo gi piny . Ne omiyo gik mantie owuok kuom gik maonge .
Yie ema nomiyo Habil otimo ni Nyasaye misango malong’o , moloyo misango mane Kain otimo . Kuom yie mare Nyasaye noyie kode ni en ng’at makare , nikech Nyasaye noyie gi gik mane ochiwo , kendo kuom yieneno pod owuoyo , kata obedo ni osetho .
Yie ema nomiyo okaw Enoka , oter e ngima , mak okadho e tho . Muma wacho niya , “ Ne obedo maonge , nikech Nyasaye nosegole . ” Wang’eyo ni yie mane en-go ema ne omiyo ogole , nimar Muma bende wacho ni , “ Kane pok ogole ne en ng’at malong’o ni Nyasaye . ”
To ng’at maonge gi yie ok nyal bet malong’o ni Nyasaye , nimar ng’ama dwaro biro ir Nyasaye nyaka yie ni Nyasaye nitie , kendo ni en gi mich momiyo joma dware .
Yie ema nomiyo Nowa owinjo siem mane Nyasaye osiemego kuom gik mabiro . Ne omako wach , omiyo nohondho yie mi oresogo joode . Kamano noketo ni piny bura , kendo en owuon yieneno nomiyo obedo e winjruok gi Nyasaye .
Yie ema nomiyo Ibrahim oyie luong mar Nyasaye , mi odhi e piny mane Nyasaye osingore ni nomiye , kendo noweyo pinygi ka okia kuma odhiye .
Yie ema nomiyo odak mana ka jadak e piny ma ok mare , kata obedo ni ne en piny mane Nyasaye osingore ni nomiye . Ne odak e hema , mana kaka Isaka kod Jakobo bende nodak . Gin bende Nyasaye nosesingorenigi kamano .
Ibrahim nodak e hema kamano , nikech nogeno yudo dala man gi mise motegno , mane Nyasaye ema ochano kendo ogero .
Yie ema nomiyo Sara owuon bende onwang’o teko mar mako ich , kata obedo ni ne en migumba , kendo ndalone mar nywol nosekadho kamano . Noyudo tekono nikech nokwano ni Jal mane osesingorene en jaadiera .
Kuom mano Ibrahim , mane chalo gi ng’ama osetho , noyudo nyikwayo mang’eny ka sulue manie polo , kendo mathoth ka kuoyo manie dhonam ma ok nyal kwan .
Jogo duto notho ka nigi yie . Ne ok ginwang’o gik mane Nyasaye osingorenigi ni nomigi , to ne ginenogi gi kuma bor , mi giyie ni gin gik mantie adier . Ne gihulo ratiro ni gin mana welo gi jowuoth e piny ka .
Ka ji wuoyo kamano , to mano nyiso malong’o ni gigeno yudo piny ma margi giwegi .
Ka dine pod giparo ber mar piny mane giaye , to dine giseyudo kinde mar dok kuno .
To koro ne gigombo piny maber moloyo , tiende ni piny polo . Mano emomiyo wi Nyasaye ok kuodi kiluonge ni Nyasachgi , nikech oseikonigi dala .
Yie ema nomiyo Ibrahim ochiwo Isaka ka misango , kane Nyasaye oteme . Kata obedo ni Nyasaye nosesingorene ,
kendo onyise ni joka Isaka kende ema nobed nyikwaye , to pod ne oyie mana chiwo wuode ma midermano .
Ibrahim noyie ni Nyasaye nyalo chiero nga’t motho , kendo chutho nodwokne Isaka mana ka gima osechier oa kuom joma otho .
Yie ema nomiyo Isaka oguedho Jakobo gi Esau , kendo ema nomiyo owuoyo kuom gik mabiro timore .
Bende kane Jakobo chiegni tho , to yie ema nomiyo oguedho yawuot Josef moro ka moro , kendo olamo Nyasaye koyiengore e ludhe .
Yie ema ne omiyo Josef owuoyo kuom wuok jo-Israel e piny Misri , kane ochiegni tho . Nogolo chik bende kuom gima onego otim gi chokene .
Yie ema ne omiyo , kane onywol Musa to jonywolne nopande kuom dueye adek , nikech ne gineno ka en nyathi man gi chia . Mano omiyo ne gibedo gi chir , mi giketho chik ruodh Misri .
Yie ema ne omiyo Musa odagi ni kik luonge ni wuod nyar Farao , kane osedoko ng’ama duong’ .
Noyiero mondo osande gi jo-Nyasaye , kar bedo gi mor mar richo marumo bang’ ndalo matin ,
nimar noneno ni achaya miyudo nikech Mesia nigi mwandu maduong’ moloyo mwandu mag Misri . Noketo chunye kuom pok mane Nyasaye biro miye .
Yie ema nomiyo owuok Misri ka ok oluoro mirimb ruoth . Ne odhil mana ka ng’ama oneno Nyasaye ma ok ne .
Yie bende ema ne omiyo oloso Sap Pasaka , kendo okiro remo e sirni mag dhoudi , mondo Malaika ma Janek kik mul jo-Israel makayo .
Yie ema ne omiyo jo-Israel ong’ado Nam Makwar , mana ka gima en lowo motwo . Jo-Misri to kane otemo ng’ade , to pi noimo .
Yie ema ne omiyo ohinga mar Jeriko opodho kane jo-Israel oseluore kuom ndalo abiriyo .
Yie ema ne omiyo Rahab , dhako mane jachode , ok onegi kane inego joma ne otamore winjo wach Nyasaye . Ne ok onege nikech ne oserwako jombetre gi ng’wono .
To an dachak awach ang’o ? Thuolo ditama mar wuoyonu kuom Gidion gi Barak gi Samson gi Jeftha gi Daudi gi Samwel kod jonabi .
Yie ema ne omiyo giloyo pinje mamoko , kendo girito ji gi bura makare , mi giyudo ni Nyasaye ochopo singruokne .
Yie ema ne omiyo giumo dho sibuoche , kendo ginego gero mar mach , bende gitony e lweny . Kata obedo ni ne gin joma nyap , to yie nomiyo gibedo joma rateke , kendo gidoko joma ger e lweny , mi giriembo jolweny mane oa e pinje mamoko .
Yie ema ne omiyo ochier ni mon moko jogi mane osetho . Jomoko ne osand malit , kane ok oyie ni mondo oresi , nikech ne gidwaro ni chieng’ moro gichier e ngima maber moloyo .
Jomoko ne oyany kendo ochwadi , to jomoko ne otue mi oketi e jela .
Moko ne ogo gi kite , to moko nong’ad sirunda , to moko bende noneg gi ligangla . Ne girwakore gi piende rombe kod piende diek , ka gidhier kendo kisandogi , bende ka gin gi chandruok malit .
Ne gin joma beyo gilala ma ok owinjore bed e pinyni . Ne gibayo abaya e thimbe kod gode ka gidak e rogo kod buche manie lowo .
Jogo duto Nyasaye ne oyiego nikech yie mane gin-go , to kata kamano ne ok ginwang’o gik mane Nyasaye osesingore ni nomigi nikech nosechano gima ber moloyo , koparowa , tiende ni ne ok odwar miyo gidoko joma kare mak mana ka wan kaachiel kodgi .
Emomiyo ka koro oganda mang’ongo mar joneno opie molworowa ka bor polo kama , to wan bende waweuru ting’ duto kod richo maduodowa , kendo waringuru matek , kwanano ni ng’uech moseketwae .
Nyaka wachom wang’wa kuom Yesu ma jatendwa e yor yie , a chakruok nyaka giko . Ne oyie tho e msalaba , kochayo wichkuot mar tho ma kamano , nikech mor mane obiro yudo achien . To koro osebet piny e bat korachwich mar komduong’ mar Nyasaye .
Parieuru Jal mane odhil gi sigu mager mane joricho nigo kode mondo un bende kik uol kendo chunyu kik a .
E lweny mukedoe gi richo , pok ukedoe nyaka jomoko kuomu otho .
Koso wiu osewil gi weche Muma ma Nyasaye jiwougi , kowuoyo kodu kaka nyithinde niya , “ Wuoda , kik icha kum ma Ruoth Nyasaye kumigo , kata kik chunyi nyosre ka okweri ,
nikech ng’ama Ruoth ohero ema okumo . Adier , yawuote duto moyiego ema ochwado . ”
Nyaka ubed modhil nikech un joma ipuonjo , nimar chandruoku nyiso ni Nyasaye okawou mana ka yawuote . Koso bende nitie wuowi moro ma wuon ok kum ?
Ka Nyasaye ok kumu kaka okumo yawuote duto , to mano nyiso ni ok un yawuote hie , to un mana kimirwa .
To bende wuonewa mag pinyni ne kumowa , kendo ne wamiyogi luor kaka owinjore . To koro Wuonwa mar chuny dwami luor malich machal nadi mondo wayud ngima !
Wuonewago ne kumowa kuom kinde matin kaka ne giparo ni bernigi . Nyasaye to kumowa koparo gima dikonywa , ni mondo wadok joma ler , mana kaka en bende oler .
E sa mikumoe ng’ato , to kum ok nenre ka gima ber , to onenore mana malit . Achien to , joma osepuonji e yor kum nyago olemo mokue , tiende ni ngima maler .
Emomiyo jing’uru bedeu mobengore kod chongeu monyosore .
Losuru yore muluwo ochikre tir , eka tiendeu malit ok nowil , to nochangi .
Temuru mondo ubed gi kue kod ji duto , kendo beduru gi ngima maler , nikech ka ng’ato ok ler , to ok none Ruoth .
Ritreuru mondo une ni onge ng’ato kuomu molal , kendo oweyo ng’wono mar Nyasaye , bende kik sigu moro bed e kindu , manyalo kelo chandruok , mi keth ji mang’eny .
Ritreuru mondo kik ng’ato kuomu bed ng’ama terore kata ng’ama ok oluoro Nyasaye ka Esau , mane ong’iewo duong’ne mar nywol mana ni mondo ochiem dichiel kende !
Ung’eyo ni bang’e , kane odwaro mondo wuon mare oguedhe gi gueth ma wuowi makayo onego oyudi to ne okwere , nikech ne ok onyal yudo yo molokogo gima nosetimo , kata obedo ni ne odwaro yo ma dolokego gi pi wang’ kamano .
Un ok uchal gi jo-Israel machon . Ok uchung’ e nyim gima unyalo mulo , kaka ne gichung’ e nyim got Sinai , kama mach kaknie , gi mudho mandiwa kod ong’weng’o , gi kalausi mager ,
gi koko mar tung’ maywak , kod dwol malich . Joma ne owinjo dwolno nokwayo ni mondo owegi kik gichak giwinje kendo .
Luoro nomakogi nikech chik mane omigi ni , kata mana le kogere e godno to nyaka go gi kite , mi tho .
Gima ne ginenono ne lich mokadho , omiyo Musa nowacho niya , “ Luoro omaka , kendo atetni . ”
Ooyo , un uchung’ e nyim got Sayun , dala mar Nyasaye mangima , ma en Jerusalem manie polo , kendo uchung’ e nyim malaika gana gi gana . Unie nyim chokruok ma galamoro mar nyithind Nyasaye .
En chokruok mar nyithind Nyasaye makayo , ma nyinggi ondiki e polo . Uchung’ e nyim Nyasaye ma Jang’ad Bura ni ji duto , kendo e nyim chuny joma beyo ma Nyasaye osemiyo odoko joma kare .
Usebiro ir Yesu , jagach mosekelo winjruok manyien , ma rembe mokir nyiso wach maber moloyo wach mane remb Habil onyiso .
Ritreuru mondo kik utamru winjo dwond Jal mawuoyo kodu . Joma notamore winjo dwond Musa kane Nyasaye omiyo owuoyo gi ji e piny , ne ok otony . Wan to dwatony nadi ka watamore winjo Jal mawuoyo kodwa gie polo ?
Adier , dwonde noyiengo piny e ndalono , to koro osesingore niya , “ Pod abiro yiengo piny nyadichiel kendo . To ok piny kende ema abiro yiengo , to koda ka polo bende abiro yiengo . ”
To wach mawachoni , “ Pod nyadichiel kende , ” nyisowa ni ibiro golo gik mayiengni , tiende ni gik moko mosechue mondo gik ma ok yiengni ema odong’ osiki .
Emomiyo wagouru erokamano ni Nyasaye , nikech wanwang’o piny manyien ma ok nyal yiengni , walameuru kaka owinjore , ka wamiye duong’ kod luor ,
nikech Nyasachwa en mach ma tieko gik mowang’o duto .
Hera ma owete kuom Kristo oherorego mondo osiki .
Kik uwe mak urwako welo e miechu , nikech rwako welo nomiyo jomoko opo mana korwako malaika !
Paruru joma nie jela , mana ka gima un bende otueu kodgi . Joma chandore bende paruru mana ka gima un bende un kodgi .
Ji duto mondo okwan kend ka gima duong’ , kendo singruok ma joma okendore osingorego nyaka rit matek , nikech Nyasaye nokum joma terore , bed ni gin yawuowi gi nyiri , kata chwo gi mon .
Kik ubed joma ohero pesa , to gik ma un-go ema mondo oromu , nikech Nyasaye owuon osewacho niya , “ Ok anaweyi , kata jwang’i ok anajwang’i ngang’ . ”
Mano emomiyo wanyalo wacho gi chir niya , “ Ruoth e jakonyna , emomiyo ok nabed maluor . Ere gima dhano ditimna ? ”
Paruru jotendu mane owachonu wach Nyasaye . Paruru kaka ngimagi ne chalo , kod tich mane gitiyo , mondo un bende ubed gi yie machalo gi yie mane gin-go .
Yesu Kristo ok lokre , to en achiel , nyoro , tinende , kendo nyaka chieng’ .
Puonj moro mayore kendo magalagala kik golu e yo . En gima ber ka chunywa yudo teko kuom ng’wono mar Nyasaye , to ok kuom rito chike mag chiemo michamo , nikech rito chike ma kamago pok okonyoe ng’at moritogi .
Wan gi kendo-mar-misango ma jodolo matiyo e Hema Maler onge gi ratiro mar chamo misengni motimie .
Jadolo maduong’ tero remb jamni Kama Ler Moloyo mondo ochiw ka misango mar golo richo . Ringregi to iwang’o oko mar kambi .
Mano emomiyo Yesu bende ne onegi oko mar dala Jerusalem mondo opuodh ji gi rembe owuon .
Omiyo koro wawuoguru wadhi ire oko mar kambi , kwating’o achaye mane en bende oting’o ,
nimar e pinyni waonge gi dala mosiko , to wageno yudo dala mapod biro .
Emomiyo , kuom Yesu , pile watimuru ni Nyasaye misango mar pak . Adier , dhowa mohulo nyinge mondo opake pile .
Kik uwe mak utimo timbe ng’wono , kendo poguru giu ni joma chandore , nikech mago e misengni ma Nyasaye morgo .
Winjuru wach jotendu , kendo timuru gik ma giwacho . Giritou odiechieng’ gotieno ma ok giyue , nikech nyaka ginyis Nyasaye wach kaka gisetiyo . Ka uluorogi , to gibiro tiyo gi mor to ka uchayogi to ginyalo tiyo ka gijur , to mano ok nyal konyou .
Lemnwauru alema , nikech wang’eyo ni waonge gi wach ma chunywa ketonwae bura , nimar wadwaro mana timo maber e yore duto .
Akwayou gi chunya duto ni , lemnauru mondo Nyasaye odwoga iru piyo .
Nyasach kue mane ochiero Ruodhwa Yesu oa kuom joma otho gi teko mar remb muma mochwere , mi okete Jakwath Maduong’ mar rombe ,
To akwayou owetena ni yieuru gi wach ma ajiwougoni , nikech asendiko mana weche manok kende .
Adwaro ni mondo ung’e ni owadwa Timotheo osegony , kendo ka ochopo ka piyo , to anabi kode ka abiro nenou .
Mosnauru jotendu duto , kod jo-Nyasaye duto . Owetewa ma jo-Italia bende omosou .
Ng’wono obed kodu un duto . Amin .
An Jakobo , misumba Nyasaye kod Ruoth Yesu Kristo , amoso jo-Nyasaye duto ma oseke e piny ngima .
Owetena , ka uyudo tem mayoreyore , to kwanreuru ka johawi ,
nimar ung’eyo ni tem mitemogo yieu ema miyo ubedo gi kinda .
To nyaka utim kinda nyaka giko mondo ubed joma olony kendo makare chutho , ma ok urem e yo moro amora .
To ka ng’ato kuomu riekone orem , to ber mondo okwa Nyasaye , kendo Nyasaye nomedne rieko , nikech ochiwo gi ng’wono mak ochayo ng’ato .
To ka ukwayo , to nyaka ubed gi yie , ma ok uriwo gi kiawa kata matin , nikech ng’ama riwo gi kiawa chalo gi apaka mar nam ma yamo tugo kendo tagore .
Ng’at ma kamano kik par ni doyud gimoro kuom Ruoth ,
Ka Nyasaye oting’o owadwa moro modhier malo , to mondo obed mamor .
To owadwa ma jamoko bende mondo obed mamor ka Nyasaye odwoke piny , nikech jamoko biro lal nono mana ka maua mae thim .
Ka chieng’ owuok makech to wang’o maua kendo thiepene lwar piny , bang’e kite maber lal nono . Kamano e kaka jamoko bende biro lal nono mana ka tiyo tichne .
Ng’at ma nano ka iteme en jahawi , nikech koseloyo tem to noyud osimbo mar ngima ma Ruoth nosingore ni nomi jogo mohere .
To ng’at ma itemo kik wach ni Nyasaye teme , nikech onge richo manyalo temo Nyasaye , kendo en owuon ok otem ng’ato .
To ng’ato ka ng’ato gombone owuon ema temo kendo yondho .
Eka ka gombo osemako ich , to onywolo richo , to richo kosedongo mogik to kelo tho .
Owetena mahero , ng’ato kik wuondu .
Mich mabeyo duto , kod chiwo malong’o duto , a e polo malo . Gia kuom Nyasaye Wuoro mane ochueyo ler mag polo . En ok olokre , bende ok owichre owewa e mudho .
Kuom dwarone owuon ne ochweyowa manyien kuom wach mar adiera , mondo wabed kaka olemo mokwongo nyak kuom chuechne duto .
Owetena mahero , mago duto ung’eyo . To ng’ato ka ng’ato nyaka bed ng’at mawinjo wach piyo , kendo materore mos kuom wuoyo , kendo ma mirima ok mak piyo .
Nikech mirimb dhano ok kel tim makare ma Nyasaye dwaro .
Emomiyo wituru gik mochido , gi timbe maricho mogundho . Bolreuru e nyim Nyasaye , kendo yieuru wach mane opidhi e chunyu , nikech en gi teko mar warou .
To kik uwuondru , kuwinjo wach awinja , to beduru joma timo gima uwinjo .
Ng’at ma winjo wach awinja to ok tim , chalo gi ng’at mang’iyore e rang’i .
Koseng’iyo kamano , to bang’e odhi , to piyopiyo nono wiye wil gi kite kaka chalo .
To ng’at mang’iyo chik makare mamiyo wabedo thuolo , kendo mosiko ka timo kamano , bende ma ok winj wach mi wiye wilgo to tiyo gi wachno , e ng’at ma oguedhi e gimoro amora motimo .
Ka ng’ato galo ni en jalemo maber to ok orito lewe , to mano owuondore awuonda , kendo lemo mare onge tich .
Lemo mar adier kendo maler e nyim Nyasaye wuoro , en limo nyithi kiye gi mond liete e chandruokgi , kendo bende gi ritruok kuom richo mag piny .
Owetena , kaka un joma oyie kuom Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo ma Ruodh duong’ , omiyo kik uluor wang’ ji .
Kamoro nyalo bet ni jamoko moro man gi tere mang’eny mag dhahabu , kendo morwakore maber , obiro e chokruok maru , to eka jachan moro morwako lewni mokidhore bende obiro e chokruokuno .
To ka unyalo dewo mana wang’ ng’at morwakore maberno , mi uwachne ni , “ In , yie ibed ka , ” to jachan to uwachone ni , “ In to , chung’ kucha , ” kata ni , “ Bed piny e tienda ka , ”
to koro donge upogoru kendu , kendo udoko jong’ad bura ma pachgi richo ?
Owetena mahero , winjuru gima awacho . Donge Nyasaye noyiero joma piny kwano ka jochan mondo obed jomwandu korka yie , kendo obed joma yudo gueth mar Loch Nyasaye , mane osingore ni nomi joma ohero ?
To un usekuodo wi jachan ! To donge jomwandu e joma thagou ? Koso donge gin ema giywayou ka giterou e bura ?
Koso ok gin ema giwuoyo marach kuom nying moluor mochakuno ?
Ka umako chik Ruoth ma ondiki e Muma ni , “ Her wadu kaka iherori iwuon , ” to utimo gima kare .
To ka uluoro wang’ ji , to utimo richo , kendo Chik oloyou gi bura ni un joketho .
Kata ka ng’ato omako Chike duto , to oketho achiel kende , to bura oloye kuom chikego duto ,
nikech Jal mane owacho ni , “ Kik iterri ” , e Jal mane owacho bende ni , “ Kik ineki . ” Kata da bed ni ok iterori , to ineko , to iseketho Chik .
Omiyo , wecheu gi timbeu mondo obed machal gi weche kod timbe mag joma ibiro ng’adonigi bura kaluore gi Chik ma miyo ji bedo thuolo .
Jang’ad bura ok nokech ng’at ma ok kech ji . Ng’at ma kecho ji to onge gima oluoro kuom jang’ad bura .
Owetena , ere ohala ka ng’ato owacho ni , “ An gi yie , ” to ok otim gik manyiso ni en gi yie ? Bende yieneno direse ?
Ka owadwa kata nyaminwa moro onge lewni , kendo onge kata mana chiemb odiechieng’ achiel ,
to eka achiel kuomu wachone ni , “ Dhi gi kue , kendo rwakri gi lewni , bende bed gi chiemo moromi ” , to ok omiye gimoro ma ochando , koro ere ohala ma wachone kamano ?
Yie bende chalo mana kamano . Ka en kende , ma onge tim , to en mana gima otho .
To ng’ato nyalo wacho niya , “ Ng’at moro nigi yie , to ng’ama chielo nigi tim . ” Ng’at ma kamano to adwoko ni , “ Nyisae kaka ng’ato nyalo bedo gi yie , to onge gi tim . An to gik ma atimo ema nyiso ni angi yie . ”
Donge iyie ni Nyasaye en achiel ? Mano ber ! To kata mana jochiende bende nigi yie ma kamano , to yiegino miyo gikirni !
In ng’at mofuwo , idwaro ni mondo onyisi ni yie maonge tim en mana gima nono koso ?
Par ane Ibrahim kwarwa . Ere kaka ne obet e winjruok gi Nyasaye ? Donge timne ema ne omiyo obedo e winjruok kode , kane ochiwo Isaka wuode e kendo-mar-misango ?
Donge inyalo neno ni yie mare gi timne notiyo kaachiel , omiyo yiene nodoko malong’o nikech gima ne otimo ? .
Kamano wach manie Muma nochopo kare , mawacho niya , “ Ibrahim noyie kuom Nyasaye , mi yieneno ema nomiyo Nyasaye okwane ka ng’ama kare . ” Mano nomiyo Nyasaye oluonge ni osiepne .
Kamano uneno ni gik ma ng’ato timo ema miyo obet e winjruok gi Nyasaye , to ok yie kende .
Paruru bende Rahab , dhako ma jachode . Donge Nyasaye nomiyo obet e winjruok kode nikech gik mane otimo kane orwako joote , mi bang’e nomiyo gitony e yo machielo ?
Kaka ringruok maonge muya otho , e kaka yie bende maonge tim otho .
Owetena , kik ji mang’eny kuomu bed jopuonj , nimar nyaka ung’e ni wan jopuonj nong’adnwa bura malit moloyo ji moko .
Waduto wachwanyore pile , to ng’at ma ok chwanyre e gima owacho e ng’at malong’o chutho . Ng’at ma kamano nyalo ritore e yore duto .
Ka waketo chuma matin e dho faras ni mondo owinjwa , to wamiyo odhi kamoro amora mwahero .
Parieuru yiedhi bende . Kata obedo ni gidongo ahinya kamano , kendo kata obedo ni yembe matek ema riembogi , to pod jakwang’ chikogi achika kamoro amora modwaro gi ngai matin nono .
Lep bende chalo kamano . En fuoni matinie moloyo , to onyalo wuorore ngang ! Parieuru bende kaka pilni mach matin nono nyalo moko mach mawang’ bungu maduong’ .
Kamano lep bende en mach . En piny mopong’ gi timbe maricho . Kuom fuondewa , lep ema ketho ringrewa duto , kendo omoko mach e ngima dhano duto . En owuon to imoke e mach mak tho .
Onge le moro amora , kata winyo , kata gik mamol , kata rech , ma dhano ok nyal boyo , kata ma pok oboyo .
To onge ng’at ma nyalo boyo lep . En gima rach ma ok ling , kendo mopong’ gi kwich tho .
En ema wapako kode Nyasaye , ma Ruodhwa kendo Wuonwa , to kendo en ema wayanyo kode ji mochwe e kido machalo gi Nyasaye .
Kamano dhok achielno ema pak kod ayany wuokie . Owetena , mano ok onego obed kamano .
Pi maber gi pi makech ok nyal wuok e soko achiel .
Owetena , ng’owo ok nyal nyago zeituni , kendo mzabibu bende ok nyal nyago ng’owo . Kamano pi makech ok nyal lokore pi maber .
Ka ng’ato kuomu paro ni oriek kata ong’eyo gimoro , to ber mondo timne makare kendo mamuol onyis ni en ng’ama riek adier .
To ka chunyu opong’ gi nyiego marach kod piem to kik upakru , kendo kik uriambi ka uumo adiera .
Rieko ma kamano ok oa e polo malo , to en rieko mar piny gi mar dhano kod mar jochiende ,
nikech kama nyiego gi piem nitie e kama koko gi timbe maricho duto nitie .
To rieko moa e polo malo , opogore gi mano . Mokwongo oler , kendo okelo kue . Omuol , bende oikore winjo wach . Opong’ gi ng’wono , kendo onyago timbe mabeyo . Ok odew wang’ ji to bende ok ogang wach .
Kodhi mopidhi gi kue nyago timbe mabeyo ni joma kelo kue mopidhogi .
Ang’o makelo lweny kod dhaw duto manie kindu ? Donge giwuok kuom gombou makedo e dendu pile mondo utim dwarogi ?
Ugombo , to ok uyudi , omiyo uneko ! Nyiego makou nikech gima ok unyal nwang’o ? Omiyo upiem kendo ukedo . To gimomiyo ok unyal yuda gima udwaro en nikech ok ukwa Nyasaye .
To kata ka ukwayo , to ok dwoku , nikech ukwayo gi paro marach , kudwaro timo mana gima un uwegi ema udwaro .
Un joma ok rit singruok mana ka mon moweyo chwogi ! Donge ung’eyo ni ka uhero piny , to un wasik Nyasaye ?
Koso uparo ni Muma wacho kayiem ni , “ Chuny ma Nyasaye oketo ei dhano en chuny ma janyiego ” ?
To ng’wono ma Nyasaye ochiwo ni dhano duong’ moloyo nyiego . En mana kaka Muma owacho niya , “ Nyasaye miyo joma muol ng’wono , to odagi josunga . ”
Emomiyo , winjuru Nyasaye . Tamuru Satan to noringu .
Nyasaye to kusudo ire to nosud iru . Un joricho , lwokuru luetu , kendo un johubagabaga , puodhuru chunyu .
Koro ma e kinde ma onego ubedie gi kuyo , kuywak kendo ugoyo nduru . Ber mondo nyiero munyierogo olokre ywak , kendo mor ma un-go olokre kuyo .
Bolreuru e nyim Nyasaye , eka enoting’u malo .
Owetena , ng’ato ka ng’ato kik wuo marach kuom wadgi . Ng’at mawuoyo marach kuom wadgi , kata mang’adone bura , to wuoyo marach mana kuom Chik , kendo ng’ado ni Chik bura . Ka ing’ado ni Chik bura , to itimori ng’at ma ng’ado bura , kar bedo ng’at ma rito Chik .
Ng’at achiel kende e wuon Chik , kendo en jang’ad bura . En ema onyalo reso ng’ato , kata onyalo nego . In to in ng’a ma ing’ado ni wadu bura ?
Jomoko kuomu nyalo wacho ni , “ Kawuono kata kiny wabiro dhi dala moro mondo wadag kuno kuom higa achiel , walokie ohala , mi wayud pesa . ” To winjuru !
Ukia gima kiny notimre kiny ! Uparo ni ngimau en ang’o ? Donge un mana ong’ueng’o mineno kuom kinde matin , to bang’e lal nono ?
Kuom mano , gima onego uwachi en ma : “ Ka Ruoth oyie , to wanabed mangima , kendo wanatim gik ma wasechano . ”
To kar timo kamano , to upakoru kusungoru ! Pakruok duto ma kamago gin richo .
Ka ng’ato ong’eyo gima ber monego otim to ok otim , to odoko jaricho .
Koro un jomwandu , winjuru wachna ! Ywaguru kendo gouru nduru nikech masiche mabiro makou .
Mwandu osetop , kendo lepu olwenda ochamo .
Dhahapu gi fethu bende nyal osechamo , kendo nyal nogo nodok ranyisi ni useketho , mi nowang’ ringreu ka mach . Usekano mwandu e ndalo ma piny chiegni rumoeni !
To pok uchulo misach jotich mane okayonu cham . Winjieuru kaka giywak ! Adier , ywak jokeyogo osechopo e it Ruoth Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto .
Usedak e pinyka kudhialoru , kendo kukak . Usebedo jowuoro mudoko machwe ka chiayo , to koro chieng’ yeng’o osechopo !
Useng’ado bura ni joma onge ketho , mi unego , to ok gitamou .
Emomiyo owetewa , horeuru mos nyaka Ruoth bi . Neyeuru kaka japur hore mos ka rito puothe mondo onyagne cham mabeyo . Ohore mos nyaka oyud kodh chuoyo kod koth machiego cham .
Un bende nyaka uhoru mos , kendo uchiw chunyu , nikech biro mar Ruoth chiegni .
Owetena , kik ng’ato ng’ur gi wadgi , mondo chieng’ moro Nyasaye kik ng’adnu bura . Jang’ad bura ni ka kendo ochung’ mana e dhoot .
Owetena , ka udwaro neno kaka onego uhoru mos e sand , to paruru jonabi mane owuoyo e nyim Ruoth ,
nimar wakwano joma ohore mos nyaka giko ni gin johawi . Usewinjo bende kaka ne Ayubu ohore mos , kendo ung’eyo gik mane Ruoth omiye e giko , nimar Ruoth ng’won gi lala , kendo okecho ji .
To owetena , gima duong’ie moloyo gik moko duto en ni , ka usingoru e wach moro , to kik ukuongru , bed ni ukuong’oru gi polo , kata gi piny , kata gi gimoro amora . Kudwaro wacho ni , “ Ee , ” to wachuru mana ni , “ Ee ” kende . Kata kudwaro wacho ni , “ Ooyo , ” to wachuru mana ni , “ Ooyo , ” mondo kik buch Nyasaye lou .
Ka ng’ato kuomu nigi chandruok , to onego olem . To ka ng’ato nigi mor , to onego ower wende pak .
Bende ka nitie ng’ato matuo , to onego oluong jodong kanyakla mar jo-Kristo mondo lemne , kendo owire gi mo e nying Ruoth .
Ka joma lemonego bende nigi yie , to obiro chango , mi Ruoth mi oa malo e kitandane , kendo ka osetimo richo to nowene .
Emomiyo , ng’ato ka ng’ato mondo ohul richone ni wadgi , kendo ng’ato ka ng’ato olem ni wadgi mondo obed mangima . Lemo mar ng’at makare nigi teko kendo timo gik madongo .
Elija ne en mana dhano ka wan . Nolemo matek mondo koth kik chue , mi koth ne ok ochue e piny kuom higni adek gi nus .
Bang’e ne ochako olemo kendo , mi koth ochwe , kendo piny ochiek .
Owetena , ka ng’ato kuomu obayo yo , mi oweyo adiera , to eka ng’at moro odwoke e yo ,
to ng’euru ni ng’ama odwoko jaricho mobayo yono oreso chunye e tho bende omiyo richo mathoth owe .
An Petro , jaote mar Yesu Kristo , andikonu un jo-Nyasaye moke e pinje mag Ponto gi Galatia gi Kapadokia gi Asia kod Bithunia , kuma untie ka jodak .
Nyasaye Wuoro noyierou chon kaka dwarone obet , mondo opwodhu gi Roho , umak chik Yesu Kristo , kendo mondo rembe okir kuomu . Ng’wono gi kue mogundho obed kodu .
Duong’ obed ni Nyasaye Wuon Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo . Kuom ng’wonone maduong’ nonywolowa gi nywol manyien kuom chiero Yesu oa kuom joma otho . Mano miyo wabedo gi geno mangima .
En geno mar yudo mwandu mosiko nyaka chieng’ . Okanonugo e polo , kuma ok onyal kethoree kata towie .
Adier obiro ritou nyaka chop warruok , ma oselosi mondo oel e chieng’ giko , bi .
Beduru mamor kuom wachno , kata obedo ni usebedo kuchandoru kuom tem mopogore opogore kuom kinde matin .
Gik makamago timore mondo otemugo one ane ka un gi yie maradier . Kata mana dhahabu ma nyalo kethore bende itemo gi mach . Omiyo yie maru , ma nengone tek moloyo dhahabu , nyaka tem mondo ong’ego ka en yie maradier . Eka nuyud pak gi duong’ kod luor , chieng’ ma Yesu Kristo ofwenyore .
Kata obedo ni pok uneno Yesu , to pod uhere ahera , bende kata obedo ni ok unene sani , to pod uyie ayiea kuome , kendo upong’ gi mor maduong’ mokadho awacha ,
kuyudo pok mogik ma yieu okelo , tiende ni warruok mar chunyu .
Wach warruokni ema ne jonabi onono kendo omanyo matek , kane gikoro wach gueth mane Nyasaye biro miyou .
Roho mar Kristo mane ni kuomgi nonyisogi chon masiche mane Kristo biro yudo , kod duong’ mane biro luwo masichego , omiyo ne gitemo manyo kinde mane gigo biro timore , kendo kaka gibiro timore .
Ne onyisgi ni tich koro mane gitiyo ne ok giti ni gin giwegi , to ne gitiyo mana ni un , kendo koro joland wach mane okelonu Injili kuom teko mar Roho Maler mane oor koa e polo , osehulonu wechego ratiro . Gin e weche ma kata mana malaika bende gombo ng’eyo ahinya .
Emomiyo beduru motang’ , ka parou bith . Keturu chunyu duto kuom gueth ma Yesu Kristo biro kelonu kuom ng’wonone ka obiro .
Luoruru Nyasaye kubedo ka nyithindo ma winjo wach , kendo kik uyie gombo mane un-go e ndalo moko kane pod ukia Nyasaye chak telnu e ngimau .
Kaka Jal mane oluongou ler , e kaka un bende nyaka ubed maler e timu duto .
Paruru gima Nyasaye wacho e Muma ni , “ Nyaka ubed joma ler , nikech an aler . ”
Ka ulemo , to uluongo Nyasaye ni Wuoro , Jal mang’ado ni ji duto bura , kaka tim ng’ato ka ng’ato obet , ma ok odewo wang’ ng’ato , omiyo nyaka uluore ndalo duto ma udakgo ka welo e pinyka .
Ung’eyo ni kane owaru kuom timbeu manono mane uyudo kuom kwereu , to ne ok owaru gi gik matow kaka fedha kata dhahabu ,
to nowaru gi remo ma nengone tek mar Kristo , mane ochiw ka nyarombo motimgo misango ma onge songa kata mbala .
Nyasaye ne oseyiere chon kane pok ochue piny , to ne ofwenye ni ji e ndalo mogikni nikech un ,
nimar en ema omiyo uyie kuom Nyasaye mane ochiere oa kuom joma otho , kendo omiye duong’ . Adier , en ema omiyo ubedo gi yie kod geno kuom Nyasaye .
Koro kaka usepwodho chunyu kuom winjo wach mar adiera , kendo uheroru maonge miganga kaka owete , omiyo herreuru chuth gi chunyu duto ,
nikech kuom wach mangima kendo mosiko mar Nyasaye , osenyuolu nywol manyien , to ok kaka nyithind joma otho , to kaka nyithind Jal ma ok tho .
En mana kaka Muma wacho ni , “ Dhano duto chalo gi lum , kendo duong’ duto ma en-go chalo gi thiepe lum . Lum ner , kendo thiepe two .
Wach Nyasaye to osiko nyaka chieng’ . ” Wachno e Wach Maber mane olandnu .
Kuom mano , weuru richo duto , kaka ich lit , gi wuond , gi gango wach gi nyiego kod ayany .
Kaka nyithindo mayom gombo cha minegi , e kaka un bende onego ugomb chak maliw mar chuny , mamiyo udongo nyaka chop e warruok ,
nimar kaka Muma wacho , usebilo ng’wono mar Ruoth .
Omiyo biuru ire . En kidi mangima mane ji odagi ni onge tich . Nyasaye to ne oyiere , kendo omiye duong’ .
Biuru ire ka gima un kite mangima , mondo ubed jodolo maler matimo misengni mag chuny ma Nyasaye oyiego kuom Yesu Kristo ,
kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Neuru , aketo kidi moyier e Sayun . En kidi motegno man gi duong’ moriwo kor ot . Ng’at moyie kuome to ok none wichkuot . ”
Un joma uyie ema ung’eyo ni kidino nengone tek , to joma ok oyie to , “ Kidi mane jogedo odagi osedoko kidi motegno moriwo kor ot . ”
Muma kama chielo to wacho ni , “ En e kidi mabiro chwanyo ji ; Lwanda ma nomi gipodhi . ” Gichwanyore nikech gidagi winjo Wach Maber . Mano e gima ne Nyasaye owalonigi .
To un e dhoot moyier , kendo kanyakla mar jodolo mag Ruoth , kod oganda maler ma Nyasaye okawo ka joge , mondo oland timbe madongo mag Jal mane oluongou ua e mudho , mi okelou e lerne miwuoro !
“ Chon ne ok un oganda kata matin , to tinde un oganda Nyasaye . Chon ne un mabor gi ng’wono mar Nyasaye , to koro useyudo ng’wonone . ”
Osiepena , akwayou ni kaka un welo kendo jodak e pinyni , beduru motang’ gi gombo mag ringruok makedo gi chunyu pile .
Timu onego obed maber ahinya e nyim joma ok oyie , mondo kata obedo ni gihangou ni un joma richo , to gine timbeu mabeyo , mi gipak Nyasaye chieng’ ma obiroe ng’ado bura .
Winjuru chike duto ma joloch oketo , nikech uhero Ruoth Yesu . Adier , rituru chike mag ruodh piny , ma en ng’ama duong’ moloyo ,
kendo rituru bende chike mag jotelo ma gin joma en ema oketo mondo okum joma ketho , to opak joma timo maber .
Nyasaye dwaro mondo timbeu mabeyo omak dho joma ofuwo makia .
Beduru joma ni thuolo , to kik ulok thuolo ma un-go bed gima uumogo richou , to beduru wasumb Nyasaye .
Miuru ji duto duong’ , kendo heruru oweteu kuom Ruoth . Luoruru Nyasaye , to ruodh piny bende miuru duong’ .
Un wasumbni , nyaka uwinj ruodhiu kumiyogi luor duto , bed ni gin jomamuol kendo mabeyo , kata gin joma kwiny .
Ka ng’ato ong’eyo ni Nyasaye ni kode , kendo mano omiyo odhil e sandruok moyudo , kata obedo ni onge ketho moro mosetimo , to mano e gima Nyasaye oyiego .
Ere pak ma unyalo yudo ka udhil kichwadou kuom ketho musetimo ? To kudhil kisandou nikech usetimo gima ber , to mano e gima Nyasaye oyiego .
Mano e gima Nyasaye noluongou mondo utim , nimar Kristo owuon bende nosandore nikech un , mi oweyonu ranyisi mondo uluw timne . ,
Muma wacho niya , “ Ne ok otimo richo , bende miriambo ne ok owuok e dhoge . ”
Kane oyanye , to ne ok oyenyo , kendo kane oneno masira , to ne ok osiemo ng’ato , to nochiwore e lwet Jal mang’ado bura kare .
En owuon ne oting’o richowa e ringre e msalaba , mondo watho ni richo , eka wabed mangima ni tim makare , kendo osechangu mana nikech chwat mane ochwadego .
Ne oyudo ulal ka rombe , to koro useduogo ir Jakwadhu , kendo Jarit chunyu .
Un mon bende nyaka uluor chwou , mondo ka nitie chwo moko ma ok oyie , to gilokre ka gineno kaka ngimau chal ,
kendo kaka timu ler , kendo kaka uluoro Nyasaye , kata ka ok uwachonigi gimoro .
Kik ulosru maber mana ni mondo oneu , kukado yie wiu maber , kendo kurwako tigo mag dhahabu kod lewni mabeyo .
To beyou onego obed mana mar chuny . En ber ma ok rum , kendo mamuol , kendo modembore , kendo ma nengone tek e nyim Nyasaye .
Mano e kaka chon mon maler mane oketo genogi kuom Nyasaye , ne obidhore kuom winjo chwogi .
Sara ne achiel kuom mon ma kamago . Ne omiyo Ibrahim luor , kendo ne oluonge ni , “ Ruodha . ” Koro un udoko nyige ka utimo gik mabeyo , kendo ok uwe gimoro bwog chunyu .
Un chwo bende daguru gi mondu ka ung’eyo ni gin chuech mang’aw . Omiyo nyaka umigi luor , nimar gin bende giyudo kodu mich mar ngima ma Nyasaye chiwo kuom ng’wonone . Kutimo kamano , to onge gimoro mabiro monou lemo .
Mogik to uduto nyaka ubed gi chuny achiel , kendo gi paro achiel . Herreuru kaka owete , bende beduru mamuol kendo mang’won .
Kik uchul richo kar richo , kata ayany kar ayany . Kar timo kamano , to guedhuru aguedha , kung’eyo ni kane Nyasaye oluongou , to noluongou ni mondo uyud gueth ,
mana kaka Muma wacho niya , “ Ka ng’ato ohero ngima , kendo dwaro mondo obed mamor , to nyaka ogeng’ lewe kuom weche maricho , kendo dhoge kik wach miganga .
Nyaka olokre owe timo richo , mi otim gik mabeyo , kendo nyaka odwar kue kinde duto , mi oluw ,
nikech Nyasaye rango joma kare gi ng’wono , kendo pile oyie winjo lemogi , to omon gi joma timo richo . ”
Ka uketo chunyu kuom timo gik mabeyo , to ere ng’ama dihimu ?
To bende kata kapo ni uyudo sandruok nikech timbe mabeyo , to mano kaka un johawi ! Kik uluor ji , kendo kik uwe gibwogu .
Miuru Ruoth Kristo duong’ e chunyu , kendo pile beduru kuikoru dwoko ng’ato ang’ata mapenjou tiend geno ma un-go .
To timuru kamano gi muolo kod luor , kendo nyaka ubed gi chuny maler , mondo timu maber kaka jo-Kristo okuod wi jogo mayanyou , kendo hangonu wach .
Ber mondo uyud chandruok nikech tim mabeyo , kapo ni mano e gima Nyasaye dwaro , moloyo yudo chandruok kuom tim maricho ,
nimar Kristo owuon notho dichiel kendo mogik nikech richou . Kata obedo ni en ne en ng’ama kare kamano , to notho ni joma ok kare , mondo oterwa ir Nyasaye . Ne oneg ringre , to Nyasaye nomiyo chunye obedo mangima ,
kendo kuom chuny nodhi molando wach ni chuny mane nie tuech .
Mago e chuny mag joma nodagi winjo wach Nyasaye , kane pod Nyasaye rito mos e kinde mane Nowa hondhoe yie . Yieno noreso ji manok ( ma kwangi oromo aboro ) e pi .
Pigno en ranyisi mar batiso , ma koro resou sani . Batiso ok en golo chilo kuom ringruok , to en singruok motim ni Nyasaye gi chuny maler . Oresou nikech chier mar Yesu Kristo ,
ma osedhi e polo , mi obet e bat korachwich mar Nyasaye , gi ruodhi mag polo duto , kendo kuom teko duto .
Emomiyo , kaka Kristo noneno masira e ringre , un bende ikreuru gi paro achielno , nikech ka ng’ato oneno masira e ringre , to osea e richo .
Ikreuru kamano , mondo kuom ndalo mapod udakgo e piny , kik utim mana gik ma dhano gombo , to timuru mana gik ma Nyasaye dwaro .
E ndalo mosekadho , ne un gi kinde malach moromou timo gik ma joma ok oyie dwaro . Ne utimo timbe maricho , kaka owruok , gi gombo , gi mer , gi dwanyruok , gi metho mag anjawo , kod lamo nyiseche manono , ma en gima Chik okwero .
To tinde ka ok urip gi joma kamago e owruok mar ngima monjawni , to giwuoro , kendo giyanyou !
To chieng’ moro ginidwok wach e nyim Jal moikore ng’ado bura ni joma ngima gi joma otho .
Joma otho nong’adnigi bura kane pod gin e pinyka , mana kaka ing’ado ni jomoko duto . Wach Maber to ne olandnigi bang’ thogi , mondo gibed mangima kuom chuny , kaka Nyasaye bende ngima .
Giko mar gik moko duto chiegni . Emomiyo , beduru mariek , kuritoru mondo uikru ni lemo .
To moloyo nyaka uherru gi chunyu duto , nikech hera miyo iweyo ni ji richo mang’eny .
Rwakuru joweteu ma ok ung’ur .
Nyasaye osemiyou mich mopogore opogore , omiyo ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu nyaka rit michgo maber , mi otigo kokonyogo jomoko .
Ka ng’ato en jaland wach , to wach mowacho nyaka bed mana Wach Nyasaye , kendo ka ng’ato tiyo ni ji , to mondo oti mana gi teko ma Nyasaye chiwo , mondo Nyasaye oyud duong’ kuom gik moko duto mutimo kuom Yesu Kristo . En e wuon duong gi teko nyaka chieng’ . Amin .
Osiepena , ka uyudo tem mager mawang’ou ka mach , to kik ubuogi , ka gima ok ung’eyo ni gik ma kamago nyaka timrenu , nikech mano timore mana ni mondo otemugo .
To beduru mamor , kaka joma oriwore gi Kristo e masichene , mondo ubed gi mor mathoth , chieng , ma duong’ne maler ofwenyore .
Ka iyanyou nikech nying Kristo , to kwanreuru ni un johawi , nikech koro Roho man gi duong’ ma en Roho mar Nyasaye , obedo kuomu .
Ka ng’ato kuomu yudo masira , to kik bed ni oyudo masira nikech oneko , kata nikech okwelo , kata nikech otimo timbe moko maricho , kata nikech ochwogore e weche jomoko .
To ka ng’ato kuomu yudo masira nikech en ja-Kristo , to ok onego one wichkuot , to onego omi Nyasaye duong’ , nikech iluonge gi nying Kristo .
Ndalo mar ng’ado bura osechopo , kendo jo-Nyasaye ema ikwongo ng’ad nigi bura ! To ka wan ema bura ochakore kuomwa kamano , to jogo ma otamore winjo Wach Maber mar Nyasaye to nobed nadi ,
nikech Muma wacho niya , “ Ka en gima tek mondo joma kare oyud warruok , to koro joma ok oluoro Nyasaye kod joricho to nobed nadi ? ”
Emomiyo , ber mondo joma neno masira kaluore gi dwaro mar Nyasaye , osik ka timo timbe mabeyo , kendo ochiwre e lwet Jachwechgi , ma en Jal mogen .
Koro an gi wach moro ma adwaro kwayou , un jodongo . Awuoyo kodu kaka jaduong’ wadu , mane oneno kaka Kristo sandore , kendo mageno yudo pok kuom duong’ mabiro fwenyore .
Beduru jokwadh kueth ma nyasaye osemiyou , kendo ritgiuru gi chuny mamor kaka Nyasaye dwaro , to ok kuom achune . Kik utim kamano mondo uyudie ohala , to timeuru mana nikech uhero .
Kik utimru ruodhi ni jogo moketi e lwetu ka kueth mondo uriti , to nyaka udok nigi ranyisi maber .
Eka ka jakwath maduong’ obiro , to unuyud osimbo mar duong’ ma ok kethre , manyiso ni uselocho .
Kamano bende un joma tindo , nyaka uwinj jodongu , kendo un duto nyaka urwak muolo ka law , kukonyoru e kindu uwegi , nimar Muma wacho niya , “ Nyasaye dagi josunga , to joma muol ema omiyo ng’wono . ”
Omiyo beduru mamuol e bwo bad Nyasaye man gi teko , mondo obi oting’u malo e ndalo mowinjore .
Keturu parruok duto ma un-go kuome , nikech oparou .
Beduru motang’ kurito , nikech jasiku ma Satan bayo kuonde duto ka sibuor magoyo asumbi , ka dwaro ng’ama dongam !
Chung’uru motegno kuom yie ma un-go , mondo utame , ka ung’eyo ni oweteu moyie manie piny duto , bende yudo chandaruok ma kamago .
To ka usenwang’o chandruok kuom kinde matin , to Nyasach ng’wono duto , ma oseluongou kuom Kristo e duong’ne mochwere , noduog chunyu , mi miu teko , kendo omiu chuny motegno , koketou e mise ma ok yiengni .
En e wuon loch nyaka chieng’ . Amin .
Andikonu barua machiekni , ka Silvano , ma ageno kaka owadwa maradier , konya . Adwaro jiwou kendo nyisou ni mano e kaka ng’wonono mar adier mar Nyasaye chalo . Omiyo chung’uru motegno kuom ng’wonono .
Kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Babulon , mane Nyasaye oyiero , omosou . Wuoda Marika bende omosou .
Yogreuru gi mos maler mar hera . Kue obed kodu uduto ma un kuom Kristo .
An Simon Petro , ma misumba Yesu Kristo kendo jaotene , ema andikonu baruani , un joma osenwang’o yie ma nengone tek marom gi yiewa , nimar Nyasachwa kendo Jawarwa Yesu Kristo ema ne omiyowago kuom adierane .
Ng’wono kod yie mogundho miyudo kuom ng’eyo Nyasaye kod Yesu Ruodhwa obed kodu .
Teko mar Nyasaye osemiyowa gik moko duto mamiyo wabedo mangima , kwaluoro Nyasaye . Ngimano wanwang’o kuom ng’eyo Jal mane oluongowa mondo wayud pok kuom duong’ne kod berne .
Kamano osemiyowa singruok madongo kendo ma nengogi tek , mondo kuom singruokgo utony e kethruok ma gombo osekethogo piny , mondo ukaw kit Nyasaye owuon .
Omiyo temuru matek mondo ujiw yieu gi timbe mabeyo , to timbeu mabeyo ujiw gi rieko .
Rieko to jiwuru gi ritruok , to ritruok to ujiw gi kinda , to kinda ujiw gi luoro Nyasaye .
Luoro Nyasaye to jiwuru gi hero owete , hero owete to jiwuru gi hera maradier .
Ka un gi michgo , kendo umedo bedo kodgi mogundho , to gibiro miyou teko , kendo gibiro miyo unyag olemo mabeyo , kumedo ng’eyo Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo .
Ng’ama onge kodgi to en muofu maneno mana matiptip , kendo wiye owil ni richone machon ne osepwodhi .
Emomiyo owetena , temuru matek moloyo mondo unyis ni oseluongu kendo oseyieru adier . Ka utimo kamano , to ok unuchwanyru .
Kamano nomiu thuolo maduong’ mar donjo e piny mochwere mar Ruodhwa kendo Jawarwa Yesu Kristo .
Kuom mano , abiro paronu wechego pile , kata obedo ni useng’eyogi , kendo uguroru motegno kuom adiera ma useyudo .
Aneno ni en kare mondo , kapod anie kiru mar ringruokni , to aparnu wechegi ,
nikech ang’eyo ni achiegni weyo kiru mar ringruokni , kaka Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo osenyisa .
Omiyo abiro temo matek mondo ane ni nitie yo ma unyalo parogo wechegi kinde duto ka asea .
Kane wanyisou kaka Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo biro gi duong’ maler , to ne ok wakonyore gi sigendini ma dhano ochuogo , to wan wawegi ne wanene gi wang’wa , ka en gi duong’ne maler duto .
Nyasaye Wuoro nomiye duong’ gi pak kane dwol obirone moa kuom duong’ mar polo , kawacho niya , “ Ma e Wuoda mahero ! Chunya mor kode ! ”
Wan wawegi ne wawinjo dwolno kaa e polo , nikech ne wan kode kuno e got maler .
Omiyo wamedo yie matek moloyo kuom wach mane jonabi okoro . Ber mondo urt wachno chuth , nikech en kaka taya maliel kama otimo mudho , nyaka piny yawre , mi sulue mar okinyi wuog karieny e chunyu .
To mokwongo nyaka ung’e ni onge ng’ama loko tiend weche manie Muma kende owuon ,
nikech onge wach mane okor mana nikech dwaro mar dhano . To ji ne wacho wach moa kuom Nyasaye , mana kaka Roho Maler ne telonigi .
To jonabi mag miriambo bende nowuok kuom oganda Nyasaye e ndalo mokadho . Kamano bende e kaka jopuonj mag miriambo biro wuok kuomu . Ginikel ling’ling’ puonj mag miriambo maketho ji , kendo ginikwed kata mana Ruoth mane owarogi , mi gimi tiekgi piyopiyo nono .
Kata kamano , ji mang’eny noluw timgi mag anjawo , kendo ji nowuo marach kuom Yor Adiera , nikech timbegigo .
Kuom gombo chamo gik malang’ , jopuonj mag miriambo nokaw giu gi weche mag wuond . To jang’ad bura oseng’ado buchgi chon ! Kum ema oritogi , kendo ng’ama biro tiekogi ok nindi !
Nyasaye ne ok oweyo malaika mane oketho mak okumo , to nowitogi e mach ma ok tho , kuma otuegie e mudho gi nyororo ka girito Chieng’ Bura .
Bende Nyasaye ne ok oweyo piny machon mak otieko , kane okelo ataro e piny joricho , to noreso mana Nowa , mane jaland Wach Makare , kod ji mamoko abiriyo .
Nyasaye nokumo mier mag Sodom gi Gomora , kowang’ogi , mi gilokore buru . Kamano nolokogi ranyisi mar gima biro timore ni joma ok oluoro Nyasaye .
Lut to noreso nimar ne en ng’at maber , kendo chunye ne chandore ahinya nikech tim anjawo mag joma timbegi richo .
Ng’at makareno nodak e kind jogo , kendo pile ka pile nowinjo kendo oneno gik ma gitimo , omiyo chunye nochandore ahinya kuom timbegi mag dwanyruok .
Kamano waneno ni Ruoth ong’eyo reso joma oluore kuom tem mochomogi , kendo ong’eyo keto joricho e kum nyaka chop Chieng’ Bura ,
to moloyo jogo matimo dwaro mag ringruok kuom gombo mochido , kendo chayo teko mar Nyasaye . Jopuonj mag miriambo nigi chir , kendo wang’gi tek , bende ok giluoro yanyo joma nigi duong e polo .
To kata mana malaika man gi teko kod nyalo moloyogi , to ok donjnigi gi weche maricho e nyim Ruoth .
To jogo chalo gi le maonge rieko , mane onywol mana ni mondo omaki kendo onegi . Giwuoyo marach kuom gik ma gikia , omiyo gin bende notiekgi mana ka le maonge rieko .
Giniyud pok mar richo , kar richo ma gisetimo . Timo gik ma gombogi dwaro odiechieng’ alanga ema miyogi mor . Ka gichiemo kodu to gikelonu wichkuot , kendo gimiyo nyingu kethore , ka giowore gi timbegi mag wuond !
Wengegi rango mon mana gi gombo maricho , kendo gombo ma gin-go mar dwaro timo richo ok rum . Giywayo joma yiegi yomyom , gitero e richo , bende chunygi ong’iyo gi gombo gik moko . Gin joma okuong !
Giseweyo yo ma oriere tir , mi gilal , nimar giseluwo mana yor Balaam wuod Boer , mane oketo chunye kuom yudo pok mar tim maricho .
To kanyna mamomo nowuoyo gi dwond dhano , kokwero janabino kuom kethone , mi otieko neko mare .
Jogo chalo gi sokni maonge pi , kendo gichalo gi ong’ueng’o ma yamb koth riembo . Gin , gima okannigi en mana mudho mandiwa .
Giwuorore gi weche manono , kendo kuom gombo mag ringruok gihoyo joma dwaro tony kaa kuom joma timbegi nono .
Gisesingore ni jogo ni gibiro miyogi thuolo , to gin giwegi gin wasumbini mag gik makelo kethruok , nimar ng’ato doko misumba gimoro amora moloyo chunye .
Ka ji osetony e kethruok mar pinyni nikech ging’eyo Ruodhwa kendo Jawarwa Yesu Kristo , to eka gichako giduodore e kethruok , mi kethruok makogi , to ngima ma gibedogo achien doko marach moloyo ngima mane gin-go mokwongo .
Dine obedonigi maber ka dine ok ging’eyo yo makare , moloyo ng’eyogo , to bang’e gidok chien giweyo chik maler mane omigi .
Osetimorenigi mana kaka ngero wacho ni , “ Guok odok nang’o ng’okne , ” kendo ni , “ Ngurue moselwoki odok ng’ielore e chuodho . ”
Osiepena , ma eri barua mar ariyo ma koro asendikonu . E barupenago duto asetemo mondo ami upar maber ,
kaparonu weche mane jonabi maler owacho e ndalo machon , kod chik mar Ruoth kendo Jawar mane jooteu okelonu .
Mokwongo nyaka ung’eni e ndalo giko , jomoko nowuog ma luwo mana gombogi giwegi . Ginicharu ,
ka giwacho niya , “ Donge ne osingore ni oduogo ? To koro erego ? Nyaka ne kwerewa tho , gik moko duto osiko ochwere , mana kaka ne gibet chakre chuech piny ! ”
To gitamore yie mar oyiem ni kata obedo ni polo osebetie nyaka nene , to Nyasaye nowuoyo mi piny obetie koa kuom pi , kendo pi ema ne ocheyego .
To bende pigno ema ne olokore ataro , mi okethogo piny machon .
To Nyasaye osewuoyo bende ni , polo kod piny ma kawuono okan ni Chieng’ Bura , mondo mach obi otieki kaachiel gi ji duto ma ok oluoro Nyasaye .
To osiepena , kik wiu wil gi wach achiel ni , kuom Ruoth , ndalo achiel romre gi higni alufu achiel , bende higni alufu achiel romre gi ndalo achiel .
To kik upar ni Ruoth odeko kuom timo gima osesingore ni obiro timo kaka jomoko paro . Ooyo , ohorenu mos kapod orito , nikech ok odwar ni mondo ng’ato olal , to odwaro ni mondo ji duto olokre owe richogi .
To chieng’ Ruoth nobi mana ka jakuo , kendo chieng’ onogo polo nolal nono ka riadore matek , kendo gik mae kor polo nowang’ mi rum pep . Piny bende nolal kaachiel gi gik manie iye .
Ka gigo duto biro leny nono kamano , koro un uparo ni onego ubed joma chal nadi ? Donge onego ubed joma ler , mochiwore ni Nyasaye ,
ka urito chieng’ Nyasaye , kendo utiyo mondo orure piyo ? En chieng’ ma polo nowang’ie mi rum pep , kendo gik manie kor polo noleny nono e mach .
To wan warito polo manyien kod piny manyien , kuma tim makare nitie , kaka ne Nyasaye osingorenwa .
Emomiyo osiepena , e kinde mapod uritoe gigo mondo otimre , to temuru matek mondo ubed maler kendo maonge ketho e nyim Nyasaye , kendo ubed gi kue kode .
Parieuru kaka Ruodhwa hore mos , komiyou thuolo mondo uyud warruok . Mano e gima owadwa Paulo mwahero nondikonu gi rieko mane Nyasaye omiye .
Adier , kane owuoyo kuom wechego , to mano e gima nowacho e barupene duto . Nitie weche moko matek winjo e barupenego , ma joma kia kendo ma johubagahubaga guenyo mana ni kethruokgi giwegi , mana kaka gitimo weche mamoko mondiki e Muma bende .
To un osiepena , useng’eyo wechegi chon , omiyo beduru motang’ mondo kik joma ok luw chik wuondu , mi ukier uwe kama uchung’ie motegno .
To donguru kuom ng’wono , kumedo ng’eyo Ruodhwa kendo Jawarwa Yesu Kristo . Duong’ obedne kawuono kendo nyaka chieng’ . Amin .
Wandikonu kuom Wach mar ngima , mosebetie a chakruok . Wasewinje kendo wasenene . Adier , wasenene gi wang’wa kendo lweta bende osemule .
Kane ngimano osefwenyore , to ne wanene . Mano emomiyo wawuoyo kuome , kwanyisou wach ngima mochwere nyaka chieng’ mane ni kod Wuoro , kendo mane ofwenyorenwa .
Wanyisou bende gik ma waseneno , kendo ma wasewinjo , mondo ubed e achiel kodwa , kaka wan bende wan e achiel gi Wuoro kod Wuode Yesu Kristo .
Wandikonu gigi mondo morwa orom chuth .
Wach mane wawinjo ka Yesu wacho , kendo ma koro wanyisou e ma : Nyasaye en ler , kendo mudho onge kuome kata matin .
Ka wawacho ni wan e achiel kode , to eka pod wawuotho e mudho , to wariambo , kendo ok wawuoth e adiera .
To ka wawuotho e ler kaka Nyasaye ni e ler , to wan e achiel ng’ato gi ng’ato , kendo remb Yesu Wuode pwodhowa kuom richowa duto .
Ka wawacho ni waonge richo , to wawuondore kendwa , kendo adiera onge e chunywa .
To ka wahulo richowa , to oweyonwagi , kendo opwodhowa kuom tim duto ma ok odhi kare , nikech en jaadiera , kendo otimo mana gima kare .
To ka wawacho ni ok wasetimo richo , to wamiyo odoko jamriambo , kendo wachne onge e chunywa .
Nyithinda , andikonu wechegi mondo kik utim richo , to ka ng’ato otimo richo , to wan gi Jakony masayonwa Wuoro . En Yesu Kristo , Jal makare .
En e misango magolo richowa , to ok richowa kende ema ogolo , to ogolo koda ka richo mar piny duto bende .
Ka warito chik Nyasaye , eka wan gi ratiro ni wang’eye .
To ka ng’ato wacho ni ong’eyo Nyasaye , to ok orito chikene , to en jamriambo , kendo adiera onge e chunye .
To ng’ama orito wach Nyasaye ema hera moherogo Nyasaye oselosi mobedo malong’o chuth . Mano e kaka wanyalo bedo gi ratiro ni wan jo-Nyasaye .
Ka ng’ato wacho ni en ng’at Nyasaye , to nyaka ngimane bed machal gi ngima Yesu .
Osiepena , chik ma andikonuni ok en chik manyien , to en chik machon ma usebedogo nyaka a chakruok .
To kata kamano , chik ma andikonu en chik manyien , kendo adiera mare ineno kuom Kristo , kendo ineno kuomu , nikech mudho rumo , kendo ler maradier koro osechako rieny .
Ng’at mawacho ni nie ler to mon gi wadgi , pod nie mudho .
Ng’at mohero wadgi osiko e ler , kendo onge gimoro kuome madimi ochwanyre .
To ng’at mamon gi wadgi nie mudho , kendo wuotho e mudho . Ok ong’eyo kuma odhiye , nikech mudho oimo wang’e .
Nyithinda , andikonu nimar richou owenu e nying Yesu .
Wuone , andikonu nikech ung’eyo Jal ma osebetie nyaka a chakruok . Yawuowi , andikonu nikech useloyo Ng’ama Rach .
Un nyithinda , asendikonu nikech ung’eyo Wuoro . Un wuone , asendikonu nikech ung’eyo Jal ma osebetie nyaka a chakruok . To un yawuowi asndikonu nikech utegno , kendo Wach Nyasaye odak e iu , kendo useloyo Ng’ama Rach .
Kik uher piny kata gik manie piny , ka ng’ato ohero piny to hera mar Wuoro ok nie iye ,
nikech gik moko duto manie piny , kaka gombo mag ringruok gi gombo mar wang’ , kod sunga ma ji sungorego kuom gik ma gin-go , ok a kuom Wuoro , to gin mana mag pinyni .
Piny kadho kaachiel gi gombone , to ng’ama timo gima Nyasaye dwaro to osiko nyaka chieng’ .
Nyithinda , giko koro chiegni ! Ne onyisu ni Jasik Kristo nobi , to koro wasik Kristo mang’eny osetucho , omiyo wang’eyo ni giko chiegni .
Ne giweyowa nikech ne ok gin jowa , to ka dine gibed jowa , to dine gisiko kodwa . To ne giweyowa mondo ong’ere malong’o ni giduto ok gin jowa .
Un ema Ng’ama Ler osewirou , omiyo un duto ung’eyo adiera .
Andikonu , nikech ung’eye , bende ung’eyo ni onge miriambo mawuok kuom adiera kata matin .
Jamriambo en ng’a ? Donge en mana ng’at makwer ni Yesu ok en Kristo ? En e Jasik Kristo , nikech odagi Wuoro kaachiel gi Wuowi .
Ng’at modagi Wuowi ok nigi Wuoro bende , to ng’at moyie Wuowi ema nigi Wuoro bende .
Un to neuru ni wach musewinjo nyaka a chakruok osiko e chunyu . Ka gima nuwinjo nyaka a chakruokno osiko e chunyu , to pile unusik ka unie achiel gi Wuowi kod Wuoro .
Ma e singruok mar ngima ma nyaka chieng’ mane osingore ni nomiwa .
Asendikonu wechegi kuom jogo madwaro wuondou .
Un to , Roho mane Kristo omiyou osiko kuomu , omiyo ok uchando ng’at mapuonjou gik moko duto , kendo puonj mare en adier , ma ok miriambo . Kuom mano , sikuru kuom Kristo mana kaka Roho osepuonjou .
Adier nyithinda , sikuru kuome mondo ka chieng’ moro ofwenyore , to wabed gi chir , ka waonge gi gima dimi wiwa kuodi e nyime .
Ka ung’eyo ni en ng’at makare , to nyaka ung’e bende ni ng’ato ka ng’ato matimo gik makare en nyathi Nyasaye .
Mano hera maduong’ manadi ma Wuoro osenyisowa kuom luongowa ni nyithind Nyasaye ! Adier , wan nyithinde ! Gimomiyo piny ok ong’eyowa en ni , piny kia Nyasaye .
Osiepna , kata mana sani wan nyithind Nyasaye , to kaka wabiro bet pok ofwenyore , to wang’eyo ni ka Kristo ofwenyore , to wanabed machal kode , nikech wananene kaka ochal .
Ng’ato ka ng’ato man gi genoni kuom Kristo pwodhore owuon mondo obed maler , mana kaka Kristo bende ler .
Ng’at matimo richo ketho chik , nikech richo en ketho chik .
Ung’eyo ni Kristo nofwenyore mondo ogol richowa . En to oonge gi richo .
Kuom mano ng’at mosiko kuome ok tim richo . To ng’at matimo richo pok onene , bende ok ong’eye .
Nyithinda , kik ng’ato wuondu , mi ulal . Ng’at matimo gik makare e ng’ama kare , mana kaka Kristo bende ng’ama kare .
To ng’at matimo richo en ng’at Satan , nikech Satan osiko katimo richo nyaka a chakruok . To Wuod Nyasaye nofwenyore mana ni mondo otiek Satan .
Ng’at ma Nyasaye onywolo ok tim richo , nikech koth Nyasaye nie iye . Ok onyal timo richo nikech en ng’at ma Nyasaye onywolo .
Pogruok manie kind nyithind Nyasaye gi nyithind Satan ong’ere kama : Ng’at ma ok tim gima kare , kata ma ok ohero wadgi , ok en nyathi Nyasaye .
Wach musewinjo nyaka a chakruok en ni ng’ato ka ng’ato nyaka her wadgi .
Kik wachal gi Kain , mane odoko nyathi Ng’ama Rach , mi onego owadgi . To ere gimomiyo Kain nonego owadgi ? Donge nonege nikech timbene ne richo en owuon , to timbe owadgi ne kare ?
Owetena , kik ubwogi ka uneno ka piny mon kodu .
Wang’eyo ni wasea e tho , mi wadonjo e ngima . Wangeyo kamano nikech wahero owete . Ng’at ma ok ohero wadgi to osiko e tho .
Ng’at mamon gi wadgi en janek , to ung’eyo ni janek onge gi ngima ma nyaka chieng’ kuome .
Koro waseng’eyo ni hera en ang’o , nikech Kristo nochiwo ngimane nikech wan . Kuom mano , wan bende onego wachiw ngimawa nikech owetewa .
Ka ng’ato man gi mwandu oneno wadgi moro ka onge gi gima dokonyrego , to otamore konye , koro ere kaka hera mar Nyasaye nyalo siko e chunye ?
Nyithinda , kik waher ji mana gi dhok kende , to nyaka waher ji gi tim , kendo gi adiera .
Mano e kaka wabiro ng’eyo ni wan joma luwo adiera kendo ok wanabed gi luoro e nyim Nyasaye
Osiepena , ka chunywa nyisowa ni bura ok oloyowa , to wanyalo biro e nyim Nyasaye gi chir
mondo wayud gik moko duto ma wakwayo kuome , nikech wamako chikene , kendo watimo gik malong’o e nyim Nyasaye .
To chik ma Nyasaye omiyowa en ni mondo wayie kuom nying Wuode Yesu Kristo , kendo waherre ng’ato gi ng’ato mana kaka nochikowa .
Ng’at momako chik Nyasaye osiko kuom Nyasaye , to Nyasaye bende osiko kuome . Wang’eyo ni Nyasaye osiko kuomwa nikech Roho ma osemiyowa .
Osiepena , kik uyie ni ji duto mawacho ni nigi Roho , nigi Roho adier , to temgiuru mondo une ane ka Roho ma gin-go oa kuom Nyasaye , nikech johul wach mang’eny mag miriambo osebiro e piny
To yo ma unyalo ng’eyogo ni en Roho mar Nyasaye e ma : Ng’ato ka ng’ato ma hulo ni Yesu Kristo osebiro e ringruok nigi Roho mar Nyasaye .
To ng’ato ka ng’ato ma ok hul ni Yesu nobiro e ringruok onge gi Roho mar Nyasaye . Mano e tich ma Jasik Kristo tiyo . Usewinjo ni Jasiguno onego bi , to kata mana koroni enie piny .
Nyithinda , un nyithind Nyasaye , kendo useloyo johul wach mag miriambogo , nikech Jal manie iu duong’ moloyo jal manie piny .
Gin to gin mag piny , omiyo giwuoyo kuom gik mag piny , kendo piny winjogi .
Wan to wan mag Nyasaye , omiyo ng’at mong’eyo Nyasaye ema winjowa , to ng’at ma ok ja-Nyasaye ok winjwa . Mano e yo ma wang’eyogo pogruok manie kind Roho mar adiera , gi roho mar miriambo .
Osiepena , waherreuru , nimar hera en mar Nyasaye , omiyo ka ng’ato nigi hera , to en nyathi Nyasaye .
To ng’at maonge gi hera ok ong’eyo Nyasaye , nikech Nyasaye en hera .
Nyasaye nyisowa hera moherowago kuom oro Wuode ma miderma e piny ni mondo wayud ngima kuome .
To hera maradier ok en hera mane waherogo Nyasaye , to en hera mane Nyasaye oherowago kuom oro Wuode ma miderma mondo odok misango mar golo richowa .
Osiepena , ka kamano e kaka Nyasaye noherowa , to owinjore wan bende waherre .
Kata obedo ni nyaka nene onge ng’at moseneno Nyasaye , to ka waherore waduto , to Nyasaye osiko e iwa , kendo herane chopo tichne kuomwa chuth .
Wang’eyo ni wasiko kuom Nyasaye , kendo ni Nyasaye bende osiko kuomwa , nikech osemiyowa Roho mare .
Waseneno ni Wuoro nooro Wuode mondo obed Jawar mar piny , kendo wanyiso ji wachno .
Ka ng’ato oyie ni Yesu en Wuod Nyasaye , Nyasaye osiko e iye , kendo en bende osiko ei Nyasaye .
Wang’eyo hera ma Nyasaye oherowago , kendo wageno kuom herano . Nyasaye en hera kendo ng’at mosiko ei hera , osiko ei Nyasaye , kendo Nyasaye osiko e iye .
Ka hera malong’o opong’o chunywa , to wanyalo bedo gi chir Chieng’ Bura , nikech ngimawa e pinyni chalo gi mar Kristo .
Luoro onge ei hera , kendo hera maradier riembo luoro . Luoro en kum , omiyo ka ng’ato nigi luoro , to pok ochopo e hera maradier .
Nyasaye ema noherowa mokwongo , mano emomiyo wahere kaachiel gi ji mamoko bende .
Ka ng’ato wacho ni ohero Nyasaye to omon gi owadgi , to ojamriambo , nikech ok nyal bet ni ng’ama ok ohero owadgi ma oneno , nyalo hero Nyasaye mapok oneno .
To chik ma waseyudo kuom Nyasaye e ma : Ng’ama ohero Nyasaye nyaka her owadgi bende .
Ng’ato ka ng’ato moyie ni Yesu e Mesia , en nyathi Nyasaye , kendo ng’at mohero wuon nyathi , to ohero nyathi bende .
Kuom mano , ka wahero Nyasaye , kendo wamako chikene , to eka wang’eyo ni wahero nyithind Nyasaye ,
nikech hero Nyasaye en mako chikene . Chike Nyasaye ok tek rito ,
nikech nyithind Nyasaye duto loyo piny . Yie ma wan-go kuom Nyasaye ema oseloyo piny .
Ere ng’ama oloyo piny ? Ng’ama oloyo piny en mana ng’ama oyie ni Yesu Kristo en Wuod Nyasaye .
Yesu Kristo e jal mane obiro gi pi mar batisone , kod remo mar thone . To winjuru ni ne ok obiro gi pi kende , to nobiro gi pi kod remo . Roho owuon nyiso ni mano en adier , nikech Roho e adiera .
Nitie gik moko adek manyiso ni mano en adier :
gin Roho gi pi kod remo , kendo gik moko adekgo nyiso mana gimoro achiel .
Ka wanyalo yie ni weche ma dhano wacho gin adier , to nyaka wayie gima Nyasaye wacho moloyo , kendo Nyasaye owuon osenyisowa ni gima owacho kuom Wuode en adier .
Ng’at moyie kuom Wuod Nyasaye to ong’eyo e chunye ni gima Nyasaye wacho en adier . To ng’at ma ok oyie Nyasaye miyo Nyasaye doko jamriambo , nikech ok oseyie gi gima Nyasaye osewacho kuom Wuode .
To gima Nyasaye osewacho e ma : Osemiyowa ngima ma nyaka chieng’ , kendo ngimano ni kuom Wuode .
Ng’at man gi Wuowi to nigi ngimano , to ng’at maonge gi Wuod Nyasaye to onge gi ngimano .
Andikonu wechegi , un joma oyie kuom nying Wuod Nyasaye , mondo ung’e ni un gi ngima ma nyaka chieng’ .
Wageno kuome chuth nikech wang’eyo ni ka wakwaye gimoro mowinjore gi dwarone , to owinjowa .
To ka wang’eyo ni pile owinjo kwayowa kamano , to wang’eyo bende ni ose mana miyowa gik ma wakwayo .
Ka ng’ato oneno wadgi katimo richo ma ok kel tho , to mondo olamne Nyasaye , to Nyasaye biro miyo owadgino ngima . Mano timore mana ni joma osetimo richo ma ok kel tho . To nitie richo makelo tho . Ok awachi ni mondo olem ni ng’at mosetimo richo ma kamano .
Gik moko duto ma ok kare gin richo , to nitie richo ma ok kel tho .
Wang’eyo ni onge nyathi Nyasaye mosiko katimo atima richo , nikech Wuod Nyasaye orite , omiyo Ng’ama Rach ok nyal mule .
Wang’eyo ni wan mag Nyasaye , to piny duto bende nie lwet Ng’ama Rach .
Wang’eyo bende ni Wuod Nyasaye osebiro , mi omiyowa rieko mondo wang’ego Nyasaye maradier . Wan kuom Jal maradier , ma en Yesu Kristo Wuod Nyasaye . En e Nyasaye maradier , kendo en e ngima ma nyaka chieng’ .
Nyithinda , tang’uru ni nyiseche manono .
An jaduong’ , andikoni in Minwa ma Nyasaye oyiero , kendo andiko ni nyithindi ma ahero adier . Ok an kenda ema aheri to ji duto moseng’eyo adiera bende oheri ,
nikech adiera manie iwa , kendo ma osiko kodwa nyaka chieng’ .
Ng’wono gi miwafu kod kue moa kuom Nyasaye Wuoro gi Yesu Kristo Wuod Wuoro nobed kodwa e adiera .
Ne amor ahinya kane ayudo ni nyithindo moko wuotho e adiera , ka giluwo chik mane wayudo kuom Wuoro ,
omiyo koro Minwa , akwayi ni mondo ng’ato ka ng’ato kwomwa oher wadgi . Gima andikoni ok en chik manyien , to en chik ma wasebedogo nyaka a chakruok .
To hera ma awuoyo kuomeni dwaro ni mondo wawuothi kaka chik Nyasaye dwaro . En e chik achiel ma usewinjo a chakruok , ni , “ Daguru e hera . ”
Jowuond mathoth osewuok e piny . Gin e jogo ma ok oyie ni Yesu Kristo nobiro kaka dhano . Ng’at ma kamano en jawuond , kendo en Jasik Kristo .
Ritreuru mondo kik gima usetiyone lalnu , to uyud poku duto .
Ng’at makalo tong’ , kendo ok sik e puonj Kristo ok nigi Nyasaye . To ng’at mosiko e puonj Kristo nigi Wuoro , kaachiel gi Wuowi .
Ka ng’ato obiro iru ma ok okelo puonj Kristo , to kik urwake e uteu , kata mana mos kik umose ,
nimar ng’at momose , bende oriwore kode e timbene maricho .
Kata obedo ni an gi weche mathoth ma adwaro nyisou , to ok abi ndikogi e barua , to ageno ni abiro biro iru mondo alos kodu wang’ gi wang’ , mondo waduto wabed mamor kaachiel .
Nyithind Nyameru , ma bende Nyasaye oyiero , omosi .
An jaduong’ , andikoni in Gayo , osiepna ma ahero gi hera maradier .
Osiepna , akwayo Nyasaye ni mondo idhi maber e yore duto , kendo ibed mangima e ringri mana kaka ang’eyo ni ingima e chunyi bende .
Ne abedo mamor ahinya kane owete moko obiro , mowacho kaka isiko kuom adiera , kendo kaka iwuotho e ngima mar adiera .
Onge gima miya mor moloyo ka awinjo ni nyithinda wuotho e adiera .
Osiepna , in jaadiera kuom gimoro amora mitimo ni owete , kata ka gin joma welo .
Gisewuoyo kuom heranino e nyim kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man ka . Yie ikonygi e wuodhgi , kikowogi e yo malong’o ni Nyasaye mwatiyone ,
nimar ne giwuok gidhi e tich Kristo , ma ok giyie kawo kony moro amora kuom joma ok oyie .
Omiyo wan jo-Kristo onego wakony joma kamago mondo wanywak kodgi tich mar lando adiera .
Ne andiko ni jo-Kristo muchokorugo , to Diotrefe , madwaro bet jatendgi , notamore winjo gima wawacho .
Omiyo ka abiro to anael gik ma otimo e lela , kaka ohangowa gi weche mamono maricho . To ewi mago duto , otamore rwako owete bende , to ok mano kende , to bende otamo joma dwaro timo kamano e kanyakla mar jo-Kristo .
Osiepna , kik iluw tim marach , to luw tim maber . Ng’at matimo maber en ng’at Nyasaye , to ng’at matimo marach , to pok oneno Nyasaye .
Ji duto wuoyo maber kuom Demetrio . Adiera lilo ema wachore kuome . Wan bende wayie ni timbene beyo kendo ing’eyo ni gima wawacho en adier .
An gi weche mathoth ma adwaro nyisi , to kata kamano ok adwar ndikogi e barua .
To ageno ni abiro neni machiegni mondo walos wang’ gi wang’ .
Kue obed kodi . Osiepewa duto omosi . In bende mosnwa osiepewa achiel achiel .
