An Juda , ma misumba Yesu Kristo , kendo ma owadgi Jakobo , ema andikonu baruani un joma Nyasaye ohero kendo ma oseluongo , kendo ma Yesu Kristo rito gi tekone .
Ng’wono gi kue kod hera mogundho obed kodu .
Osiepena , ne agombo ahinya mondo andiknu kuom warruok ma waduto wan-go , to koro aneno ni nyaka andiknu , kajiwou mondo umed kedo matek ni wach yie ma Nyasaye osemiyo joge dichiel kendo mogik .
Nyaka andik kamano nimar jomoko ma ok oluoro Nyasaye , ma gin joma oseketi ni bura oloyo chon nikech wachni , osedonjo kuomu ling’ling’ , ka gitemo mondo gilok ng’wono mar Nyasachwa obed anjawo , kendo gidagi Ruodhwa achiel kende , ma en Ruoth Yesu Kristo .
Adwaro mondo aparnu weche moko , kata obedo ni useng’eyogi duto kamano . Ruoth noreso jo-Israel , mi ogolo e piny Misri . To achien notieko jogo mane odagi yie .
Malaika mane okalo tong’ mar teko momigi , mi oweyo kuma onego gibedie , bende Ruoth oseketo e mudho , kotue mochwere gi nyororo , nyaka chop ng’ad buchgi , Chieng’ Maduong’ .
Bende paruru Sodom gi Gomora kod mier mokiewo kodgi . Gin bende ne gidonjo e tim terruok kod dwanyruok madhoch , mi giyudo kum mar mach mak tho , mondo obed ranyisi ni ji duto .
Mano e kaka jogi bende chalo . Lek ma gileko miyo gidwanyo ringregi , kendo gidagi teko ma Ruoth nigo , kendo giyanyo joma nigi duong e polo .
To eka kata mana Mikael , malaika maduong’ , kane laro gi Satan ringre Musa , to ne ok ohedhore yanye gi weche maricho , to nowachone mana niya , “ Ruoth mondo okweri . ”
Jogi to yanyo gimoro amora ma ok ging’eyo to gik ma ging’eyo mana kuom gombo mag ringregi ka le ma onge rieko e gik matiekogi .
Mano kaka ginine malit ! Gise mana luwo yo mane Kain oluwo , kendo gisemwomore e ketho mar Baalam nikech gihero pesa , bende giseng’anyo kaka Korah nong’anyo , mi girumo mana kaka en bende norumo .
Jogi gin mbelni e sewni mutimo mag hera , ka gichiemo kodu maonge wichkuot . Gin jokwath maparo mana gin giwegi kende ! Gichalo rumbi ma yamo riembo to ok kel koth , kendo gichalo yiend olemo ma ok nyagi e ndalo oro , kendo mopudh gi tiendgi , mi otho chuth .
Bende ka gitimo timbegi mag wichkuot , to gichalo apaka mager mag nam mathuogo buoyo , kendo gichalo sulue moweyo yorgi , ma mudho mandiwa ema okannigi nyaka chieng’ .
Enoka , nyakwar Adam kuom tieng’ mar abiriyo , nokoro wach jogo , kane owacho niya , “ Neuru ! Ruoth osebiro gi oganda mang’ongo mar joge maler ,
mondo okum piny duto , kendo omi jogo ma ok oluoro Nyasaye yie timbegi maricho , kod weche malit duto , ma gin joricho ma ok oluoro Nyasaye , gisewacho kuome . ”
Jogi gin joma keko akeka , kendo ng’ur ang’ura . Giluwo mana gombo mag ringregi giwegi , bende gisungore marach , kendo giwuondo ji gi weche mamit mondo giyud gik ma gidwaro .
To osiepna , nyaka upar gima ne joote mag Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo okoro .
Ne giwachonu niya , “ E ndalo giko ji moko nobi ma nochau . Gin ji ma ok oluoro Nyasaye , kendo maluwo mana gombogi giwegi . ”
Mago e joma kelo pogruok . Gin joma gombo mag ringruok ema chiko , kendo gionge gi Roho .
To un osiepena , meduru mana geroru kuom teko mar Roho Maler .
Nyaka ubed e hera mar Nyasaye , mondo urit ngima ma nyaka chieng’ ma Ruoth Yesu Kristo biro miyou kuom ng’wonone .
Kechuru joma riwo gi kiawa .
Resgiuru , kugologi e mach . Ji moko nitie ma bende nyaka ukechi , to mana ka uluor , kendo kubedo mosin kata mana gi lepgi ma gombogi mag richo osechido .
Wapakuru Jal manyalo ritou mondo kik upodhi , kendo manyalo miyo uchung’ e nyim duong’ne maler kumor kendo kuonge ketho .
En e Nyasaye ma Jawarwa kuom Yesu Kristo Ruodhwa , man gi duong’ gi teko kod loch , nyaka nene , kendo kawuono , kendo nyaka chieng’ . Amin .
Ma e fweny mane Nyasaye omiyo Yesu Kristo mondo onyisgo jotichne gik ma nyaka timre piyo . To Kristo nooro malaikane ir Johana jatichne mondo odhi onyise wach fwenyno ,
mi Johana nonyiso ji gik moko duto mane oneno . Adier , noneno gik mane Nyasaye dwaro timo , kendo mane Yesu Kristo bende osewacho ni adier .
Ng’at masomo kitabuni kod joma winjo weche mokorgi , kendo momako gik mondikie , gin johawi , nikech ndalo ma gigi biro timoree chiegni .
An Johana andiko ni kanyakla abiriyo mag jo-Kristo man e piny Asia , kawacho kama : Beduru gi ng’wono kod kue moa kuom Nyasaye mantie , kendo mane nitie , bende mapod biro biro , kendo moa kuom Roho abiriyo manie nyim kom duong’ne ,
kendo moa kuom Yesu Kristo ma janeno maradier , mane okwongo chier oa kuom joma otho , kendo ma jatend ruodhi mag piny . Oherowa kendo osegonyowa kuom richowa gi rembe ,
mi omiyo wadoko oganda ruodhi matiyone kaka jodolo mag Nyasache kendo Wuon mare . Duong’ kod teko obedne nyaka chieng’ ! Amin .
Neuru , obiro gi boche polo , kendo ng’ato ka ng’ato nonene . Jogo mane ochwowe nonene , kendo ogendini duto mag piny nobed gi kuyo nikech en . Ber mondo obed kamano ! Amin .
Ruoth Nyasaye wacho niya , “ An e Chakruok kendo e Giko . An e Ruoth Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto , Jal mantie , kendo mane nitie , kendo mapod biro betie . ”
An owadu Johana , an e achiel kodu e sand gi loch kod kinda ma wan-go kuom Kristo Yesu . Ne oketa e chula miluongo ni Patmo nikech nalando wach Nyasaye , kendo awuoyo kuom Yesu e lela .
To chieng’ Ruoth , Roho ne omaka , mi awinjo dwol maduong’ maywak ka tung’ ka wuoyo gi yoka ng’eya .
Nowacho niya , “ Gik moko duto mineno , ndiki e kitabu . Bang’e ior kitabuno ni kanyakla abiriyo mag jo-Kristo man : Efeso , Smurna , Pergamo , Thuatiro , Sarde , Filadelfia , kod Laodikia . ”
Eka nalokora mondo ane ni ng’ano maloso koda , mi aneno teyni abiriyo mag dhahabu ,
to e dier teynigo ne nitie gimoro machalo dhano , morwakore gi kandhu mochopo nyaka e tiende piny , kendo otweyo kore gi okanda mar dhahabu .
Yie wiye ne rachar ka yie rombo kendo tar ka pe . Wengene ne liel ka ligek mach ,
kendo tiendene ne pakni ka mula mosepwodhi gi mach . Dwonde to ne mor ka pi mawuo .
Ne en gi sulue abiriyo e lwete ma korachwich , kendo ligangla mabith ma dhoge abiriyo ne wuok e dhoge . Pat wang’e ne nenore ka wang’chieng’ mang’angni gi tekone duto .
Kane anene to ne apodho e tiende ka ng’at mosetho . To noyieyo lwete ma korachwich kuoma , kowacho niya , “ Kik iluor , an e Jal Mokwongo kendo Mogik ,
kendo an e Jal Mangima . Ne atho , to koro angima nyaka Piny Joma Otho .
Omiyo koro ndik gik miseneno duto , ok mana gik mantie kende , to gik mabiro timore achien bende .
To koro adwaro nyisi tiend wach mopandi mar sulue abiriyo mineno e lweta ma korachwichgi , kod teyni abiriyo mag dhahabu : Sulue abiriyo gin e malaika mag kanyakla abiriyo mag jo-Kristo , kendo teyni abiriyo gin e kanyakla abiriyogo .
“ Ndik ni malaika mar kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Efeso kama : “ ‘ Weche mag Jal man gi sulue abiriyo e lwete ma korachwich , kendo ma wuotho e kind teyni abiriyo mag dhahabu e magi :
Ang’eye timbeni gi tichni matek kod kinda misetimo , kendo ang’eyo bende ni in ok inyal yie gi joma richo , bende isetemo joma luongore ni joote , to ok gin joote , mi inwang’o ni gin jomriambo .
In jakinda , kendo isechandori malit nikech an , to ok iseol .
To kata kamano pod an gi wach kodi ni , koro ok ihera kaka ne ihera mokwongo .
Parie kama iseaye ka ipodho ! Lok chunyi mondo itim gik mane itimo mokwongo . To ka ok iloko chunyi , to anabi mi agol tachi kare .
To kata kamano nitie gimoro maber ma itimo , en ni imon gi timbe mag jo-Nikolao , mana kaka an bende amon-go .
“ ‘ Ng’at man gi it mondo owinj gima Roho wacho ni kanyakla mag jo-Kristo . Ng’at molocho to anami ratiro mar chamo olemb yadh ngima manie puoth Nyasaye . ’ .
“ Ndik ni malaika mar kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Smurna kama : ‘ Weche mag Jal Mokwongo kendo Mogik e magi . En e Jal mane otho , kendo ochako obedo mangima .
“ ‘ Ang’eyo chandruok ma ineno , kod chan mari , to chutho in jamoko ! Bende ing’eyo ayany ma joma wacho ni gin jo-Yahudi , to ok gin jo-Yahudi , yanyigo . Chutho , gin mana oganda jolemo mar Satan .
Kik iluor sand ma ibiro yudo , nikech jachien biro bolo jomoko kuomu e jela mondo otemu , kendo ubiro yudo sandruok kuom ndalo apar . To bed jaadiera nyaka kar tho , mi anamiyi osimbo mar ngima , kaka ranyisi ni iselocho .
“ ‘ Ng’at man gi it to mondo owinj gima Roho wacho ni kanyakla mag jo-Kristo . Ng’at molocho to tho mar ariyo ok nomul ngang’ . ’ .
“ Ndik ni malaika mar kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Pergamo kama : ‘ Jal man gi ligangla mabith ma dhoge ariyo wacho niya ,
“ ‘ Ang’eyo kama idake . En kama kom mar duong’ mar Satan nitie . To irito nyinga ahinya , kendo ne ok ikwedo yie ma iyiego kuoma , kata mana e ndalo mane Antipa , janeno mara mar adier , onegi e dalau , kama Satan odakie .
To kata kamano , an kodi gi weche moko , nikech in gi ji moko kanyo maluwo puonj mar Baalam , mane opuonjo Balak kaka onyalo miyo jo-Israel tim richo kuom chamo chiemo mosetimgo ni nyiseche manono misango , kendo kuom terruok .
Kamano bende in gi jomoko maluwo puonj jo-Nikolao , machalo gi puonj Balaamno .
Emomiyo lok chunyi ! To ka ok ilokori , to abiro biro iri piyo , mi aked kodgi gi ligangla mawuok e dhoga !
“ ‘ Ng’at man gi it to mondo owinj gima Roho wacho ni kanyakla mag jo-Kristo . Ng’at molocho to anami chiemo moko mopandi miluongo ni Manna , kendo anamiye kidi marachar mondikie nying manyien , maonge ng’at mong’eyo , mak mana jal monwang’e .
“ ‘ Ndik ni malaika mar kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Thuatira kama : ‘ Wuod Nyasaye , ma en Jal ma wengene rieny ka ligek mach , kendo ma tiendene pakni ka mula , wacho niya ,
“ ‘ Ang’eyo timbeni duto , gi herani , gi tichni mar konyo ji , kod kindani , kendo kaka isebedo jaadiera . Bende ang’eyo ni tijeni machien beyo moloyo mokwongo .
To kata kamano an kodi gi wach moro nikech iyie gi dhako ma Jezebel maluongore ni janabi . En ema omiyo jotichna lal kuom puonjogi mondo giterre , kendo mondo gicham chiemo motimgo misango ni nyiseche manono .
Ne amiye kinde mondo olok chunye , to otamore weyo terruokne .
Omiyo anabole e kitanda mar rem , kendo anami joma terore kode yud chandruok malit , ka ok giloko chunygi , mi giweyo gik ma opuonjogi mondo gitim .
Nyithinde bende abiro nego , eka kanyakla duto mag jo-Kristo nong’e ni an ema ang’eyo chuny ji gi parogi , kendo ni amiyo ng’ato ka ng’ato kuomu pok mowinjore gi timne .
“ ‘ To un ji mamoko duto man Thuatira , ma ok oseluwo puonjno , bende mapok ong’eyo gima jomoko luongo ni , ‘ Weche matut mag Satan’ , ok amiu ting’ moro mapek .
To awachonu mana ni mondo umak gima un go matek nyaka abi .
To ng’at molocho , kendo motiyo tichna nyaka giko , anami teko mar bedo gi loch kuom ogendini , mana kaka an bende Wuora ne omiya teko .
Ng’at molochono norit ogendini gi ludh nyinyo ,
kendo notogi matindotindo ka mbalatago . To bende anamiye sulue mar okinyi .
Ng’at man gi it to mondo owinj gima Roho wacho ni kanyakla mag jo-Kristo . ’ .
“ Ndik ni malaika mar kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Sarde niya , ‘ Weche mag Jal man gi Roho abiriyo mag Nyasaye , kod sulue abiriyo e magi : “ ‘ Ang’eyo timbeni duto , bende ang’eyo ni in gi nying’ ni ingima , to kata kamano isetho .
Kuom mano , chiew mondo ijiw gima pod in-go , kapok otho chuth , nimar ayudo ni timbeni pod ok beyo ruok e nyim Nyasacha .
Omiyo par ane gima ne opuonji , kendo mane iwinjo . Make , kendo ilok chunyi iwe richoni . To ka ok ichiew , to abiro poyi ka jakuo , ka ok ing’eyo sa ma abiroe .
Kata kamano , pod in gi ji manok e dala mar Sarde ma ok osechido lepgi . Gin giniwuoth koda gi lewni marachere , nikech mano ema owinjore kodgi .
Ng’at molocho bende norwakne lewni marachere , mana kaka girwako , kendo ok naruch nyinge oko ngang’ e kitap ngima , to anahul nyinge e nyim Wuora , kendo e nyim malaika mage .
Ng’at man gi it to mondo owinj gima Roho wacho ni kanyalka mag jo-Kristo . ’ .
“ Ndik ni malaika mar kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Filadelfia niya , ‘ Magi e weche Jal maler kendo maradier , man gi rayaw mar Daudi . Ka oyawo gimoro , to onge ng’ama nyalo loro , kendo ka oloro gimoro , to onge ng’ama nyalo yawo . Owacho niya ,
“ ‘ Ang’eyo timbeni duto . Winji ! Aseketo dhoot moyaw e nyimi , maonge ng’ama nyalo loro . Ang’eyo ni kata in gi teko matin kamano , to iserito wachna , kendo pok ikwedo nyinga .
To winji , nitie jomoko mag oganda jolemo mar Satan , maluongore ni jo-Yahudi , to ok gin jo-Yahudi , to giriambo ariamba . Abiro miyo gibiro , mi gipodhi e tiendi , kendo ging’e ni aheri .
Ne amiyi chik ni mondo itim kinda , kendo iserito chiknano , omiyo an bende abiro riti e ndalo mar masira mabiro kwako piny ngima , mondo otemgo ji duto modak e piny .
Abiro biro piyo , omiyo mak gima in-go matek , mondo kik ng’ato mayi osimboni .
To ng’at molocho anami bed siro e Hekalu mar Nyasacha , mi ok nochak owuog kanyo kendo nyaka chieng’ . Anandik nying Nyasacha kuome , kod nying dala mar Nyasacha , ma en Jerusalem manyien , mabiro lor kaa e polo kuom Nyasacha . Nyinga maler bende nandik kuome .
Ng’at man gi it to mondo owinj gima Roho wacho ni kanyakla mag jo-Kristo ! ’
“ Ndik ni malaika mar kanyakla mar jo-Kristo man Laodikia niya , ‘ Jal miluongo ni Amin , ma en janeno migeno kendo maradier , kendo chuech duto mag Nyasaye noa kuome wacho kama :
“ ‘ Ang’eyo timbeni duto . Ang’eyo ni ok ing’ich , bende ok iliet . To daber kibedo maliet kata mang’ich .
To kaka koro indhemndhem , to ok iliet kata ok ing’ich , abiro ng’ogi oko !
Iwacho ni in jamoko man gi mwandu mathoth , kendo onge gima ichando , to ikia ni in ng’at machandore moloyo . In ng’at modhier chuth ma jachan , Kendo in muofu bende in duk .
To ang’adoni rieko ni mondo ing’iew kuoma dhahabu mopwodhi gi mach mondo inwang’ mwandu . Lewni marachere bende ing’iew kuoma irwakrigo mondo igeng’go dugi makeloni wichkuot . Yath bende ng’iew , iwirgo wang’i mondo inen .
Joma ahero ema akwero kendo akumo . Emomiyo ket chunyi mondo ilokri iwe richoni .
Winji ! Achung’ e dhoot kendo adwong’o . Ka ng’ato owinjo dwonda , mi oyawo dhoot , to anadonj ire , kendo anachiem kode , to en bende nochiem koda .
To ng’at molocho anami bed koda e kom duong’na , mana kaka an bende ne alocho , mi abet kod Wuora e kom duong’ne .
Ng’at man gi it to mondo owinj gima Roho wacho ni kanyakla mag jo-Kristo ! ’ ”
Bang’ mano , ne arango polo , mi aneno dhoot moro moyawore e polo , kendo dwol machalo gi dwond tung’ mane akwongo winjo kawuoyo koda cha , nowachona niya , “ Bi malo ku , mondo anyisi gik mabiro timore bang’ magi . ”
Gikanyono , Roho nomaka , mi aneno kom duong’ moket e polo , ma ng’ato obetie .
To ng’at mane obetno ne nigi kido machal gi kite ma nengogi tek miluongo ni jasper gi sardius , kendo lihudu man gi kido machalo zumaridi nolworo komno koni gi koni .
To e alwora mar komno ne nitie kombe mamoko piero ariyo gang’wen , ma jodongo piero ariyo gang’wen obetie . Ne girwako lewni marachere , kendo ne gisidho osimbe mag dhahabu e wigi .
Mil polo makakni ne wuok e kom duong’no , kendo dwol moko bende ne winjore , kaachiel gi mor polo . To e nyim komno ne nitie teyni abiriyo maliel . Gin e Roho abiriyo mag Nyasaye .
E nyim komno bende ne nitiere gimoro machalo gi nam mar rang’i , marieny ka pi . To e dier komno tir , kendo e alwora mare , ne nitie gik mangima ang’wen man gi wenge mogundho yoka nyimgi kendo yoka ng’egi .
Gima ngima mokwongo ne chalo gi sibuor , to mar ariyo ne chalo gi nyaroya . Mar adek to ne nigi lela wang’ machalo gi lela wang’ dhano , to mar ang’wen ne chalo gi ongo mahuyo .
Gik mangima ang’wen-go ne nigi bwombe auchiel moro ka moro , kendo ne gin gi wenge mang’eny e dendgi duto kendo e igi . Ne giwer odiechieng’ gotieno mak giling’ niya , “ Mano kaka Ruoth Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto ler ! Oler adier ! Yaye ! Mano kaka oler ! En e Jal mane nitie , kendo mantie , kendo mapod biro betie ! ”
To e kinde ka kinde ma gik mangimago goyoe erokamano ni Jal mantie nyaka chieng’ mobet e kom duong’ , kendo miye duong’ gi pak ,
to jodongo piero ariyo gang’wen-go podho e nyim Jal mobet e kom duong’no , kendo gilamo Jal mantie nyaka chieng’ . Gibolo osimbegi e nyim komno , ka giwacho niya ,
“ A Ruodhwa kendo Nyasachwa ! Owinjore miyi duong’ gi pak kod teko , nikech in ema nichueyo gik moko duto . Adier , in ema ne imiyo ochuegi , kendo gisiko gintie . ”
Bang’ mano , ne aneno kitabu ma Jal mane obet e kom duong’no oting’o e lwete ma kor achwich . Ne ondik iye gi toke bende , kendo ne odine gi kido abiriyo .
Eka ne aneno malaika maratego kalando wach gi dwol maduong’ niya , “ Ere ng’ama owinjore ketho kidogi , mi el kitabuni ? ”
To onge ng’ato e polo , kata e piny , kata e bwo piny , mane nyalo elo kitabuno , kata ng’iyo iye .
Ne aywak malit kane aneno ni onge ng’ama ne nyalo elo kitabuno kata ng’iyo iye !
To ng’at achiel kuom jodongogo nokona niya , “ We ywak , nikech Sibuor moa e dhood Juda , ma nyakwar Daudi , ema oselocho ! Emomiyo en gi ratiro mar ketho kido abiriyogo , mi oel kitabuno . ”
Eka naneno Nyarombo kochung’ e dier kom maduong’ , kama ne gik mangima ang’wen kod jodongo olworo . Nyarombo ne nenore ka gima osenegi , to ne en gi tunge abiriyo , ma gin Roho abiriyo mag Nyasaye , ma oseor e piny ngima .
Ne odhi mokawo kitabu ma Jal mane obet e kom duong’no oting’o e lwete ma korachwich .
Kane Nyarombo okawo kitabuno kamano , gik moko ang’wen mangima kod jodongo piero ariyo gang’wen-go , nopodho piny e nyime . Moro ka moro kuomgi ne nigi thum kod tewni mag dhahabu ma ubani opong’o . Tep ubanigo ochung’ kar lemo mag jo-Nyasaye .
Ne giwero wer manyien niya “ In ema iwinjori kawo kitabuni , mi iketh kido modinego , nikech in ema ne onegi kendo rembi ema ne ing’iewogo ni Nyasaye ji moa e dhoudi duto kendo mawacho dhok duto kendo moa e ogendini duto kod pinje duto .
Ne itimogi oganda joka ruoth matiyo ni Nyasachwa kaka jodolo , kendo ginibed jotend piny . ”
Eka ne achako ang’icho , mi awinjo dwond malaika mang’eny molworo kom duong’ kaachiel gi gik mangima kod jodongogo . Kwan-gi ne gana gi gana , kendo tara gi tara .
Ne giwer matek niya , “ Nyarombo mane onegi owinjore yud teko gi mwandu gi rieko gi loch kod luor gi duong’ kod pak ! ”
Bende ne awinjo ka gik manie polo gi manie piny kendo manie bwo piny kod manie pi , tiende ni gik moko duto mochue , kawacho niya , “ Pak gi luor gi duong’ kod loch obed ni Jal mobet e kom duong’ , kendo obed ni Nyarombo nyaka chieng’ ! ”
Eka gik mangima ang’wen-go nodwoko ni , “ Obed kamano ” , kendo jodongo nopodho piny mi olemo .
Bang’ mano ne aneno ka Nyarombo ketho kido achiel kuom kido abiriyo modin-go kitabu , mi awinjo ka achiel kuom gik mangima ang’wengo wacho gi dwol machalo mor polo niya , “ Bi ”
Eka ne ang’icho mi aneno faras marachar . Ng’at moidhe noting’o atung’ , kendo ne osidhne osimbo , mi nowuok kaka jalocho madhi mondo olochi .
Kane Nyarombo oketho kido mar ariyo , ne awinjo gima ngima mar ariyo kawacho niya , “ Bi ! ”
Eka faras machielo ma silwal nowuok . To ng’at moidhe nomi teko mar kelo lweny e piny , mondo ji onegre , kendo ne omiye ligangla maduong’ !
Bang’ mano Nyarombo noketho kido mar adek , kendo ne awinjo gima ngima mar adek kawacho ni , “ Bi ! ” Ne ang’icho mi aneno faras marateng’ . Ng’at moidhe noting’o rapim mar ratil e lwete .
Eka ne awinjo gimoro machalo gi dwol kawuok e dier gik mangima ang’wen-go kawacho niya , “ Ogudu mar bel koro nengone romo pok jatich kuom odiechieng’ achiel , kendo ogute adek mag oduma bende nengone mana kamano ! To nengo mor zeituni gi divai to kik imedi . ”
To kane Nyarombo oketho kido mar ang’wen , ne awinjo dwond gima ngima mar ang’wen kawacho niya , “ Bi ! ”
Eka ne ang’icho mi aneno faras marabuor . Nying ng’at moidhe ne Tho , to Piny Joma Otho ne luwo machiegni . Ne omigi teko kuom bath piny moromo achiel kuom ang’wen , mondo gimi lweny kata kech kata tuoche kata ondiegi maricho mae piny oneg ji .
Kane Nyarombo oketho kido mar abich , ne aneno chuny jomoko e bwo kendo-mar-misango . Ne gin joma ne osenegi nikech Wach Nyasaye , kendo nikech ne gisiko ka gihulo ni giyie kuome .
Ne gikok matek niya , “ Yaye , Ruoth Maler kendo Maradiera ! Nyaka karang’o mapod ibiro bet ka ok ing’adoe bura ni joma odak e piny , kichulo kuor kuom rembwa ? ”
Eka ne omigi law marachar ng’ato ka ng’ato , kendo ne owachnigi ni mondo gimed yueyo mondi matin nyaka chop kar romb jotich wetegi kod owetegi mane ibiro nego kaka gin , rom .
Eka ne ang’icho , kendo kane Nyarombo oketho kido mar auchiel , to piny noyiengni matek . Wang’chieng’ nolokore marateng’ ti , kendo due nolokore makwar ka remo .
Sulue mae polo nolwar piny mana kaka ng’owo mapok ochiek lwar ka yamo makudho matek ouko .
Polo noban ka kalatas , mi olal nono , kendo gode gi chulni duto nogol oa kuonde ma gintie .
Eka ruodhi mag piny , gi ji madongodongo , gi jotelo mag lweny , gi jomwandu , kod joma rateke , kaachiel gi wasumbini kod joma ni thuolo duto , nopondo e buche kendo e bwo lwendni mag gode .
Ne giwacho ni gode gi lwendnigo niya , “ Ruombreuru kuomwa , mondo ugeng’wa kuom wang’ Jal mobet e kom duong’ kendo kuom mirima mager mar Nyarombo ,
nikech chieng’ maduong’ mar mirimbgi mager osechopo ! To ere ng’ama disir mirima ma kamano ? ”
Bang’ wechego ne aneno malaika ang’wen kochung’ e tunge ang’wen mag piny . Ne gimako yembe ang’wen mag piny , mondo yamo kik kudhi e piny , kata e nam , kaka kuom yath moro .
Eka ne aneno malaika machielo kawuok yo wuok chieng’ , koting’o gima igoyogo alama mar Nyasaye mangima . Nokok matek ni malaika ang’wen mane osemi teko mondo ohiny piny kod nam ,
kokwerogi niya , “ Kik uhiny piny , kata nam , kata yien , nyaka chop waket kido e lela wang’ jotich Nyasachwa . ”
Bang’ mano , ne awinjo kar romb joma ne oketnigi kidono . Ne giromo ji alufu mia achiel gi piero ang’wen gang’wen , ( 144,000 ) mowuok e dhout jo-Israel duto .
E dhood Juda ji mane oket kido kuomgi ne alufu apar gariyo . E dhood Reuben ji alufu apar gariyo . E dhood Gad ji alufu apar gariyo
E dhood Asher ji alufu apar gariyo . E dhood Naftali ji alufu apar gariyo . E dhood Manase ji alufu apar gariyo .
E dhood Simeon ji alufu apar gariyo . E dhood Lawi ji alufu apar gariyo . E dhood Isakar ji alufu apar gariyo .
E dhood Zebulun ji alufu apar gariyo . E dhood Josef ji alufu apar gariyo . E dhood Benjamin ji alufu apar gariyo .
Bang’ mano , ne ang’icho mi aneno ji mang’eny mokadho akwana moa e pinje duto gi dhoudi duto kod ogendini duto . Ne gichung’ e nyim kom duong’ , kendo e nyim Nyarombo , ka girwakore gi lewni marachere , kendo giting’o othidhe e lwetgi .
Ne gikok matek niya , “ Warruok oa kuom Nyasachwa mobet e kom duong’ kendo oa kuom Nyarombo . ”
Eka malaika duto nochung’ koluoro kom duong’ gi jodongo kod gik mangima ang’wen-go , mi okulore piny nyaka e lowo e nyim kom duong’ , mi gilamo Nyasaye ,
ka giwacho niya , “ Amin ! Pak gi duong’ gi rieko gi erokamano gi pwoch gi teko kod nyalo obed ni Nyasachwa nyaka chieng’ ! Amin ! ”
Eka achiel kuom jodongo nopenja niya , “ Joma orwako lewni maracheregi gin ng’a gini , to gia kune ? ”
To ne adwoke ni , “ Jaduong’ , in ema ing’eyo . ” Eka ne owachona niya , “ Magi e joma oseneno Sand Maduong’ . Giselwoko lepgi e remb Nyarombo , mi gimiyo odoko marachere .
Mano emomiyo gin e nyim kom duong’ mar Nyasaye , ka gilame odiechieng’ gotieno e Hekalune , kendo Jal mobet e kom duong’ biro dak kodgi .
Kech ok nochak okagi , kendo riyo ok nochak ologi , bende liet mar wang’chieng’ ok nowang’gi ,
nikech Nyarombo manie dier kom duong’ tir nobed jakwadhgi . Notelnigi e sokni mag pi ngima , kendo Nyasaye noywe pi wang’gi duto . ”
Kane Nyarombo oketho kido marabiriyo , to polo noling’ thi kuom kinde ma dirom nus sa .
Eka ne aneno malaika abiriyo mochung’ e nyim Nyasaye , kendo ne omigi tunge abiriyo .
Eka malaika moro nobiro mochung’ e nyim kendo-mar-misango , ka en gi tap ubani mar dhahabu . Ne omiye ubani mathoth mondo ochiw gi lemo mar jo-Nyasaye duto e kendo-mar-misango mar dhahabu mane ni e nyim kom duong’ .
Iro mar ubani manie lwet malaikano nodum malo e nyim Nyasaye kaachiel gi lemo mag jo-Nyasaye .
Malaika nokawo tap ubani mi ogangoe mach mane okawo kuom kendo-mar-misango , bang’e nobolo majno piny . Bang’ mano , polo nomor kariadore matek , kendo duol moko nowinjore , bende polo nomil , kendo piny noyiengni .
Eka malaika abiriyo man gi tunge abiriyogo ne oikore mondo ogo tungego .
Malaika mokwongo nogoyo tung’ne , mi pe kod mach mokikore gi remo obiro , mi opuk e piny , mi bath piny moromo achiel kuom adek nowang’ kendo achiel kuom adek mar yien bende nowang’ . Lum mang’ich duto bende nowang’ .
Bang’e malaika mar ariyo nogoyo tung’ne , mi gima chalo gi got maduong’ maliel ka mach nowiti e nam , mi bath nam moromo achiel kuom adek nolokore remo ,
kendo achiel kuom adek mar gik mangima manie nam notho , bende achiel kuom adek mar yiedhi manie nam nokethore .
Eka malaika mar adek nogoyo tung’ne , mi sulue maduong maliel ka meny nolwar oa e polo . Ne olwar kuom achiel mar adek mar aore duto , kendo kuom sokni duto .
Nying sulueno en ‘ Gima kech’ . Bath pi moromo achiel kuom adek nolokore makech , mi ji mang’eny otho nikech pigego nolokore makech .
Bang’e malaika mar ang’wen nogoyo tung’ne , mi achiel kuom adek mar wang’chieng’ , gi achiel kuom adek mar due kod achiel kuom adek mar odiechieng’ kod otieno , notimo mudho .
Eka nang’icho mi awinjo ongo ka huyo e kor polo kaywak matek niya , “ Lit ! Lit ! Mano kaka unune malit , un joma odak e piny , nikech tunge modong’ ma malaika adek biro goyo ! ”
Eka malaika mar abich nogoyo tung’ne , mi aneno sulue moro mane oselwar e piny koa e polo . Sulueno ne omi rayaw mar Bur Matut Maonge Gikone .
Ne oyawo burno , mi iro owuoke machalo gi ich mach maduong’ , mi wang’chieng gi kor polo otimo mudho nikech iro mane owuok e burno .
Bonyo nowuok e irono mopiyo e piny , kendo ne omigi teko machalo gi teko ma thomoni mae piny nigo .
To nokwergi ni kik giketh lum manie piny , kata gimoro mang’ich , kata yath moro , to giketh mana jogo maonge gi alama mar Nyasaye e lela wengegi .
Ne omi bonyogo thuolo mar sando jogo kuom dueye abich , to ne ok oyienigi mondo gineggi . Rem mane jogo nigo ne chalo gi rem maramo ng’at ma thomoni okayo .
E ndalo ma gigo notimre ji nodwar tho , to ok ginitho ngang’ ! Adier , ginigomb tho ahinya , to tho noringgi aringa !
Bonyogo ne chalo gi farese moikore ni lweny . E wigi ne nitie gik machalo gi osimbo mag dhahabu . Wang’gi to ne chalo gi wang’ dhano .
Ne gin gi yie wich machalo gi yie wi mon , to lekegi ne chalo gi leke sibuoche .
Ne girwako gilweny mag akor machalo gi akor mag nyinyo , kendo bwombegi ne wuo mana kaka geche lweny wuo ma farese mang’eny ywayo ka ringo dhi e lweny .
Iwgi ne chalo gi iw thomoni , kendo iwgigo ema ne gikayogo ji , kendo ng’at ma gikayo ne bedo gi rem kuom dueye abich .
Ruodhigo to ne malaika mar Bur Matut Maonge Gikone . Nyinge ne iluongo gi dho Hibrania ni Abadon , to gi dho Grik ni Apoluon , tiende ni Jaketh .
Masira mokwongo koro osekadho , to masiche ariyo mamoko pod biro .
Bang’ mano , malaika mar auchiel nogoyo tung’ne , mi awinjo dwol moro moa e tunge ang’wen mag kendo-mar-misango mar dhahabu manie nyim Nyasaye .
Dwolno nowacho ni malaika mar auchiel man gi tung’ niya , “ Gony malaika ang’wen motue e aora maduong’ mar Yufrate . ”
Omiyo ne ogony malaika ang’wen mane oseiki ni sano gi odiechieng’no gi dueno kod higano , mondo oneg achiel kuom adek mar ji duto .
Ne onyisa ni kar romb jolweny mane oidho farese ne oromo tara mia ariyo .
To farese mane aneno e fwenyno ne chalo kama : Joma ne oidhogi ne orwakore gi gilweny mag akor mag nyinyo makwar ka mach , kendo mambulu , kod ma onuria . Wi faresego to ne chalo gi wi sibuoche , kendo mach gi iro kod pilni mach ne wuok e dhogi .
Masiche adekgo , ma gin mach gi iro kod pilni mach mane wuok e dho faresego nonego achiel kuom adek mar ji duto ,
nimar teko mane faresergo nigo ne nie dhogi kendo e wigi . Iwgi , mane nigi wigi , ne chalo gi thuonde , kendo iwgigo ema ne gihinyogo ji .
To joma odong’ mane masichego ok onego , pod ne ok oloko chunygi oa kuom gik mane giseloso gi lwetgi , to ne gimedo mana lamo jochiende gi nyiseche manono molos gi dhahabu gi fedha gi mula gi kidi kod bao , ma gin gik ma ok nyal neno , kata winjo wach , kata wuotho .
Bende ne ok giloko chunygi giweyo nek , kata timbe juok , kata terruok , kata kuo , mane gisebedo ka gitimo .
Bang’e ne aneno malaika machielo maratego koa e polo . Ne orwakore gi bor polo , kendo lihudu nolworo wiye , to wang’e ne chalo gi sirni makakni ka mach .
Ne en gi kitabu matin moel e lwete . Tiende ma korachwich nonyono nam , to tiende ma koracham nonyono piny .
Nokok gi dwol maduong’ machalo mana dwond sibuor maruto . Kane osekok kamano , to polo abiriyo nomor ,
kendo kane polo abiriyogo osemor kamano to ne adwaro ndiko gima ne asewinjo ka giwacho , to ne awinjo dwol moro koa e polo mawacho niya , “ Kik indik gima polo abiriyogo osewacho , to ling’go mana e chunyi . ”
Eka malaika mane aneno ka onyono nam kod piny cha noting’o bade kochiko polo ,
mi okuong’ore gi nying Jal mantie nyaka chieng’ , kendo mane ochueyo polo gi piny gi nam kod gik moko duto manie igi . Nowacho niya , “ Deko moro ok nochak obedie ,
to ka malaika mar abiriyo ogoyo tung’ne to Nyasaye nochop chenone mopondo kaka osenyiso jotichne ma jonabi . ”
Bang’ mano , dwol mane asewinjo kawuoyo koa e polo cha nochako owuoyo koda ka wacho niya , “ Dhiyo mondo ikaw kitabu moel manie lwet malaika ma onyono nam kod piny . ”
Omiyo ne adhi ir malaikano , mi akwaye mondo omiya kitabu matinno . To nowachona niya , “ Kawe , mondo ichame . Obiro bedo mamit e dhogi ka mor kich ; iyi to obiro chando . ”
Eka ne akawo kitabu matinno e lwet malaikano , mi achamo , kendo ne omit e dhoga ka mor kich , to kane asechame kamano to nochando iya .
Bang’ mano , ne owachna niya , “ Nyaka ichak ikor wach kuom ogendini mang’eny , gi pinje mang’eny , kod joma wacho dhok mang’eny , kod ruodhi mang’eny . ”
Eka ne omiya odundu machalo gi luth mar rapim , mi owachna niya , “ A malo mondo ipim Hekalu mar Nyasaye kod kendo-mar-misango , kendo mondo ikwan joma lemo e iye kanyo .
To iwe laru maoko manie nyim Hekalu mak ipimo , nimar osemiye joma ok jo-Yahudi , kendo gibiro nyono dala maler gi tiendegi kuom dueye piero ang’wen gariyo .
To abiro miyo jonenona ariyo teko . Ginirwakre gi gunia , kendo ginihul wach moa kuom Nyasaye kuom ndalo alufu achiel gi mia ariyo kod piero auchiel . ”
Joneno ariyogo gin yien ariyo mag zeituni , kendo gin teyni ariyo mochung’ e nyim Ruodh piny ngima .
Ka wasikgi dwaro hinyogi , to mach wuok e dhogi kendo tiekogi . Mano e tho ma ng’ato ang’ata madwaro hinyogi nyaka thogo .
Gin gi teko mar loro polo mondo koth kik chue e ndalo ma gihuloe wach . Bende gin gi teko mar loko pige doko remo , kendo gin gi teko mar kelo tuoche mopogore opogore e piny e kinde akinda ma gidwaro .
To ka gisetieko hulo wach momigi , to ondiek mowuok e Bur Matut Maonge Gikone noked kodgi , mi logi kendo neggi .
Ringregi noriere e yo mar dala maduong’ ma iluongo gi ngero ni Sodom kata Misri , ma en dala mane ogurie Ruodhgi .
To ji moa e ogendini duto gi dhoudi duto , kendo mawacho dhok duto , bende moa e pinje duto , nong’i ringregi kuom ndalo adek gi nus , kendo ok giniyie mondo oyikgi .
Ji duto modak e piny nogo siboi kuom thogi , kendo ginimire chiwo , nikech jonabi ariyogo nosebedo kasando joma odak e piny .
To bang’ ndalo adek gi nusgo muya mar ngima moa kuom Nyasaye nodonjo kuomgi , mi gichung’ gi tiendegi . Kibaji maduong’ nomako joma ne onenogi !
Bang’ mano , jonabi ariyogo nowinjo dwol makok matek gie polo , kawachonigi niya , “ Biuru malo ku ! ” Kuom mano ne giidho malo mana ka wasikgi nenogi
Gikanyono , piny noyiengni matek , mi bath dalano moromo achiel kuom apar nomukore , kendo ji alufu abiriyo notho . To joma odong’ nobwok malich , kendo nomiyo Nyasaye duong’ !
Masira mar ariyo koro osekadho , to neuru , masira mar adek biro biro piyo .
Eka malaika mar abiriyo nogoyo tung’ne , kendo dwol moko nokok matek e polo kawacho niya , “ Loch mar pinyni koro osedoko mar Ruodhwa kod Mesia mare , kendo obiro locho nyaka chieng’ . ”
Eka jodongo piero ariyo gang’wen mobedo e kombegi mag duong’ e nyim Nyasaye kande , nokulore piny nyaka e lowo , mi olamo Nyasaye ,
kawacho niya , “ A Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto ! In Ruoth mantie kendo mane nitie ! Wagoyoni erokamano nikech isekawo tekoni maduong’ , kendo isechako locho .
Mirima nomako ogendini , to koro chieng’ mirimbi iwuon osechopo . Kinde osechopo ma iyaloe joma otho , kendo ichiwoe pok ni jotichni ma jonabi , kod jogi , kaachiel gi ji duto madongo gi matindo moluoro nyingi . En kinde mitiekoe jogo maketho piny . ”
Eka Hekalu mar Nyasaye manie polo noyawore , kendo Sandug Muma nonenore e Hekalu , mi polo omil kakakni ka mach . Dwol moko makok matek nowinjore , kendo polo nomor , bende piny noyiengni , kendo pe nochue mang’eny .
Bang’ mano , ranyisi malich ne onenore e kor polo . Ne en dhako morwakore gi wang’chieng’ . Due ne nie bwo tiende , to wiye nosidh e osimb sulue apar gariyo .
Ne en gi ich , kendo noywak ka muoch kaye , ka en gi rem mar nywol .
Eka ranyisi machielo bende ne onenore e polo . Ne en thuol mang’ongo , makwar kendo malich , man gi wiye abiriyo kod tunge apar , kendo ma osimbo abiriyo osidhi e wiyego .
Iwe noywayo achiel kuom adek mar sulue mae polo mi owito e piny . Thuol malichno nochung’ e nyim dhako mane dwaro nywolno mondo ocham nyathine kosenywolo .
Dhakono nonywolo nyathi mawuowi , mabiro rito ogendini gi ludh nyinyo . To nyathineno ne oyudhi moter malo ir Nyasaye e kom duong’ mar Nyasaye .
Dhakono to noringo modhi e thim kuma ne Nyasaye oikonee kar bet , mondo oritee ka imiye chiemo kuom ndalo alufu gi mia ariyo kod piero auchiel .
Eka lweny nowuok e polo . Mikael gi malaikane nokedo gi thuol malichno . Thuol gi malaikane bende nokedo kodgi ,
to ne ologi , mi kargi ne ok ochako obetie e polo kata matin .
Thuol maduong’no ne owit mwalo e piny kaachiel gi malaikane duto . En e thuol mang’ongo machon miluongo ni Jachien kata Satan , mane owuondo piny ngima .
Eka ne awinjo dwol maduong moa e polo , kawacho niya , “ Koro Nyasachwa oselocho . En kinde mar tekone gi lochne kaachiel gi mar Mesia mare , ma bende oyudo lochne . Oselo jadonj ni owetewa , madonjonigi e nyim Nyasaye odiechieng’ gotieno , mi owite e piny .
Owetewa ne oloye gi remb Nyarombo kendo gi Wach Nyasaye mane gihulo , bende ne ok gidewo ngimagi nyaka kar tho .
Omiyo , polo kod joma odakie mondo obed mamor ! To mano kaka nobednu malit un piny gi nam , nimar Satan oselor obiro iru ka nigi mirima mager nikech ong’eyo ni odongne mana ndalo matin kende . ”
To kane thuol malichno oneno ni osewite e piny , ne olawo dhako mane osenywolo nyathi ma wuowi cha .
To ne omi dhakono buom ariyo mag ongo maduong’ mondo ohugo ochop kare e thim , kuma ne idhi ritee kimiye chiemo kuom higni adek gi nus , ka en mabor gi thuol .
To thuol nong’ogo pi moa e dhoge mondo oyuogo dhakono , mi pigno nomol bang’ dhakono mana ka aora .
To piny noyawo dhoge , momwonyo pi mane thuol ong’ogono , mi okonyo dhakono .
Kuom mano , thuol nokecho gi dhakono , mi odhi mondo oked gi nyithind dhakono modong’ , marito chik Nyasaye , kendo mahulo ni giyie kuome ,
kendo ne ochung’ e kuoyo manie dhonam . Eka ne aneno Ondiek moro kawuok e nam . Ne en ni tunge apar kod wiye abiriyo . To nosidho osimbo apar e tungego , kendo wich ka wich nondikie nying mayanyo Nyasaye .
To ondiek mane anenono ne chalo gi kwach , to tiendene ne chalo gi tiende dubu , kendo dhoge ne chalo gi dho sibuor . To thuol malichno nomiye tekone owuon gi kome mar duong’ , mi obedo gi loch .
Wiye achiel ne nenore ka gima ogo lero mar tho , to wiye mane ogo lerono nosechango . Ji duto manie piny ngima ne luwo bang’ ondiegno , kawuoro lichne .
To bende ne gilamo thuondno nikech nosemiyo ondiek tekone owuon . Ondiek bende ne gilamo , ka giwacho niya , “ Ere ng’ama romo gi ondiek , koso ere ng’ama diked kode ? ”
Ne omi Ondiegno dhok mawacho weche mag warruok kod ayany , kendo ne oyiene kedo gi loch kuom dueye piero ang’wen gariyo .
Eka nochako yanyo Nyasaye , ka oyanyo nyinge kod kama odakie , kaachiel gi joma odak e polo .
Bende noyiene mondo oked gi jo-Nyasaye kendo ologi , kendo ne omiye teko kuom dhoudi duto .
Ji duto modak e piny lame , mak mana jogo ma nyinggi ondiki e kitap ngima mar Nyarombo mane onegi , chakre chuech piny .
Ng’at man gi it mondo owinji !
Ng’at ma onego tue nyaka tue , kendo ng’at monego negi e lweny , to nyaka negi e lweny , ma e kinde ma jo-Nyasaye nyaka timie kinda kendo nyaka bedie motegno .
Eka ne achako aneno ondiek machielo kawuok ei piny . Ne en gi tunge ariyo machalo gi mag nyarombo , to nowuoyo kaka thuol wuoyo .
To notiyo gi teko duto mar Ondiek mokwongono ka en e nyim Ondiegno . Nochuno piny kaachiel gi ji duto modakie mondo olam Ondiek mokwongo mane ogo lero mar tho , to nosechango cha .
Ondiek mar aeiyono notimo honni madongo ma kata mana mach omiyo lor e polo , biro e piny mana ka ji duto neno .
To honni mane oyiene ni mondo otim e nyim Ondiek mokwongo ema nowuondogo joma odak e piny . Ne ogolo chik mondo joma odak e piny olos gima ket gi ondiek mane ogo lero mar tho gi ligangla , to ne ok otho .
Ne oyiene mondo omi gima ket gi Ondiek mokwongo cha muya , mondo owuo kendo oneg ji duto ma otamore lamo gima ket gi ondiek mar ariyono .
Ondiegno nochuno ji duto , madongo gi matindo , jomwandu gi jochan , wasumbini gi joma ni thuolo , mondo giduto oket alama e luetgi ma korachwich kata e lela wengegi .
Ng’ato ne ok nyal ng’iewo gimoro kata loko gimoro mak mana ka en gi alama , tiende ni nying Ondiegno kata namba mochung’ kar nying’no .
To fwenyo tiend wachno dwaro rieko . Ng’at man gi rieko mondo okwan namba mar Ondiek , nikech nambano ochung’ kar nying dhano . Nambane en mia auchiel gi piero auchiel gauchiel .
Eka ne ang’icho , mi aneno Nyarombo kochung’ e got Sayun . Ne en gi ji alufu mia achiel gi piero ang’wen gang’wen , ( 144,000 ) kendo nyinge owuon gi nying Wuon mare nondiki e lela wang’ jogo .
Ne awinjo dwol moro moa e polo kawuo ka pi mang’eny , kendo machalo gi polo mamor matek . Chutho , dwol mane awinjono ne chalo mana gi dwond joma goyo thum .
Ne giwero wer manyien e nyim kom duong’ kendo e nyim gik mangima ang’wen kod jodongo kande . To onge ng’ama ne nyalo puonjore wendno mak mana ji alufu mia achiel gi mia ang’wen gang’wen , ( 144,000 ) ma gin kende e joma ne owar oa e piny .
Magi e joma ne ok odwanyore gi mon , to ne giritore maler . Giluwo Nyarombo kamoro amora modhiye . Osewargi kuom ji mana kaka olemo mokwongo nyak , michiwo ni Nyasaye kendo ni Nyarombo .
Miriambo ne ok owuok e dhogi , kendo gionge gi ketho moro kata achiel .
Eka ne aneno malaika moro ka huyo e kor polo . Ne en gi Wach Maber mochwere mondo oland ni joma odak e piny . Nolando wachno ni pinje duto , kod ogendini duto .
Nokok matek niya , “ Luoruru Nyasaye , kendo miyeuru duong’ , nikech sa mong’adoe bura osechopo ! Lamuru Jal mane ochueyo polo gi piny kaachiel gi nam kod sokni . ”
Eka malaika mar ariyo noluwe kawacho niya , “ Yaya Babulon , dala maduong’ , osepodho ! Osepodho ! En e dhako mane omiyo ogendini duto omadho divai mar terruokne . En divai makelo mirimb Nyasaye . ”
Bang’ mano , malaika mar adek nobiro bang’gi kawacho matek niya , “ Ng’ato ang’ata malamo ondiek kod gima ket kode , mi oyudo alama e lela wang’e kata e lwete ,
nyaka madh divai mar mirimb Nyasaye moruw makech e kikombe mar mirimbe . Noyud sand mar mach makakni e nyim malaika maler , kendo e nyim Nyarombo .
To iro mar mach masandogi nodum malo nyaka chieng’ . Bende jogo malamo Ondiek kod gima ket kode , kata moyudo alama mar nyinge , ok noyud yueyo odiechieng’ gotieno . ”
Ka eri ema idwaroe kinda mar jo-Nyasaye , kendo ma ok we yie ma gin-go kuom Yesu !
Eka ne awinjo dwol moa e polo kawacho niya , “ Ndik ni , ‘ Chakre kawuono , jogo matho kogeno kuom Ruoth , gin johawi ! ’ ” Roho bende wacho ni , “ Ee , gin johawi adier , nikech giniyue kuom tichgi matek , nimar gik ma gisetimo dhi kodgi . ”
Eka ne ang’icho mi aneno bor polo marachar , to ewi bor polono ne nitie gima obetie machalo gi dhano . Ne osidho osimbo mar dhahabu e wiye , kendo ne oting’o pala mar keyo mabith e lwete .
Eka malaika machielo nowuok e Hekalu kakok matek ni jal mane obet e bor polono niya , “ Kaw pandi mar keyo mondo ike nikech kinde mar keyo osechopo , kendo piny ochiek mokadho ! ”
Omiyo jal mane obet e bor polo notiyo gi pande mar keyo e piny mi okayo piny .
Bang’ mano , malaika moro nowuok e Hekalu manie polo . En bende ne en gi pand keyo mabith .
Eka malaika machielo man gi teko kuom mach noa e kendo-mar-misango . Ne okok matek ni malaika mane nigi pand keyo mabithno niya , “ Kaw pandi mar keyo mabithno mondo ichok olemb mzabibu mag piny nikech olembene ochiek ahinya ! ”
Omiyo , malaikano notiyo gi pande mar keyo e piny , mi ochoko olemb mzabibu mag piny , mobologi kar biyo mzabibu maduong’ mar mirimb Nyasaye .
Olembe ne obi kinyono kar bichono e alap mar dala , kendo remo mamol kawuok kar bichono , mochopo kilomita adek koa e dala , to tut remono ne dirom mita ariyo .
Bang’e ne aneno ranyisi machielo malich kendo miwuoro e polo ! Gima ne aneno ne gin malaika abiriyo moting’o masiche abiriyo . Mago ne masiche mogik , nikech ka girumo to mirimb Nyasaye bende orumo kodgi .
Eka ne aneno gima chalo gi nam mar rang’i moruwore gi mach . Bende ne aneno joma ne oseloyo Ondiek gi gima ket kode kod namba mar nyinge . Ne gichung’ e dir nam mar rang’i ka gin gi thumbe mag Nyasaye e luetegi .
Ne giwero wend Musa jatich Nyasaye , kod wend Nyarombo , niya , “ A Ruoth Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto ! Mano kaka tijeni dongo ! A Ruodh ogendini , mano kaka yoreni kare kendo adier !
A Ruoth , en ng’ano ma ok nyal luori , kata ma ok nyal miyo nyingi duong’ ? In kendi ema iler ! Ogendini duto nobi , mi kulre e nyimi , nikech timbeni makare osenenore ratiro . ”
Bang’ mano , ne ang’icho mi aneno ka Hekalu mar Hemb Rapar oyawore e polo .
Malaika abiriyo man gi masiche abiriyogo nowuok e Hekalu . Ne girwakore gi lewni maler kendo marieny , kendo ne gitueyo okanda mag dhahabu e korgi .
Eka achiel kuom gik mangima ang’wen-go nomiyo malaika abiriyogo tewni abiriyo mag dhahabu ma opong’ gi mirimb Nyasaye mantie nyaka chieng’ .
To iro moa kuom duong’ maler mar Nyasaye gi tekone nopong’o Hekalu , omiyo onge ng’ama ne nyalo donjo e Hekalu ka masiche abiriyo mag malaika abiriyogo pok orumo .
Bang’e ne awinjo dwol maduong’ moa e Hekalu kawacho ni malaika abiriyogo niya , “ Dhiuru uol tewni abiriyo mag mirimb Nyasaye e piny . ”
Kuom mano , malaika mokwongo nodhi moolo tape e piny , mi adhonde maricho kendo malit nomako joma ne nigi alama mar Ondiek , kendo mane lamo gima ket kode .
Eka malaika mar ariyo noolo tape e nam , mi pi nam nolokore remo machalo remb ng’at motho , kendo gik mangima duto mae nam notho .
Kamano bende malaika mar adek noolo tape e aore gi sokni , mi pigegi nolokore remo .
Eka ne awinjo malaika man gi teko kuom pige kawacho niya , “ A Ng’ama Ler , mantie kendo mane nitie ! Bura miseng’ado ni , iseng’ado e yo makare ,
nikech joma nochuero remb jo-Nyasaye kod jonabi isemiyo remo mondo omadhi ! ”
Eka ne awinjo kendo-mar-misango kawacho niya , “ Adier , in Ruoth Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto , ing’ado bura madieri kendo makare ! ”
Bang’ mano , malaika mar ang’wen noolo tape e wang’chieng’ , mi wang’ chieng’ nomi teko mar wang’o ji ka mach .
Omiyo ji nowang’ malit ahinya , to kata kamano ne giyanyo ayanya nying Nyasaye man gi teko mar kelo masichego , kendo ne gitamore loko chunygi mondo gimiye duong’ .
Eka malaika mar abich noolo tape e kom duong’ mar Ondiek malichno , mi piny Ondiek notimo mudho ! Ji nokayo lewgi nikech rem malit mane gin-go ,
to ne giyanyo ayanya Nyasach polo nikech rem kod adhonde ma gi-go , to kendo ne ok gilokore giweyo timbegigo .
Bang’e malaika mar auchiel noolo tape e aora maduong’ mar Yufrate , mi pige nodwono mondo yo olosre ni ruodhi mane biro a yo wuokchieng’ .
Bang’ mano naneno chuny adek mochido machalo gi ogwende , kawuok e dho Thuol malich , kendo e dho Ondiek , kendo e dho Janabi mar Miriambo .
Chunygo gin jochiende , kendo gin gi teko mar timo honni . Gidhi ir ruodhi duto mag piny ngima mondo gichokgi ni lweny manobedie Chieng’ Maduong’ mar Nyasaye Manyalo gik Moko Duto .
( Neuru ! Abiro ka jakuo ! Ng’at ma neno , kendo ma orwako lepe mondo wiye kik kuodi kowuotho duk , en jahawi ! )
Chunygo nochoko ruodhigo kama iluongo gi dho Hibrania ni Harmagedon .
Malaika mar abiriyo noolo tape e kor yamo , mi dwol maduong’ nowuok e kom duong’ manie Hekalu kawacho niya , “ Osetimore ! ”
Bang’ mano , ne nitie mil polo makakni , gi dwol moko , kod mor polo . Piny bende noyiengni matek mapok oyiengnie kamano nyaka a chuech dhano . Adier , ne en yiengni piny marachie moloyo !
Dala maduong’ nobarore didek , kendo mich ogendini duto mae piny nomukore . Nyasaye noparo Babulon dala maduong’ , mi ne omiyo omadho kikombe mar divai mar mirimbe mager !
Chulni duto nolal nono kaachiel gi gode duto .
Kite mag pe madongongo , ma achiel pekne dirom kilo piero abich , noa e polo mogoyo ji , mi ne giyanyo Nyasaye nikech masich peno , nimar ne en masira marach ahinya !
Eka achiel kuom malaika abiriyo man gi tewni abiriyo nobiro ira , mi owachona niya , “ Bi mondo anyisi bura mong’adi ni jachode maduong’ , ma en dala maduong’ moger e wi pige mang’eny !
En ema ruodhi mag piny oseterore kode , kendo ji duto modak e piny bende osemadho divai mar terruokne mi omer . ”
Bang’e Roho nomaka , mi malaika nokawa motera e thim , kuma nanenoe dhako moro koidho ondiek makwar . Nying mag ayany nondik e dend ondiegno duto , kendo ne en gi wiye abiriyo kod tunge apar .
Dhakono norwako law maralik gi makwar , kendo nolichore gi dhahabu kod kite ma nengogi tek , kod lulu . To e lwete noting’oe kikombe mar dhahabu mopong’ gi gik modwanyore kod gik mochido mag terruokne .
Nying moro ma tiende opondo nondiki e lela wang’e niya , “ Babulon maduong’ , min jochiende duto , kendo min gik modwanyore mag piny . ”
Bende ne aneno ka remb jo-Nyasaye , kod remb joma ohulo ni Yesu e Ruoth , omero dhakono . Kane anene to ne awuoro ahinya ,
to malaika cha nopenja ni , “ Ere gima omiyo iwuoro ? Abiro nyisi tiend wach mopondo mar dhakono kod ondiek ma oidho man gi wiye abiriyo kod tunge apar .
Ondiek mane inenono , yande nitie , to tinde oonge . To obiro wuok e Bur Matut Maonge Gikone mi tieke . Ji duto modak e piny , ma nyinggi ok ondiki e kitap ngima chakre chuech piny , nowuor ka gineno ondiegno , nimar yande entie , to tinde oonge , to nochak oduog kendo .
“ Ng’eyo tiend wachni dwaro paro mariek . Wiye abiriyogo gin gode abiriyo ma dhakono obetie .
To bende gin ruodhi abiriyo , ma abich kuomgi osepodho , to achiel pod nitie , kendo machielo pok obiro . To ka obiro to nobed kuom kinde matin kende .
To ondiek ma yande nitie , to tinde ongeno , en ruoth mar aboro , to bende en achiel kuom ruodhi abiriyogo , kendo ibiro tieke .
Tunge apar mane inenogo to gin ruodhi apar mapok ochako bedo gi loch , to ibiro miyogi teko mar loch kaka ruodhi , kaachiel gi ondiegno , kuom sa achiel kende .
To giduto gin gi paro achiel , kendo ginichiw tekogi kod lochgi ni ondiek mondo obed jatendgi .
Giniked gi Nyarombo , to Nyarombo nologi , nimar en Jaduong’ mar jodongo , kendo Ruodh ruodhi , kendo nikech joma luwe gin joma oluongi kendo ma oyier , kendo moyie kuome .
Eka malaikano nowachona niya , “ Pige mane ineno kama dhako ma jachodeno obetie , gin mana ji gi ogendini gi dhoudi kod joma wacho dhok mopogore opogore .
To tunge apar mane ineno , kaachiel gi ondiegno , nobed mamon gi dhako ma jachodeno . Ginikeye nono mi giweye duk . Ginicham ringre , kendo giniwang’e pep gi mach ,
nimar Nyasaye oseketo paro moro e chunygi mondo gitim gima odwaro gi chuny achiel , kendo mondo gimi ondiek lochgi , nyaka wach Nyasaye chopi .
“ To dhako mane inenono , en dala maduong’ man gi loch kuom ruodhi mag piny . ”
Bang’ wechego naneno malaika machielo kalor a e polo . Ne en gi teko maduong’ , kendo ler mare ne menyo piny .
Nokok matek niya , “ Yaye ! Babulon dala maduong’ osepodho ! Osepodho ! Osedoko kar dak mar jochiende kendo odoko gunda ma chuny duto mochido odakie , kaachiel gi winy duto ma ok ler kendo makuero .
Mano osetimore nikech ogendini duto osemadho divai makech mag terruokne . Ruodhi mag piny oseterore kode , kendo joohala mag piny bende osedoko jomwandu nikech ohala ma ngimane mamalo osekelonigi . ”
Eka ne achako awinjo dwol machielo moa e polo kawacho niya , “ Un joga , auru kuom dalano , mondo kik uriwru e richone , kendo kik unwang’ masichene ,
nikech richone osebiwore mochopo nyaka e polo , kendo Nyasaye koro oseparo timbene mamonogo .
Timneuru kaka osetimo ! Medneuru nyadiriyo kuom gik ma osetimo ! Kikombe mane omiyo jomoko omadho , ema mondo uolne nyadiriyo !
Miyeuru sand kod ywagruok moromore mana gi duong’ mane omiyore owuon kodak e ngima mamalo ! Owacho e chunye niya , ‘ An Ruoth , kendo ok nane gima dimi aywag ngang’ . ’ .
Mano omiyo masichene chieng’ moro nopoye chieng’ achiel . Masichego gin tho gi ywagruok kod kech , kendo nowang’e pep gi mach , nimar Ruoth Nyasaye moseng’adone bura nigi teko maduong’ ! ”
To ruodhi mag piny moseterore kode , kendo mosedak kode e ngimane mamalo noywage kasedo kod nyinge , kaneno ich mach mawang’e kadhuolore .
Ginichung’ gi kuma bor , ka kihondko omakogi nikech sandruok moyudo , kendo giniwach niya , “ Yaye ! Mano kaka dala maduong’ neno malit ! Yaye ! In Babulon , dala man gi teko , osetieki mana e sa achiel kende ! ”
Johala mag piny bende noywage kadengo , nikech onge ng’at ma koro nochak ong’iew mwandugi , ma gin :
Dhahabu gi fedha gi kite ma nengogi tek gi lulu gi nanga maber gi nanga maratiglo kod nanga mareprep gi nanga makwar gi yien duto madum tik mamit , gi gik moko duto molos gi lak liech , kod molos gi yien ma nengogi tek , kod molos gi mula , kod molos gi nyinyo , kendo molos gi kite mabeyo ,
kod gik moko kaka dalasini gi gik mang’ue ng’ar , gi uvumba , gi mor wir madum tik mamit , gi ubani , kod divai gi mo kod mogo mayom gi ngano kod rombe gi dhok kod farese gi geche lweny , gi joma otue wasumbini , kod ngima mag ji .
Johala nowach ni dala Babulon niya , “ Gik mabeyo duto ma yande iketo e chunyi oserumo ! Adier , gik mapakni gi gik malombo wang’ oselal nono . Ok nichak ibed kodgi ng’ang’ ! ”
Johala mane odoko momew nikech ne giloko ohala e dalano , nochung’ gi kuma bor , ka kihondko omakogi nikech sandruokne . Giniywagi ka giwacho niya ,
“ Yaye ! Mano gima lit manade ma osetimore ni dala maduong’ni ! Ne orwakore gi nanga maber , gi maratiglo gi makwar , kendo nolichore gi dhahabu gi kite ma nengogi tek kod lulu .
Yaye ! Mano kaka oseketh mwandune duto mana kuom sa achiel kende ! ” To ji duto ma weg yiedhi gi jokwang’ gi jonam kod ji duto maloko ohala e nam ne ochung’ gi kuma bor .
Kane gineno ich mach mawang’o Babulon ne giywak ka gikok niya , “ Onge dala moro maduong mosebedoe machal gi dalani ! ”
Ne gibuko wigi buru ka giywak kendo gidengo niya , “ Yaye ! Mano gima lit manade mosetimore ni dala maduong’ni ! En dala ma ji duto mane nigi yiedhi odokoe joma omew nikech mwandune mathoth . To osekethe mana kuom sa achiel kende , mi odoko gunda !
“ To in polo , gone siboi nikech osekethe . Un jo-Nyasaye gi joote kod jonabi , beduru mamor , nimar Nyasaye osekume kuom gima notimonu !
“ Eka malaika maratego noting’o kidi machalo gi pong’ maduong’ , mi obolo e nam , kowacho niya , “ Mano e kaka dala maduong’ mar Babulon nobol piny , mi ok nochak onene kendo ngang’ !
Dwond joma goyo thum gi jower gi joma goyo asili gi joma goyo tung’ ok nochak owinj kuomi ngang’ . Bende jotich matiyo tich moro amora ok nochak oyudi kuomi ngang’ , kata dwond pong’ marego bende ok nowinji kuomi kendo .
Ler mar taya ok nochak orieny kuomi , kata dwond wuon kisera gi dwond miaha ok nowinji kuomi kendo ng’ang’ . Joohala magi ne gin joohala madongo e piny , bende ne iwuondo ogendini duto gi timbeni mag jwok . ”
Babulon ne okum kamano nikech remb jonabi gi remb jo-Nyasaye gi remb ji duto mane osenegi e piny , ne oyud kuome .
Bang’ wechego nawinjo gima chalo gi koko maduong’ mar oganda mang’ongo e polo kawacho niya , “ Opak Nyasaye ! Warruok gi duong’ maler kod teko gin mag Nyasachwa ,
nikech pile ong’ado bura e yo ma adier kendo makare . Nong’ado bura ni jachode maduong’ mane oketho piny gi terruokne . Adier , Nyasaye osekume nikech nonego jotich Nyasaye . ”
Eka ne gichako gikok kendo niya , “ Opak Nyasaye ! Iro mar dala maduong’ mawang’no nodum nyaka chieng’ ! ”
To jodongo piero ariyo gang’wen gi gik mangima ang’wen kande , nopodho piny mi olamo Nyasaye mobet e kom duong’ , kawacho ni , “ Ber mondo obed kamano ! Opak Nyasaye ! ”
Bang’ mano , duol moro noa e kom duong’ kawacho niya , “ Pakuru Nyasachwa un jotichne duto madongo gi matindo ma oluore ! ”
Bang’e ne achako awinjo gima chalo gi koko oganda mang’ongo , kendo machalo gi pige mang’eny kawuo , bende machalo gi polo mamor matek , kawacho niya , “ Opak Nyasaye ! Ruoth Nyasachwa Manyalo Gik Moko Duto osekawo lochne .
Wabeduru mamor ahinya , kendo wamiyeuru duong’ nikech kinde mar kend mar Nyarombo osechopo . Chiege oseikore ,
kendo Nyasaye oseyiene mondo orwakre gi nanga maber mapichni kendo maler . ” ( Nanga maberno ochung’ kar tim makare mar jo-Nyasaye )
Eka malaikano nowachona ni , “ Ndik niya , ‘ Joma oluongi e kisera mar Nyarombo gin johawi . ’ . ” Eka nomedo wachona niya , “ Mano e wach mar adier mar Nyasaye . ”
Ne apodho piny e tiende mondo olame , to nokwera ni , “ Ngang’ ! Kik itim kamano ! An mana jatich wadu matiyo kodi kaachiel gi oweteni mamoko . Wan duto wahulo wach man kuom Yesu . Nyasaye kende ema mondo ilam . Adiera ma Yesu kelo ema miyo jonabi koro wach . ”
Eka ne aneno polo ka oyawore , kendo ne aneno faras marachar ka ni kanyo , to Jal mane oidhe iluongo ni Ng’ama Igeno , kendo Jaadiera . Iluonge kamano nikech ong’ado bura kare , kendo okedo e yo makare .
Wengene liel ka ligek mach , kendo osidhne osimbo mang’eny e wiye . En gi nying mondik kuome , ma onge ng’ama ong’eyo , to mak mana en owuon ,
kendo orwakore gi law moling’ore e remo . Iluonge ni Wach Nyasaye .
Ogend lweny mag polo ne luwo bang’e koidho farese marachere , kendo korwakore gi lewni mabeyo kendo maler .
To ligangla mabith wuok e dhoge kendo ochwowogo ogendini . Obiro ritogi gi ludh nyinyo , kendo obiro ng’adonigi bura gi mirimb Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto .
En gi nying moro mondiki e lawe kendo eme ni , “ Ruodh ruodhi , kendo Jaduong’ jodongo . ”
Eka ne ang’iyo wang’chieng’ mi aneno malaika moro kochung’ kuno . Ne okok matek ni winy duto mane huyo e kor polo niya , “ Chokreuru ubi e sawo maduong’ mar Nyasaye ,
mondo ucham ring ruodhi , gi ring jodong lweny , gi ring joma rateke , kod ring farese gi joma idhogi , kaachiel gi ring ji duto , joma ni thuolo gi wasumbini , joma tindo gi joma dongo . ”
Eka naneno Ondiek malichno gi ruodhi mag piny kod ogendni mag lweny kochokore mondo oked gi Jal moidho faras gi ogandane mar lweny .
To ne olo Ondiek , mi omaki kaachiel gi Janabi mar Miriambo , mane osebedo katimo honni e nyime . Honnigo ema ne osewuondogo joma ne oketnigi alama mar Ondiek , kendo mane lamo gima ket gi Ondiegno . Ondiek gi Janabi ne owit kangima e ataro mar ligek mach .
To joma odong’ ne oneg gi ligangla mane wuok e dho Jal moidho faras , kendo ringgi noyieng’o winy duto .
Eka naneno malaika moro koa e polo lor piny , koting’o rayaw mar Bur Matut Maonge Gikone e lwete kod nyororo maduong’ .
Ne omako Thuol malichno , tiende ni thuol machon miluongo ni Jachien kata Satan , mi otweyo gi nyororo kuom higni alufu achiel .
Ne obole e Bur Matut Maonge Gikone , mi oloro dho bur kendo otueyo , mondo kik ochak owuond ogendini nyaka higni alufu achielgo rum . To bang’e nogonye kuom kinde matin .
Bang’ mano ne aneno kombe mag duong’ , kendo joma ne obet e kombego ne omi teko mar ng’ado bura . Bende ne aneno chuny joma noseng’ad wiyegi nikech ne gihulo wach man kuom Yesu , kendo nikech ne gilando wach Nyasaye . Gin ne ok gilamo Ondiek kata gima ket kode , bende ne ok oketnigi alama mar Ondiek e lela wengegi kata e luetgi . Ne gidoko mangima , mi gilocho gi Kristo kuom higni alufu achiel . Mano e chier mokwongo .
( Joma otho modong’ to ne ok odoko mangima kendo , nyaka higni alufu achiel orumo . )
Joma ochier e chier mokwongoni gin johawi kendo gin joma ler . Tho mar ariyo onge gi teko kuomgi , to ginibed jodolo mag Nyasaye kod mag Kristo , kendo giniloch kode kuom higni alufu achielgo .
To ka higni alufu achielgo oserumo , to nogony Satan e bur motueyeno ,
kendo nowuog oko mondo odhi owuond Gog gi Magog , tiende ni ogendini manie tunge piny duto koni gi koni , mi ochokgi ni lweny . To kar rombgi chalo gi kwoyo mae dhonam .
Ne gikwako piny te , mi gilworo kambi mar jo-Nyasaye kod dala ma Nyasaye ohero . To mach ne oa e polo motiekogi ,
kendo Satan mane owuondogi ne owit e ataro mar ligek mach , kama Ondiek kod Janabi mar Miriambo bende nitie . Kuno ginisandre odiechieng’ gotieno nyaka chieng’ .
Eka ne aneno kom duong’ mang’ongo marachar kod jal mobetie . Piny gi polo noringo oa e nyime mi olal nono .
Bende ne aneno joma otho , madongo gi matindo , kochung’ e nyim kom duong’ , kendo noel kitepe . Eka kitabu machielo , ma en kitap ngima bende noel . Joma otho nong’adnigi bura kuom gik mane gitimo , kaluwore gi weche mane ondik e kitepego .
Nam nogolo joma otho manie iye , kendo Tho gi Piny Joma Otho , bende nochiwo joma otho manie igi , kendo ng’ato ka ng’ato nong’adne bura kuom gik mane osetimo .
Eka Tho gi Piny Joma Otho ne owit e ataro mar mach . Ataro mar machno en tho mar ariyo .
Ng’ato ang’ata mane nyinge ok onwang’ kondik e kitap ngima , ne owit e ataro mar mach .
Bang’ mano , naneno polo manyien gi piny manyien . Polo mokwongo gi piny mokwongo noserumo , kendo nam bende noselal nono .
Eka ne aneno Dala Maler , ma en Jerusalem manyien , kalor piny a e polo kuom Nyasaye , koikore ka miaha moikore ni chwore .
Ne awinjo dwol maduong’ moa e kom maduong’ kawacho niya , “ Koro Nyasaye osebiro dak gi ji ! Obiro dak kodgi kendo ginibed joge . Nyasaye owuon biro bet kodgi , mi obed Nyasachgi .
Enoywe pi wang’gi duto , kendo tho kata ywak kata nduru kata rem ok nochak obedie nikech gik machon noserumo . ”
Eka Jal mane obet e kom duong’ nowacho niya , “ Neuru ! Aloso gik moko duto bedo manyien ! ” Bende nokona ni , “ Ndik wachno , nikech wechegi gin weche migeno kendo ma adiera . ”
Bang’ mano nowachona niya , “ Gik moko duto osetimore ! An e Alfa gi Omega , tiende ni Chakruok gi Giko . Ng’at ma riyo oloyo anami pi soko mar ngima nono , ma ok ochulo gimoro .
Ng’at molocho noyud gigo , kendo anabed Nyasache , to enobed wuoda .
To ngoche , gi joma ok oyie , kod jomriambo duto , kargi nobed mana ataro maliel gi ligek mach , ma en tho mar ariyo ! ”
Eka achiel kuom malaika abiriyo mane nigi tewni moting’o masiche mogik abiriyo , nobiro ira , mowuoyo koda . Nowachona niya , “ Bi mondo anyisi Miaha , ma en chi Nyarombo . ”
Eka malaikano notera malo ewi got maduong’ kendo mabor , ka an ei Roho , mi onyisa Jerusalem , Dala Maler , kalor piny a e polo kuom Nyasaye ,
ka nigi duong’ maler duto mar Nyasaye . Lerne ne rieny ka kidi ma nengone tek , kaka jasper maler ahinya .
Ne en gi ohinga maduong’ kendo mabor man gi dhorangeye apar gariyo , ma malaika apar gariyo rito . To nying dhoudi apar gariyo mag nyithind Israel nondiki e dhorangeyego .
Dhorangeye adek ne ni yo wuokchieng’ , kendo adek yo nyandwat , to adek mamoko yo milambo , kendo adek yo podho chieng’ .
To ohinga mar dalano ne nigi kite mag mise apar gariyo ma ondikie nying joote apar gariyo mag Nyasaye .
Malaika mane wuoyo kodano , ne nigi luth mar rapim molos gi dhahabu mopimogo dalano gi dhorangeyene kod ohingane .
Bor gi lach mar dalano romre koni gi koni . Malaikano nopime gi ludhno , mi oyudo ni oromo kilomita alufu ariyo . Borne gi lachne kod borne modhi malo ne romre duto .
Eka nopimo ohingane , mi oyudo ni oromo bede mia achiel gi piero ang’wen , kipimo gi bat mar dhano , ma en rapim mane malaika otiyogo .
Kor ohinga noger ji jasper , to dala hie ne dhahabu lilo marieny ka rang’i maler .
Mise mar ohinga mar dala , nolos gi kite ma nengogi tek mopogore opogore . Kidi mokwongo mar mise ne jasper , to mar ariyo ne safir , to mar adek ne kalkedo , to mar ang’wen ne zumaridi ,
to mar abich ne sardonikso , to mar auchiel ne sardius , to mar abiriyo ne krusolith , to mar aboro ne berul , to mar ochiko ne topaz , to mar apar ne krusopraso , to mar apar gachiel ne huakintho , to mar apar gariyo ne amethuso .
Dhorangeye apar gariyogo to ne kite apar gariyo ma nengogi tek , miluongo ni lulu , kendo dhorangach ka dhorangach nolos gi lulu achiel achiel . Yor dalano ne dhahabu lilo marieny ka rang’i .
Ne ok aneno Hekalu e dalano , nimar Ruoth Nyasaye Manyalo Gik Moko Duto kod Nyarombo ema obedo Hekalu mare .
Dalano ok dwar chieng’ kata due marieny kuome , nikech duong’ maler mar Nyasaye ema miye ler , kendo Nyarombo e tache .
Ogendini mag piny nowuoth e lerne , kendo ruodhi mag piny nokel duong’gi e iye .
Dhorangeyene ok nolor godiechieng’ , to gotieno bende nobed maonge kuno .
Duong’ gi mwandu mag ogendini nokel e iye .
To gimoro amora ma ok ler , kata ng’at matimo gik mamono , kata mariambo , ok nodonjie ngang’ to mak mana jogo ma nyinggi ondiki e kitap Nyarombo mar ngima .
Bang’ mano , malaikano nonyisa aora mar pi ngima marieny ahinya , kendo mamol kaa e kom duong , mar Nyasaye gi mar Nyarombo .
Ne omol e dier yor dalano , to e bath aora koni gi koni , ne nitie yath mar ngima manyago olembe kido apar gariyo . To olembego chiek due ka due , kendo pot yadhno ema ithiedhogo ogendini .
Gik ma Nyasaye okwedo to nolal nono . Kom duong’ mar Nyasaye gi Nyarombo ema nobedie , kendo jotichne nolame .
Gininene wang’ gi wang’ , kendo nyinge nobed e lela wang’gi .
Otieno ok nochak obedie , kendo ok ginidwar ler mar taya kata mar chieng’ , nikech Ruoth Nyasaye nomigi ler , kendo ginibed gi loch nyaka chieng’ .
Eka malaikano nowachona niya , “ Wechegi gin weche migeno kendo ma adiera , kendo Ruoth Nyasaye ma oro Roho mare ni jonabi oseoro malaikane mondo onyis jotichne gik mabiro timore piyopiyo . ”
Yesu owacho ni , “ Winji ! Abiro piyo ” Ng’at momako weche mokor manie kitabuni en jahawi !
An Johana ema ne awinjo gigi kendo anenogi . Kane awinjogi kendo anenogi kamano , to ne apodho piny e tiend malaika mane nyisagi .
To ne okwera ni , “ Ngang’ ! Kik itim kamano ! An mana jatich wadu matiyo kodi kaachiel gi owetena ma jonabi kod joma omako weche manie kitabuni . Nyasaye kende ema mondo ilam ! ”
Bang’ mano malaikano nowachona niya , “ Kik iling’ gi weche mokor manie kitabuni , nikech kinde moketi chiegni !
We ng’at matimo richo otim atima richo , kendo ng’at ma ochido gie chunye , obed abeda mochido gie chunye . To ng’ama kare , obed abeda makare , kendo ng’ama ler , obed abeda maler . ”
Yesu wacho niya , “ Winji ! Abiro piyo , kendo akelo pok ma an-go mondo ami ng’ato ka ng’ato moromo gi tichne .
An Alfa gi Omega , tiende ni Jal Mokwongo kendo Mogik , kendo Chakruok gi Giko . ”
“ Joma oselwoko lepgi gin johawi , nimar ginibed gi thuolo mar chamo olemb yadh ngima , kendo mar donjo e dhorangeye mag dala .
To guogi gi jojuogi , gi joma terore , gi jonek , gi joma lamo nyiseche manono , kod ji duto ma ohero miriambo kendo matimo gik ma ok adiera , nobed oko .
“ An Yesu aseoro malaikana mondo ohulnu wechegi ukonygo kanyakla mag jo-Kristo . An Nyakwar Daudi , kendo an sulue mar okinyi . ”
Roho gi Miaha wacho ni , “ Bi ! ” Ng’ama owinjo , bende mondo owach ni , “ Bi ! ” To ng’ama riyo oloyo , mondo obi oyud pi mar ngima nono , mak ochulo gimoro .
An Johana asiemo ng’ato ka ng’ato mawinjo weche mokor manie kitabuni niya , “ Ka ng’ato omedo wach moro kuomgi , to Nyasaye nomedne masiche mondik e kitabuni .
Bende ka ng’ato ogolo wach moro kuom weche mokor manie kitabuni , to Nyasaye nogol kuome pok ma doyudo kuom yadh ngima kendo kuom Dala Maler mondiki e kitabuni . ”
Jal manyiso wechegi duto wacho niya , “ Adier , abiro piyo ! ” Obed kamano ! Bi , Ruoth Yesu !
Ng’wono mar Ruodhwa Yesu Kristo obed kodu uduto .
